if not exists (select * 
               from sys.certificates 
               where certificate_id = cert_id('EncryptionCert')) begin
  create certificate EncryptionCert encryption by
    password = 'dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m'
    with subject = 'Encryption Certificate',
    start_date = '20100101',
    expiry_date = '20790101'
end
GO

if not exists (select *
               from sys.symmetric_keys 
               where symmetric_key_id = key_id('EncryptionKey')) begin
  create symmetric key EncryptionKey
    with algorithm = des
    encryption by certificate EncryptionCert
end
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
declare @procedure_nm nvarchar(200)

declare sp_curs cursor for
  select ''drop procedure dbo.'' + [name] 
  from sys.objects 
  where type in (N''P'')
    and is_ms_shipped = 0
  order by [name]

  open sp_curs
  fetch next from sp_curs into @procedure_nm
  while (@@fetch_status=0) begin
    exec sp_executesql @procedure_nm
    fetch next from sp_curs into @procedure_nm
  end
  close sp_curs
deallocate sp_curs'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
declare @function_nm nvarchar(200)

declare udf_curs cursor for
  select ''drop function dbo.'' + [name]
  from sys.objects 
  where type in (N''FN'')
  order by [name]

  open udf_curs
  fetch next from udf_curs into @function_nm 
  while (@@fetch_status=0) begin
    exec sp_executesql @function_nm 
    fetch next from udf_curs into @function_nm 
  end
  close udf_curs
deallocate udf_curs'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[EncryptString]
(
  @String varchar(100)
)
RETURNS varbinary(128)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @EncryptedString varbinary(128)

  set @EncryptedString = EncryptByKey(Key_GUID(''EncryptionKey''), @String)

  return @EncryptedString

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[DecryptString]
(
  @String varbinary(128)
)
RETURNS varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @DecryptedString varchar(100)

  set @DecryptedString = convert(varchar(100), DecryptByKey(@String))

  return @DecryptedString

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetPaymentTotal]
(
  @SalesID int,
  @PaymentTypeID tinyint
)
RETURNS money
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @TotalAmount money

  if (@PaymentTypeID = 0) begin
    select @TotalAmount = sum(round(isnull(PaidAmount, 0), 2))
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and Voided = 0
  end
  else begin
    select @TotalAmount = sum(round(isnull(PaidAmount, 0), 2))
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PaymentTypeID = @PaymentTypeID
      and Voided = 0
  end

  return isnull(@TotalAmount, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetTipTotal]
(
  @SalesID int,
  @PaymentTypeID tinyint
)
RETURNS money
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @TotalAmount money

  if (@PaymentTypeID in (1, 2, 6, 9, 11)) begin
    select @TotalAmount = sum(isnull(TipAmount, 0))
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PaymentTypeID = @PaymentTypeID
      and Voided = 0
  end
  else if (@PaymentTypeID in (3, 4, 5, 7, 8)) begin
    select @TotalAmount = sum(isnull(TipAmount, 0))
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PaymentTypeID in (3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
      and Voided = 0
  end
  else begin
    select @TotalAmount = sum(isnull(TipAmount, 0))
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and Voided = 0
  end  

  return isnull(@TotalAmount, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetRGBColorValue]
(
  @color_value int
)
RETURNS varchar(11)
AS
BEGIN
  declare @tmp_color_value int, @result varchar(24), 
          @R tinyint, @G tinyint, @B tinyint, @bit bit, @bit_position tinyint

  set @color_value = abs(@color_value)
  set @tmp_color_value = 0
  set @result = ''''
  set @R = 0
  set @G = 0
  set @B = 0
  set @bit_position = 1

  while @color_value > 0 begin
    set @tmp_color_value = @color_value / 2
    set @result = @result + cast((@color_value % 2) as varchar)
    set @color_value = @tmp_color_value
  end

  set @result = replicate(''0'', 24 - len(reverse(@result))) + reverse(@result)

  while @bit_position <= 24 begin
    set @bit = convert(bit, substring(@result, @bit_position, 1))
    if (@bit_position <= 8)
      set @B = @B + (@bit * power(2, 8-(case when @bit_position%8 = 0 then 8 else @bit_position%8 end)))
    else if (@bit_position >= 9 and @bit_position <= 16)
      set @G = @G + (@bit * power(2, 8-(case when @bit_position%8 = 0 then 8 else @bit_position%8 end)))
    else 
      set @R = @R + (@bit * power(2, 8-(case when @bit_position%8 = 0 then 8 else @bit_position%8 end)))
    set @bit_position = @bit_position + 1
  end

  return cast(@R as varchar) + ''|'' + cast(@G as varchar) + ''|'' + cast(@B as varchar)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[IsExtraChargeItem]
(
  @ItemID smallint
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN

  declare @IsExtraChargeItem bit

  if exists (select *
             from tblAvailableSize a, tblItem i
             where a.ItemID = i.ID
               and a.SizeID = 1
               and i.ID = @ItemID
               and i.Taste = 1
               and a.UnitPrice > 0) 
     or
     exists (select *
             from tblItem
             where ID = @ItemID
               and Taste = 1
               and OpenItem = 1)

    set @IsExtraChargeItem = 1

  else

    set @IsExtraChargeItem = 0

  return @IsExtraChargeItem

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetHourCharge] 
(
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @PersonIndex tinyint
)
RETURNS smallmoney
AS
BEGIN

  declare @UnitPrice smallmoney, @HourCharge smallmoney, @ApplyBaseRate bit, @BaseRateAppliedMinutes tinyint

  select @UnitPrice = UnitPrice
  from tblAvailableSize
  where ItemID = @ItemID
    and SizeID = 1

  select @ApplyBaseRate = case upper(dbo.GetMiscValue(''ABRTI'')) when ''TRUE'' then 1 else 0 end 
  select @BaseRateAppliedMinutes = convert(int, dbo.GetMiscValue(''BRAM''))

  select @HourCharge = case when (isnull(@ApplyBaseRate, 0) = 1) and sum(datediff(n, StartDateTime, case when [Stopped] = 1 then EndDateTime else convert(smalldatetime, getdate()) end)) < @BaseRateAppliedMinutes then round(isnull(@UnitPrice, 0) / (60.0 / @BaseRateAppliedMinutes), 2)
                            else sum(round((datediff(n, StartDateTime, case when [Stopped] = 1 then EndDateTime else convert(smalldatetime, getdate()) end) / 60.0) * isnull(@UnitPrice, 0), 2))
                       end
  from tblTimeStartEnd
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and ItemID = @ItemID
    and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex

  return isnull(@HourCharge, isnull(@UnitPrice, 0))

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetHourChargeStatus]
(
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @PersonIndex tinyint
)
RETURNS varchar(10)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Stopped bit, @Status varchar(10)

  select @Stopped = t.Stopped
  from tblTimeStartEnd t
  where t.SalesID = @SalesID
    and t.ItemID = @ItemID
    and t.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
    and exists (select t2.SalesID, t2.ItemID, max(t2.ID)
                from tblTimeStartEnd t2
                where t2.SalesID = t.SalesID
                  and t2.ItemID = t.ItemID
                  and t2.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
                group by t2.SalesID, t2.ItemID
                having max(t2.ID) = t.ID)
	
  set @Status = case when isnull(@Stopped, 0) = 1 then ''Stopped'' else '''' end                              
   
  --set @Status = case when isnull(@Stopped, 0) = 1 then 
  --                     ''Stopped'' + case when dbo.CheckIfSplitTimeChargeItemExists(@SalesID, @ItemID, @PersonIndex) = 1 then ''(S)'' else '''' end                              
  --                   else '''' 
  --              end

  return @Status

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetMiscValue]
(
  @Code varchar(5)
)
RETURNS varchar(255)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Value varchar(255)

  select @Value = [Value]
  from tblMisc
  where Code = @Code

  return ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@Value, '''')))

END'
GO

CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[CleanupInvalidChars]
(
  @String varchar(255)
)
RETURNS varchar(255)
AS
BEGIN

  declare @CleanedupString varchar(255)

  set @CleanedupString = replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(
                         @String, '','', ''''), 
                                  '';'', ''''),
                                  ''\'', ''''),
                                  ''^'', ''''),
                                  ''`'', ''''),
                                  ''|'', ''''),
                                  ''~'', ''''),
                                  '''''''', '''')

  return @CleanedupString

END'
GO

  @ErrorDescription varchar(3000),
  @ErrorStoredProcedureName varchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblErrorLog (ErrorDateTime, ErrorDescription, ErrorStoredProcedureName)
  values (getdate(), @ErrorDescription, @ErrorStoredProcedureName)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetErrorLog]
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblErrorLog
  where ErrorDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and ErrorDateTime <  dateadd(d, 1, @ToDateTime)
  order by ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByHour]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID    
    from tblStation
  end

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin
    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */
    end
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin    
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */  
    end
    else begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  declare @i tinyint

  select 0 as SalesHour
  into #tmp_hour

  set @i = 1
  while @i <= 23 begin
    insert into #tmp_hour (SalesHour)
    values (@i)
    set @i = @i + 1
  end

  select t.SalesHour,
         case when t.SalesHour < 12 then replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour))) + convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour) + '' AM''
              when t.SalesHour = 12 then convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour) + '' PM''
              when t.SalesHour > 12 then replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour - 12))) + convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour - 12) + 
                                         case when t.SalesHour + 1 = 24 then '' AM'' else '' PM'' end
         end + '' - '' +
         case when t.SalesHour + 1 < 12 then replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour + 1))) + convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour + 1) + '' AM''
              when t.SalesHour + 1 = 12 then convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour + 1) + '' PM''
              when t.SalesHour + 1 > 12 then replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour - 11))) + convert(varchar(2), t.SalesHour - 11) + '' PM''
         end as SalesHourRange,
         isnull(s.TransCount, 0) as TransCount, 
         isnull(s.TotalAmt, 0) as TotalAmt,
         isnull(s.TotalTaxAmt, 0) as TotalTaxAmt
  from #tmp_hour t left join (select datepart(hh, s1.SaleDateTime) as SalesHour, 
                                     count(s1.ID) as TransCount, 
                                     isnull(round(sum(s1.SubTotal - s1.DSCAmt + s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt + s1.PST2Amt),2),0) as TotalAmt,
                                     isnull(round(sum(s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt + s1.PST2Amt),2),0) as TotalTaxAmt
                              from tblSales s1
                                inner join #tmp_station t1 on s1.StationID = t1.StationID
                              where s1.TransType in (0, 1)
                                and s1.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
                                and s1.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
                                and case when @EmployeeID > 0 then 
                                           case when s1.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
                                         else 1
                                    end = 1
                              group by datepart(hh, s1.SaleDateTime)) s on t.SalesHour = s.SalesHour
  order by t.SalesHour

  drop table #tmp_hour
  drop table #tmp_station

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByDay]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID    
    from tblStation
  end

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin
    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */
    end
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */
    end
    else begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  declare @i tinyint

  select 0 as WeekDayIndex, datename(dw, 0) as WeekDayName
  into #tmp_day

  set @i = 1
  while @i <= 7 begin
    insert into #tmp_day (WeekDayIndex, WeekDayName)
    select @i, datename(dw, @i - 2)
    set @i = @i + 1
  end

  delete
  from #tmp_day
  where WeekDayIndex = 0

  select t.WeekDayIndex,
         t.WeekDayName, 
         isnull(s.TransCount, 0) as TransCount, 
         isnull(s.TotalAmt, 0) as TotalAmt,
         isnull(s.TotalTaxAmt, 0) as TotalTaxAmt
  from #tmp_day t left join (select datepart(dw, s1.SaleDateTime) as WeekDayIndex, 
                                    count(s1.ID) as TransCount, 
                                    isnull(round(sum(s1.SubTotal - s1.DSCAmt + s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt + s1.PST2Amt),2),0) as TotalAmt,
                                    isnull(round(sum(s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt + s1.PST2Amt),2),0) as TotalTaxAmt
                             from tblSales s1
                               inner join #tmp_station t1 on s1.StationID = t1.StationID
                             where s1.TransType in (0, 1)
                               and s1.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
                               and s1.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
                               and case when @EmployeeID > 0 then 
                                          case when s1.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
                                        else 1
                                   end = 1
                             group by datepart(dw, s1.SaleDateTime)) s on t.WeekDayIndex = s.WeekDayIndex
  order by t.WeekDayIndex

  drop table #tmp_day
  drop table #tmp_station

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteMenuLayout] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblMenuLayout) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuLayoutBackup]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U''))
      drop table tmpMenuLayoutBackup

    select *
    into tmpMenuLayoutBackup
    from tblMenuLayout

  end
  
  delete 
  from tblMenuLayout
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RestoreLastSavedMenuLayout]
  @LayoutModeType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete 
  from tblMenuLayout
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

  insert into tblMenuLayout
  select *
  from tmpMenuLayoutBackup
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByMonth]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID    
    from tblStation
  end

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin
    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */
    end
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin    
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */  
    end
    else begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  declare @i tinyint

  select 0 as MonthIndex, ''         '' as [MonthName]
  into #tmp_month

  set @i = 1
  while @i <= 12 begin
    insert into #tmp_month (MonthIndex, [MonthName])
    select @i, case @i when 1 then ''January''
                       when 2 then ''February''
                       when 3 then ''March''
                       when 4 then ''April''
                       when 5 then ''May''
                       when 6 then ''June''
                       when 7 then ''July''
                       when 8 then ''August''
                       when 9 then ''September''
                       when 10 then ''October''
                       when 11 then ''November''
                       when 12 then ''December''                    
               end
    set @i = @i + 1
  end

  delete
  from #tmp_month
  where MonthIndex = 0

  select t.MonthIndex,
         t.[MonthName], 
         isnull(s.TransCount, 0) as TransCount, 
         isnull(s.TotalAmt, 0) as TotalAmt,
         isnull(s.TotalTaxAmt, 0) as TotalTaxAmt
  from #tmp_month t left join (select datepart(mm, s1.SaleDateTime) as MonthIndex, 
                                      count(s1.ID) as TransCount, 
                                      isnull(round(sum(s1.SubTotal - s1.DSCAmt + s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt),2),0) as TotalAmt,
                                      isnull(round(sum(s1.GSTAmt + s1.PSTAmt),2),0) as TotalTaxAmt
                               from tblSales s1
                                 inner join #tmp_station t1 on s1.StationID = t1.StationID
                               where s1.TransType in (0, 1)
                                 and s1.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
                                 and s1.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
                                 and case when @EmployeeID > 0 then 
                                            case when s1.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
                                          else 1
                                     end = 1
                               group by datepart(mm, s1.SaleDateTime)) s on t.MonthIndex = s.MonthIndex
  order by t.MonthIndex

  drop table #tmp_month  
  drop table #tmp_station

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPayment]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select p.ID, p.SalesID, p.PaymentTypeID, p.PaidAmount, p.TipAmount,
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber) end as CardNumber, 
         case when p.CardExpiryDate is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardExpiryDate) end as CardExpiryDate,
         isnull(p.AuthorizationNo, '''') as AuthorizationNo, 
         --isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''') as SequenceNo,
         case when charindex(''['', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, 1, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransPaymentID,
         case when charindex('']'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransOrderID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransReferenceID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, 32) else '''' end as CardTransExternalPaymentID,
         isnull(p.CardReceipt, '''') as CardReceipt,
         pt.PaymentType,
         case p.Voided when 1 then ''Voided'' else '''' end as [Status],
         --p.BatchNo, p.ItemNo, p.RevisionNo, 
         p.BatchClosed,   
         dbo.ExtractCloverTransactionDateTime(p.CardReceipt) as CardTransDateTime,     
         replace(substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'') + '' '' + 
           substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 109), 13, 8) + '' '' + 
           substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 109), 25, 2) as PaidDateTime
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
  order by p.ID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCardReceipt]
  @SalesID int,
  @PaymentTypeID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblPayment
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and case when @PaymentTypeID > 0 then
               case when PaymentTypeID = @PaymentTypeID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               case when PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8) then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and isnull(CardReceipt, '''') <> ''''
  order by ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPaidAmount]
  @SalesID int,
  @TotalPaidAmount smallmoney = 0 output,
  @TotalPaidTipAmount smallmoney = 0 output
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @TotalPaidAmount = sum(PaidAmount),
         @TotalPaidTipAmount = sum(TipAmount)
  from tblPayment
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and Voided = 0

  set @TotalPaidAmount = isnull(@TotalPaidAmount, 0)
  set @TotalPaidTipAmount = isnull(@TotalPaidTipAmount, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTableInfo] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @ShowOrders bit
  --@ShowSubTotal bit
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  exec sp_AssignUnlinkedOrdersToEmptyTables

  --declare @tmp_subTotal_by_table table
  --(
  --  [ID] [int] NOT NULL,
  --  [SubTotal] [smallmoney] NOT NULL
  --)

  --if (@ShowSubTotal = 1) begin

  --  insert into @tmp_subTotal_by_table (ID, SubTotal)
  --  select t.ID, sum(round(p.Qty * p.UnitPrice, 2)) as SubTotal    
  --  from tblTable t, tblPendingOrders p
  --  where t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
  --  group by t.ID

  --end

  select distinct t.ID, dbo.CheckIfAnyTimeChargedItemStopped(p.SalesID) as StoppedItemExists
  into #tmp_tables_with_time_charged_item
  from tblPendingOrders p
    inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblTable t on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where p.SizeID = 1
    and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1
    and p.Qty > 0

  if (@ShowOrders = 1) begin

    select t.*, 
           substring(convert(varchar, t.TimeIn, 107), 1, 7) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, t.TimeIn, 100), 13, 7) as OrderedTime,
           case when (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) / 60) > 0 then
                  convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) / 60)) + '' hrs ''
                else ''''
           end +
           convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) % 60)) + '' min'' as ElapsedTime,
           case isnull(u.ID, 0) when 1 then ''Default''
                                when 0 then ''''
                                else u.FName 
           end as [Server],
           p.Qty, 
           case SizeID when 1 then case when ltrim(rtrim(isnull(p.ItemName2, ''''))) = '''' then p.ItemName 
                                        else p.ItemName2 
                                   end 
                       else ''('' + p.SizeName + '')'' + case when ltrim(rtrim(isnull(p.ItemName2, ''''))) = '''' then p.ItemName 
                                                          else p.ItemName2 
                                                     end 
           end as ItemName,
           --isnull(s.SubTotal, 0) as SubTotal,
           tl.Caption,
           cast(case when ((ltrim(rtrim(t.OnlineOrderNumber)) <> '''') or (t.OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0)) and 
                          (abs(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(t.OrderNum, 0) - t.TotalAmt) <= 0.03) then 1 else 0 end as bit) as FullyPaid,
           isnull(c.PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, 0) as PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber,
           isnull(c.[Integrated], 0) as IntegratedOnlineOrderTable
    into #tmp_tables1
    from tblTable t   
      left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
      left join tblPendingOrders p on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID  
      left join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
      --left join @tmp_subTotal_by_table s on t.ID = s.ID
      inner join (select TableID, Caption
                  from tblTableLayout
                  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
                    and TableID > 0) tl on tl.TableID = t.ID
    where t.linked = 1 

    select t.*, cast(case when isnull(tci.ID, 0) > 0 then 1 else 0 end as bit) as IsWithTimeChargedItem
    from #tmp_tables1 t
      left join #tmp_tables_with_time_charged_item tci on tci.ID = t.ID

    drop table #tmp_tables1

  end
  else begin
  
    select t.*, 
           substring(convert(varchar, t.TimeIn, 107), 1, 7) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, t.TimeIn, 100), 13, 7) as OrderedTime,
           case when (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) / 60) > 0 then
                  convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) / 60)) + '' hrs ''
                else ''''
           end +
           convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, convert(smalldatetime, getdate())) % 60)) + '' min'' as ElapsedTime,
           case isnull(u.ID, 0) when 1 then ''Default''
                                when 0 then ''''
                                else u.FName 
           end as [Server],
           --isnull(s.SubTotal, 0) as SubTotal,
           tl.Caption,
           cast(case when ((ltrim(rtrim(t.OnlineOrderNumber)) <> '''') or (t.OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0)) and 
                          (abs(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(t.OrderNum, 0) - t.TotalAmt) <= 0.03) then 1 else 0 end as bit) as FullyPaid,
           isnull(c.PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, 0) as PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber,
           isnull(c.[Integrated], 0) as IntegratedOnlineOrderTable
    into #tmp_tables2
    from tblTable t  
      left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID 
      left join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
      --left join @tmp_subTotal_by_table s on t.ID = s.ID
      inner join (select TableID, Caption
                  from tblTableLayout
                  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
                    and TableID > 0) tl on tl.TableID = t.ID
    where t.linked = 1

    select t.*, cast(case when isnull(tci.ID, 0) > 0 then 1 else 0 end as bit) as IsWithTimeChargedItem, 
           isnull(tci.StoppedItemExists, 0) as StoppedItemExists
    from #tmp_tables2 t
      left join #tmp_tables_with_time_charged_item tci on tci.ID = t.ID

    drop table #tmp_tables2

  end

  drop table #tmp_tables_with_time_charged_item

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByEmployee]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
 
  select U.ID, 
         (U.FName + '' '' + U.LName) as Employee, 
         isnull(U.TipOutPercentage, 0) as TipOutPercentage, 
         count(S.ID) as TransCount,
         sum(round(isnull(S.SubTotal - S.DSCAmt + S.GSTAmt + S.PSTAmt + S.PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt, 
         sum(round(isnull(S.SubTotal - S.DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt, 
         sum(round(isnull(S.DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt, 
         sum(round(isnull(S.GSTAmt,0),2)) as GSTAmt, 
         sum(round(isnull(S.PSTAmt,0),2)) as PSTAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(S.PST2Amt,0),2)) as PST2Amt,
         cast(0 as money) as CashPaidAmt,         
         cast(0 as money) as DebitPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as VisaPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as McPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as AmexPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CouponPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as JcbPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as int) as CashPaymentCount, 
         cast(0 as int) as DebitPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as VisaPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as McPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as AmexPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as CouponPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as DiscoverPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as JcbPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as GiftCardPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as RewardPointPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as int) as ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount,
         cast(0 as money) as CashTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as FoodTotal,
         cast(0 as money) as NonAlcoholTotal,
         cast(0 as money) as AlcoholTotal,
         cast(0 as money) as DineInTotal,
         cast(0 as int) as DineInCount,
         cast(0 as money) as TakeOutTotal,
         cast(0 as int) as TakeOutCount,
         cast(0 as money) as DeliveryTotal,
         cast(0 as int) as DeliveryCount,
         cast(0 as money) as OnlineTotal,
         cast(0 as int) as OnlineCount
  into #tmp_employee_summary
  from tblSales S
    inner join tblUser U on S.CashierID = U.ID
  where S.TransType in (0, 1)
    and S.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and S.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1
             else case when S.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
  group by U.ID, (U.FName + '' '' + U.LName), isnull(U.TipOutPercentage, 0) 
  order by (U.FName + '' '' + U.LName)    

  if exists (select *
             from #tmp_employee_summary) begin

    declare @ID int,
            @CashPaidAmt money, @DebitPaidAmt money, @VisaPaidAmt money, @McPaidAmt money, @AmexPaidAmt money, 
            @CouponPaidAmt money, @DiscoverPaidAmt money, @JcbPaidAmt money, @GiftCardPaidAmt money, @RewardPointPaidAmt money,
            @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt money, 

            @CashTipPaidAmt money, @DebitTipPaidAmt money, @CreditTipPaidAmt money, 
            @VisaTipPaidAmt money, @McTipPaidAmt money, @AmexTipPaidAmt money, 
            @CouponTipPaidAmt money, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt money, @JcbTipPaidAmt money, 
            @GiftCardTipPaidAmt money, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt money, @TotalTipPaidAmt money, 
          
            @CashPaymentCount int, @DebitPaymentCount int, @VisaPaymentCount int, @McPaymentCount int, @AmexPaymentCount int, 
            @CouponPaymentCount int, @DiscoverPaymentCount int, @JcbPaymentCount int, @GiftCardPaymentCount int, 
            @RewardPointPaymentCount int, @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount int,

            @FoodSubTotal money, @FoodGSTTotal money, @FoodPSTTotal money, @FoodPST2Total money,
            @NonAlcoholSubTotal money, @NonAlcoholGSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholPSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholPST2Total money,
            @AlcoholSubTotal money, @AlcoholGSTTotal money, @AlcoholPSTTotal money, @AlcoholPST2Total money,

            @DineInTotal money, @TakeOutTotal money, @DeliveryTotal money, @OnlineTotal money, 
            @DineInCount int, @TakeOutCount int, @DeliveryCount int, @OnlineCount int

    declare curs_employee cursor for
      select ID
      from #tmp_employee_summary

      open curs_employee
      fetch next from curs_employee into @ID
      while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
        
        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        exec spr_PaymentSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @ID,
                                @CashPaidAmt output, @DebitPaidAmt output, @VisaPaidAmt output, 
                                @McPaidAmt output, @AmexPaidAmt output, @CouponPaidAmt output,
                                @DiscoverPaidAmt output, @JcbPaidAmt output, @GiftCardPaidAmt output, 
                                @RewardPointPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt output,
                                @CashTipPaidAmt output, @DebitTipPaidAmt output, @CreditTipPaidAmt output, 
                                @VisaTipPaidAmt output, @McTipPaidAmt output, @AmexTipPaidAmt output,
                                @CouponTipPaidAmt output, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt output, @JcbTipPaidAmt output, 
                                @GiftCardTipPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt output,
                                @TotalTipPaidAmt output, @CashPaymentCount output, @DebitPaymentCount output, 
                                @VisaPaymentCount output, @McPaymentCount output, @AmexPaymentCount output, 
                                @CouponPaymentCount output, @DiscoverPaymentCount output, @JcbPaymentCount output, 
                                @GiftCardPaymentCount output, @RewardPointPaymentCount output, 
                                @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount output

        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        /* Food * Non-Alcohol * Alcohol Summary                                                              */
        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        exec spr_GetFoodAlcoholSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @ID,
                                       @FoodSubTotal output, @FoodGSTTotal output, @FoodPSTTotal output, @FoodPST2Total output,
                                       @NonAlcoholSubTotal output, @NonAlcoholGSTTotal output, @NonAlcoholPSTTotal output, @NonAlcoholPST2Total output,
                                       @AlcoholSubTotal output, @AlcoholGSTTotal output, @AlcoholPSTTotal output, @AlcoholPST2Total output

        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        /* Order Type Summary                                                                                */
        /*****************************************************************************************************/
        exec spr_GetOrderTypeSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @ID, 
                                     @DineInTotal output, @DineInCount output, 
                                     @TakeOutTotal output, @TakeOutCount output, 
                                     @DeliveryTotal output, @DeliveryCount output,
                                     @OnlineTotal output, @OnlineCount output
        
        update #tmp_employee_summary
        set CashPaidAmt = @CashPaidAmt,
            DebitPaidAmt = @DebitPaidAmt,
            VisaPaidAmt = @VisaPaidAmt,
            McPaidAmt = @McPaidAmt,
            AmexPaidAmt = @AmexPaidAmt,
            CouponPaidAmt = @CouponPaidAmt,
            DiscoverPaidAmt = @DiscoverPaidAmt,
            JcbPaidAmt = @JcbPaidAmt,
            GiftCardPaidAmt = @GiftCardPaidAmt,
            RewardPointPaidAmt = @RewardPointPaidAmt,
            ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
            CashPaymentCount = @CashPaymentCount,
            DebitPaymentCount = @DebitPaymentCount,
            VisaPaymentCount = @VisaPaymentCount,
            McPaymentCount = @McPaymentCount,
            AmexPaymentCount = @AmexPaymentCount,
            CouponPaymentCount = @CouponPaymentCount,
            DiscoverPaymentCount = @DiscoverPaymentCount,
            JcbPaymentCount = @JcbPaymentCount,
            GiftCardPaymentCount = @GiftCardPaymentCount,
            RewardPointPaymentCount = @RewardPointPaymentCount,
            ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount = @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount,
            CashTipPaidAmt = @CashTipPaidAmt,
            DebitTipPaidAmt = @DebitTipPaidAmt,
            CreditTipPaidAmt = @CreditTipPaidAmt,
            CouponTipPaidAmt = @CouponTipPaidAmt,
            GiftCardTipPaidAmt = @GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
            ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
            TotalTipPaidAmt = @TotalTipPaidAmt,
            FoodTotal = @FoodSubTotal + @FoodGSTTotal + @FoodPSTTotal + @FoodPST2Total,
            NonAlcoholTotal = @NonAlcoholSubTotal + @NonAlcoholGSTTotal + @NonAlcoholPSTTotal + @NonAlcoholPST2Total,
            AlcoholTotal = @AlcoholSubTotal + @AlcoholGSTTotal + @AlcoholPSTTotal + @AlcoholPST2Total,
            DineInTotal = @DineInTotal,
            DineInCount = @DineInCount,
            TakeOutTotal = @TakeOutTotal,
            TakeOutCount = @TakeOutCount,
            DeliveryTotal = @DeliveryTotal,
            DeliveryCount = @DeliveryCount,
            OnlineTotal = @OnlineTotal,
            OnlineCount = @OnlineCount
        where ID = @ID

        fetch next from curs_employee into @ID
      end
      close curs_employee
    deallocate curs_employee 

  end
 
  select *
  from #tmp_employee_summary
 
  drop table #tmp_employee_summary

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_BringUpHistoryOrder]
  @PurchaseOrderID int
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @SenderEmail varchar(100), @RecipientEmail varchar(100),
          @Subject varchar(200), @AttachmentFilePath varchar(200),
          @Message nvarchar(4000)

  select @SenderEmail = SenderEmail,
         @RecipientEmail = RecipientEmail, 
         @Subject = [Subject],
         @AttachmentFilePath = AttachmentFilePath,
         @Message = [Message]
  from tblPurchaseOrder
  where ID = @PurchaseOrderID

  select p.ID, pic.PurchaseItemCategoryName, p.PurchaseItemName, p.Unit, 
         isnull(convert(varchar(20), t.Qty), '''') as Qty,
         @SenderEmail as SenderEmail, @RecipientEmail as RecipientEmail, 
         @Subject as [Subject], @AttachmentFilePath as Attachment, 
         @Message as [Message]
  from tblPurchaseItem p left join (select * 
                                    from tblPurchaseOrderDetail
                                    where PurchaseOrderID = @PurchaseOrderID) t 
                         on t.PurchaseItemID = p.ID,
       tblPurchaseItemCategory pic
  where p.PurchaseItemCategoryID = pic.ID
  order by pic.PurchaseItemCategoryName, p.PurchaseItemName

END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPurchaseOrderedItems]
  @PurchaseOrderID int
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select pic.PurchaseItemCategoryName, p.PurchaseItemName, p.Unit, po.Qty
  from tblPurchaseOrderDetail po, tblPurchaseItem p, tblPurchaseItemCategory pic
  where po.PurchaseItemID = p.ID  
    and p.PurchaseItemCategoryID = pic.ID
    and po.PurchaseOrderID = @PurchaseOrderID
  order by pic.PurchaseItemCategoryName, p.PurchaseItemName

END'
GO

  where p.PurchaseItemCategoryID = pic.ID
    and p.Status = 1

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeletePurchaseItemCategory]
  @PurchaseItemCategoryID int,
  @Deleted bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblPurchaseItem
                 where PurchaseItemCategoryID = @PurchaseItemCategoryID) begin
    delete 
    from tblPurchaseItemCategory
    where ID = @PurchaseItemCategoryID

    set @Deleted = 1
  end
  else
    set @Deleted = 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCalledOrderNumbers]
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select top 8 convert(varchar, OrderNumber) as OrderNumber, 
               --''Called at '' + 
               --substring(convert(varchar, CalledDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' +
               --substring(convert(varchar, CalledDateTime, 109), 25, 2) 
               '''' as CalledDateTime, 
               datediff(s, CalledDateTime, getdate()) as SecondsPassed,
               --''Since called: '' + 
               convert(varchar, datediff(s, CalledDateTime, getdate()) / 60) + '':'' + 
               replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, datediff(s, CalledDateTime, getdate()) % 60))) +
               convert(varchar, datediff(s, CalledDateTime, getdate()) % 60) + '' '' as CalledTimePassed
  from tblOrderNumber
  where datediff(n, CalledDateTime, getdate()) < 30
  order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCalledOrderNumber]
  @OrderNumber int
AS
BEGIN
  -- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
  -- interfering with SELECT statements.
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete
  from tblOrderNumber
  where OrderNumber = @OrderNumber

  insert into tblOrderNumber (OrderNumber, CalledDateTime)
  values (@OrderNumber, getdate())

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByCategory]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @IncludeTaxAmount bit

  set @IncludeTaxAmount = convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAORB''))

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID    
    from tblStation
  end

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin
    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */
    end
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */
    end
    else begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  select c.ID, c.CatName, s.TransType, s.GSTRate, s.PSTRate, s.PST2Rate, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.ApplyPST2,
         case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SoldQty,
         sd.UnitPrice * case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SoldAmt
  into #tmpSummaryByCategory1
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID 
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1) 
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

  select ID, CatName, 
         sum(SoldQty) as SoldQty,
         case when @IncludeTaxAmount = 1 then
                round(sum(SoldAmt + (SoldAmt * (case when ApplyGST = 1 then GSTRate else 0 end +
                                                case when ApplyPST = 1 then PSTRate else 0 end +
                                                case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then PST2Rate else 0 end)) + 0.00001), 2)
              else 
                sum(round(SoldAmt + 0.00001, 2))
         end as SoldAmt
  into #tmpSummaryByCategory2
  from #tmpSummaryByCategory1
  group by ID, CatName 
  
  select sum(round(SoldAmt + 0.00001, 2)) as TotalSoldAmt
  into #tmpSummaryByCategory3
  from #tmpSummaryByCategory2

  select t2.*,
         case t3.TotalSoldAmt when 0 then 0
                              else round(t2.SoldAmt / t3.TotalSoldAmt * 100, 2)
         end as SoldPercentage          
  from #tmpSummaryByCategory2 t2
    inner join #tmpSummaryByCategory3 t3 on 1 = 1
  order by t2.CatName

  drop table #tmp_station
  drop table #tmpSummaryByCategory1
  drop table #tmpSummaryByCategory2
  drop table #tmpSummaryByCategory3

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryBySoldItemCount]
  @AccessLevel tinyint,
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @TotalSalesQty int, @TotalSalesAmount smallmoney

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select c.CatName, i.IName, s.TransType, s.GSTRate, s.PSTRate, s.PST2Rate, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.ApplyPST2, 
         case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SalesQty,
         sd.UnitPrice * case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SalesAmount
  into #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1) 
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime

  if convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAORB'')) = 1 begin

    select @TotalSalesQty = sum(SalesQty),
           @TotalSalesAmount = round(sum(SalesAmount + (SalesAmount * (case when ApplyGST = 1 then GSTRate else 0 end +
                                                                       case when ApplyPST = 1 then PSTRate else 0 end +
                                                                       case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then PST2Rate else 0 end))), 2)
    from #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount

    select CatName, IName, sum(SalesQty) as SalesQty, 
           sum(SalesAmount + (SalesAmount * (case when ApplyGST = 1 then GSTRate else 0 end +
                                             case when ApplyPST = 1 then PSTRate else 0 end +
                                             case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then PST2Rate else 0 end))) as SalesAmount,
           case when @TotalSalesQty = 0 then 0
                else round(sum(SalesQty) * 1.0 / @TotalSalesQty * 100, 2)
           end as SalesQtyPercentage,
           case when @TotalSalesAmount = 0 then 0
                else round(round(sum(SalesAmount + (SalesAmount * (case when ApplyGST = 1 then GSTRate else 0 end +
                                                                   case when ApplyPST = 1 then PSTRate else 0 end +
                                                                   case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then PST2Rate else 0 end))), 2) * 1.0 / @TotalSalesAmount * 100, 2) 
           end as SalesAmountPercentage
    from #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount
    group by CatName, IName
    order by CatName, SalesAmount desc

  end
  else begin

    select @TotalSalesQty = sum(SalesQty),
           @TotalSalesAmount = round(sum(SalesAmount), 2)
    from #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount

    select CatName, IName, sum(SalesQty) as SalesQty, sum(SalesAmount) as SalesAmount,
           case when @TotalSalesQty = 0 then 0
                else round(sum(SalesQty) * 1.0 / @TotalSalesQty * 100, 2)
           end as SalesQtyPercentage,
           case when @TotalSalesAmount = 0 then 0
                else round(round(sum(SalesAmount), 2) * 1.0 / @TotalSalesAmount * 100, 2) 
           end as SalesAmountPercentage
    from #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount
    group by CatName, IName
    order by CatName, SalesAmount desc

  end

  drop table #tmpSummaryBySoldItemCount

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  from tblCategory
  order by CatName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByItem]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @AlcoholOnly bit,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0,
  @ShowAllItems bit = 0
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @IncludeTaxAmount bit

  set @AlcoholOnly = isnull(@AlcoholOnly, 0)
  set @IncludeTaxAmount = convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAORB''))

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID    
    from tblStation
  end  

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin
    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */
    end
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin    
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */  
    end
    else begin
      select @FromDateTime = FromDateTime,
             @ToDateTime = ToDateTime
      from tblClosingReportDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  select s.TransType, s.GSTRate, s.PSTRate, s.PST2Rate, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.ApplyPST2, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID,
         case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SoldQty,
         sd.UnitPrice * case s.TransType when 0 then -1 * sd.Qty else sd.Qty end as SoldAmt,
         case when sd.SizeID > 1 then ltrim(rtrim(sd.ItemName)) + '' ('' + sd.SizeName + '')'' 
              else ltrim(rtrim(sd.ItemName))
         end as IName,
         case when ltrim(rtrim(sd.ItemName2)) <> '''' then
                case when sd.SizeID > 1 then ltrim(rtrim(sd.ItemName2)) + '' ('' + sd.SizeName + '')'' 
                     else ltrim(rtrim(sd.ItemName2))
                end
              else ''''
         end as IName2,
         case when sd.SizeID = 1 then '''' else sd.SizeName end as SizeName,
         --sd.SizeName,
         --case when sd.SizeID > 1 then ltrim(rtrim(i.IName)) + '' ('' + z.SizeName + '')'' 
         --     else ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))
         --end as IName,
         --case when ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2)) <> '''' then
         --       case when sd.SizeID > 1 then ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2)) + '' ('' + z.SizeName + '')'' 
         --            else ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2))
         --       end
         --     else ''''
         --end as IName2,
         --z.SizeName, 
         c.CatName,
         i.BarCode as ItemCode
  into #tmpSummaryByItem1
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
    inner join tblSize z on sd.SizeID = z.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1) 
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @AlcoholOnly > 0 then 
               case when i.Alcohol = @AlcoholOnly then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

  select CatName, ItemID, SizeID, IName, IName2, SizeName, ItemCode,
         sum(SoldQty) as SoldQty,
         case when @IncludeTaxAmount = 1 then
                round(sum(SoldAmt + (SoldAmt * (case when ApplyGST = 1 then GSTRate else 0 end +
                                                case when ApplyPST = 1 then PSTRate else 0 end +
                                                case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then PST2Rate else 0 end)) + 0.00001), 2)
              else 
                sum(round(SoldAmt + 0.00001, 2))
         end as SoldAmt
  into #tmpSummaryByItem2
  from #tmpSummaryByItem1
  group by CatName, ItemID, SizeID, IName, IName2, SizeName, ItemCode

  select CatName, sum(round(SoldAmt + 0.00001, 2)) as TotalSoldAmtByCategory
  into #tmpSummaryByItem3
  from #tmpSummaryByItem2
  group by CatName

  select sum(round(SoldAmt + 0.00001, 2)) as TotalSoldAmt
  into #tmpSummaryByItem4
  from #tmpSummaryByItem2

  if (@ShowAllItems = 0) begin

    select t2.*, 
           case t3.TotalSoldAmtByCategory when 0 then 0
                                          else round(t2.SoldAmt / t3.TotalSoldAmtByCategory * 100, 2)
           end as SoldPercentageInCategory,
           case t4.TotalSoldAmt when 0 then 0
                                else round(t2.SoldAmt / t4.TotalSoldAmt * 100, 2)
           end as SoldPercentage          
    from #tmpSummaryByItem2 t2
      inner join #tmpSummaryByItem3 t3 on t3.CatName = t2.CatName
      inner join #tmpSummaryByItem4 t4 on 1 = 1
    order by t2.CatName, t2.IName

  end
  else begin

    select c.CatName, i.ID as ItemID, s.ID as SizeID, i.IName, i.IName2, s.SizeName, i.BarCode as ItemCode,
           isnull(t2.SoldQty, 0) as SoldQty, isnull(t2.SoldAmt, 0) as SoldAmt,
           case t3.TotalSoldAmtByCategory when 0 then 0
                                          else round(t2.SoldAmt / t3.TotalSoldAmtByCategory * 100, 2)
           end as SoldPercentageInCategory,
           case t4.TotalSoldAmt when 0 then 0
                                else round(t2.SoldAmt / t4.TotalSoldAmt * 100, 2)
           end as SoldPercentage    
    from tblItem i
      inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
      inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
      inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
      left join #tmpSummaryByItem2 t2 on t2.ItemID = i.ID
                                     and t2.SizeID = s.ID
      left join #tmpSummaryByItem3 t3 on t3.CatName = t2.CatName
      left join #tmpSummaryByItem4 t4 on 1 = 1
    where i.Status = 1
    order by c.CatName, i.IName

  end

  drop table #tmp_station
  drop table #tmpSummaryByItem1
  drop table #tmpSummaryByItem2
  drop table #tmpSummaryByItem3
  drop table #tmpSummaryByItem4

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetFoodAlcoholAmt]
  @StrFromDate varchar(19),
  @StrToDate varchar(19)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @FromDate smalldatetime, @ToDate smalldatetime, @GSTRate decimal(5, 4), @PSTRate decimal(5, 4), @PST2Rate decimal(5, 4),
          @SubTotal smallmoney, @DSCAmt smallmoney, @GSTAmt smallmoney, @PSTAmt smallmoney, @PST2Amt smallmoney,
          @FoodAmt smallmoney, @FoodGSTAmt smallmoney, @FoodPSTAmt smallmoney, @FoodPST2Amt smallmoney,
          @NonAlcoholAmt smallmoney, @NonAlcoholGSTAmt smallmoney, @NonAlcoholPSTAmt smallmoney, @NonAlcoholPST2Amt smallmoney,
          @AlcoholAmt smallmoney, @AlcoholGSTAmt smallmoney, @AlcoholPSTAmt smallmoney, @AlcoholPST2Amt smallmoney

  set @FromDate = @StrFromDate
  set @ToDate = @StrToDate
  if (len(ltrim(rtrim(@StrToDate))) > 10) begin
    set @ToDate = dateadd(ss, 1, @ToDate)
  end

  set @GSTRate = 0
  set @PSTRate = 0
  set @PST2Rate = 0
  set @SubTotal = 0
  set @DSCAmt = 0
  set @GSTAmt = 0
  set @PSTAmt = 0
  set @PST2Amt = 0
  set @FoodAmt = 0
  set @FoodGSTAmt = 0
  set @FoodPSTAmt = 0
  set @FoodPST2Amt = 0
  set @NonAlcoholAmt = 0
  set @NonAlcoholGSTAmt = 0
  set @NonAlcoholPSTAmt = 0
  set @NonAlcoholPST2Amt = 0
  set @AlcoholAmt = 0
  set @AlcoholGSTAmt = 0
  set @AlcoholPSTAmt = 0
  set @AlcoholPST2Amt = 0

  select @GSTRate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''GST''))
  select @PSTRate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''PST''))
  select @PST2Rate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''PST2''))

  select @SubTotal = sum(SubTotal),
         @DSCAmt = sum(DSCAmt),
         @GSTAmt = sum(GSTAmt),
         @PSTAmt = sum(PSTAmt),
         @PST2Amt = sum(PST2Amt)
  from tblSales
  where SaleDateTime >= @FromDate
    and SaleDateTime < @ToDate
    and TransType in (0, 1)
     
  select @AlcoholAmt = sum(round((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt, 2)),
         @AlcoholGSTAmt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @GSTRate, 2)),
         @AlcoholPSTAmt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @PSTRate, 2)),
         @AlcoholPST2Amt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @PST2Rate, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDate
    and s.SaleDateTime < @ToDate
    and i.Alcohol = 1
    and s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and sd.Voided = 0

  select @NonAlcoholAmt = sum(round((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholGSTAmt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @GSTRate, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholPSTAmt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @PSTRate, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholPST2Amt = sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * @PST2Rate, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDate
    and s.SaleDateTime < @ToDate
    and i.Alcohol = 0
    and i.NonAlcohol = 1
    and s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and sd.Voided = 0

  set @FoodAmt = (@SubTotal - @DSCAmt) - @AlcoholAmt - @NonAlcoholAmt
  set @FoodGSTAmt = @GSTAmt - @AlcoholGSTAmt - @NonAlcoholGSTAmt
  set @FoodPSTAmt = @PSTAmt - @AlcoholPSTAmt - @NonAlcoholPSTAmt
  set @FoodPST2Amt = @PST2Amt - @AlcoholPST2Amt - @NonAlcoholPST2Amt

  select @SubTotal as SubTotal, @DSCAmt as DSCAmt, @GSTAmt as GSTAmt, @PSTAmt as PSTAmt, @PST2Amt as PST2Amt,
         @FoodAmt as FoodAmt, @FoodGSTAmt as FoodGSTAmt, @FoodPSTAmt as FoodPSTAmt, @FoodPST2Amt as FoodPST2Amt,
         @NonAlcoholAmt as NonAlcoholAmt, @NonAlcoholGSTAmt as NonAlcoholGSTAmt, @NonAlcoholPSTAmt as NonAlcoholPSTAmt, @NonAlcoholPST2Amt as NonAlcoholPST2Amt,
         @AlcoholAmt as AlcoholAmt, @AlcoholGSTAmt as AlcoholGSTAmt, @AlcoholPSTAmt as AlcoholPSTAmt, @AlcoholPST2Amt as AlcoholPST2Amt

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetPrepaidCardSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @DailyChargeAmtOnPC money = 0 output, 
  @DailyUsedAmtOnPC money = 0 output,
  @DailyDiscountAmtOnPC money = 0 output,
  @TotalChargeAmtOnPC money = 0 output,
  @TotalUsedAmtOnPC money = 0 output,
  @TotalDiscountAmtOnPC money = 0 output,
  @TotalBalanceOnPC money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @TotalChargeAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.Amount),0),2),
         @TotalDiscountAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.DiscountAmt),0),2)
  from tblPrepaidCardChargeHistory h
    inner join tblSales s on h.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where h.ChargeDate < @ToDateTime

  select @TotalUsedAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.AmtUsed),0),2)
  from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory h
    inner join tblSales s on h.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where DateTimeUsed < @ToDateTime

  select @DailyChargeAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.Amount),0),2),
         @DailyDiscountAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.DiscountAmt),0),2)
  from tblPrepaidCardChargeHistory h
    inner join tblSales s on h.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID 
  where ChargeDate >= @FromDateTime
    and ChargeDate <  @ToDateTime

  select @DailyUsedAmtOnPC = round(isnull(sum(h.AmtUsed),0),2) 
  from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory h
    inner join tblSales s on h.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID 
  where DateTimeUsed >= @FromDateTime
    and DateTimeUsed <  @ToDateTime
  
  set @DailyChargeAmtOnPC = isnull(@DailyChargeAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @DailyUsedAmtOnPC = isnull(@DailyUsedAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @DailyDiscountAmtOnPC = isnull(@DailyDiscountAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @TotalChargeAmtOnPC = isnull(@TotalChargeAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @TotalUsedAmtOnPC = isnull(@TotalUsedAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @TotalDiscountAmtOnPC = isnull(@TotalDiscountAmtOnPC, 0)
  set @TotalBalanceOnPC = @TotalChargeAmtOnPC - @TotalUsedAmtOnPC  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetOrderTypeSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @DineInTotal money = 0 output,
  @DineInCount int = 0 output,
  @TakeOutTotal money = 0 output,
  @TakeOutCount int = 0 output,
  @DeliveryTotal money = 0 output,
  @DeliveryCount int = 0 output,
  @OnlineTotal money = 0 output,
  @OnlineCount int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if object_id(''tempdb..#tmp_station'') is null begin
    /* Create reporting station list */
    select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
    into #tmp_station 
    from tblStation
  end

  declare @IsTakeOut bit, @IsDelivery bit, @IsOnline bit, @Count int, @Total money

  declare curs_sales cursor for
    select s.TakeOutOrder, 
           case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(tb.Delivery, 0) else 0 end as Delivery, 
           case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(tb.Online, 0) else 0 end as [Online],
           count(*), round(sum(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt),2)
    from tblSales s 
      left join tblTable tb on s.TableID = tb.ID
      inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
    where s.TransType in (0, 1)
      and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1
               else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1
    group by s.TakeOutOrder,
             case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(tb.Delivery, 0) else 0 end,
             case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(tb.Online, 0) else 0 end

    open curs_sales
    fetch next from curs_sales into @IsTakeOut, @IsDelivery, @IsOnline, @Count, @Total
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@IsTakeOut = 0) begin
        set @DineInTotal = @Total
        set @DineInCount = @Count
      end
      else begin
        if (@IsDelivery = 1) begin
          set @DeliveryTotal = @Total
          set @DeliveryCount = @Count
        end
        else if (@IsOnline = 1) begin
          set @OnlineTotal = @Total
          set @OnlineCount = @Count
        end
        else begin
          set @TakeOutTotal = @Total
          set @TakeOutCount = @Count
        end
      end
      fetch next from curs_sales into @IsTakeOut, @IsDelivery, @IsOnline, @Count, @Total
    end
    close curs_sales
  deallocate curs_sales    

  set @DineInTotal = isnull(@DineInTotal, 0)
  set @DineInCount = isnull(@DineInCount, 0)
  set @TakeOutTotal = isnull(@TakeOutTotal, 0)
  set @TakeOutCount = isnull(@TakeOutCount, 0)
  set @DeliveryTotal = isnull(@DeliveryTotal, 0)
  set @DeliveryCount = isnull(@DeliveryCount, 0)
  set @OnlineTotal = isnull(@OnlineTotal, 0)
  set @OnlineCount = isnull(@OnlineCount, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_OrderTypeSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  declare @IsTakeOut bit, @Count int, @Total money, 
          @DineInTotal money, @DineInCount int, @TakeOutTotal money, @TakeOutCount int

  declare curs_sales cursor for
    select TakeOutOrder, count(*), 
            round(sum(SubTotal - DSCAmt + GSTAmt + PSTAmt + PST2Amt),2)
    from tblSales 
    where TransType in (0, 1)
      and SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1
               else case when CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1
    group by TakeOutOrder

    open curs_sales
    fetch next from curs_sales into @IsTakeOut, @Count, @Total
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@IsTakeOut = 0) begin
        set @DineInTotal = @Total
        set @DineInCount = @Count
      end
      else begin
        set @TakeOutTotal = @Total
        set @TakeOutCount = @Count
      end
      fetch next from curs_sales into @IsTakeOut, @Count, @Total
    end
    close curs_sales
  deallocate curs_sales    

  select isnull(@DineInTotal, 0) as DineInTotal,
         isnull(@DineInCount, 0) as DineInCount,
         isnull(@TakeOutTotal, 0) as TakeOutTotal,
         isnull(@TakeOutCount, 0) as TakeOutCount

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetFoodAlcoholSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @FoodSubTotal money = 0 output,
  @FoodGSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @FoodPSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @FoodPST2Total money = 0 output,
  @NonAlcoholSubTotal money = 0 output,
  @NonAlcoholGSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @NonAlcoholPSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @NonAlcoholPST2Total money = 0 output,
  @AlcoholSubTotal money = 0 output,
  @AlcoholGSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @AlcoholPSTTotal money = 0 output,
  @AlcoholPST2Total money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if object_id(''tempdb..#tmp_station'') is null begin
    /* Create reporting station list */
    select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
    into #tmp_station 
    from tblStation
  end
  
  declare @SubTotal money, @GSTTotal money, @PSTTotal money, @PST2Total money,
          @NonAlcoholDSCAmt money, @GSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt money, @PSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt money, @PST2OnNonAlcoholDSCAmt money,
          @NonAlcoholRefundSubTotal money, @NonAlcoholRefundGSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholRefundPSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholRefundPST2Total money,          
          @AlcoholDSCAmt money, @GSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt money, @PSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt money, @PST2OnAlcoholDSCAmt money,
          @AlcoholRefundSubTotal money, @AlcoholRefundGSTTotal money, @AlcoholRefundPSTTotal money, @AlcoholRefundPST2Total money

  select @SubTotal = sum(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt),
         @GSTTotal = sum(s.GSTAmt),
         @PSTTotal = sum(s.PSTAmt),
         @PST2Total = sum(s.PST2Amt),
         @AlcoholDSCAmt = sum(s.AlcoholDSCAmt),
         @GSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(round(s.AlcoholDSCAmt * s.GSTRate, 2)),
         @PSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(round(s.AlcoholDSCAmt * s.PSTRate, 2)),
         @PST2OnAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(round(s.AlcoholDSCAmt * s.PST2Rate, 2)) /* This may have to be like "case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end" as well */
  from tblSales s
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1

  select @NonAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * sd.DiscountAmt),
         @GSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * round(sd.DiscountAmt * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @PSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * round(sd.DiscountAmt * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @PST2OnNonAlcoholDSCAmt = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * round(sd.DiscountAmt * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and i.Alcohol = 0
    and i.NonAlcohol = 1

  select @AlcoholSubTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2)),
         @AlcoholGSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @AlcoholPSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @AlcoholPST2Total = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType = 1
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1

  select @NonAlcoholSubTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholGSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholPSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholPST2Total = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType = 1
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 0
    and i.NonAlcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1

  select @AlcoholRefundSubTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2)),
         @AlcoholRefundGSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @AlcoholRefundPSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @AlcoholRefundPST2Total = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType = 0
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1

  select @NonAlcoholRefundSubTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholRefundGSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholRefundPSTTotal = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)),
         @NonAlcoholRefundPST2Total = sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType = 0
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 0
    and i.NonAlcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
    and case when @EmployeeID = 0 then 1 
             else case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1

  set @AlcoholSubTotal = isnull(@AlcoholSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholRefundSubTotal, 0)
  set @AlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(@AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholRefundGSTTotal, 0)
  set @AlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholRefundPSTTotal, 0)
  set @AlcoholPST2Total = isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholRefundPST2Total, 0)

  set @NonAlcoholSubTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholRefundSubTotal, 0)
  set @NonAlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholRefundGSTTotal, 0)
  set @NonAlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholRefundPSTTotal, 0)
  set @NonAlcoholPST2Total = isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholRefundPST2Total, 0)

  if (isnull(@AlcoholSubTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @AlcoholSubTotal = isnull(@AlcoholSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @AlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(@AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@GSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @AlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@PSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0) > 0)
    set @AlcoholPST2Total = isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@PST2OnAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)

  if (isnull(@NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @NonAlcoholSubTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @NonAlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@GSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) > 0)
    set @NonAlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@PSTOnNonAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)
  if (isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) > 0)
    set @NonAlcoholPST2Total = isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@PST2OnNonAlcoholDSCAmt, 0)

  set @FoodSubTotal = isnull(@SubTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholSubTotal, 0)
  set @FoodGSTTotal = isnull(@GSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholGSTTotal, 0)
  set @FoodPSTTotal = case when (isnull(@PSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0)) < 0 then 0
                           else (isnull(@PSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0))
                      end
  set @FoodPST2Total = case when (isnull(@PST2Total, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0)) < 0 then 0
                            else (isnull(@PST2Total, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0))
                       end

  if (@PSTTotal <> (isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) + isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0))) begin
    set @AlcoholPSTTotal = @AlcoholPSTTotal + (isnull(@PSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0))
    if @AlcoholPSTTotal < 0 
      set @AlcoholPSTTotal = 0
  end
  
  if (@PST2Total <> (isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) + isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0))) begin
