    set @AlcoholPST2Total = @AlcoholPST2Total + (isnull(@PST2Total, 0) - isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) - isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0))
    if @AlcoholPST2Total < 0 
      set @AlcoholPST2Total = 0
  end

  if (@FoodSubTotal + @NonAlcoholSubTotal = 0) begin
    set @AlcoholGSTTotal = @AlcoholGSTTotal + @FoodGSTTotal
    set @AlcoholPSTTotal = @AlcoholPSTTotal + @FoodPSTTotal
    set @AlcoholPST2Total = @AlcoholPST2Total + @FoodPST2Total
    set @NonAlcoholGSTTotal = 0
    set @NonAlcoholPSTTotal = 0
    set @NonAlcoholPST2Total = 0
    set @FoodGSTTotal = 0
    set @FoodPSTTotal = 0
    set @FoodPST2Total = 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_DailySalesSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @CashPaidAmt money, @DebitPaidAmt money, @VisaPaidAmt money, @McPaidAmt money, @AmexPaidAmt money, 
          @CouponPaidAmt money, @DiscoverPaidAmt money, @JcbPaidAmt money, @GiftCardPaidAmt money, @RewardPointPaidAmt money,
          @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt money, 

          @CashTipPaidAmt money, @DebitTipPaidAmt money, @CreditTipPaidAmt money, 
          @VisaTipPaidAmt money, @McTipPaidAmt money, @AmexTipPaidAmt money, 
          @CouponTipPaidAmt money, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt money, @JcbTipPaidAmt money, 
          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt money, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt money, @TotalTipPaidAmt money, 
          
          @CashPaymentCount int, @DebitPaymentCount int, @VisaPaymentCount int, @McPaymentCount int, @AmexPaymentCount int, 
          @CouponPaymentCount int, @DiscoverPaymentCount int, @JcbPaymentCount int, @GiftCardPaymentCount int, 
          @RewardPointPaymentCount int, @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount int

  exec spr_PaymentSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, 0,
                          @CashPaidAmt output, @DebitPaidAmt output, @VisaPaidAmt output, 
                          @McPaidAmt output, @AmexPaidAmt output, @CouponPaidAmt output,
                          @DiscoverPaidAmt output, @JcbPaidAmt output, @GiftCardPaidAmt output, 
                          @RewardPointPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt output,
                          @CashTipPaidAmt output, @DebitTipPaidAmt output, @CreditTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @VisaTipPaidAmt output, @McTipPaidAmt output, @AmexTipPaidAmt output,
                          @CouponTipPaidAmt output, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt output, @JcbTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt output,
                          @TotalTipPaidAmt output, @CashPaymentCount output, @DebitPaymentCount output, 
                          @VisaPaymentCount output, @McPaymentCount output, @AmexPaymentCount output, 
                          @CouponPaymentCount output, @DiscoverPaymentCount output, @JcbPaymentCount output, 
                          @GiftCardPaymentCount output, @RewardPointPaymentCount output, 
                          @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Sales Summary                                                                                     */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  select isnull(count(TransType),0) as TransCount,
         sum(round(isnull(SubTotal - DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(GSTAmt,0),2)) as GSTAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(PSTAmt,0),2)) as PSTAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(PST2Amt,0),2)) as PST2Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(SubTotal - DSCAmt + GSTAmt + PSTAmt + PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt,
         @CashPaidAmt as CashPaidAmt,
         @DebitPaidAmt as DebitPaidAmt,
         @VisaPaidAmt as VisaPaidAmt,
         @McPaidAmt as McPaidAmt,
         @AmexPaidAmt as AmexPaidAmt,
         @CouponPaidAmt as CouponPaidAmt,
         @DiscoverPaidAmt as DiscoverPaidAmt, 
         @JcbPaidAmt as JcbPaidAmt, 
         @GiftCardPaidAmt as GiftCardPaidAmt, 
         @RewardPointPaidAmt as RewardPointPaidAmt,
         @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
         @CashTipPaidAmt as CashTipPaidAmt,
         @DebitTipPaidAmt as DebitTipPaidAmt,
         @CreditTipPaidAmt as CreditTipPaidAmt,
         @VisaTipPaidAmt as VisaTipPaidAmt, 
         @McTipPaidAmt as McTipPaidAmt, 
         @AmexTipPaidAmt as AmexTipPaidAmt, 
         @CouponTipPaidAmt as CouponTipPaidAmt, 
         @DiscoverTipPaidAmt as DiscoverTipPaidAmt, 
         @JcbTipPaidAmt as JcbTipPaidAmt, 
         @GiftCardTipPaidAmt as GiftCardTipPaidAmt, 
         @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt, 
         @TotalTipPaidAmt as TotalTipPaidAmt,
         isnull(sum(Guests),0) as TransGuestCount
  from tblSales
  where TransType in (0, 1)
    and SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_DailySalesSummaryByType]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @NoGroupByType bit = 0
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @HoursShifted smallint

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  if (dbo.IsStoreClosedAfterMidnight() = 1)
    set @HoursShifted = -6
  else
    set @HoursShifted = 0

  select convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)) as SaleDate,
         case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end as TransType, 
         isnull(count(TransType),0) as TransCount,
         sum(round(isnull(SubTotal - DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(GSTAmt,0),2)) as GSTAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(PSTAmt,0),2)) as PSTAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(PST2Amt,0),2)) as PST2Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(SubTotal - DSCAmt + GSTAmt + PSTAmt + PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(AlcoholDSCAmt,0),2)) as AlcoholDSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(AlcoholDSCAmt,0) * GSTRate,2)) as GSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(AlcoholDSCAmt,0) * PSTRate,2)) as PSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(AlcoholDSCAmt,0) * PST2Rate,2)) as PST2OnAlcoholDSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  1),0),2)) as CashPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  2),0),2)) as DebitPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  3),0),2)) as VisaPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  4),0),2)) as McPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  5),0),2)) as AmexPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  6),0),2)) as CouponPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  7),0),2)) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  8),0),2)) as JcbPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID,  9),0),2)) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID, 10),0),2)) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID, 11),0),2)) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  1),0),2)) as CashTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  2),0),2)) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  3),0),2)) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  6),0),2)) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  9),0),2)) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID, 11),0),2)) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(ID,  0),0),2)) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
         isnull(sum(Guests),0) as TransGuestCount,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as FoodSubTotal, 
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as FoodGSTTotal, 
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as FoodPSTTotal, 
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as FoodPST2Total,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as NonAlcoholSubTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as NonAlcoholGSTTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as NonAlcoholPSTTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as NonAlcoholPST2Total,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as AlcoholSubTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as AlcoholGSTTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as AlcoholPSTTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as AlcoholPST2Total,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as DineInTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as TakeOutTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as DeliveryTotal,
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as OnlineTotal,
         cast(0 as smallint) as DineInCount,
         cast(0 as smallint) as TakeOutCount,
         cast(0 as smallint) as DeliveryCount,
         cast(0 as smallint) as OnlineCount
  into #tmp_daily_sales_summary1
  from tblSales
  where TransType in (0, 1)
    and SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  group by convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)), 
           case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end
  order by SaleDate, TransType

  select convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)) as SaleDate,
         case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end as TransType, 
         sum(round((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt, 2)) as AlcoholSubTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)) as AlcoholGSTTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)) as AlcoholPSTTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2)) as AlcoholPST2Total
  into #tmp_daily_sales_summary2
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
  group by convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)), 
           case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end

  select convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)) as SaleDate,
         case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end as TransType, 
         sum(round((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt, 2)) as NonAlcoholSubTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end, 2)) as NonAlcoholGSTTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end, 2)) as NonAlcoholPSTTotal,
         sum(round(((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) - sd.DiscountAmt) * case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end, 2)) as NonAlcoholPST2Total
  into #tmp_daily_sales_summary3
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and i.Alcohol = 0
    and i.NonAlcohol = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
  group by convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)), 
           case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end

  select convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)) as SaleDate,
         case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end TransType,
         s.TakeOutOrder,
         case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(t.Delivery, 0) else 0 end as Delivery, 
         case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(t.Online, 0) else 0 end as [Online],
         count(*) as OrderTypeCount, round(sum(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt),2) as OrderTypeTotal
  into #tmp_daily_sales_summary4
  from tblSales s
    left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  group by convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)), 
           case when @NoGroupByType = 0 then s.TransType else 1 /*Sale*/ end, s.TakeOutOrder,
           case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(t.Delivery, 0) else 0 end,
           case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then isnull(t.Online, 0) else 0 end

  update t1
  set t1.FoodSubTotal = t1.SubTotalAmt - case when isnull(t2.AlcoholSubTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t2.AlcoholSubTotal, 0) /*- t1.AlcoholDSCAmt*/ else 0 end
                                       - case when isnull(t3.NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t3.NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) else 0 end,
      t1.FoodGSTTotal = t1.GSTAmt - case when isnull(t2.AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t2.AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) /*- t1.GSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt*/ else 0 end
                                  - case when isnull(t3.NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t3.NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) else 0 end,
      t1.FoodPSTTotal = t1.PSTAmt - case when isnull(t2.AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t2.AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) /*- t1.PSTOnAlcoholDSCAmt*/ else 0 end
                                  - case when isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) > 0 then isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) else 0 end,
      t1.FoodPST2Total = t1.PST2Amt - case when isnull(t2.AlcoholPST2Total, 0) > 0 then isnull(t2.AlcoholPST2Total, 0) /*- t1.PST2OnAlcoholDSCAmt*/ else 0 end
                                    - case when isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) > 0 then isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) else 0 end,
      
      t1.NonAlcoholSubTotal = isnull(t3.NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0),
      t1.NonAlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(t3.NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0),
      t1.NonAlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0),
      t1.NonAlcoholPST2Total = isnull(t3.NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0),

      t1.AlcoholSubTotal = isnull(t2.AlcoholSubTotal, 0),
      t1.AlcoholGSTTotal = isnull(t2.AlcoholGSTTotal, 0),
      t1.AlcoholPSTTotal = isnull(t2.AlcoholPSTTotal, 0),
      t1.AlcoholPST2Total = isnull(t2.AlcoholPST2Total, 0)
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1 t1
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary2 t2 on t2.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t2.TransType = t1.TransType
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary3 t3 on t3.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t3.TransType = t1.TransType

  update t1
  set t1.DineInTotal = isnull(t4.OrderTypeTotal, 0),
      t1.DineInCount = isnull(t4.OrderTypeCount, 0)
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1 t1
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary4 t4 on t4.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t4.TransType = t1.TransType
  where t4.TakeOutOrder = 0

  update t1
  set t1.TakeOutTotal = isnull(t4.OrderTypeTotal, 0),
      t1.TakeOutCount = isnull(t4.OrderTypeCount, 0)
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1 t1
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary4 t4 on t4.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t4.TransType = t1.TransType
  where t4.TakeOutOrder = 1
    and t4.Delivery = 0
    and t4.[Online] = 0

  update t1
  set t1.DeliveryTotal = isnull(t4.OrderTypeTotal, 0),
      t1.DeliveryCount = isnull(t4.OrderTypeCount, 0)
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1 t1
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary4 t4 on t4.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t4.TransType = t1.TransType
  where t4.TakeOutOrder = 1
    and t4.Delivery = 1
    and t4.[Online] = 0

  update t1
  set t1.OnlineTotal = isnull(t4.OrderTypeTotal, 0),
      t1.OnlineCount = isnull(t4.OrderTypeCount, 0)
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1 t1
    left join #tmp_daily_sales_summary4 t4 on t4.SaleDate = t1.SaleDate
                                          and t4.TransType = t1.TransType
  where t4.TakeOutOrder = 1
    and t4.Delivery = 0
    and t4.[Online] = 1

  select *
  from #tmp_daily_sales_summary1
  order by SaleDate, TransType

  drop table #tmp_daily_sales_summary1
  drop table #tmp_daily_sales_summary2
  drop table #tmp_daily_sales_summary3
  drop table #tmp_daily_sales_summary4

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetLastEmailInfo]
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  select top 1 SenderEmail, RecipientEmail, [Subject], [Message]
  from tblPurchaseOrder
  order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_SaveEmailInfo]
  @PurchaseOrderID int,
  @SenderEmail varchar(100),
  @RecipientEmail varchar(100),
  @Subject varchar(200),
  @Message text,
  @AttachmentFilePath varchar(200)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  update tblPurchaseOrder
  set SenderEmail = @SenderEmail,
      RecipientEmail = @RecipientEmail,
      [Subject] = @Subject,
      [Message] = @Message,
      AttachmentFilePath = @AttachmentFilePath
  where ID = @PurchaseOrderID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPurchaseOrder] 
  @FromDate smalldatetime,
  @ToDate smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblPurchaseOrder
  where PurchaseOrderDate >= @FromDate
    and PurchaseOrderDate < dateadd(d, 1, @ToDate)
  order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPurchaseOrder]
  @SenderEmail varchar(50),
  @RecipientEmail varchar(50),
  @Subject varchar(200),
  @Message text,
  @AttachmentFilePath varchar(200),
  @NewPurchaseOrderID int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblPurchaseOrder (PurchaseOrderDate, SenderEmail, RecipientEmail, [Subject], [Message], AttachmentFilePath)
  values (getdate(), @SenderEmail, @RecipientEmail, @Subject, @Message, @AttachmentFilePath)

  set @NewPurchaseOrderID = scope_identity()
 
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_PayoutSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit  
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @PayType char(5), @Count int, @SubTotal money, @GST money, @PST money,          
          @CashPayoutSubTotal money, @CashPayoutGST money, @CashPayoutPST money, 
          @DebitPayoutSubTotal money, @DebitPayoutGST money, @DebitPayoutPST money, 
          @CreditPayoutSubTotal money, @CreditPayoutGST money, @CreditPayoutPST money, 
          @ChequePayoutSubTotal money, @ChequePayoutGST money, @ChequePayoutPST money, 
          @PayoutSubTotal money, @PayoutGST money, @PayoutPST money, @PayoutTotal money, 
          @PayoutCount int

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  set @CashPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @DebitPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @CreditPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @ChequePayoutSubTotal = 0

  set @CashPayoutGST = 0
  set @DebitPayoutGST = 0
  set @CreditPayoutGST = 0
  set @ChequePayoutGST = 0

  set @CashPayoutPST = 0
  set @DebitPayoutPST = 0
  set @CreditPayoutPST = 0
  set @ChequePayoutPST = 0

  set @PayoutCount = 0

  declare curs_payout cursor for
    select ltrim(rtrim(PayType)), 
           isnull(count(PayType), 0),
           isnull(round(sum(SubTotalAmt), 2), 0),
           isnull(round(sum(GSTAmt), 2), 0), 
           isnull(round(sum(PSTAmt), 2), 0)
    from tblPayOut
    where PayDate >= @FromDateTime 
      and PayDate <  @ToDateTime 
    group by PayType

    open curs_payout 
    fetch next from curs_payout into @PayType, @Count, @SubTotal, @GST, @PST
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@PayType = ''C'') begin
        set @CashPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal
        set @CashPayoutGST = @GST 
        set @CashPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''D'') begin
        set @DebitPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @DebitPayoutGST = @GST
        set @DebitPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''R'') begin
        set @CreditPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @CreditPayoutGST = @GST
        set @CreditPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''Q'') begin
        set @ChequePayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @ChequePayoutGST = @GST
        set @ChequePayoutPST = @PST
      end
      set @PayoutCount = @PayoutCount + @Count
      fetch next from curs_payout into @PayType, @Count, @SubTotal, @GST, @PST
    end
    close curs_payout
  deallocate curs_payout

  set @PayoutSubTotal = @CashPayoutSubTotal + @DebitPayoutSubTotal + @CreditPayoutSubTotal + @ChequePayoutSubTotal
  set @PayoutGST = @CashPayoutGST + @DebitPayoutGST + @CreditPayoutGST + @ChequePayoutGST
  set @PayoutPST = @CashPayoutPST + @DebitPayoutPST + @CreditPayoutPST + @ChequePayoutPST
  set @PayoutTotal = @PayoutSubTotal + @PayoutGST + @PayoutPST

  select @PayoutSubTotal as PayoutSubTotal, 
         @PayoutGST as PayoutGST, 
         @PayoutPST as PayoutPST, 
         @PayoutTotal as PayoutTotal, 
         (@CashPayoutSubTotal + @CashPayoutGST + @CashPayoutPST) as CashPayoutTotal,
         (@DebitPayoutSubTotal + @DebitPayoutGST + @DebitPayoutPST) as DebitPayoutTotal, 
         (@CreditPayoutSubTotal + @CreditPayoutGST + @CreditPayoutPST) as CreditPayoutTotal,
         (@ChequePayoutSubTotal + @ChequePayoutGST + @ChequePayoutPST) as ChequePayoutTotal, 
         @PayoutCount as PayoutCount

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetPayoutSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @PayoutSubTotal money = 0 output, 
  @PayoutGST money = 0 output, 
  @PayoutPST money = 0 output, 
  @PayoutTotal money = 0 output, 
  @CashPayoutTotal money = 0 output,
  @DebitPayoutTotal money = 0 output, 
  @CreditPayoutTotal money = 0 output,
  @ChequePayoutTotal money = 0 output, 
  @PayoutCount int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @PayType char(5), @Count int, @SubTotal money, @GST money, @PST money,          
          @CashPayoutSubTotal money, @CashPayoutGST money, @CashPayoutPST money, 
          @DebitPayoutSubTotal money, @DebitPayoutGST money, @DebitPayoutPST money, 
          @CreditPayoutSubTotal money, @CreditPayoutGST money, @CreditPayoutPST money, 
          @ChequePayoutSubTotal money, @ChequePayoutGST money, @ChequePayoutPST money           

  set @CashPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @DebitPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @CreditPayoutSubTotal = 0
  set @ChequePayoutSubTotal = 0

  set @CashPayoutGST = 0
  set @DebitPayoutGST = 0
  set @CreditPayoutGST = 0
  set @ChequePayoutGST = 0

  set @CashPayoutPST = 0
  set @DebitPayoutPST = 0
  set @CreditPayoutPST = 0
  set @ChequePayoutPST = 0

  set @PayoutCount = 0

  declare curs_payout cursor for
    select ltrim(rtrim(p.PayType)), 
           isnull(count(p.PayType), 0),
           isnull(round(sum(p.SubTotalAmt), 2), 0),
           isnull(round(sum(p.GSTAmt), 2), 0), 
           isnull(round(sum(p.PSTAmt), 2), 0)
    from tblPayOut p
      inner join #tmp_station t on p.StationID = t.StationID
    where p.PayDate >= @FromDateTime
      and p.PayDate <  @ToDateTime
    group by p.PayType

    open curs_payout 
    fetch next from curs_payout into @PayType, @Count, @SubTotal, @GST, @PST
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@PayType = ''C'') begin
        set @CashPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal
        set @CashPayoutGST = @GST 
        set @CashPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''D'') begin
        set @DebitPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @DebitPayoutGST = @GST
        set @DebitPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''R'') begin
        set @CreditPayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @CreditPayoutGST = @GST
        set @CreditPayoutPST = @PST
      end
      else if (@PayType = ''Q'') begin
        set @ChequePayoutSubTotal = @SubTotal 
        set @ChequePayoutGST = @GST
        set @ChequePayoutPST = @PST
      end
      set @PayoutCount = @PayoutCount + @Count
      fetch next from curs_payout into @PayType, @Count, @SubTotal, @GST, @PST
    end
    close curs_payout
  deallocate curs_payout

  set @PayoutSubTotal = @CashPayoutSubTotal + @DebitPayoutSubTotal + @CreditPayoutSubTotal + @ChequePayoutSubTotal
  set @PayoutGST = @CashPayoutGST + @DebitPayoutGST + @CreditPayoutGST + @ChequePayoutGST
  set @PayoutPST = @CashPayoutPST + @DebitPayoutPST + @CreditPayoutPST + @ChequePayoutPST
  set @PayoutTotal = @PayoutSubTotal + @PayoutGST + @PayoutPST
  set @CashPayoutTotal = @CashPayoutSubTotal + @CashPayoutGST + @CashPayoutPST
  set @DebitPayoutTotal = @DebitPayoutSubTotal + @DebitPayoutGST + @DebitPayoutPST
  set @CreditPayoutTotal = @CreditPayoutSubTotal + @CreditPayoutGST + @CreditPayoutPST
  set @ChequePayoutTotal = @ChequePayoutSubTotal + @ChequePayoutGST + @ChequePayoutPST
  
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTable] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @TakeOut bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@TakeOut = 0) begin

    if (@LayoutModeType = 1) or (@LayoutModeType = 2) begin

      select ID, Linked, TakeOut, TableName,
             case Linked when 1 then ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID) + '' (Linked)'' 
                         else ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID) 
             end as LinkedStatus,
             ''Table'' + char(13) + char(10) + ''#'' + rtrim(convert(varchar(3), ID)) as TableNo
      from tblTable 
      where ID <= 200

      union all

      select ID, Linked, TakeOut, TableName,
             case Linked when 1 then ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 100) + '' (Linked)'' 
                         else ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 100) 
             end as LinkedStatus,
             ''Table'' + char(13) + char(10) + ''#'' + rtrim(convert(varchar(3), ID - 100)) as TableNo
      from tblTable 
      where ID > 300
        and ID <= 1099

      order by ID

    end
    else begin

      select t.ID, t.Linked, t.TakeOut, t.TableName,
             tl.Caption as LinkedStatus,
             tl.Caption as TableNo
      from tblTable t
        inner join tblTableLayout tl on tl.TableID = t.ID
      where t.ID <= 200
        and t.Linked = 1
        and tl.LayoutModeType = 1 /* Since linked dine-in tables are applicable for Self-Order */

    end

  end
  else begin

    select ID, Linked, TakeOut, TableName,
           case Linked when 1 then ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 200) + '' (Linked)'' 
                       else ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 200) 
           end as LinkedStatus,
           ''TakeOut'' + char(13) + char(10) + ''#'' + rtrim(convert(varchar(3), ID - 200)) as TableNo
    from tblTable 
    where ID > 200
      and ID <= 300
    
    union all

    select ID, Linked, TakeOut, TableName,
           case Linked when 1 then ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 999) + '' (Linked)'' 
                       else ''#'' + convert(char(3), ID - 999) 
           end as LinkedStatus,
           ''TakeOut'' + char(13) + char(10) + ''#'' + rtrim(convert(varchar(3), ID - 999)) as TableNo
    from tblTable 
    where ID > 1099
      and ID <= 1998

    order by ID
  
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteTableLayout] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblTableLayout) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTableLayoutBackup]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U''))
      drop table tmpTableLayoutBackup

    select tl.*, isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName, t.TakeOut, t.Delivery, t.[Online], t.StayOn, t.ApplySpecialPricing, 
           t.SpecialPricingRate, t.BellNumber, t.StationID, t.OnlineOrderCompanyID, t.AccessPermissionRequired, t.AppliedUnitPriceType
    into tmpTableLayoutBackup
    from tblTableLayout tl
      left join tblTable t on tl.TableID = t.ID
    order by tl.LayoutModeType, tl.TabIndex, tl.[Level], tl.ControlIndex

  end

  update t
  set t.Linked = 0,
      t.TimeIn = getdate(),
      t.ServerID = 0,      
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.TableName = '''',
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      --t.TakeOut = 0,
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,       
      t.BellNumber = 0,
      t.CallType = 255,
      t.Delivery = 0,
      t.[Online] = 0,
      t.StayOn = 0,
      t.PickupDate = getdate(),
      t.TotalAmt = 0,
      t.ApplySpecialPricing = 0,
      t.SpecialPricingRate = 0,      
      t.StationID = 0,
      t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = 0,
      t.AccessPermissionRequired = 0,
      t.AppliedUnitPriceType = 1
  from tblTable t
    inner join tblTableLayout l on l.TableID = t.ID
  where l.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

  update t
  set t.Linked = 0,
      t.TimeIn = getdate(),
      t.ServerID = 0,      
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.TableName = '''',
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      --t.TakeOut = 0,
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,       
      t.BellNumber = 0,
      t.CallType = 255,
      t.Delivery = 0,
      t.[Online] = 0,
      t.StayOn = 0,
      t.PickupDate = getdate(),
      t.TotalAmt = 0,
      t.ApplySpecialPricing = 0,
      t.SpecialPricingRate = 0,      
      t.StationID = 0,
      t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = 0,
      t.AccessPermissionRequired = 0,
      t.AppliedUnitPriceType = 1
  from tblTable t
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblTableLayout l
                    where l.TableID = t.ID)

  delete 
  from tblTableLayout
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RestoreLastSavedTableLayout]
  @LayoutModeType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete 
  from tblTableLayout
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

  insert into tblTableLayout
  select [Level], TabIndex, ControlIndex, TableID, Caption, AlignTop, AlignLeft, Height, Width, FontName, FontSize, 
         FontBold, FontItalic, FontColor, Color, ImageFileName, TableImage, TableImageFileType, LayoutModeType
  from tmpTableLayoutBackup
  where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType

  update t
  set t.Linked = 1,
      t.TableName = tl.TableName,
      --t.TakeOut = tl.TakeOut,
      t.Delivery = tl.Delivery,
      t.[Online] = tl.[Online],
      t.StayOn = tl.StayOn,
      t.ApplySpecialPricing = tl.ApplySpecialPricing,
      t.SpecialPricingRate = tl.SpecialPricingRate,
      t.BellNumber = tl.BellNumber,
      t.StationID = tl.StationID,
      t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = tl.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
      t.AccessPermissionRequired = tl.AccessPermissionRequired,
      t.AppliedUnitPriceType = tl.AppliedUnitPriceType
  from tblTable t
    inner join tmpTableLayoutBackup tl on tl.TableID = t.ID
  where tl.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTableLayout] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @Level tinyint,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select t1.*, isnull(t2.TableName, '''') as TableName, isnull(t2.TakeOut, 0) as TakeOut, isnull(t2.Delivery, 0) as Delivery, 
         isnull(t2.[Online], 0) as Online, isnull(t2.StayOn, 0) as StayOn, isnull(t2.ApplySpecialPricing, 0) as ApplySpecialPricing, 
         isnull(t2.SpecialPricingRate, 0) as SpecialPricingRate, isnull(t2.BellNumber, 0) as BellNumber, isnull(t2.StationID, 0) as StationID,
         isnull(t2.OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0) as OnlineOrderCompanyID, isnull(t2.AccessPermissionRequired, 0) as AccessPermissionRequired, 
         isnull(t2.AppliedUnitPriceType, 1) as AppliedUnitPriceType, 
         isnull(c.CompanyName, '''') as CompanyName, isnull(c.CompanyColor, 0) as CompanyColor, isnull(c.ShowNameOnButton, 0) as ShowNameOnButton, 
         isnull(c.PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, 0) as PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, 
         isnull(c.PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder, 0) as PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder,
         isnull(c.PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, 0) as PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber,
         isnull(c.[Integrated], 0) as IntegratedOnlineOrderTable
  from tblTableLayout t1 
    left join tblTable t2 on t1.TableID = t2.ID  
    left join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on t2.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
  where t1.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
    and t1.[Level] = @Level
    and case when (@LayoutModeType = 3) and (@Level = 1) and (@StationID > 0) then 
               case when (t1.TableID = 0) or (t2.StationID = @StationID) then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by t1.TabIndex, t1.ControlIndex

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertTableLayout]
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @Level tinyint, 
  @TabIndex tinyint,
  @ControlIndex tinyint, 
  @TableID smallint, 
  @Caption varchar(200),
  @AlignTop smallint, 
  @AlignLeft smallint, 
  @Height smallint, 
  @Width smallint, 
  @FontName varchar(20), 
  @FontSize tinyint, 
  @FontBold bit, 
  @FontItalic bit, 
  @FontColor int, 
  @Color int,
  @ImageFileName varchar(100),
  @TakeOut bit,
  @Delivery bit,
  @Online bit,
  @StayOn bit,
  @TableImage image,
  @TableImageFileType varchar(5),
  @ApplySpecialPricing bit,
  @SpecialPricingRate smallint,
  @BellNumber smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint,
  @AccessPermissionRequired bit,
  @AppliedUnitPriceType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert tblTableLayout ([Level], TabIndex, ControlIndex, TableID, Caption, AlignTop, AlignLeft, Height, Width, 
                         FontName, FontSize, FontBold, FontItalic, FontColor, Color, ImageFileName, TableImage, 
                         TableImageFileType, LayoutModeType)
  values (@Level, @TabIndex, @ControlIndex, @TableID, @Caption, @AlignTop, @AlignLeft, @Height, @Width, 
          @FontName, @FontSize, @FontBold, @FontItalic, @FontColor, @Color, @ImageFileName, @TableImage, 
          @TableImageFileType, @LayoutModeType)

  update tblTable
  set Linked = 1,
      TableName = replace(@Caption, char(13) + char(10), '' ''),
      TakeOut = @TakeOut,
      Delivery = @Delivery,
      [Online] = @Online,
      StayOn = @StayOn,
      ApplySpecialPricing = @ApplySpecialPricing,
      SpecialPricingRate = @SpecialPricingRate,
      BellNumber = @BellNumber,
      StationID = @StationID,
      OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID,
      AccessPermissionRequired = @AccessPermissionRequired,
      AppliedUnitPriceType = @AppliedUnitPriceType
  where ID = @TableID
 
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTableLinkedStatus] 
  @TableID smallint,
  @Linked bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblTable
  set Linked = @Linked,
      TakeOut = case when ((@Linked = 1) and 
                           (((@TableID > 200) and (@TableID <= 300)) or 
                            ((@TableID > 1099) and (@TableID <= 1998))
                           )
                          ) then 1 else 0 end
  where ID = @TableID
  
  update tblTableLayout
  set TableID = 0
  where TableID = @TableID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateUnlinkedTables]
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update t 
  set t.Linked = 0,
      t.TakeOut = 0
  from tblTable t
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblTableLayout t2
                    where t2.TableID = t.ID)
    and t.Linked = 1

  update t
  set t.TableID = 0
  from tblTableLayout t
    inner join tblTable t2 on t.TableID = t2.ID
  where t2.Linked = 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetItemsByCategory] 
  @CategoryID tinyint,
  @Status bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select i.*, case when isnull(i.IName2, '''') <> '''' then i.IName + '' ('' + i.IName2 + '')'' else i.IName end as ItemName,
         cast(case when ml.ItemID is null then 0 else 1 end as bit) as LinkedStatus
  from tblItem i
    left join (select ItemID
               from tblMenuLayout
               group by ItemID) ml on ml.ItemID = i.ID
  where i.CategoryID = @CategoryID
    and i.[Status] = @Status
  order by i.IName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetMenuLayout] 
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @Level tinyint 
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@Level <> 2) and (@Level <> 4) begin  

    select m.[Level], m.TabIndex, m.ControlIndex, m.ItemID, m.ItemName, m.Caption, m.AlignTop, m.AlignLeft, m.Height, m.Width, 
           m.FontName, m.FontSize, m.FontBold, m.FontItalic, m.FontColor, m.Color, m.ImageFileName, m.ScaleItem, m.TasteModifier,
           m.NextItemID, m.NextItemName, m.ItemImage, m.ItemImageFileType, m.SoldOut, m.LayoutModeType, 
           isnull(i.OpenItem, 0) as OpenItem, isnull(i.SideDish, 0) as SideDish, isnull(i.Taste, 0) as Taste, 
           isnull(i.GroupItem, 0) as GroupItem, isnull(i.CategoryID, 0) as CategoryID, isnull(i.HourlyChargedItem, 0) as HourlyChargedItem
    from tblMenuLayout m 
      left join tblItem i on m.ItemID = i.ID
    where m.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
      and m.[Level] = @Level
    order by m.TabIndex, m.ControlIndex
  
  end
  else begin /* Taste or Menu Selection Page Level */

    select m.[Level], m.TabIndex, m.ControlIndex, m.ItemID, m.ItemName, m.Caption, m.AlignTop, m.AlignLeft, m.Height, m.Width, 
           m.FontName, m.FontSize, m.FontBold, m.FontItalic, m.FontColor, m.Color, m.ImageFileName, m.ScaleItem, m.TasteModifier,
           m.NextItemID, m.NextItemName, m.ItemImage, m.ItemImageFileType, m.SoldOut, m.LayoutModeType, 
           isnull(i.OpenItem, 0) as OpenItem, isnull(i.SideDish, 0) as SideDish, isnull(i.Taste, 0) as Taste, 
           isnull(i.GroupItem, 0) as GroupItem, isnull(i.CategoryID, 0) as CategoryID, isnull(i.HourlyChargedItem, 0) as HourlyChargedItem
    from tblMenuLayout m 
      left join tblItem i on m.ItemID = i.ID
    where m.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
      and m.[Level] = @Level
      and exists (select *
                  from tblMenuLayout m2
                  where m2.LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
                    and m2.[Level] = @Level + 1
                    and m2.TabIndex = m.TabIndex)
    order by m.TabIndex, m.ControlIndex

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPayment] 
  @SalesID int,
  @PaymentTypeID tinyint,
  @PaidAmount smallmoney,
  @TipAmount smallmoney,
  @CardNumber varchar(20),
  @CardExpiryDate varchar(10),
  @AuthorizationNo varchar(20),
  @SequenceNo varchar(100),
  @CardReceipt nvarchar(4000),
  @BatchNo varchar(1),
  @ItemNo varchar(3),
  @RevisionNo varchar(1),
  @StationName varchar(20),
  @TrackData varchar(100),
  @PaidDateTime datetime
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  insert into tblPayment (SalesID, PaymentTypeID, PaidAmount, TipAmount, CardNumber, CardExpiryDate, AuthorizationNo,  
                          SequenceNo, CardReceipt, BatchNo, ItemNo, RevisionNo, StationName, TrackData, TipAdjusted, PaidDateTime)
  values (@SalesID, @PaymentTypeID, @PaidAmount, @TipAmount, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardNumber, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@CardNumber) end, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardExpiryDate, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@CardExpiryDate) end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@AuthorizationNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @AuthorizationNo end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@SequenceNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @SequenceNo end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardReceipt, ''''))) when '''' then null else @CardReceipt end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@BatchNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @BatchNo end, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@ItemNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @ItemNo end, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@RevisionNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @RevisionNo end,
          @StationName, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@TrackData, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@TrackData) end,
          case when @TipAmount > 0 then 1 else 0 end,
          case when @PaidDateTime is null then getdate() else @PaidDateTime end)

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSetClosingTime]
  @Get bit,
  @HalfDay bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @Now datetime, @ClosingTime varchar(20), @Code varchar(5)
  
  if (@HalfDay = 0) 
    set @Code = ''LCT''
  else
    set @Code = ''HDCT''

  if (@Get = 1) begin
    
    select @ClosingTime = dbo.GetMiscValue(@Code)

  end
  else begin
    set @Now = getdate()
    set @ClosingTime = replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), month(@Now)))) + 
                       convert(varchar(2), month(@Now)) + ''/'' +
                       replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), day(@Now)))) + 
                       convert(varchar(2), day(@Now)) + ''/'' +
                       convert(varchar(4), year(@Now)) + '' '' +
                       replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), datepart(hh, @Now)))) +
                       convert(varchar(2), datepart(hh, @Now)) + '':'' +
                       replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), datepart(n, @Now)))) +
                       convert(varchar(2), datepart(n, @Now)) + '':'' +
                       replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar(2), datepart(ss, @Now)))) +
                       convert(varchar(2), datepart(ss, @Now))

    update tblMisc
    set [Value] = ltrim(rtrim(@ClosingTime))
    where Code = @Code
  end

  select ltrim(rtrim(@ClosingTime)) as ClosingTime

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertMenuLayout]
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @Level tinyint, 
  @TabIndex smallint,
  @ControlIndex tinyint, 
  @ItemID smallint, 
  @OpenItem bit, 
  @SideDish bit,
  @Taste bit, 
  @ItemName varchar(30), 
  @Caption varchar(200),
  @AlignTop smallint, 
  @AlignLeft smallint, 
  @Height smallint, 
  @Width smallint, 
  @FontName varchar(20), 
  @FontSize tinyint, 
  @FontBold bit, 
  @FontItalic bit, 
  @FontColor int, 
  @Color int,
  @ImageFileName varchar(100),
  @ScaleItem bit,
  @TasteModifier bit,
  @NextItemID smallint,
  @NextItemName varchar(200),
  @GroupItem bit,
  @ItemImage image,
  @ItemImageFileType varchar(5),
  @SoldOut bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if ((@Level in (1, 5)) and /* Menu Button should not point to itself. Level 3, which is Taste Button in Taste Group, was not included since NextItemID would be the Size ID */
     (@ItemID > 0) and (@NextItemID > 0) and (@ItemID = @NextItemID)) begin
    set @NextItemID = 0
    set @NextItemName = ''''
  end

  insert tblMenuLayout ([Level], TabIndex, ControlIndex, ItemID, OpenItem, SideDish, Taste, ItemName, 
                        Caption, AlignTop, AlignLeft, Height, Width, FontName, FontSize, FontBold, 
                        FontItalic, FontColor, Color, ImageFileName, ScaleItem, TasteModifier, 
                        NextItemID, NextItemName, GroupItem, ItemImage, ItemImageFileType, SoldOut, LayoutModeType)
  values (@Level, @TabIndex, @ControlIndex, @ItemID, @OpenItem, @SideDish, @Taste, @ItemName, 
          @Caption, @AlignTop, @AlignLeft, @Height, @Width, @FontName, @FontSize, @FontBold, 
          @FontItalic, @FontColor, @Color, @ImageFileName, @ScaleItem, @TasteModifier, 
          @NextItemID, @NextItemName, @GroupItem, @ItemImage, @ItemImageFileType, @SoldOut, @LayoutModeType)
 
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_PaymentSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @CashPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @DebitPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @VisaPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @McPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @AmexPaidAmt money = 0 output,   
  @CouponPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @DiscoverPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @JcbPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @GiftCardPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @RewardPointPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @CashTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @DebitTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @CreditTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @VisaTipPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @McTipPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @AmexTipPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @CouponTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @DiscoverTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @JcbTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @GiftCardTipPaidAmt money = 0 output, 
  @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @TotalTipPaidAmt money = 0 output,
  @CashPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @DebitPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @VisaPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @McPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @AmexPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @CouponPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @DiscoverPaymentCount int = 0 output, 
  @JcbPaymentCount int = 0 output, 
  @GiftCardPaymentCount int = 0 output,
  @RewardPointPaymentCount int = 0 output, 
  @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if object_id(''tempdb..#tmp_station'') is null begin
    /* Create reporting station list */
    select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
    into #tmp_station 
    from tblStation
  end

  declare @PaymentTypeID tinyint, @PaymentCount int, @PaidAmount money, @TipAmount money
 
  set @CashPaidAmt = 0
  set @DebitPaidAmt = 0
  set @VisaPaidAmt = 0
  set @McPaidAmt = 0
  set @AmexPaidAmt = 0
  set @CouponPaidAmt = 0
  set @DiscoverPaidAmt = 0
  set @JcbPaidAmt = 0
  set @GiftCardPaidAmt = 0
  set @RewardPointPaidAmt = 0
  set @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = 0
  set @CashTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @DebitTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @CreditTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @VisaTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @McTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @AmexTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @CouponTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @DiscoverTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @JcbTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @GiftCardTipPaidAmt = 0 
  set @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @TotalTipPaidAmt = 0
  set @CashPaymentCount = 0
  set @DebitPaymentCount = 0
  set @VisaPaymentCount = 0
  set @McPaymentCount = 0
  set @AmexPaymentCount = 0
  set @CouponPaymentCount = 0
  set @DiscoverPaymentCount = 0
  set @JcbPaymentCount = 0
  set @GiftCardPaymentCount = 0
  set @RewardPointPaymentCount = 0
  set @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount = 0

  declare curs_payment cursor for
    select p.PaymentTypeID, 
           --count(p.PaymentTypeID),
           sum(case when p.PaidAmount <> 0 then 1 else 0 end),
           sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)),
           sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2))
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
      inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
    where s.TransType in (0, 1, 9)
      --and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      --and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and p.Voided = 0
      and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
                  case when (s.CashierID = @EmployeeID) then 1 else 0 end
                else 
                  1
          end = 1
    group by p.PaymentTypeID

    open curs_payment
    fetch next from curs_payment into @PaymentTypeID, @PaymentCount, @PaidAmount, @TipAmount
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      if (@PaymentTypeID = 1) begin
        set @CashPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @CashTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount       
        set @CashPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 2) begin
        set @DebitPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @DebitTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @DebitPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 3) begin
        set @VisaPaidAmt = @PaidAmount        
        set @VisaTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @VisaPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 4) begin
        set @McPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @McTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @McPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 5) begin
        set @AmexPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @AmexTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @AmexPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 6) begin
        set @CouponPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @CouponTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @CouponPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 7) begin
        set @DiscoverPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @DiscoverTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @DiscoverPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 8) begin
        set @JcbPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @JcbTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @JcbPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 9) begin
        set @GiftCardPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @GiftCardTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @GiftCardPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 10) begin
        set @RewardPointPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
--        set @RewardPointTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount  /* No option to pay tip with reward points */
        set @RewardPointPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end
      else if (@PaymentTypeID = 11) begin
        set @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = @PaidAmount
        set @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount
        set @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount = @PaymentCount
      end

      fetch next from curs_payment into @PaymentTypeID, @PaymentCount, @PaidAmount, @TipAmount
    end
    close curs_payment
  deallocate curs_payment

  if exists (select *
             from tblMisc
             where Code = ''HTCOA'' /* Hold Transactions Paid By Charge On Account */
               and upper(ltrim(rtrim(Value))) = ''TRUE'') begin

    declare curs_payment cursor for
      select p.PaymentTypeID, 
             --count(p.PaymentTypeID),
             sum(case when p.PaidAmount <> 0 then 1 else 0 end),
             sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2))
      from tblBillCollectHistory bch
        inner join tblSales s on bch.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
      where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        --    p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        --and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        and p.Voided = 0
        and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
                   case when (s.CashierID = @EmployeeID) then 1 else 0 end
                 else 
                   1
            end = 1
      group by p.PaymentTypeID

      open curs_payment
      fetch next from curs_payment into @PaymentTypeID, @PaymentCount, @PaidAmount, @TipAmount
      while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

        if (@PaymentTypeID = 1) begin
          set @CashPaidAmt = @CashPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @CashTipPaidAmt = @CashTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount     
          set @CashPaymentCount = @CashPaymentCount - @PaymentCount  
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 2) begin
          set @DebitPaidAmt = @DebitPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @DebitTipPaidAmt = @DebitTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @DebitPaymentCount = @DebitPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 3) begin
          set @VisaPaidAmt = @VisaPaidAmt - @PaidAmount        
          set @VisaTipPaidAmt = @VisaTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @VisaPaymentCount = @VisaPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 4) begin
          set @McPaidAmt = @McPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @McTipPaidAmt = @McTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @McPaymentCount = @McPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 5) begin
          set @AmexPaidAmt = @AmexPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @AmexTipPaidAmt = @AmexTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @AmexPaymentCount = @AmexPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 6) begin
          set @CouponPaidAmt = @CouponPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @CouponTipPaidAmt = @CouponTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @CouponPaymentCount = @CouponPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 7) begin
          set @DiscoverPaidAmt = @DiscoverPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @DiscoverTipPaidAmt = @DiscoverTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @DiscoverPaymentCount = @DiscoverPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 8) begin
          set @JcbPaidAmt = @JcbPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @JcbTipPaidAmt = @JcbTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @JcbPaymentCount = @JcbPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 9) begin
          set @GiftCardPaidAmt = @GiftCardPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
          set @GiftCardTipPaidAmt = @GiftCardTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
          set @GiftCardPaymentCount = @GiftCardPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        else if (@PaymentTypeID = 10) begin
          set @RewardPointPaidAmt = @RewardPointPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
  --        set @RewardPointTipPaidAmt = @TipAmount  /* No option to pay tip with reward points */
          set @RewardPointPaymentCount = @RewardPointPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        end
        --else if (@PaymentTypeID = 11) begin
        --  set @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt - @PaidAmount
        --  set @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt - @TipAmount
        --  set @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount = @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount - @PaymentCount
        --end

        fetch next from curs_payment into @PaymentTypeID, @PaymentCount, @PaidAmount, @TipAmount
      end
      close curs_payment
    deallocate curs_payment

  end
  
  set @CreditTipPaidAmt = @VisaTipPaidAmt + @McTipPaidAmt + @AmexTipPaidAmt + @DiscoverTipPaidAmt + @JcbTipPaidAmt
  set @TotalTipPaidAmt = @CashTipPaidAmt + @DebitTipPaidAmt + @CreditTipPaidAmt + @CouponTipPaidAmt + @GiftCardTipPaidAmt + @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetDeletedItemsSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @DeletedItemsCount int = 0 output,
  @DeletedAmount money = 0 output,
  @PriceChangedItemsCount int = 0 output,
  @PriceChangedAmount money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @DeletedItemsCount = isnull(sum(di.Qty), 0),
         @DeletedAmount = isnull(sum(di.Qty * cast(di.UnitPrice as money)), 0)
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblDeletedItems di on di.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  
  select @PriceChangedItemsCount = count(di.SalesID),
         @PriceChangedAmount = sum(case when isnumeric(ltrim(rtrim(substring(di.DeleteReason, charindex(''Amount:'', di.DeleteReason) + 8, 10)))) = 1 then 
                                          convert(money, ltrim(rtrim(substring(di.DeleteReason, charindex(''Amount:'', di.DeleteReason) + 8, 10))))
                                        else cast(0 as money) end)
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblDeletedItems di on di.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and upper(di.DeleteReason) like ''%PRICE CHANGE%''

  select @PriceChangedItemsCount = isnull(@PriceChangedItemsCount, 0) + count(di.UserID),
         @PriceChangedAmount = isnull(@PriceChangedAmount, 0) + 
                               isnull(sum(case when isnumeric(ltrim(rtrim(substring(di.DeleteReason, charindex(''Amount:'', di.DeleteReason) + 8, 10)))) = 1 then 
                                                 convert(money, ltrim(rtrim(substring(di.DeleteReason, charindex(''Amount:'', di.DeleteReason) + 8, 10))))
                                               else cast(0 as money) end), 0)
  from tblDeletedUnsavedItems di
  where di.DeletedDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and di.DeletedDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then
               case when di.UserID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and upper(di.DeleteReason) like ''%PRICE CHANGE%''

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /* Create reporting station list */
  select cast(ID as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 
  from tblStation
  where ID = @StationID

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID
    from tblStation
  end

  /* Run sales summary report */
  declare @Count int, @SubTotalAmt money, @DSCAmt money, @GSTAmt money, @PSTAmt money, @PST2Amt money, @TotalAmt money,
          
          @CashPaidAmt money, @DebitPaidAmt money, @VisaPaidAmt money, @McPaidAmt money, @AmexPaidAmt money, 
          @CouponPaidAmt money, @DiscoverPaidAmt money, @JcbPaidAmt money, @GiftCardPaidAmt money, @RewardPointPaidAmt money,
          @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt money, 

          @CashTipPaidAmt money, @DebitTipPaidAmt money, @CreditTipPaidAmt money, @VisaTipPaidAmt money, @McTipPaidAmt money, 
          @AmexTipPaidAmt money, @CouponTipPaidAmt money, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt money, @JcbTipPaidAmt money, 
          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt money, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt money, @TotalTipPaidAmt money, 
          
          @CashPaymentCount int, @DebitPaymentCount int, @VisaPaymentCount int, @McPaymentCount int, @AmexPaymentCount int, 
          @CouponPaymentCount int, @DiscoverPaymentCount int, @JcbPaymentCount int, @GiftCardPaymentCount int, 
          @RewardPointPaymentCount int, @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount int,

          @SalesSubTotal money, @SalesDSC money, @SalesGST money, @SalesPST money, @SalesPST2 money, @SalesTotal money, 
          @RefundSubTotal money, @RefundDSC money, @RefundGST money, @RefundPST money, @RefundPST2 money, @RefundTotal money,  
          @NetSubTotal money, @NetDSC money, @NetGST money, @NetPST money, @NetPST2 money, @NetTotal money,  

          @NetCash money, @NetDebit money, @NetCredit money, @NetVisa money, @NetMc money, @NetAmex money, @NetCoupon money, 
          @NetDiscover money, @NetJcb money, @NetGiftCard money, @NetRewardPoint money, @NetChargeOnAccount money, 

          @NetCashTip money, @NetDebitTip money, @NetCreditTip money, @NetVisaTip money, @NetMcTip money, @NetAmexTip money,
          @NetCouponTip money, @NetDiscoverTip money, @NetJcbTip money, @NetGiftCardTip money, @NetChargeOnAccountTip money,
          @NetTip money,

          @TotalBalanceWithSalesTotal money,
          @TransType tinyint, @TransCount int, @SalesCount int, @RefundCount int, @ChargeOnAccSalesCount int,
          @NoSaleCount int, @TransGuestCount int, @GuestCount int, @VoidCount int, @AverageSaleAmount money,

          @OverHours tinyint

  if (@PartialClosing = 1) begin   
 
    set @ToDateTime = getdate() --convert(varchar, getdate(), 101) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8)

    if (@EmployeeID = 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin
    
      select @FromDateTime = isnull(convert(datetime, dbo.GetMiscValue(''LCT'')), dateadd(d, 1, getdate())) 

      update tblClosingReportDateTime
      set FromDateTime = @FromDateTime,
          ToDateTime = @ToDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''HCR'' /* Half Day Closing Report */   

      update tblMisc
      set [Value] = convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 101) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 114), 1, 8) 
      where Code = ''LCT''
    end 
    else if (@EmployeeID > 0) and (@StationID = 0) begin    
      select @FromDateTime = isnull(LastClosingTime, dateadd(d, 1, getdate()))
      from tblUser
      where ID = @EmployeeID
    
      update tblClosingReportDateTime
      set FromDateTime = @FromDateTime,
          ToDateTime = @ToDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''ECR'' /* Employee Closing Report */

      update tblUser
      set LastClosingTime = @ToDateTime
      where ID = @EmployeeID
    end
    else if (@StationID > 0) begin    
      select @FromDateTime = isnull(LastClosingTime, dateadd(d, 1, getdate()))
      from tblStation
      where ID = @StationID

      update tblClosingReportDateTime
      set FromDateTime = @FromDateTime,
          ToDateTime = @ToDateTime
      where ClosingReportCode = ''SCR'' /* Station Closing Report */

      update tblStation
      set LastClosingTime = @ToDateTime
      where ID = @StationID
    end
  end
  else begin
    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  end

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Sales Summary                                                                                     */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  if (@EmployeeID = 0) begin
    declare curs_summary cursor for
      select s.TransType, 
             isnull(count(s.TransType),0),
             sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.DSCAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.GSTAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.PSTAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.PST2Amt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt,0),2)),
             isnull(sum(s.Guests),0)
      from tblSales s, #tmp_station t
      where s.StationID = t.StationID
        and s.TransType in (0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 9)
        and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      group by s.TransType
  end
  else begin
    declare curs_summary cursor for
      select s.TransType, 
             isnull(count(s.TransType),0),
             sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.DSCAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.GSTAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.PSTAmt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.PST2Amt,0),2)),
             sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt,0),2)),
             isnull(sum(s.Guests),0)
      from tblSales s, #tmp_station t
      where s.StationID = t.StationID
        and s.TransType in (0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 9)
        and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime 
        and s.CashierID = @EmployeeID
      group by s.TransType
  end

    open curs_summary 
    fetch next from curs_summary into @TransType, @Count, @SubTotalAmt, @DSCAmt, @GSTAmt, 
                                      @PSTAmt, @PST2Amt, @TotalAmt, @TransGuestCount
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      if (@TransType = 0) begin
        set @RefundCount = @Count
        set @RefundSubTotal = @SubTotalAmt
        set @RefundDSC = @DSCAmt
        set @RefundGST = @GSTAmt
        set @RefundPST = @PSTAmt
        set @RefundPST2 = @PST2Amt
        set @RefundTotal = @TotalAmt
        set @GuestCount = isnull(@GuestCount, 0) - @TransGuestCount        
      end
      else if (@TransType = 1) begin
        set @SalesCount = @Count
        set @SalesSubTotal = @SubTotalAmt
        set @SalesDSC = @DSCAmt
        set @SalesGST = @GSTAmt
        set @SalesPST = @PSTAmt
        set @SalesPST2 = @PST2Amt
        set @SalesTotal = @TotalAmt
        set @GuestCount = isnull(@GuestCount, 0) + @TransGuestCount
      end
      else if (@TransType = 2) begin
        set @NoSaleCount = @Count
      end
      else if (@TransType in (3, 4)) begin
        set @VoidCount = isnull(@VoidCount, 0) + @Count
      end
      else if (@TransType = 9) begin
        set @ChargeOnAccSalesCount = isnull(@ChargeOnAccSalesCount, 0) + @Count
      end

      fetch next from curs_summary into @TransType, @Count, @SubTotalAmt, @DSCAmt, @GSTAmt, 
                                        @PSTAmt, @PST2Amt, @TotalAmt, @TransGuestCount
    end
    close curs_summary
  deallocate curs_summary

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  exec spr_PaymentSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID,
                          @CashPaidAmt output, @DebitPaidAmt output, @VisaPaidAmt output, 
                          @McPaidAmt output, @AmexPaidAmt output, @CouponPaidAmt output,
                          @DiscoverPaidAmt output, @JcbPaidAmt output, @GiftCardPaidAmt output, 
                          @RewardPointPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt output,
                          @CashTipPaidAmt output, @DebitTipPaidAmt output, @CreditTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @VisaTipPaidAmt output, @McTipPaidAmt output, @AmexTipPaidAmt output,
                          @CouponTipPaidAmt output, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt output, @JcbTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt output,
                          @TotalTipPaidAmt output, @CashPaymentCount output, @DebitPaymentCount output, 
                          @VisaPaymentCount output, @McPaymentCount output, @AmexPaymentCount output, 
                          @CouponPaymentCount output, @DiscoverPaymentCount output, @JcbPaymentCount output, 
                          @GiftCardPaymentCount output, @RewardPointPaymentCount output, 
                          @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Food * Non-Alcohol * Alcohol Summary                                                              */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @FoodSubTotal money, @FoodGSTTotal money, @FoodPSTTotal money, @FoodPST2Total money,
          @NonAlcoholSubTotal money, @NonAlcoholGSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholPSTTotal money, @NonAlcoholPST2Total money,
          @AlcoholSubTotal money, @AlcoholGSTTotal money, @AlcoholPSTTotal money, @AlcoholPST2Total money

  exec spr_GetFoodAlcoholSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID,
                                 @FoodSubTotal output, @FoodGSTTotal output, @FoodPSTTotal output, @FoodPST2Total output,
                                 @NonAlcoholSubTotal output, @NonAlcoholGSTTotal output, @NonAlcoholPSTTotal output, @NonAlcoholPST2Total output,
                                 @AlcoholSubTotal output, @AlcoholGSTTotal output, @AlcoholPSTTotal output, @AlcoholPST2Total output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Order Type Summary                                                                                */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @DineInTotal money, @TakeOutTotal money, @DeliveryTotal money, @OnlineTotal money, 
          @DineInCount int, @TakeOutCount int, @DeliveryCount int, @OnlineCount int

  exec spr_GetOrderTypeSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID, 
                               @DineInTotal output, @DineInCount output, 
                               @TakeOutTotal output, @TakeOutCount output, 
                               @DeliveryTotal output, @DeliveryCount output,
                               @OnlineTotal output, @OnlineCount output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Prepaid Card Summary                                                                              */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @TotalChargeAmtOnPC money, @TotalUsedAmtOnPC money, @TotalDiscountAmtOnPC money, 
          @DailyChargeAmtOnPC money, @DailyUsedAmtOnPC money, @DailyDiscountAmtOnPC money,
          @TotalBalanceOnPC money          

  if (@EmployeeID = 0) begin 
    exec spr_GetPrepaidCardSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime,  
                                   @DailyChargeAmtOnPC output, @DailyUsedAmtOnPC output, @DailyDiscountAmtOnPC output,
                                   @TotalChargeAmtOnPC output, @TotalUsedAmtOnPC output, @TotalDiscountAmtOnPC output,
                                   @TotalBalanceOnPC output
  end

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Refund & Discount Summary                                                                         */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @DSCAmtGeneral money, @DSCAmtEmployee money, @DSCAmtType1 money, @DSCAmtType2 money

  exec spr_GetDiscountSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID,
                              @DSCAmtGeneral output, @DSCAmtEmployee output,  
                              @DSCAmtType1 output, @DSCAmtType2 output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Payout Summary                                                                                    */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @PayoutSubTotal money, @PayoutGST money, @PayoutPST money, @PayoutTotal money, 
          @CashPayoutTotal money, @DebitPayoutTotal money, @CreditPayoutTotal money,
          @ChequePayoutTotal money, @PayoutCount int

  if (@EmployeeID = 0) begin 
    exec spr_GetPayoutSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime,
                              @PayoutSubTotal output, @PayoutGST output, @PayoutPST output, 
                              @PayoutTotal output, @CashPayoutTotal output, @DebitPayoutTotal output, 
                              @CreditPayoutTotal output, @ChequePayoutTotal output, @PayoutCount output
  end

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Credit Summary                                                                                    */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @GivenCreditAmt money, @ReceivedCreditAmt money, @NetCreditAmt money

  exec spr_CreditSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID, 0 /*@CustomerID*/, @GivenCreditAmt output, @ReceivedCreditAmt output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Deleted Items Summary                                                                             */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @DeletedItemsCount int, @DeletedAmount money, @PriceChangedItemsCount money, @PriceChangedAmount money

  exec spr_GetDeletedItemsSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID, 
                                  @DeletedItemsCount output, @DeletedAmount output,
                                  @PriceChangedItemsCount output, @PriceChangedAmount output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Sold Items Summary                                                                             */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  declare @SoldItemsCount int, @SoldAmount money

  exec spr_GetSoldItemsSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @EmployeeID, 
                               @SoldItemsCount output, @SoldAmount output

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Summary                                                                                           */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/  
  set @NetSubTotal = isnull(@SalesSubTotal, 0) + isnull(@RefundSubTotal, 0)
  set @NetDSC = isnull(@SalesDSC, 0) + isnull(@RefundDSC, 0)
  set @NetGST = isnull(@SalesGST, 0) + isnull(@RefundGST, 0)
  set @NetPST = isnull(@SalesPST, 0) + isnull(@RefundPST, 0)
  set @NetPST2 = isnull(@SalesPST2, 0) + isnull(@RefundPST2, 0)
  set @NetTotal = isnull(@SalesTotal, 0) + isnull(@RefundTotal, 0)
  set @NetCash = isnull(@CashPaidAmt, 0) - isnull(@CashPayoutTotal, 0)
  set @NetDebit = isnull(@DebitPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetVisa = isnull(@VisaPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetMc = isnull(@McPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetAmex = isnull(@AmexPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetDiscover = isnull(@DiscoverPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetJcb = isnull(@JcbPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetCredit = @NetVisa + @NetMc + @NetAmex + @NetDiscover + @NetJcb
  set @NetCoupon = isnull(@CouponPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetGiftCard = isnull(@GiftCardPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetRewardPoint = isnull(@RewardPointPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetChargeOnAccount = isnull(@ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetCashTip = isnull(@CashTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetDebitTip = isnull(@DebitTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetCreditTip = isnull(@CreditTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetVisaTip = isnull(@VisaTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetMcTip = isnull(@McTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetAmexTip = isnull(@AmexTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetCouponTip = isnull(@CouponTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetDiscoverTip = isnull(@DiscoverTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetJcbTip = isnull(@JcbTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetGiftCardTip = isnull(@GiftCardTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetChargeOnAccountTip = isnull(@ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt, 0)
  set @NetTip = isnull(@TotalTipPaidAmt, 0)

  set @NetCreditAmt = @ReceivedCreditAmt + @GivenCreditAmt

  set @TotalBalanceWithSalesTotal = @NetTotal + isnull(@DailyChargeAmtOnPC, 0) + isnull(@DailyDiscountAmtOnPC, 0) - isnull(@DailyUsedAmtOnPC, 0)
  
  set @SalesCount = isnull(@SalesCount, 0)
  set @RefundCount = isnull(@RefundCount, 0)
  set @NoSaleCount = isnull(@NoSaleCount, 0)
  set @PayoutCount = isnull(@PayoutCount, 0)
  set @VoidCount = isnull(@VoidCount, 0)
  set @ChargeOnAccSalesCount = isnull(@ChargeOnAccSalesCount, 0)
  set @TransCount = @SalesCount + @RefundCount + @NoSaleCount + @PayoutCount + @VoidCount + @ChargeOnAccSalesCount
  set @DineInCount = isnull(@DineInCount, 0)
  set @TakeOutCount = isnull(@TakeOutCount, 0)
  if (@GuestCount > 0) 
    set @AverageSaleAmount = round(isnull(@NetTotal / @GuestCount, 0), 2)
  else
    set @AverageSaleAmount = 0

  select @NetSubTotal as SubTotal, -1*@NetDSC as DSC, @NetGST as GST, @NetPST as PST, @NetPST2 as PST2, @NetTotal as Total,
         @FoodSubTotal as FoodSubTotal, @FoodGSTTotal as FoodGSTTotal, @FoodPSTTotal as FoodPSTTotal, @FoodPST2Total as FoodPST2Total,
         isnull(@NonAlcoholSubTotal, 0) as NonAlcoholSubTotal, isnull(@NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 0) as NonAlcoholGSTTotal, 
         isnull(@NonAlcoholPSTTotal, 0) as NonAlcoholPSTTotal, isnull(@NonAlcoholPST2Total, 0) as NonAlcoholPST2Total,
         isnull(@AlcoholSubTotal, 0) as AlcoholSubTotal, isnull(@AlcoholGSTTotal, 0) as AlcoholGSTTotal, 
         isnull(@AlcoholPSTTotal, 0) as AlcoholPSTTotal, isnull(@AlcoholPST2Total, 0) as AlcoholPST2Total,
         @DineInTotal as DineInTotal, @DineInCount as DineInCount, @TakeOutTotal as TakeOutTotal, @TakeOutCount as TakeOutCount, 
         @DeliveryTotal as DeliveryTotal, @DeliveryCount as DeliveryCount, @OnlineTotal as OnlineTotal, @OnlineCount as OnlineCount,
         @TotalBalanceWithSalesTotal as TotalSum, @NetCash as NetCash, @NetDebit as NetDebit, @NetCredit as NetCredit, 
         @NetVisa as NetVisa, @NetMc as NetMc, @NetAmex as NetAmex, @NetCoupon as NetCoupon, @NetDiscover as NetDiscover, 
         @NetJcb as NetJcb, @NetGiftCard as NetGiftCard, @NetRewardPoint as NetRewardPoint, @NetChargeOnAccount as NetChargeOnAccount,
         @NetCashTip as NetCashTip, @NetDebitTip as NetDebitTip, @NetCreditTip as NetCreditTip,
         @NetVisaTip as NetVisaTip, @NetMcTip as NetMcTip, @NetAmexTip as NetAmexTip, @NetCouponTip as NetCouponTip, 
         @NetDiscoverTip as NetDiscoverTip, @NetJcbTip as NetJcbTip, @NetGiftCardTip as NetGiftCardTip, 
         @NetChargeOnAccountTip as NetChargeOnAccountTip, @NetTip as NetTip, @CashPaymentCount as CashPaymentCount, @DebitPaymentCount as DebitPaymentCount, 
         @VisaPaymentCount as VisaPaymentCount, @McPaymentCount as McPaymentCount, @AmexPaymentCount as AmexPaymentCount,
         @CouponPaymentCount as CouponPaymentCount, @DiscoverPaymentCount as DiscoverPaymentCount, @JcbPaymentCount as JcbPaymentCount,
