         @GiftCardPaymentCount as GiftCardPaymentCount, @RewardPointPaymentCount as RewardPointPaymentCount,
         @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount as ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount,
         isnull(@DailyChargeAmtOnPC, 0) as DailyChargeAmtOnPC, -1*abs(isnull(@DailyUsedAmtOnPC, 0)) as DailyUsedAmtOnPC, isnull(@DailyDiscountAmtOnPC, 0) as DailyDiscountAmtOnPC,
         isnull(@TotalChargeAmtOnPC, 0) as TotalChargeAmtOnPC, -1*abs(isnull(@TotalUsedAmtOnPC, 0)) as TotalUsedAmtOnPC, isnull(@TotalDiscountAmtOnPC, 0) as TotalDiscountAmtOnPC,         
         isnull(@TotalBalanceOnPC, 0) as TotalBalanceOnPC, isnull(@RefundSubTotal, 0) as RefundSubTotal,
         isnull(@RefundGST, 0) as RefundGST, isnull(@RefundPST, 0) as RefundPST, isnull(@RefundPST2, 0) as RefundPST2, isnull(@RefundTotal, 0) as RefundTotal,
         isnull(@PayoutSubTotal, 0) as PayoutSubTotal, isnull(@PayoutGST, 0) as PayoutGST, isnull(@PayoutPST, 0) as PayoutPST, 
         isnull(@PayoutTotal, 0) as PayoutTotal, isnull(@CashPayoutTotal, 0) as CashPayoutTotal, 
         isnull(@DebitPayoutTotal, 0) as DebitPayoutTotal, isnull(@CreditPayoutTotal, 0) as CreditPayoutTotal, 
         isnull(@ChequePayoutTotal, 0) as ChequePayoutTotal, 
         @GivenCreditAmt as GivenCreditAmt, @ReceivedCreditAmt as ReceivedCreditAmt, @NetCreditAmt as NetCreditAmt,
         @SalesCount as SalesCount, @RefundCount as RefundCount, @NoSaleCount as NoSaleCount, @ChargeOnAccSalesCount as ChargeOnAccSalesCount,
         isnull(@PayoutCount, 0) as PayoutCount, @VoidCount as VoidCount, @TransCount as TransCount, isnull(@GuestCount, 0) as GuestCount,
         @AverageSaleAmount as AverageSaleAmount, 
         -1*@DSCAmtGeneral as DSCAmtGeneral, -1*@DSCAmtEmployee as DSCAmtEmployee,
         -1*@DSCAmtType1 as DSCAmtType1, -1*@DSCAmtType2 as DSCAmtType2,
         isnull(@DeletedItemsCount, 0) as DeletedItemsCount, isnull(@DeletedAmount, 0) as DeletedAmount,
         isnull(@PriceChangedItemsCount, 0) as PriceChangedItemsCount, isnull(@PriceChangedAmount, 0) as PriceChangedAmount,
         isnull(@SoldItemsCount, 0) as SoldItemsCount, isnull(@SoldAmount, 0) as SoldAmount,
         dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX1'') as Tax1Name, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX2'') as Tax2Name, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX3'') as Tax3Name

  drop table #tmp_station

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetConstant]
  @TransType varchar(20),
  @Code char(5),
  @Value char(10)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblConstants
  where [TransType] = @TransType
    and [Code] = @Code
    and [Value] = substring(@Value, 1, charindex('']'', @Value))

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTipAmount]
  @SalesID int,
  @CashTipAmount smallmoney,
  @DebitTipAmount smallmoney,
  @CreditTipAmount smallmoney,
  @CouponTipAmount smallmoney,
  @GiftCardTipAmount smallmoney,
  @ChargeOnAccountTipAmount smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  update tblPayment
  set TipAmount = 0
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  if (@CashTipAmount > 0) begin
    if not exists (select *
                   from tblPayment
                   where SalesID = @SalesID
                     and PaymentTypeID = 1) begin
      declare @PaidDateTime datetime
      set @PaidDateTime = getdate()
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 1, 0, @CashTipAmount, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime
    end
    else begin
      update p
      set p.TipAmount = @CashTipAmount 
      from tblPayment p
      where p.SalesID = @SalesID
        and p.PaymentTypeID = 1
        and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                    from tblPayment p2
                    where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                      and p2.PaymentTypeID = p.PaymentTypeID)
    end
  end
  
  if (@DebitTipAmount > 0) begin
    update p
    set p.TipAmount = @DebitTipAmount 
    from tblPayment p
    where p.SalesID = @SalesID
      and p.PaymentTypeID = 2
      and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                  from tblPayment p2
                  where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                    and p2.PaymentTypeID = p.PaymentTypeID)
  end
 
  if (@CreditTipAmount > 0) begin
    update p
    set p.TipAmount = @CreditTipAmount 
    from tblPayment p
    where p.SalesID = @SalesID
      and p.PaymentTypeID in (3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
      and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                  from tblPayment p2
                  where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                    and p2.PaymentTypeID in (3, 4, 5, 7, 8))
  end

  if (@CouponTipAmount > 0) begin
    update p
    set p.TipAmount = @CouponTipAmount 
    from tblPayment p
    where p.SalesID = @SalesID
      and p.PaymentTypeID = 6
      and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                  from tblPayment p2
                  where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                    and p2.PaymentTypeID = p.PaymentTypeID)
  end 

  if (@GiftCardTipAmount > 0) begin
    update p
    set p.TipAmount = @GiftCardTipAmount 
    from tblPayment p
    where p.SalesID = @SalesID
      and p.PaymentTypeID = 9
      and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                  from tblPayment p2
                  where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                    and p2.PaymentTypeID = p.PaymentTypeID)
  end   

  if (@ChargeOnAccountTipAmount > 0) begin
    update p
    set p.TipAmount = @ChargeOnAccountTipAmount 
    from tblPayment p
    where p.SalesID = @SalesID
      and p.PaymentTypeID = 11
      and p.ID = (select max(p2.ID)
                  from tblPayment p2
                  where p2.SalesID = p.SalesID
                    and p2.PaymentTypeID = p.PaymentTypeID)
  end            

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSalesDetail]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select case when sd.ItemName <> '''' then sd.ItemName else i.IName end as IName, 
         case when sd.ItemName2 <> '''' then sd.ItemName2 else i.IName2 end as IName2,
         case when sd.SizeID > 1 then 
                case when sd.SizeName <> '''' then sd.SizeName else isnull(z.SizeName, '''') end
              else '''' 
         end as SizeName, 
         --i.IName, i.IName2, 
         --case when z.ID > 1 then z.SizeName else '''' end as SizeName, 
         sd.Qty, sd.UnitPrice, round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2) as ExtTotal, sd.DiscountAmt, 
         sd.SalesID, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, s.GSTRate, s.PSTRate, s.PST2Rate, 
         i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.ApplyPST2, 
         dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(sd.Tastes, '','') as Tastes, i.Alcohol
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize z on sd.SizeID = z.ID
  where sd.Voided = 0
    and sd.SalesID = @SalesID
  order by IName, SizeName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSalesTransactions]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ShowVoidTrans bit,
  @OrderBy varchar(50),
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(500)

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderBy)) = '''') set @OrderBy = ''ID desc''

  select s.ID, 
         s.CashierID, 
         s.SaleDateTime, 
         round(s.SubTotal,2) as SubTotalAmt,
         round(s.DSCAmt,2) as DSCAmt,
         round(s.GSTAmt,2) as GSTAmt,
         round(s.PSTAmt,2) as PSTAmt,
         round(s.PST2Amt,2) as PST2Amt,
         round(s.SubTotal-s.DSCAmt+s.GSTAmt+s.PSTAmt+s.PST2Amt, 2) as TotalAmt,        
         cast(0 as money) as CashPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DebitPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as VisaPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as McPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as AmexPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CouponPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as JcbPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CashTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
         case when s.TransType = 0 then ''Refund''
              when s.TransType = 1 then ''Sale''
              when s.TransType = 2 then ''NoSale''
              when s.TransType = 3 then ''Void''
              when s.TransType = 4 then ''SalesVoid''
              when s.TransType = 5 then ''Training''
              when s.TransType = 9 then ''Unpaid''
              else '''' 
         end as TransType,
         s.OriginalTransType, 
         s.DailyOrderNumber,
         isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName,
         rtrim(u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as Cashier, 
         case when soo.OnlineOrderNumber is null then
                rtrim(c.FName + '' '' + c.LName)
              else
                isnull(soo.OnlineOrderCustomerName, '''')
         end as Customer,
         c.CustomerNum,
         c.Phone as CustomerPhone,
         cast(0 as tinyint) as PaymentCount,
         isnull(n.StationName, '''') as StationName,
         isnull(s.CreatedDateTime, s.SaleDateTime) as CreatedDateTime,
         isnull(soo.OnlineOrderNumber, '''') as OnlineOrderNumber,
         isnull(soo.OnlineOrderCustomerName, '''') as OnlineOrderCustomerName,
         isnull(ooc.CompanyName, '''') as OnlineOrderCompanyName
  into #tmp_transactions
  from tblSales s 
    left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
    inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
    inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
    inner join tblStation n on s.StationID = n.ID
    left join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders soo on soo.SalesID = s.ID
    left join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on soo.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and (case when @ShowVoidTrans = 1 then 1
              else case when s.TransType in (3, 4) then 0 else 1 end
         end = 1)

  select s.ID, p.PaymentTypeID, 
         sum(round(isnull(PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount, 
         sum(round(isnull(TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount,
         count(p.PaymentTypeID) as PaymentCount
  into #tmp_payment
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by s.ID, p.PaymentTypeID

  update t
  set t.CashPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CashTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 1

  update t
  set t.DebitPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.DebitTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 2
   
  update t
  set t.VisaPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 3

  update t
  set t.McPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = t.CreditTipPaidAmt + p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 4

  update t
  set t.AmexPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = t.CreditTipPaidAmt + p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 5

  update t
  set t.CouponPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CouponTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 6

  update t
  set t.DiscoverPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = t.CreditTipPaidAmt + p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 7

  update t
  set t.JcbPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = t.CreditTipPaidAmt + p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 8

  update t
  set t.GiftCardPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.GiftCardTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 9

  update t
  set t.RewardPointPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 10

  update t
  set t.ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount,
      t.ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = p.TipAmount,
      t.PaymentCount = t.PaymentCount + p.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_transactions t
    inner join #tmp_payment p on t.ID = p.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID = 11 
  
  update t
  set t.TotalTipPaidAmt = t.CashTipPaidAmt + t.DebitTipPaidAmt + t.CreditTipPaidAmt + 
                          t.CouponTipPaidAmt + t.GiftCardTipPaidAmt + t.ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt
  from #tmp_transactions t

  --update t
  --set t.PaymentCount = p.PaymentCount
  --from #tmp_transactions t
  --  inner join (select ID, sum(PaymentCount) as PaymentCount
  --              from #tmp_payment
  --              group by ID) p on t.ID = p.ID

  set @script = ''select *, cast(case when (TotalAmt = 0) or '' +
                                          ''abs(TotalAmt - (CashPaidAmt + DebitPaidAmt + VisaPaidAmt + McPaidAmt + AmexPaidAmt + '' +
                                                          ''CouponPaidAmt + DiscoverPaidAmt + JcbPaidAmt + GiftCardPaidAmt + '' +
                                                          ''RewardPointPaidAmt + ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt)) = 0 then 0 '' +
                                    ''else 1 end as bit) as DiscrepancyExists '' +
                ''from #tmp_transactions '' +
                ''order by '' + @OrderBy
  exec sp_executesql @script

  drop table #tmp_transactions
  drop table #tmp_payment

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_VoidCardTransaction]
  @PaymentID int,
  @SalesID int,
  @CardReceipt nvarchar(4000)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblPayment
  set Voided = 1,
      CardReceipt = substring(ltrim(rtrim(CardReceipt)) + char(13) + char(10) + ltrim(rtrim(@CardReceipt)), 1, 4000)
  where ID = @PaymentID

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblPayment
                 where SalesID = @SalesID
                   and Voided = 0) begin
    update tblSales
    set TransType = 3 /* Void after payment */
    where ID = @SalesID

    exec sp_VoidOrUndoVoidRewardPoint @SalesID, 1
  end 
  else begin
    update s
    set s.SubTotal = s.SubTotal - (p.PaidAmount * (1 - s.GSTRate)),
        s.GSTAmt = dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 0) - (s.SubTotal - (p.PaidAmount * (1 - s.GSTRate)))
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    where p.ID = @PaymentID
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCardTransInfo]
  @AuthorizationNo varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select top 1 
         ID, SalesID, PaymentTypeID, PaidAmount, TipAmount, 
         case when CardNumber is null then '''' 
              else replicate(''*'', len(dbo.DecryptString(CardNumber)) - 4) + 
                   reverse(substring(reverse(dbo.DecryptString(CardNumber)), 1, 4)) end as CardNumber,
         dbo.DecryptString(CardNumber) as CreditCardNumber,
         dbo.DecryptString(CardExpiryDate) as CreditCardExpiryDate,
         case when CardExpiryDate is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(CardExpiryDate) end as CardExpiryDate,
         case PaymentTypeID when 2 then ''Debit''
                            when 3 then ''Visa''
                            when 4 then ''MC''
                            when 5 then ''Amex''
                            when 7 then ''Discover''
                            when 8 then ''JCB''
                            else ''''
         end as PaymentType, 
         isnull(AuthorizationNo, '''') as AuthorizationNo,
         isnull(SequenceNo, '''') as SequenceNo,
         isnull(BatchNo, '''') as BatchNo, 
         isnull(ItemNo, '''') as ItemNo,
         isnull(RevisionNo, '''') as RevisionNo,
         Voided, BatchClosed
  from tblPayment
  where isnull(AuthorizationNo, '''') like ''%'' + @AuthorizationNo + ''%''
    and PaymentTypeID in (2,3,4,5,7,8)
  order by ID desc

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_VoidSalesTransaction]
  @RecordTrans bit,
  @SalesID int, 
  @TableID int,
  @SubTotalAmt money,
  @DSCAmt money,
  @GSTAmt money,
  @PSTAmt money,
  @PST2Amt money
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  if (@RecordTrans = 1) begin
    update s
    set s.SubTotal = @SubTotalAmt, 
        s.DSCAmt = @DSCAmt, 
        s.GSTAmt = @GSTAmt, 
        s.PSTAmt = @PSTAmt,
        s.PST2Amt = @PST2Amt,
        s.TransType = 4, /* Sales Void */ 
        s.SaleDateTime = getdate(), 
        s.Guests = 1, 
        s.CustomerID = 1, 
        s.TableID = @TableID
    from tblSales s
    where s.ID = @SalesID

    insert into tblSalesDetail (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, PricePerWeightUnit, MeasuredWeight, 
                                DecimalPlaces, DiscountAmt, DiscountPercent, Tastes, ItemName, ItemName2, SizeName)
    select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, round(Qty * UnitPrice, 2), PricePerWeightUnit, MeasuredWeight,
           DecimalPlaces, isnull(DSCAmt, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0), 
           DiscountPercent, Tastes, ItemName, ItemName2, SizeName
    from tblPendingOrders 
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and Qty <> 0

    --insert into tblSalesDetail (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice)
    --select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, sum(Qty), round(sum(Qty * UnitPrice) / sum(Qty),2)
    --from tblPendingOrders 
    --where SalesID = @SalesID
    --  and Qty <> 0
    --group by SalesID, ItemID, SizeID
  end
  else begin
    update s
    set s.SubTotal = 0, 
        s.DSCAmt = 0, 
        s.GSTAmt = 0, 
        s.PSTAmt = 0,
        s.PST2Amt = 0,
        s.TransType = 2, /* No Sale */ 
        s.SaleDateTime = getdate(), 
        s.Guests = 0, 
        s.CustomerID = 1, 
        s.TableID = 0
    from tblSales s
    where s.ID = @SalesID
  end

  delete
  from tblPendingOrders 
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  exec sp_DeleteOrdersToBePrinted @SalesID

  exec sp_DeleteCheckedOrders @SalesID

  update t 
  set t.OrderNum = 0, 
      t.ServerID = 0, 
      t.NumOfGuests = 0, 
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.PickupTime = '''', 
      t.PhoneNum = '''', 
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0, 
      t.BillPrinted = 0 
  from tblTable t 
  where t.ID = @TableID
    and not exists (select * 
                    from tblPendingOrders p 
                    where p.SalesID = t.OrderNum)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetOpenTables]
  @ServerID smallint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblTable
  where OrderNum > 0
    and case when @ServerID > 0 then
               case when ServerID = @ServerID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteUser]
  @UserID smallint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction delete_user

  update u
  set u.UserAccessCode = ''D'' + u.UserAccessCode,
      u.Status = 0
  from tblUser u
  where u.ID = @UserID
    and u.Status = 1
    and exists (select *
                from tblUser u2
                where u2.ID <> u.ID
                  and u2.GroupID = 1
                  and u2.Status = 1)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction delete_user
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction delete_user
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateUser]
  @UserAccessCode varchar(15),
  @LName varchar(30),
  @FName varchar(30),
  @GroupID tinyint,
  @Status bit,
  @Address varchar(255),
  @Wage smallmoney,
  @Memo varchar(255),  
  @TipOutPercentage float,
  @SystemUser bit,
  @AccessPermission bit,
  @UserID smallint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update u 
  set u.UserAccessCode = @UserAccessCode, 
      u.LName = @LName, 
      u.FName = @FName, 
      u.GroupID = case when (u.GroupID >= 2) then @GroupID 
                       when (u.GroupID = 1) and (@GroupID > 1) then
                         case when exists (select *
                                           from tblUser u2
                                           where u2.ID <> u.ID
                                             and u2.GroupID = 1
                                             and u2.Status = 1) then @GroupID
                              else u.GroupID 
                         end
                       else u.GroupID 
                  end,
      u.Status =  case when (u.GroupID = 1) and (@GroupID = 1) then
                         case when exists (select *
                                           from tblUser u3
                                           where u3.ID <> u.ID
                                             and u3.GroupID = 1
                                             and u3.Status = 1) then @Status
                              else u.Status 
                         end
                       else @Status
                  end, 
      u.Address = @Address, 
      u.Memo = @Memo,         
      u.Wage = @Wage,
      u.TipOutPercentage = @TipOutPercentage,
      u.SystemUser = @SystemUser,
      u.AccessPermission = @AccessPermission
  from tblUser u
  where u.ID = @UserID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertUser]
  @UserAccessCode varchar(15),
  @LName varchar(30),
  @FName varchar(30),
  @GroupID tinyint,
  @Status bit,
  @Address varchar(255),
  @Wage smallmoney,
  @Memo varchar(255),  
  @TipOutPercentage float,
  @SystemUser bit,
  @AccessPermission bit,
  @NewUserID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblUser (UserAccessCode, LName, FName, GroupID, [Status], [Address], Wage, Memo, LastClosingTime, TipOutPercentage, SystemUser, AccessPermission)
  values (@UserAccessCode, @LName, @FName, @GroupID, @Status, @Address, @Wage, @Memo, getdate(), @TipOutPercentage, @SystemUser, @AccessPermission)

  set @NewUserID = scope_identity()

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetLastTransInfo]
  @SalesID int,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@SalesID <= 0) begin

    select top 1 @SalesID = s.ID
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    where case when @StationID > 0 then 
                 case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
               else 1
          end = 1
      and s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112))
      and s.TransType in (0, 1, 3)
      and s.SubTotal <> 0
    order by s.SaleDateTime desc

  end

  if (isnull(@SalesID, 0) > 0) begin
    if exists (select *
               from tblSalesDetail 
               where SalesID = @SalesID) begin
      select s.*, 
             round(s.SubTotal-s.DSCAmt+s.GSTAmt+s.PSTAmt+s.PST2Amt,2) as Total, 
             u.ID as EmployeeID, u.FName, (c.FName + '' '' + c.LName) as CustomerName, c.Phone, c.Address, c.CustomerNote,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as VisaPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  4),0),2) as McPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  5),0),2) as AmexPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  7),0),2) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  8),0),2) as JcbPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 10),0),2) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  0),0),2) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
             sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, sd.Qty, sd.UnitPrice, sd.ItemName as IName, sd.ItemName2 as IName2, sd.SizeName,
             --case when (i.Taste = 1 and sd.SizeID > 1) then z.SizeName else i.IName end as IName, i.IName2, 
             --case when i.Taste = 1 then '''' else z.SizeName end as SizeName, 
             isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName, i.ScaleItem, i.OpenItem,
             sd.PricePerWeightUnit, sd.MeasuredWeight, sd.DecimalPlaces, sd.DiscountAmt, sd.DiscountPercent, sd.Tastes,
             round(isnull(h.BillCollectAmt, 0), 2) as BillCollectAmt,
             case when i.HourlyChargedItem = 1 then dbo.GetTotalTimeCharged(s.ID, i.ID) else '''' end as TotalTimeCharged,
             isnull(soo.OnlineOrderNumber, '''') as OnlineOrderNumber
      from tblSales s 
        left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
        left join tblBillCollectHistory h on s.ID = h.SalesID
        inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
        inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
        inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
        inner join tblSize z on sd.SizeID = z.ID
        left join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders soo on soo.SalesID = s.ID
      where sd.Voided = 0
        and s.ID = @SalesID
      order by isnull(sd.SequenceNo, 0)
    end
    else begin
      select s.*, 
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  0),0),2) as Total, 
             u.ID as EmployeeID, u.FName, (c.FName + '' '' + c.LName) as CustomerName, c.Phone, c.Address, c.CustomerNote,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as VisaPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  4),0),2) as McPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  5),0),2) as AmexPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  7),0),2) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  8),0),2) as JcbPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 10),0),2) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
             round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  0),0),2) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
             0 as ItemID, 0 as SizeID, 0 as Qty, 0 as UnitPrice, '''' as IName, '''' as IName2, '''' as SizeName, 
             isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName, cast(0 as bit) as ScaleItem, cast(0 as bit) as OpenItem,
             0 as PricePerWeightUnit, 0 as MeasuredWeight, 0 as DecimalPlaces, 0 as DiscountAmt, 0 as DiscountPercent, '''' as Tastes,
             round(isnull(h.BillCollectAmt, 0), 2) as BillCollectAmt,
             '''' as TotalTimeCharged,
             isnull(soo.OnlineOrderNumber, '''') as OnlineOrderNumber
      from tblSales s 
        left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
        left join tblBillCollectHistory h on s.ID = h.SalesID
        inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
        inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
        left join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders soo on soo.SalesID = s.ID
      where s.ID = @SalesID
    end
  end
  else begin
    select *
    from tblSales
    where 1 = 0
  end
  --else begin
  --  select s.*, 
  --         round(s.SubTotal-s.DSCAmt+s.GSTAmt+s.PSTAmt+s.PST2Amt,2) as Total, 
  --         u.ID as EmployeeID, u.FName, (c.FName + '' '' + c.LName) as CustomerName, c.Phone, c.Address, c.CustomerNote,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as VisaPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  4),0),2) as McPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  5),0),2) as AmexPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  7),0),2) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  8),0),2) as JcbPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 10),0),2) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  1),0),2) as CashTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  2),0),2) as DebitTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  3),0),2) as CreditTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  6),0),2) as CouponTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  9),0),2) as GiftCardTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID, 11),0),2) as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
  --         round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(s.ID,  0),0),2) as TotalTipPaidAmt,
  --         sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, sd.Qty, sd.UnitPrice, sd.ItemName as IName, sd.ItemName2 as IName2, sd.SizeName, 
  --         --case when (i.Taste = 1 and sd.SizeID > 1) then z.SizeName else i.IName end as IName, i.IName2, 
  --         --case when i.Taste = 1 then '''' else z.SizeName end as SizeName, 
  --         isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName, i.ScaleItem, i.OpenItem,
  --         sd.PricePerWeightUnit, sd.MeasuredWeight, sd.DecimalPlaces, sd.DiscountAmt, sd.DiscountPercent, sd.Tastes,
  --         round(isnull(h.BillCollectAmt, 0), 2) as BillCollectAmt,
  --         case when i.HourlyChargedItem = 1 then dbo.GetTotalTimeCharged(s.ID, i.ID) else '''' end as TotalTimeCharged
  --  from tblSales s 
  --    left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
  --    left join tblBillCollectHistory h on s.ID = h.SalesID
  --    inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
  --    inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
  --    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
  --    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  --    inner join tblSize z on sd.SizeID = z.ID
  --  where sd.Voided = 0
  --    and s.StationID = @StationID
  --    and s.SaleDateTime = (select max(s2.SaleDateTime)
  --                          from tblSales s2
  --                          where s2.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112))
  --                            and s2.TransType in (0,1)
  --                            and s2.SubTotal <> 0
  --                            and s2.StationID = s.StationID)  
  --end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertKitchenOrders]
  @SalesID int,
  @DisplayType tinyint
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_kitchen_orders

  if ((@DisplayType = 0) or (@DisplayType = 1)) begin

    declare @ItemID smallint, @SizeID smallint, @Qty smallint, @Tastes varchar(2000), @SideDishes varchar(200),
            @ItemName varchar(100), @ItemName2 varchar(30), @BarCode varchar(15), @SizeName varchar(30),
            @KitchenB bit, @KitchenF bit, @KitchenE bit, @Bar bit, @Kitchen5 bit, @Kitchen6 bit, @PersonIndex tinyint, 
            @DailyOrdNum int, @Status tinyint, @SubtractQty smallint

    declare @tmpKitchenOrders table
    (
      [ID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
      [SalesID] [int] NOT NULL,
      [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
      [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
      [Qty] [smallint] NULL,
      [Tastes] [varchar](2000) NOT NULL,
      [SideDishes] [varchar](200) NOT NULL,
      [ItemName] [varchar](100) NOT NULL,
      [ItemName2] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
      [ItemNumber] [varchar](15) NOT NULL,
      [SizeName] [varchar](20) NOT NULL,
      [KitchenB] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [KitchenF] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [KitchenE] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Bar] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Kitchen5] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Kitchen6] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [PersonIndex] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
      [DailyOrderNumber] [int] NOT NULL,
      [Status] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
      [StationID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
      [PickupTime] [varchar](8) NOT NULL,
      [InsertedDateTime] [datetime] NOT NULL
--      [ReadyQty] [smallint] NOT NULL,
--      [DeletedQty] [smallint] NOT NULL
    )

    insert into @tmpKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                   ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, Kitchen5, Kitchen6, 
                                   PersonIndex, DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime)
    select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
           ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, Kitchen5, Kitchen6, 
           PersonIndex, DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime
    from tblKitchenOrders
    where SalesID = @SalesID  

    delete
    from tblKitchenOrders
    where SalesID = @SalesID

    if (@DisplayType = 0) begin

      declare curs_insert cursor for
        select p.ItemID, p.SizeID, sum(p.Qty), p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.ItemName2,
               i.BarCode, p.SizeName, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, p.KitchenE, p.Bar, p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6, --p.PersonIndex,
               t.DailyOrdNum
        from tblPendingOrders p, tblTable t, tblItem i
        where p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          and p.ItemID = i.ID
          and p.SalesID = @SalesID
        group by p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.ItemName2,
                 i.BarCode, p.SizeName, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, p.KitchenE, p.Bar, p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6, --p.PersonIndex,
                 t.DailyOrdNum

        open curs_insert
        fetch next from curs_insert into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @SideDishes,
                                         @ItemName, @ItemName2, @BarCode, @SizeName,
                                         @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6, --@PersonIndex,
                                         @DailyOrdNum
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          if exists (select *
                     from @tmpKitchenOrders
                     where SalesID = @SalesID
                       and ItemID = @ItemID
                       and SizeID = @SizeID
                       and Tastes = @Tastes) begin
--                       and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex) begin
            
            insert into tblKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                          ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                                          DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
            select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                   ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                   DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime, Kitchen5, Kitchen6
            from @tmpKitchenOrders
            where SalesID = @SalesID
              and ItemID = @ItemID
              and SizeID = @SizeID
              and Tastes = @Tastes
--              and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
--              and [Status] in (2, 3)

            select @SubtractQty = sum(Qty)
            from tblKitchenOrders
            where SalesID = @SalesID
              and ItemID = @ItemID
              and SizeID = @SizeID
              and Tastes = @Tastes
--              and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
              
            if ((@Qty - isnull(@SubtractQty, 0)) > 0) begin

              insert into tblKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                            ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                                            DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
              values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty - isnull(@SubtractQty, 0), @Tastes, @SideDishes, @ItemName, @ItemName2, 
                      @BarCode, @SizeName, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, 0, --@PersonIndex,
                      @DailyOrdNum, 1, 0, '''', getdate(), @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6)

            end
          end
          else begin

            insert into tblKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                          ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                                          DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
            values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @SideDishes, @ItemName, @ItemName2, 
                    @BarCode, @SizeName, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, 0, --@PersonIndex,
                    @DailyOrdNum, 1, 0, '''', getdate(), @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6)

          end

          fetch next from curs_insert into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @SideDishes,
                                           @ItemName, @ItemName2, @BarCode, @SizeName,
                                           @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6, --@PersonIndex,
                                           @DailyOrdNum
        end
        close curs_insert
      deallocate curs_insert

    end
    else begin

      declare curs_insert cursor for
        select p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.Qty, p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.ItemName2,
               i.BarCode, p.SizeName, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, p.KitchenE, p.Bar, p.PersonIndex,
               t.DailyOrdNum, p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6
        from tblPendingOrders p, tblTable t, tblItem i
        where p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          and p.ItemID = i.ID
          and p.SalesID = @SalesID
  --        and (p.KitchenB = 1 or p.KitchenF = 1 or p.KitchenE = 1)
  --        and case when @DisplayType = 1 then 
  --                   case when t.TakeOut = 0 then 1 else 0 end
  --                 else
  --                   1
  --            end = 1

        open curs_insert
        fetch next from curs_insert into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @SideDishes,
                                         @ItemName, @ItemName2, @BarCode, @SizeName,
                                         @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, @PersonIndex,
                                         @DailyOrdNum, @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          while (@Qty > 0) begin

            insert into tblKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                          ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                                          DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime,
                                          Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
            values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, 1, @Tastes, @SideDishes, @ItemName, @ItemName2, 
                    @BarCode, @SizeName, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, @PersonIndex,
                    @DailyOrdNum, 1, 0, '''', getdate(), @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6)

            set @Qty = @Qty - 1

          end

          fetch next from curs_insert into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @SideDishes,
                                           @ItemName, @ItemName2, @BarCode, @SizeName,
                                           @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @KitchenE, @Bar, @PersonIndex,
                                           @DailyOrdNum, @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6
        end
        close curs_insert
      deallocate curs_insert

      declare curs_refresh cursor for
        select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Tastes, PersonIndex, [Status]
        from @tmpKitchenOrders
        where [Status] > 1
        
        open curs_refresh
        fetch next from curs_refresh into @SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Tastes, @PersonIndex, @Status
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          update t
          set t.[Status] = @Status
          from tblKitchenOrders t
          where t.ID = (select top 1 t2.ID
                        from tblKitchenOrders t2
                        where t2.SalesID = @SalesID
                          and t2.ItemID = @ItemID
                          and t2.SizeID = @SizeID
                          and t2.Tastes = @Tastes
                          and t2.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
                          and t2.[Status] <> @Status)      

          fetch next from curs_refresh into @SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Tastes, @PersonIndex, @Status
        end
        close curs_refresh
      deallocate curs_refresh

    end

  end
  else if (@DisplayType = 2) begin

    if not exists (select *
                   from tblKitchenOrders
                   where SalesID = @SalesID
                     and [Status] = 3) begin

      delete
      from tblKitchenOrders
      where SalesID = @SalesID

      insert into tblKitchenOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, ItemName2,
                                    ItemNumber, SizeName, KitchenB, KitchenF, KitchenE, Bar, PersonIndex,
                                    DailyOrderNumber, [Status], StationID, PickupTime, InsertedDateTime, 
                                    Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
      select p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.Qty, p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.ItemName2,
             i.BarCode, p.SizeName, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, p.KitchenE, p.Bar, p.PersonIndex,
             t.DailyOrdNum, 1, isnull(s.ID, 0), 
             case isnull(t.TakeOut, 0) 
               when 1 then 
                 case when isnull(t.PickupTime, ''Now'') like ''00:00%'' then 
                        replace(substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, getdate()), 100), 13, 5), '' '', ''0'') + '' '' +
                        substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, getdate()), 100), 18, 2)
                      else isnull(t.PickupTime, ''Now'')
                 end                                
               else replace(substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, getdate()), 100), 13, 5), '' '', ''0'') + '' '' +
                    substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, getdate()), 100), 18, 2) 
             end,
             getdate(),
             p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6
      from tblPendingOrders p, tblTable t, tblItem i, tblStation s
      where p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
        and p.ItemID = i.ID
        and p.SalesID = @SalesID
        and (p.KitchenB = 1 or p.KitchenF = 1 or p.KitchenE = 1)
        and s.KitchenDisplay = 1
      order by s.ID, p.ItemID

    end

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_kitchen_orders
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_kitchen_orders
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTransactionsByCustomer]
  @CustomerID int,
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select s.ID, s.CashierID, s.SaleDateTime, 
         case when s.TransType = 0 then ''Refund''
              when s.TransType = 1 then ''Sale'' 
              when s.TransType = 2 then ''NoSale''
              when s.TransType = 3 then ''Void''
              when s.TransType = 4 then ''Void''
              else '''' 
         end AS TransType, 
         round(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt, 2) AS Total, 
         cast(0 as money) as CashPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DebitPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as VisaPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as McPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as AmexPaidAmt,         
         cast(0 as money) as CouponPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as DiscoverPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as JcbPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as GiftCardPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as RewardPointPaidAmt,
         cast(0 as money) as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt,
         (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as Cashier 
  into #tmp_transactions
  from tblSales s, tblUser u
  where s.CashierID = u.ID
    and s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  order by s.ID desc

  select s.ID, p.PaymentTypeID, 
         sum(round(isnull(PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount, 
         sum(round(isnull(TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount
  into #tmp_payment
  from tblSales s, tblPayment p
  where p.SalesID = s.ID
    and s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by s.ID, p.PaymentTypeID

  update t
  set t.CashPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 1

  update t
  set t.DebitPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 2
   
  update t
  set t.VisaPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 3

  update t
  set t.McPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 4

  update t
  set t.AmexPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 5

  update t
  set t.CouponPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 6

  update t
  set t.DiscoverPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 7

  update t
  set t.JcbPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 8

  update t
  set t.GiftCardPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 9

  update t
  set t.RewardPointPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 10

  update t
  set t.ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = p.PaidAmount
  from #tmp_transactions t, #tmp_payment p
  where t.ID = p.ID
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 11

  select *
  from #tmp_transactions

  drop table #tmp_transactions
  drop table #tmp_payment

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdatePayment]
  @SalesID int,
  @CashAmount smallmoney,
  @DebitAmount smallmoney,
  @VisaAmount smallmoney,
  @McAmount smallmoney,
  @AmexAmount smallmoney,
  @CouponAmount smallmoney,
  @DiscoverAmount smallmoney,
  @JcbAmount smallmoney,
  @GiftCardAmount smallmoney,
  @RewardPointAmount smallmoney,
  @ChargeOnAccountAmount smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @NewPaymentTypeCount tinyint, @TotalPaidAmount smallmoney

  set @NewPaymentTypeCount = 0

  if (@CashAmount <> 0)            set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@DebitAmount <> 0)           set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@VisaAmount <> 0)            set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@McAmount <> 0)              set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@AmexAmount <> 0)            set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@CouponAmount <> 0)          set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@DiscoverAmount <> 0)        set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@JcbAmount <> 0)             set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@GiftCardAmount <> 0)        set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@RewardPointAmount <> 0)     set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1
  if (@ChargeOnAccountAmount <> 0) set @NewPaymentTypeCount = @NewPaymentTypeCount + 1

  select @TotalPaidAmount = sum(PaidAmount)
  from tblPayment
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  if exists (select SalesID
             from tblPayment
             where SalesID = @SalesID
             group by SalesID
             having count(PaymentTypeID) = 1) and (@NewPaymentTypeCount = 1) begin

    declare @PaidAmount smallmoney, @PaymentTypeID tinyint

    set @PaidAmount = 0
    set @PaymentTypeID = 1

    if (@CashAmount > 0) or ((@CashAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @CashAmount 
      set @PaymentTypeID = 1
    end
    else if (@DebitAmount > 0) or ((@DebitAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @DebitAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 2
    end
    else if (@VisaAmount > 0) or ((@VisaAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @VisaAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 3
    end
    else if (@McAmount > 0) or ((@McAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @McAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 4
    end
    else if (@AmexAmount > 0) or ((@AmexAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @AmexAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 5
    end
    else if (@CouponAmount > 0) or ((@CouponAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @CouponAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 6
    end
    else if (@DiscoverAmount > 0) or ((@DiscoverAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @DiscoverAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 7
    end
    else if (@JcbAmount > 0) or ((@JcbAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @JcbAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 8
    end
    else if (@GiftCardAmount > 0) or ((@GiftCardAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @GiftCardAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 9
    end
    else if (@RewardPointAmount > 0) or ((@RewardPointAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @RewardPointAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 10
    end
    else if (@ChargeOnAccountAmount > 0) or ((@ChargeOnAccountAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0)) begin
      set @PaidAmount = @ChargeOnAccountAmount
      set @PaymentTypeID = 11
    end                            

    update tblPayment
    set PaidAmount = @PaidAmount,
        PaymentTypeID = @PaymentTypeID
    where SalesID = @SalesID

  end
  else begin

    declare @TipAmount smallmoney, @PaidDateTime datetime

    select @TipAmount = round(isnull(dbo.GetTipTotal(@SalesID, 0),0),2)

    select top 1 @PaidDateTime = PaidDateTime
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID
    order by ID desc

    delete 
    from tblPayment
    where SalesID = @SalesID

    if (@CashAmount > 0) or ((@CashAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 1, @CashAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@DebitAmount > 0) or ((@DebitAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 2, @DebitAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@VisaAmount > 0) or ((@VisaAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 3, @VisaAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@McAmount > 0) or ((@McAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 4, @McAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@AmexAmount > 0) or ((@AmexAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 5, @AmexAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@CouponAmount > 0) or ((@CouponAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 6, @CouponAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@DiscoverAmount > 0) or ((@DiscoverAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 7, @DiscoverAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@JcbAmount > 0) or ((@JcbAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 8, @JcbAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@GiftCardAmount > 0) or ((@GiftCardAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 9, @GiftCardAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@RewardPointAmount > 0) or ((@RewardPointAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 10, @RewardPointAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if (@ChargeOnAccountAmount > 0) or ((@ChargeOnAccountAmount < 0) and (@TotalPaidAmount < 0))
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 11, @ChargeOnAccountAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    if not exists (select *
                   from tblPayment
                   where SalesID = @SalesID
                     and PaymentTypeID = 1) begin
      exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 1, 0, @TipAmount, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime
    end
    else begin
      update p
      set p.TipAmount = @TipAmount 
      from tblPayment p
      where p.SalesID = @SalesID
        and p.PaymentTypeID = 1
    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetLastKitchenOrders]  
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select t1.*, case when s.TakeOutOrder = 1 then '' (To Go)'' else '' (For Here)'' end as OrderType
  from tblKitchenOrders t1, tblSales s
  where t1.SalesID = s.ID
    and t1.SalesID = (select max(ID)
                      from tblSales
                      where TransType in (1, 9))
  order by t1.ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetKitchenOrders]
  @FrontKitchen bit,
  @BackKitchen bit,
  @ExtraKitchen bit,
  @Bar bit,
  @OnlyBackKitchenCheckedItems bit,
  @TakeOutOrder bit,
  @EntireOrders bit,
  @DisplayType tinyint,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete k
  from tblKitchenOrders k
  where exists (select k2.SalesID 
                from tblKitchenOrders k2
                where k2.SalesID = k.SalesID
                group by k2.SalesID 
                having count(k2.SalesID) > 200)

  declare @script nvarchar(max)

  if ((@FrontKitchen = 1) or (@BackKitchen = 1) or (@ExtraKitchen = 1) or (@Bar = 1)) begin 

    if (@DisplayType = 1) begin   

      set @script = ''select k.ID, k.SalesID, k.ItemID, k.SizeID, k.Qty, dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(k.Tastes, '''','''') as Tastes, k.SideDishes, '' +
                    ''       case when k.SizeID > 1 then ''''['''' + k.SizeName + ''''] '''' + k.ItemName else k.ItemName end + '' +
                    ''       case when isnull(s.TakeOutOrder, 0) = 1 then '''' (ToGo)'''' else '''''''' end as ItemName, '' +
                    ''       case when k.SizeID > 1 then ''''['''' + k.SizeName + ''''] '''' + k.ItemName2 else k.ItemName2 end + '' +
                    ''       case when isnull(s.TakeOutOrder, 0) = 1 then '''' (ToGo)'''' else '''''''' end as ItemName2, '' +
                    ''       k.ItemNumber, k.KitchenB, k.KitchenF, k.KitchenE, k.Bar, k.PersonIndex, k.DailyOrderNumber, '' +
                    ''       k.Status, isnull(t.TableName, '''''''') as TableName, u.FName as ServerName '' +              
                    ''from tblKitchenOrders k '' +
                    ''  inner join tblSales s on k.SalesID = s.ID '' +
                    ''  inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID '' +
                    ''  left join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID '' +
                    ''where s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112) '' 

      if (@TakeOutOrder = 0)
        set @script = @script + ''  and isnull(s.TakeOutOrder, 0) = 0 ''

      if (@EntireOrders = 0)
        set @script = @script + ''  and k.Status in (1, 2) ''

      set @script = @script + ''  and (''

      if (@FrontKitchen = 1) 
        set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenF = 1 or ''

      if (@BackKitchen = 1) begin
        if (@OnlyBackKitchenCheckedItems = 1)
          set @script = @script + ''(k.KitchenB = 1 and k.KitchenF = 0 and k.KitchenE = 0 and k.Bar = 0) or ''
                               -- + ''(k.ItemID in (118, 119, 120, 133)) or '' /* Sushi Cali Broadway */
                               -- + ''(k.ItemID in (117, 118, 120, 119, 334, 11)) or '' /* Sushi Cali Coquitlam & Surrey */
                                  --''(k.KitchenB = 1 and k.KitchenF = 1 and k.KitchenE = 1 and k.Bar = 1) or ''
        else
          set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenB = 1 or ''         
      end

      if (@ExtraKitchen = 1)
        set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenE = 1 or ''

      if (@Bar = 1)
        set @script = @script + ''k.Bar = 1 or ''
        
      set @script = @script + ''exists (select 1 from tblKitchenDisplayItems kdi where kdi.ItemID = k.ItemID and kdi.StationID = '' + convert(varchar, @StationID) + ''))''

      if (@EntireOrders = 1)
        set @script = @script + '' order by k.SalesID desc, k.ItemID, k.SizeID''
      else
        set @script = @script + '' order by k.InsertedDateTime''
--        set @script = @script + '' order by k.SalesID, k.ItemID, k.SizeID''

    end
    else if (@DisplayType = 2) begin   

      set @script = ''select k.ID, k.SalesID, k.ItemID, k.SizeID, k.Qty, k.Tastes, k.SideDishes, '' +
                    ''       replicate('''' '''', 4 - len(convert(varchar, k.Qty))) + convert(varchar, k.Qty) + ''''   '''' + k.ItemName as ItemName, '' +
                    ''       replicate('''' '''', 4 - len(convert(varchar, k.Qty))) + convert(varchar, k.Qty) + ''''   '''' + '' + 
                    ''       case when isnull(ltrim(rtrim(k.ItemName2)), '''''''') = '''''''' then k.ItemName else k.ItemName2 end as ItemName2, '' +
                    ''       k.SizeName, k.ItemNumber, k.KitchenB, k.KitchenF, k.KitchenE, k.Bar, k.PersonIndex, k.DailyOrderNumber, '' +
                    ''       k.Status, isnull(t.TableName, '''''''') as TableName '' +
                    ''from tblKitchenOrders k '' +
                    ''  inner join tblSales s on k.SalesID = s.ID '' + 
                    ''  left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID '' +
                    ''where k.Status = 1 '' +
                    ''  and s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112) ''

      if (@StationID > 0)
        set @script = @script + ''  and k.StationID = '' + convert(varchar, @StationID)                  

      set @script = @script + ''  and (''

      if (@FrontKitchen = 1) 
        set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenF = 1 or ''

      if (@BackKitchen = 1)
        set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenB = 1 or ''

      if (@ExtraKitchen = 1)
        set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenE = 1 or ''

      if (@Bar = 1)
        set @script = @script + ''k.Bar = 1 or ''
        
      set @script = @script + ''1 <> 1)'' --substring(@script, 1, len(@script) - 3) + '')''   

      set @script = @script + '' order by k.SalesID, k.PersonIndex, k.ItemID, k.SizeID''

    end

  end
  else begin
    set @script = ''select * '' +
                  ''from tblKitchenOrders '' +
                  ''where ID = 0''  
  end 

  exec sp_executesql @script

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertReadyOrderNumber]
  @KitchenOrderID int
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblReadyOrderNumber (KitchenOrderID, OrderNumber, Source)
  select ID, case when ltrim(rtrim(ItemNumber)) <> '''' then 
                       ltrim(rtrim(convert(varchar(5), DailyOrderNumber))) + ''-'' + 
                       ltrim(rtrim(convert(varchar(5), convert(int, ItemNumber))))
                  else ltrim(rtrim(convert(varchar(5), DailyOrderNumber))) 
             end as OrderNumber,
             case when KitchenF = 1 then ''A'' else ''B'' end as Source
  from tblKitchenOrders
  where ID = @KitchenOrderID
    and [Status] = 2

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateOrderStatus]
  @ID int,
  @Status tinyint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblKitchenOrders
  set [Status] = @Status
  where ID = @ID

  if (@Status = 2)
    exec sp_InsertReadyOrderNumber @ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetReadyOrderNumbers]
  @Source char(1)
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select top 6 r.OrderNumber
  from tblReadyOrderNumber r, tblKitchenOrders k
  where r.Source = @Source
    and r.KitchenOrderID = k.ID
    and k.Status = 2
  order by r.ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetAvailableTakeOutTable]
  @OldTableID smallint,
  @ServerID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @TableID smallint, @TableName varchar(20), @ServerName varchar(30)

  select @TableID = isnull(ID, 0),
         @TableName = isnull(TableName, '''')
  from tblTable
  where ID = (select isnull(min(t2.ID), 0)
              from tblTable t2
              where TakeOut = 1
                and OrderNum = 0
                and Linked = 1
                and Opened = 0)

  select @ServerName = isnull(U.FName, '''')
  from tblTable t left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
  where t.ID = @OldTableID

  if (@TableID > 0) begin
    update tblTable
    set Opened = 1,
        ServerID = @ServerID,
        NumOfGuests = 1
    where ID = @TableID

    update tblTable
    set OrderNum = 0,
        ServerID = 0,
        NumOfGuests = 0,
        Opened = 0,
        BillPrinted = 0,
        Attention = 0,
        DailyOrdNum = 0
    where ID = @OldTableID

    select @TableID as TableID, @TableName as TableName, @ServerName as ServerName
  end
  else begin
    select *
    from tblTable
    where ID = 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertOrdersToBePrinted]
  @SalesID int,
  @PrintDateTime varchar(20),
  @IsReprinting bit
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction insert_orders_to_be_printed

    if not exists (select *
                   from tblOrderPrintCue
                   where SalesID = @SalesID) begin
      insert into tblOrderPrintCue (SalesID, PrintDateTime, PrintedStatus, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut, PrintedDateTime, IsReprinting)
      values (@SalesID, @PrintDateTime, 0, getdate(), null, null, @IsReprinting)
    end
    else begin
      update tblOrderPrintCue
      set PrintDateTime = @PrintDateTime,
          PrintedStatus = 0,
          DateTimeIn = getdate(),
          DateTimeOut = null,
          PrintedDateTime = null,
          IsReprinting = @IsReprinting
      where SalesID = @SalesID
    end
    commit transaction insert_orders_to_be_printed
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction insert_orders_to_be_printed
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateOrdersToBePrinted]
  @SalesID int,
  @PrintDateTime varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_orders_to_be_printed

  update tblOrderPrintCue
  set PrintDateTime = @PrintDateTime,
      PrintedStatus = 0,
      DateTimeIn = getdate(),
      DateTimeOut = null,
      PrintedDateTime = null
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_orders_to_be_printed
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_orders_to_be_printed
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetOrdersToBePrinted]
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmpOrderPrintCue table (SalesID int, IsReprinting bit)

  delete opc
  from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  where opc.PrintedStatus = 1
    and opc.DateTimeIn < dateadd(d, -1, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  --delete opc
  --from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  --where not exists (select *
  --                  from tblPendingOrders po
  --                  where po.SalesID = opc.SalesID)

  update opc
  set opc.PrintedStatus = 1,
      opc.DateTimeOut = getdate()
  from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  where opc.PrintedStatus = 0
    and not exists (select *
                    from tblPendingOrders po
                    where po.SalesID = opc.SalesID)

  insert into @tmpOrderPrintCue (SalesID, IsReprinting)
  select opc.SalesID, opc.IsReprinting
  from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  where opc.PrintDateTime <= getdate()
    and opc.PrintedStatus = 0
    --and (opc.PrintedStatus = 0
    --     or
    --     (    opc.PrintedStatus = 1
    --      and opc.PrintDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)
    --      and opc.PrintedDateTime is null
    --      and opc.DateTimeOut > opc.DateTimeIn
    --      and exists (select *
    --                  from tblPendingOrders po
    --                  where po.SalesID = opc.SalesID))
    --    )

  update opc
  set opc.PrintedStatus = 1,
      opc.DateTimeOut = getdate()
  from tblOrderPrintCue opc
    inner join @tmpOrderPrintCue t on t.SalesID = opc.SalesID

  select SalesID, IsReprinting
  from @tmpOrderPrintCue 
  order by SalesID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetOrdersToBePrintedBySalesID]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmpOrderPrintCue table (SalesID int, PrintDateTime datetime, IsReprinting bit)

  --delete opc
  --from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  --where not exists (select *
  --                  from tblPendingOrders po
  --                  where po.SalesID = opc.SalesID)

  update opc
  set opc.PrintedStatus = 1,
      opc.DateTimeOut = getdate()
      --opc.PrintedDateTime = getdate() /* do not update with getdate(). PrintedDateTim = null means that, for this transaction, a scheduled printing was set in Sales screen */
  from tblOrderPrintCue opc
  where opc.PrintedStatus = 0
    and not exists (select *
                    from tblPendingOrders po
                    where po.SalesID = opc.SalesID)

  insert into @tmpOrderPrintCue (SalesID, PrintDateTime, IsReprinting)
  select SalesID, PrintDateTime, IsReprinting
  from tblOrderPrintCue  
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and PrintedStatus = 0

  select *
  from @tmpOrderPrintCue

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteCardInfo]
  @StationName varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  if (@StationName <> '''') begin

    update tblPayment
    set CardNumber = dbo.EncryptString(reverse(substring(reverse(dbo.DecryptString(CardNumber)), 1, 4))),
        CardExpiryDate = null,
        TrackData = null
    where upper(ltrim(rtrim(StationName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@StationName)))
      and CardExpiryDate is not null
  
  end
  else begin

    update tblPayment
    set CardNumber = dbo.EncryptString(reverse(substring(reverse(dbo.DecryptString(CardNumber)), 1, 4))),
        CardExpiryDate = null,
        TrackData = null
    where CardExpiryDate is not null

  end

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertDiscountDetail]
  @SalesID int,
  @SBSalesID int,
  @PersonIndex smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblDiscountDetail
             where case when @PersonIndex >= 0 then 
                          case when SalesID = @SBSalesID then 1 else 0 end
                        else
                          case when SalesID = @SalesID then 1 else 0 end
                   end = 1) begin

    declare @DSCAmt smallmoney, @DSCAmtEmployee smallmoney, @DSCAmtType1 smallmoney, @DSCAmtType2 smallmoney

    select @DSCAmt = sum(isnull(DSCAmt, 0)),
           @DSCAmtEmployee = sum(isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0)),
           @DSCAmtType1 = sum(isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0)),
           @DSCAmtType2 = sum(isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0))
    from tblPendingOrders 
    where case when @PersonIndex >= 0 then 
                 case when SalesID = @SalesID and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 case when SalesID = @SalesID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1

    update tblDiscountDetail
    set DSCAmt = @DSCAmt,
        DSCAmtEmployee = @DSCAmtEmployee,
        DSCAmtType1 = @DSCAmtType1,
        DSCAmtType2 = @DSCAmtType2
    where case when @PersonIndex >= 0 then 
                 case when SalesID = @SBSalesID then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 case when SalesID = @SalesID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1

  end
  else begin

    insert into tblDiscountDetail (SalesID, DSCAmt, DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2)
    select case when @PersonIndex >= 0 then @SBSalesID else SalesID end as SalesID, 
           sum(isnull(DSCAmt, 0)) as DSCAmt,
           sum(isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0)) as DSCAmtEmployee,
           sum(isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0)) as DSCAmtType1,
           sum(isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0)) as DSCAmtType2
    from tblPendingOrders
    where case when @PersonIndex >= 0 then 
                 case when SalesID = @SalesID and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 case when SalesID = @SalesID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1
    group by SalesID

  end
 
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetDiscountSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID int,
  @DSCAmt money = 0 output,
  @DSCAmtEmployee money = 0 output,
  @DSCAmtType1 money = 0 output,
  @DSCAmtType2 money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
  
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @DSCAmt = sum(d.DSCAmt),
         @DSCAmtEmployee = sum(d.DSCAmtEmployee),
         @DSCAmtType1 = sum(d.DSCAmtType1),
         @DSCAmtType2 = sum(d.DSCAmtType2)
  from tblSales s, tblDiscountDetail d, #tmp_station t
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime < @ToDateTime
    and case when @EmployeeID > 0 then
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1
    and d.SalesID = s.ID
    and s.StationID = t.StationID

  set @DSCAmt = isnull(@DSCAmt, 0)
  set @DSCAmtEmployee = isnull(@DSCAmtEmployee, 0)
  set @DSCAmtType1 = isnull(@DSCAmtType1, 0)
  set @DSCAmtType2 = isnull(@DSCAmtType2, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPendingOrdersTemp]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @TotalPersonCount tinyint

  set @TotalPersonCount = 1

  select @TotalPersonCount = max(PersonIndex) + 1 -- count(distinct PersonIndex)
  from tblPendingOrdersTemp
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  select @TotalPersonCount as TotalPersonCount, p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.Qty,
         case when (i.HourlyChargedItem = 1) then 
                case when (dbo.CheckIfSplitTimeChargeItemExists(p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex) = 0) then 
                       dbo.GetHourCharge(p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex)
                     else /* time charging must be stoppped if split exists, so get the price at the time of split */
                       p.UnitPrice 
                end
              else p.UnitPrice
         end as UnitPrice, 
         p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.SizeName, p.ApplyGST, p.ApplyPST, p.DSCAmt, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, 
         p.PersonIndex, p.SeparateBillPrint, p.Bar, p.ApplyNoDSC, p.OpenItem, p.ItemName2, p.ExtraChargeItem, p.ApplyPST2, 
         p.KitchenE, p.DSCAmtEmployee, p.DSCAmtType1, p.DSCAmtType2, i.Alcohol, p.DayHourDiscountRate, i.ScaleItem, i.RewardItem,
         i.HourlyChargedItem, p.PricePerWeightUnit, p.MeasuredWeight, p.DecimalPlaces, p.DiscountPercent, p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6
  from tblPendingOrdersTemp p
    inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
  order by p.PersonIndex

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPendingOrders]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @TotalPersonCount tinyint

  set @TotalPersonCount = 1

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblPendingOrders
                 where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

    insert into tblPendingOrders
    select *
    from tblPendingOrdersBackup
    where SalesID = @SalesID

  end

  select @TotalPersonCount = count(distinct PersonIndex)
  from tblPendingOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  select @TotalPersonCount as TotalPersonCount, p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.Qty,
         case when (i.HourlyChargedItem = 1) then 
                case when (dbo.CheckIfSplitTimeChargeItemExists(p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex) = 0) then 
                       dbo.GetHourCharge(p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex)
                     else /* time charging must be stoppped if split exists, so get the price at the time of split */
                       p.UnitPrice 
                end
              else p.UnitPrice
         end as UnitPrice, 
         p.Tastes, p.SideDishes, p.ItemName, p.SizeName, p.ApplyGST, p.ApplyPST, p.DSCAmt, p.KitchenB, p.KitchenF, 
         p.PersonIndex, p.SeparateBillPrint, p.Bar, p.ApplyNoDSC, p.OpenItem, p.ItemName2, p.ExtraChargeItem, p.ApplyPST2, 
         p.KitchenE, p.DSCAmtEmployee, p.DSCAmtType1, p.DSCAmtType2, i.Alcohol, p.DayHourDiscountRate, i.ScaleItem, i.RewardItem,
         i.HourlyChargedItem, p.PricePerWeightUnit, p.MeasuredWeight, p.DecimalPlaces, p.DiscountPercent, p.Kitchen5, p.Kitchen6
  from tblPendingOrders p
    inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
  order by p.PersonIndex

END'
GO
