EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetAllPendingOrders]
  @TakeOut bit,
  @DailyOrdNum int,
  @ShowTastes bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmp_pending_orders table
  (
    [ID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [SalesID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
    [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
    [Qty] [varchar](3) NOT NULL,
    [Tastes] [varchar](2000) NOT NULL,
    [ItemName] [varchar](200) NOT NULL,
    [PersonIndex] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
    [Status] [bit] NOT NULL,
    [TableName] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
    [DailyOrdNum] [int] NOT NULL,
    [SeparatedOrder] [bit] NOT NULL,
    [TableID] [smallint] NOT NULL
  ) 

  if (@DailyOrdNum > 0) begin

    declare @SeparatedOrder bit

    select @SeparatedOrder = case when count(distinct PersonIndex) > 1 then 1 else 0 end
    from tblCheckedOrders c, tblTable t
    where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
      and t.DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum

    insert into @tmp_pending_orders
    select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, convert(varchar(3), c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty)) as Qty, c.Tastes, 
           substring(case when c.SizeID > 1 then ''('' + c.SizeName + '')'' + c.ItemName
                          else c.ItemName 
                     end, 1, 200) as ItemName,
           c.PersonIndex, 
           case when c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) = 0 then 1
                else c.Status 
           end as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(@SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
    from tblCheckedOrders c, tblTable t
    where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
      and t.DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum
      and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) > 0
--    order by t.DailyOrdNum, c.PersonIndex, c.ID --, c.ItemName

    insert into @tmp_pending_orders
    select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, convert(varchar(3), c.DeletedQty) as Qty, c.Tastes, 
           substring(case when c.SizeID > 1 then ''('' + c.SizeName + '')'' + c.ItemName
                          else c.ItemName 
                     end, 1, 200) as ItemName,
           c.PersonIndex, 
           cast(1 as bit) as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(@SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
    from tblCheckedOrders c, tblTable t
    where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
      and t.DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum
      and c.DeletedQty > 0
      and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) >= 0

    if (@ShowTastes = 1) begin

      insert into @tmp_pending_orders
      select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, '''' as Qty, c.Tastes, 
             ''('' + dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(c.Tastes, '','') + '')'' as ItemName,
             --substring(''('' + substring(replace(replace(c.Tastes, ''|'', '',''), ''_'', '' ''), 1, len(c.Tastes) - 1) + '')'', 1, 200) as ItemName,
             c.PersonIndex, 
             case when c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) = 0 then 1
                  else c.Status 
             end as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(@SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
      from tblCheckedOrders c, tblTable t
      where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
        and t.DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum
        and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) > 0
        and len(ltrim(rtrim(c.Tastes))) > 0
  --    order by t.DailyOrdNum, c.PersonIndex, c.ID --, c.ItemName

      insert into @tmp_pending_orders
      select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, '''' as Qty, c.Tastes, 
             ''('' + dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(c.Tastes, '','') + '')'' as ItemName,
             --substring(''('' + substring(replace(replace(c.Tastes, ''|'', '',''), ''_'', '' ''), 1, len(c.Tastes) - 1) + '')'', 1, 200) as ItemName,
             c.PersonIndex, cast(1 as bit) as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(@SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
      from tblCheckedOrders c, tblTable t
      where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
        and t.DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum
        and c.DeletedQty > 0
        and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) >= 0
        and len(ltrim(rtrim(c.Tastes))) > 0

    end

    select *
    from @tmp_pending_orders
    order by DailyOrdNum, PersonIndex, ID, Qty desc

  end
  else begin

    select SalesID, cast(case when count(distinct PersonIndex) > 1 then 1 else 0 end as bit) as SeparatedOrder
    into #tmp_checked_orders
    from tblCheckedOrders
    group by SalesID
 
    insert into @tmp_pending_orders
    select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, convert(varchar(3), c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty)) as Qty, c.Tastes, 
           substring(case when c.SizeID > 1 then ''('' + c.SizeName + '')'' + c.ItemName
                          else c.ItemName 
                     end, 1, 200) as ItemName,
           c.PersonIndex, 
           case when c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) = 0 then 1
                else c.Status 
           end as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(o.SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
    from tblCheckedOrders c left join #tmp_checked_orders o on o.SalesID = c.SalesID, tblTable t
    where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
      and t.TakeOut = @TakeOut
      and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) > 0
--    order by t.DailyOrdNum, c.PersonIndex, c.ID --, c.ItemName

    insert into @tmp_pending_orders
    select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, convert(varchar(3), c.DeletedQty) as Qty, c.Tastes, 
           substring(case when c.SizeID > 1 then ''('' + c.SizeName + '')'' + c.ItemName
                          else c.ItemName 
                     end, 1, 200) as ItemName,
           c.PersonIndex, 
           cast(1 as bit) as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(o.SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
    from tblCheckedOrders c left join #tmp_checked_orders o on o.SalesID = c.SalesID, tblTable t
    where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
      and t.TakeOut = @TakeOut
      and c.DeletedQty > 0
      and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) >= 0

    if (@ShowTastes = 1) begin

      insert into @tmp_pending_orders
      select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, '''' as Qty, c.Tastes, 
             ''('' + dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(c.Tastes, '','') + '')'' as ItemName, 
             --substring(''('' + substring(replace(replace(c.Tastes, ''|'', '',''), ''_'', '' ''), 1, len(c.Tastes) - 1) + '')'', 1, 200) as ItemName,
             c.PersonIndex, 
             case when c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) = 0 then 1
                  else c.Status 
             end as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(o.SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
      from tblCheckedOrders c left join #tmp_checked_orders o on o.SalesID = c.SalesID, tblTable t
      where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
        and t.TakeOut = @TakeOut
        and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) > 0
        and len(ltrim(rtrim(c.Tastes))) > 0
  --    order by t.DailyOrdNum, c.PersonIndex, c.ID --, c.ItemName

      insert into @tmp_pending_orders
      select c.ID, c.SalesID, c.ItemID, c.SizeID, '''' as Qty, c.Tastes, 
             ''('' + dbo.ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter(c.Tastes, '','') + '')'' as ItemName,
             --substring(''('' + substring(replace(replace(c.Tastes, ''|'', '',''), ''_'', '' ''), 1, len(c.Tastes) - 1) + '')'', 1, 200) as ItemName,
             c.PersonIndex, cast(1 as bit) as [Status], t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, isnull(o.SeparatedOrder, 0), t.ID
      from tblCheckedOrders c left join #tmp_checked_orders o on o.SalesID = c.SalesID, tblTable t
      where c.SalesID = t.OrderNum
        and t.TakeOut = @TakeOut
        and c.DeletedQty > 0
        and c.Qty - convert(smallint, c.DeletedQty) >= 0
        and len(ltrim(rtrim(c.Tastes))) > 0

    end

    select *
    from @tmp_pending_orders
    order by DailyOrdNum, PersonIndex, ID, Qty desc

    drop table #tmp_checked_orders

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdatePendingOrderStatus]
  @CheckedOrderID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblCheckedOrders
  set [Status] = case when [Status] = 0 then 1 else 0 end,
      DeletedQty = case when [Status] = 0 then Qty else 0 end
  where ID = @CheckedOrderID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetAvailableSize]
  @ItemID smallint,
  @ForEdit bit,
  @StationName varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@ForEdit = 0) begin

    select 0 as OrderIndex, cast(''x'' as char(1)) as Available,
           s.*, '''' as SizeGroupName, a.*, 0 as ApplyQty, '''' as StationName
    from tblSize s
      inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where a.ItemID = @ItemID
      and s.ID = 1

    union all

    select 1 as OrderIndex, cast(''x'' as char(1)) as Available,
           s.*, isnull(sg.SizeGroupName, '''') as SizeGroupName, a.*, 0 as ApplyQty, '''' as StationName
    from tblSize s 
      left join tblSizeGroup sg on s.SizeGroupID = sg.ID
      inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where a.ItemID = @ItemID
      and s.ID > 1

    order by OrderIndex, SizeGroupName, s.DisplayOrder, s.SizeName, s.ID

  end
  else begin 

    select 0 as OrderIndex, cast(case when a.ItemID is null then '' '' else ''x'' end as char(1)) as Available,
           s.*, '''' as SizeGroupName, a.*
    from tblSize s
      left join (select *
                 from tblAvailableSizeTemp
                 where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                   and ItemID = @ItemID
                   and SizeID = 1) a on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where s.ID = 1

    union all

    select 1 as OrderIndex, cast(case when a.ItemID is null then '' '' else ''x'' end as char(1)) as Available, 
           s.*, isnull(sg.SizeGroupName, '''') as SizeGroupName, a.*
    from tblSize s left join tblSizeGroup sg on s.SizeGroupID = sg.ID
                   left join (select * 
                              from tblAvailableSizeTemp
                              where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                                and ItemID = @ItemID) a on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where s.ID > 1

    order by OrderIndex, SizeGroupName, s.DisplayOrder, s.SizeName, s.ID

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RecordInventoryChange]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @AppliedQty smallint,
  @UserID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --  if (@SalesID = 0) begin /* 0 means force update from item detail update */
--    insert into tblInventoryChangeHistory (ItemID, SizeID, OnHandQty, AppliedQty, SalesID, ChangedDateTime, UserID)
--    select @ItemID, @SizeID, OnHandQty, @AppliedQty, @SalesID, getdate(), @UserID
--    from tblAvailableSize
--    where ItemID = @ItemID
--      and SizeID = @SizeID
--      and OnHandQty <> @AppliedQty
--
--    update tblAvailableSize
--    set OnHandQty = @AppliedQty
--    where ItemID = @ItemID
--      and SizeID = @SizeID
--  end
--  else begin

    if exists (select 1
               from tblItem 
               where ManageInv = 1
                 and ID = @ItemID) begin

      if (@AppliedQty <> 0) begin   

        update tblAvailableSize
        set OnHandQty = case when OnHandQty < -30000 then 0 else OnHandQty end
        where ItemID = @ItemID
          and SizeID = @SizeID
        
        insert into tblInventoryChangeHistory (ItemID, SizeID, OnHandQty, AppliedQty, SalesID, ChangedDateTime, UserID)
        select @ItemID, @SizeID, OnHandQty, @AppliedQty, @SalesID, getdate(), @UserID
        from tblAvailableSize
        where ItemID = @ItemID
          and SizeID = @SizeID

        update tblAvailableSize
        set OnHandQty = OnHandQty + @AppliedQty
        where ItemID = @ItemID
          and SizeID = @SizeID

      end

    end

--  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetItemsForListView]
  @CategoryID tinyint,
  @Status tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select i.*, c.CatName
  from tblItem i, tblCategory c
  where i.CategoryID = @CategoryID
    and i.CategoryID = c.ID
    and case when @Status = 1 then
               case when i.Status = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             when @Status = 2 then
               case when i.Status = 0 then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by i.IName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetItemsForTreeView]
  @Status tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  select c.ID as CategoryID, c.*,
         i.ID as ItemID, i.*
  from tblItem i, tblCategory c
  where i.CategoryID = c.ID
    and case when @Status = 1 then
               case when i.Status = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             when @Status = 2 then
               case when i.Status = 0 then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by c.CatName, i.IName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetInventoryChangeHistory]
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ItemID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  if (@ItemID = 0) begin
    select h.ID, h.ItemID, i.IName, h.SizeID, h.AppliedQty, 
           case when h.SizeID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName, 
           h.OnHandQty as OnHandBefore, 
           h.OnHandQty + h.AppliedQty as OnHandAfter,            
           case when h.SalesID = 0 then ''Inv. Qty Change'' 
                else ''Transaction ID '' + convert(varchar(50), h.SalesID) end as Note,
           ChangedDateTime,
           (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as UserName
    from tblInventoryChangeHistory h, tblItem i, tblUser u, tblSize s 
    where h.ItemID = i.ID
      and h.SizeID = s.ID
      and h.UserID = u.ID
      and h.ChangedDateTime >= convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112)
      and h.ChangedDateTime < dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112))
      -- and h.OnHandQty >= 0
    order by h.ID desc
  end
  else begin
    select h.ID, h.ItemID, i.IName, h.SizeID, h.AppliedQty, 
           case when h.SizeID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName, 
           h.OnHandQty as OnHandBefore, 
           h.OnHandQty + h.AppliedQty as OnHandAfter,
           case when h.SalesID = 0 then ''Inv. Qty Change'' 
                else ''Transaction ID '' + convert(varchar(50), h.SalesID) end as Note,
           ChangedDateTime,
           (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as UserName
    from tblInventoryChangeHistory h, tblItem i, tblUser u, tblSize s 
    where h.ItemID = i.ID
      and h.SizeID = s.ID
      and h.UserID = u.ID
      and h.ChangedDateTime >= convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112)
      and h.ChangedDateTime < dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112))
      and i.ID = @ItemID
    order by h.ID desc
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateCallStatus]
  @BellNumber smallint,
  @CallType tinyint,
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@TableID > 0) begin
    update tblTable
    set CallType = 255
    where ID = @TableID
  end
  else begin
    if (@StationID > 0) begin
      update tblTable
      set CallType = @CallType
      from tblTable 
      where StationID = @StationID 
    end
    else begin
      update tblTable
      set CallType = @CallType
      where BellNumber = @BellNumber 
    end
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_AssignBellNumberToTable]
  @TableID smallint,
  @BellNumber smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblTable
  set BellNumber = 0,
      CallType = 255
  where BellNumber = @BellNumber

  update tblTable
  set BellNumber = @BellNumber
  where ID = @TableID  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfPointsDetailExists]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblPointsDetail
             where SalesID = @SalesID) 
    select cast(1 as bit) as DetailExists
  else
    select cast(0 as bit) as DetailExists

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertUpdateRewardPointsDetail]
  @SalesID int,
  @CustomerID int,
  @PointUsed int,
  @PointSaved int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@CustomerID > 1) begin

    if exists (select *
               from tblPointsDetail
               where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

      update tblCustomer
      set EarnedPoints = EarnedPoints - @PointUsed
      where ID = @CustomerID

      update tblPointsDetail
      set PointUsed = PointUsed + @PointUsed --,
          --PointSaved = PointSaved + @PointSaved
      where SalesID = @SalesID

    end
    else begin

      update tblCustomer
      set EarnedPoints = EarnedPoints - @PointUsed + @PointSaved
      where ID = @CustomerID

      insert into tblPointsDetail (SalesID, PointUsed, PointSaved)
      values (@SalesID, @PointUsed, @PointSaved)
  
    end

  end

END'
GO

  @Code varchar(5)
AS

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select dbo.GetMiscValue(@Code)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateMisc]
  @Value varchar(255),
  @Code varchar(5)
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

  update tblMisc
  set [Value] = @Value
  where Code = @Code

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_misc
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_misc
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end
  
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_BackupDatabase]
  @BackupFilePath varchar(255)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @TableName varchar(100), @IndexName varchar(100), @FragmentationPercentage decimal(4,2),
          @IndexType varchar(20), @IsPrimaryKey bit, @IsUnique bit, @script nvarchar(1000)

  declare curs_index_fragmentation_status cursor for
    select /*s.name as [Schema],*/ 
           ''['' + s.name + ''].['' + t.name + '']'' as TableName, 
           ''['' + i.name + '']'' as IndexName, 
           ddips.avg_fragmentation_in_percent,
           ddips.index_type_desc,
           i.is_primary_key,
           i.is_unique
           /*, ddips.page_count*/
    from sys.dm_db_index_physical_stats (db_id(), null, null, null, null) as ddips
      inner join sys.tables t on t.object_id = ddips.object_id
      inner join sys.schemas s on t.schema_id = s.schema_id
      inner join sys.indexes i on i.object_id = ddips.object_id
                              and ddips.index_id = i.index_id
    where ddips.database_id = db_id()
      and i.name is not null
      and ddips.avg_fragmentation_in_percent > 0
    order by TableName, IndexName -- ddips.avg_fragmentation_in_percent desc

    open curs_index_fragmentation_status
    fetch next from curs_index_fragmentation_status into @TableName, @IndexName, @FragmentationPercentage, @IndexType, @IsPrimaryKey, @IsUnique
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      if (@FragmentationPercentage >= 30) begin
        --print ''rebuilding '' + @IndexName + '' on '' + @TableName
        set @script = ''ALTER INDEX '' + @IndexName + '' ON '' + @TableName + '' REBUILD WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, ONLINE = OFF''
        if (@IsPrimaryKey = 1) or (@IsUnique = 0)
          set @script = @script + '')''
        else
          set @script = @script + '', IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF)''          
      end
      else begin
        if (@FragmentationPercentage >= 15) begin
          --print ''reorganizing '' + @IndexName + '' on '' + @TableName
          set @script = ''ALTER INDEX '' + @IndexName + '' ON '' + @TableName + '' REORGANIZE WITH (LOB_COMPACTION = ON)''
        end
      end

      exec sp_executesql @script

      fetch next from curs_index_fragmentation_status into @TableName, @IndexName, @FragmentationPercentage, @IndexType, @IsPrimaryKey, @IsUnique
    end
    close curs_index_fragmentation_status
  deallocate curs_index_fragmentation_status

  delete t
  from tblCashTip t
    inner join tblSales s on t.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -14, dbo.GetFromDateTime(getdate(), 0))

  delete
  from tblInventoryChangeHistory
  where ChangedDateTime < dateadd(m, -3, getdate())

  delete
  from tblUserLog
  where LogDateTime < dateadd(d, -14, getdate())

  delete p
  from tblPendingOrders p 
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblTable t
                    where t.OrderNum = p.SalesID)
    and s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -7, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete t
  from tblPendingOrdersTemp t
    inner join tblSales s on t.SalesID = s.ID
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblPendingOrders p
                    where p.SalesID = t.SalesID)
    and s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -1, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete t
  from tblPendingOrdersBackup t
    inner join tblSales s on t.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -7, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete t
  from tblOrderPrintCue t
  where t.DateTimeIn < dateadd(d, -7, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete t
  from tblTimeStartEnd t
    inner join tblSales s on t.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -7, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete tib
  from tblTipAmountInBill tib
    inner join tblSales s on tib.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -7, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))
    and not exists (select *
                    from tblTable t
                    where t.OrderNum = tib.SalesID)

  delete t
  from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode t
  where t.ExpiryDateTime < getdate()

  delete p
  from tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblTable t
                    where t.OrderNum = p.SalesID)
    and s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -30, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete c
  from tblCallHistory c
  where c.CalledDateTime < dateadd(d, -30, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  delete p
  from tblNonIntegratedOnlineSelfPaymentURL p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < dateadd(d, -30, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))

  update o
  set o.[Status] = 0,
      o.SalesID = -1
  from tblOnlineOrders o
  where o.RequestedDateTime < convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)
    and o.[Status] = 1
    and o.SalesID = 0

  declare @max_id int

  select @max_id = max(ID)
  from tblInventoryChangeHistory
  
  if (@max_id > 2000000000) begin

    select *
    into #tmpInventoryChangeHistory
    from tblInventoryChangeHistory
    
    truncate table tblInventoryChangeHistory
    
    insert into tblInventoryChangeHistory (ItemID, SizeID, OnHandQty, AppliedQty, SalesID, ChangedDateTime, UserID)
    select ItemID, SizeID, OnHandQty, AppliedQty, SalesID, ChangedDateTime, UserID
    from #tmpInventoryChangeHistory
    order by ID

    drop table #tmpInventoryChangeHistory

  end 

  select @max_id = max(ID)
  from tblUserLog
  
  if (@max_id > 2000000000) begin

    select *
    into #tmpUserLog
    from tblUserLog

    truncate table tblUserLog

    insert into tblUserLog (LogDateTime, UserID, UserActionID, StationName)
    select LogDateTime, UserID, UserActionID, StationName
    from #tmpUserLog
    order by ID

    drop table #tmpUserLog

  end

  select @max_id = convert(int, Value)
  from tblMisc
  where Code = ''DON''

  if (@max_id > 9999) begin

    update tblMisc
    set Value = ''1''
    where Code = ''DON''

  end

  truncate table tblOrderNumber

  declare @LogicalName varchar(20)

  select @LogicalName = [name]
  from sys.database_files
  where type_desc = ''LOG''

  ALTER DATABASE TPPro
  SET RECOVERY SIMPLE

  DBCC SHRINKFILE (@LogicalName, 1)

  ALTER DATABASE TPPro
  SET RECOVERY FULL

  BACKUP DATABASE TPPro
  TO DISK = @BackupFilePath
  WITH FORMAT

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

  @CategoryID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

                 from tblItem 
                 where CategoryID = @CategoryID) begin

    delete
    from tblCategory
    where ID = @CategoryID

      select cast(1 as bit) as Result 
    else

  end
  else

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfClockOutIsAllowed]
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblSales s, tblUser u
             where s.CashierID = u.ID
               and s.TransType in (0, 1, 2, 3, 4)
               and s.SaleDateTime > isnull(u.LastClosingTime, getdate())
               and s.CashierID = @EmployeeID)

    select cast(0 as bit) as Allowed

  else
    
    select cast(1 as bit) as Allowed

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetClockInOutInfo]
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select ts.ID, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut, ts.State, 
         convert(varchar, datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) / 60) + '' hr. '' + 
         convert(varchar, datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) % 60) + '' min.'' as WorkHour,
         u.FName + '' '' + u.LName as EmployeeName
  from tblTimeStamp ts, tblUser u
  where ts.EmployeeID = u.ID
    and u.ID = @EmployeeID
    and exists (select max(ts2.ID)
                from tblTimeStamp ts2
                where ts2.EmployeeID = ts.EmployeeID
                having max(ts2.ID) = ts.ID)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetUserLog]
  @LogFromDate smalldatetime,
  @LogToDate smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select ul.*, ua.ActionDescription, ltrim(rtrim(isnull(u.FName, '''') + '' '' + isnull(u.LName, ''''))) as UserName
  from tblUserLog ul left join tblUser u on ul.UserID = u.ID, tblUserAction ua
  where ul.UserActionID = ua.ID
    and ul.LogDateTime >= @LogFromDate
    and ul.LogDateTime <  dateadd(d, 1, @LogToDate)
  order by ul.ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RecordUserLog]
  @UserID smallint,
  @ActionCode varchar(10),
  @StationName varchar(50)
  --@Recorded bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction record_user_log

    insert into tblUserLog (LogDateTime, UserID, UserActionID, StationName)
    select getdate(), @UserID, ID, @StationName
    from tblUserAction
    where ActionCode = @ActionCode  

    commit transaction record_user_log
    --set @Recorded = 1
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction record_user_log
    --set @Recorded = 0  
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTimeChargedItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex, (p.PersonIndex + 1) as DisplayPersonIndex, t.ID as TableID, 
         case when dense_rank() over (partition by t.TableName order by t.TableName, i.IName, p.PersonIndex) = 1 then
                case when (t.TakeOut = 0) and (ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson)) <> '''') then t.PickupPerson 
                     else t.TableName 
                end
              else ''''
         end as TableName, 
         i.IName, 
         case when p.SideDishes like ''SPLIT_[HT]_%'' then ''Stopped(S)'' 
              else dbo.GetHourChargeStatus(p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.PersonIndex)
         end as [Status],
         cast(case when p.SideDishes like ''SPLIT_[HT]_%'' then 1 else 0 end as bit) as [SplitStatus],
         dense_rank() over (order by t.TableName) as DisplayOrderIndex, 
         row_number() over (order by t.TableName, i.IName, p.PersonIndex) as DisplayRowIndex
  from tblPendingOrders p
    inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblTable t on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where p.SizeID = 1
    and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1
    and p.Qty > 0
  order by t.TableName, i.IName, p.PersonIndex

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertTimeStartEnd]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @Paused bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --delete t
  --from tblTimeStartEnd t
  --where not exists (select *
  --                  from tblPendingOrders p
  --                  where p.SalesID = t.SalesID
  --                    and p.ItemID = t.ItemID)
  
  if (@ItemID > 0) begin

    if (@Paused = 0) begin

      if (dbo.CheckIfSplitTimeChargeItemExists(@SalesID, @ItemID, @PersonIndex) = 0) begin
        
        insert into tblTimeStartEnd (SalesID, ItemID, PersonIndex, StartDateTime, EndDateTime, [Stopped])
        values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @PersonIndex, getdate(), getdate(), 0)
      
        /* since only one same type of time charge item is allowed in one person index, the below script should update for one item only */
        update po
        set po.SideDishes = ''''
        from tblPendingOrders po
        where po.SalesID = @SalesID
          and po.ItemID = @ItemID
          and po.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex

      end      

    end
    else begin

      update t
      set t.EndDateTime = getdate(),
          t.[Stopped] = 1
      from tblTimeStartEnd t
      where t.SalesID = @SalesID
        and t.ItemID = @ItemID
        and t.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
        and exists (select t2.SalesID, t2.ItemID, max(t2.ID)
                    from tblTimeStartEnd t2
                    where t2.SalesID = t.SalesID
                      and t2.ItemID = t.ItemID
                      and t2.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
                    group by t2.SalesID, t2.ItemID
                    having max(t2.ID) = t.ID)

      update t
      set t.[Stopped] = 1
      from tblTimeStartEnd t
      where t.SalesID = @SalesID
        and t.ItemID = @ItemID
        and t.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
        and t.[Stopped] = 0

    end

  end
  else begin

    if exists (select *
               from tblTimeStartEnd 
               where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

      declare curs_time_charge_items cursor for
        select ItemID, PersonIndex
        from tblTimeStartEnd
        where SalesID = @SalesID

        open curs_time_charge_items
        fetch next from curs_time_charge_items into @ItemID, @PersonIndex
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
  
          if not exists (select *
                         from tblPendingOrders
                         where SalesID = @SalesID
                           and ItemID = @ItemID
                           and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex) begin

            update t
            set t.PersonIndex = po.PersonIndex
            from tblTimeStartEnd t
              inner join (select SalesID, ItemID, min(PersonIndex) as PersonIndex
                          from tblPendingOrders
                          where SalesID = @SalesID
                            and ItemID = @ItemID
                          group by SalesID, ItemID) po on po.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                                      and po.ItemID = t.ItemID
            where t.SalesID = @SalesID
              and t.ItemID = @ItemID
              and t.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
              and not exists (select *
                              from tblTimeStartEnd t2
                              where t2.SalesID = po.SalesID
                                and t2.ItemID = po.ItemID
                                and t2.PersonIndex = po.PersonIndex)

          end

          fetch next from curs_time_charge_items into @ItemID, @PersonIndex
        end
        close curs_time_charge_items
      deallocate curs_time_charge_items

    end

    insert into tblTimeStartEnd (SalesID, ItemID, PersonIndex, StartDateTime, EndDateTime, [Stopped])
    select po.SalesID, po.ItemID, po.PersonIndex, getdate(), getdate(), case when po.SideDishes like ''SPLIT_[HT]_%'' then 1 else 0 end
    from tblPendingOrders po
      inner join tblItem i on po.ItemID = i.ID
    where po.SalesID = @SalesID
      and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1
      and po.SizeID = 1
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblTimeStartEnd t
                      where t.SalesID = po.SalesID
                        and t.ItemID = po.ItemID
                        and t.PersonIndex = po.PersonIndex)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

    --set @Stopped = 0

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetUser]
  @Status tinyint,
  @UserID smallint,
  @GroupID tinyint,
  @Type tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(1000)

  if (@Type = 1)

    set @script = ''select u.ID, u.UserAccessCode, u.LName, u.FName, '' +
                  ''       u.GroupID, u.[Status], u.[Address], u.Wage, u.Memo, u.LastClosingTime, u.TipOutPercentage, '' +
                  ''       u.SystemUser, u.AccessPermission, g.GroupName, isnull(t.ClockedIn, 0) as ClockedIn '' +
                  ''from tblUser u '' +
                  ''  inner join tblGroup g on u.GroupID = g.ID '' +
                  ''  left join (select distinct EmployeeID, cast(1 as bit) as ClockedIn '' +
                  ''             from tblTimeStamp '' +
                  ''             where [State] = 0) t on t.EmployeeID = u.ID '' +
                  ''where u.SystemUser = 1 '' +
                  ''  and case when exists (select 1 '' +
                                          ''from tblMisc '' +
                                          ''where Code = ''''SCIUO'''' '' +
                                          ''  and Upper(Value) = ''''TRUE'''') then '' +
                               ''case when isnull(t.ClockedIn, 0) = 1 then 1 else 0 end '' +
                             ''else 1 end = 1 ''

  else   

    set @script = ''select u.ID, u.UserAccessCode, u.LName, u.FName, '' +
                  ''       u.GroupID, u.[Status], u.[Address], u.Wage, u.Memo, u.LastClosingTime, u.TipOutPercentage, '' +
                  ''       u.SystemUser, u.AccessPermission, g.GroupName, cast(0 as bit) as ClockedIn '' +
                  ''from tblUser u '' +
                  ''  inner join tblGroup g on u.GroupID = g.ID '' +
                  ''where 1 = 1 ''
 
  if (@GroupID > 1) begin
    if (@UserID > 0) begin
      if ((@Type = 3) and (@GroupID >= 3)) 
        set @script = @script + ''and (u.ID = '' + convert(varchar, @UserID) + '' or g.ID = '' + convert(varchar, @GroupID) + '') ''
      else
        set @script = @script + ''and (u.ID = '' + convert(varchar, @UserID) + '' or g.ID > '' + convert(varchar, @GroupID) + '') ''
    end
    else
      set @script = @script + ''and g.ID > '' + convert(varchar, @GroupID) + '' ''
  end

  if (@Status in (0, 1))
    set @script = @script + ''and u.[Status] = '' + convert(varchar, @Status) + '' ''

  if (@Type = 1) begin
    set @script = @script + 
                  ''order by ClockedIn desc, u.LName, u.FName''
  end
  else begin
    set @script = @script +
                  ''order by u.GroupID, u.FName, u.LName''
  end
               

  exec sp_executesql @script
  
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfClockedIn]
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @GroupID tinyint

  select @GroupID = GroupID
  from tblUser
  where ID = @EmployeeID

  if (isnull(@GroupID, 0) < 3) or
     exists (select ts.*
             from tblTimeStamp ts
             where ts.EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
               and ts.State = 0
               and exists (select ts2.EmployeeID, max(ts2.ID)
                           from tblTimeStamp ts2
                           where ts2.EmployeeID = ts.EmployeeID
                           group by ts2.EmployeeID
                           having max(ts2.ID) = ts.ID))

    select cast(1 as bit) as ClockedIn

  else
    
    select cast(0 as bit) as ClockedIn    

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSoldItemsSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @SoldItemsCount int = 0 output,
  @SoldAmount money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@EmployeeID = 0) begin
    select @SoldItemsCount = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * sd.Qty),
           @SoldAmount = sum(round(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2))
    from tblSales s, tblSalesDetail sd, #tmp_station t
    where sd.SalesID = s.ID
      and s.StationID = t.StationID
      and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and s.TransType in (0, 1)
      and sd.Voided = 0
  end
  else begin
    select @SoldItemsCount = sum(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * sd.Qty),
           @SoldAmount = sum(round(case when s.TransType = 0 then -1 else 1 end * sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2))
    from tblSales s, tblSalesDetail sd, #tmp_station t
    where sd.SalesID = s.ID
      and s.StationID = t.StationID
      and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and s.CashierID = @EmployeeID
      and s.TransType in (0, 1)
      and sd.Voided = 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_EmployeeWorkHourSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @LunchTimeMinutes smallint,
  @RegularWorkHours smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes smallint

  set @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes = 60 * @RegularWorkHours
  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select EmployeeID, sum(case [State] when 0 then 0 else datediff(n, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut) end) as TotalHoursInMinutes,
         convert(varchar, sum(case [State] when 0 then 0 else datediff(n, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut) end) / 60) + '':'' +
         convert(varchar, sum(case [State] when 0 then 0 else datediff(n, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut) end) % 60) as TotalWorkedHours,
         sum(round(case [State] when 0 then 0 else datediff(n, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut) end / 60.0, 2)) as AccountingTotalWorkedHours     
  into #tmp_total_work_hours
  from tblTimeStamp
  where DateTimeIn >= @FromDateTime
    and DateTimeIn <  @ToDateTime
  group by EmployeeID

  select ts.ID, ts.EmployeeID, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut, t.TotalHoursInMinutes, TotalWorkedHours, AccountingTotalWorkedHours,     
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''IN'' 
                         else ''OUT'' end as [Status],         
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''00:00''
                         else convert(varchar, datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) / 60) + '':'' +
                              convert(varchar, datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) % 60) end as WorkedHours,         
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0 
                         else datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) end as HoursInMinutes,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0 
                         else round(datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) / 60.0, 2) end as AccountingWorkedHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''00:00''
                         else convert(varchar, @LunchTimeMinutes / 60) + '':'' +
                              convert(varchar, @LunchTimeMinutes % 60) end as LunchHours, 
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0 
                         else round(@LunchTimeMinutes / 60.0, 2) end as AccountingLunchHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''00:00''
                         else convert(varchar, case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                      then @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                    else datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes 
                                               end / 60) + '':'' + 
                              convert(varchar, case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                      then @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                    else datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes 
                                               end % 60) end as ActualWorkedHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0 
                         else round(case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                           then @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                         else datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes 
                                    end / 60.0, 2) end as AccountingActualWorkedHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''00:00''
                         else convert(varchar, @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes / 60) + '':'' + 
                              convert(varchar, @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes % 60) end as RegularWorkHours, 
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0
                         else round(@RegularWorkHoursInMinutes / 60.0, 2) end as AccountingRegularWorkHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then ''00:00''
                         else convert(varchar, case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                      then datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes - @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                    else 0 end / 60) + '':'' + 
                              convert(varchar, case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                      then datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes - @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                                    else 0 end % 60) end as OverTimeHours,
         case ts.[State] when 0 then 0
                         else round(case when datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes > @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                           then datediff(n, ts.DateTimeIn, ts.DateTimeOut) - @LunchTimeMinutes - @RegularWorkHoursInMinutes 
                                         else 0 end / 60.0, 2) end as AccountingOverTimeHours,
         u.FName, u.LName, isnull(h.Wage, 0) as Wage
  from tblUser u
    inner join tblTimeStamp ts on ts.EmployeeID = u.ID
    inner join #tmp_total_work_hours t on t.EmployeeID = u.ID
    left join tblEmployeeWageHistory h on h.EmployeeID = ts.EmployeeID
                                      and exists (select max(w.EffectiveDate)
                                                  from tblEmployeeWageHistory w
                                                  where w.EmployeeID = h.EmployeeID
                                                    and w.EffectiveDate <= ts.DateTimeIn
                                                  having max(w.EffectiveDate) = h.EffectiveDate)
  where ts.DateTimeIn >= @FromDateTime
    and ts.DateTimeIn <  @ToDateTime
  order by ts.EmployeeID asc, ts.DateTimeIn desc

  drop table #tmp_total_work_hours 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_ClearDatabase]
  @InitializeDB bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@InitializeDB = 1) begin
    truncate table tblAdImages

      Attention = 0,

      StayOn = 0,

    where ID > 1

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblItem'', RESEED, 0)

    delete
    from tblCategory

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblCategory'', RESEED, 0)

    from tblOnlineOrderCompany

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblOnlineOrderCompany'', RESEED, 0)

    delete
    from tblPeripherals
    where [Code] not in (''CDKEY'', ''RAND'', ''MACAD'')

    delete
    from tblPurchaseItem

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblPurchaseItem'', RESEED, 0)

    delete
    from tblPurchaseItemCategory

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblPurchaseItemCategory'', RESEED, 0)
    
    delete
    from tblSize
    where ID > 1    

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblSize'', RESEED, 1)

    delete
    from tblTare
    where ID > 1

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblTare'', RESEED, 1)

  end

  delete
  from tblLoyaltyStampCard

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblLoyaltyStampCard'', RESEED, 0)

  delete
  from tblPrepaidCards

--  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblPrepaidCards'', RESEED, 0)

  from tblSales

  if (@InitializeDB = 1) begin

        KitchenDisplay = 0
    where ID = 1
  
  end

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteSaleTransactions]
  @SelectedDate smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @SelectedDate = dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @SelectedDate, 112))

  delete sd
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete di
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblDeletedItems di on di.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete dd
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblDiscountDetail dd on dd.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete dui
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblDeletedUnsavedItems dui on dui.LastSalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete p
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete po
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPendingOrders po on po.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete pot
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPendingOrdersTemp pot on pot.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete pd
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPointsDetail pd on pd.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete p
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory p on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete o
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete sc
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblStoreCredit sc on sc.StoreCreditSalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate
    
  delete c
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblCredit c on c.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete h
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblBillCollectHistory h on h.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete ct
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  update t
  set t.OrderNum = 0,
      t.TimeIn = getdate(),
      t.ServerID = 0,
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      t.TakeOut = 0,
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
      t.BellNumber = 0,
      t.CallType = 255
  from tblTable t
    inner join tblSales s on t.OrderNum = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  delete s
  from tblSales s
  where s.SaleDateTime < @SelectedDate

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblSales) begin

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblSales'', RESEED, 0)
    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblPayment'', RESEED, 0)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MoveTable]
  @FromTableID smallint,
  @ToTableID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @FromTableName varchar(20), @ToTableName varchar(20), @TableMoveNotificationMessage varchar(100), @SalesID int, 
          @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint, @OnlineOrderNumber varchar(20), @OnlineOrderCustomerName varchar(100), @TakeOutOrder bit

  update t2
  set t2.OrderNum = t1.OrderNum,
      t2.TimeIn = t1.TimeIn,
      t2.ServerID = t1.ServerID,
      t2.NumOfGuests = t1.NumOfGuests,
      t2.Opened = 0,
      t2.PickupTime = t1.PickupTime,
      t2.PhoneNum = t1.PhoneNum,
      t2.PickupPerson = t1.PickupPerson,
      t2.BillPrinted = t1.BillPrinted,
      t2.Attention = t1.Attention,
      t2.DailyOrdNum = t1.DailyOrdNum,
      t2.PickupDate = t1.PickupDate,
      t2.TotalAmt = t1.TotalAmt,
      t2.OnlineOrderNumber = t1.OnlineOrderNumber
  from tblTable t1
    inner join tblTable t2 on 1 = 1
  where t1.ID = @FromTableID
    and t2.ID = @ToTableID  

  update t
  set t.OrderNum = 0,
      t.ServerID = 0,
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
      t.PickupDate = null,
      t.TotalAmt = 0,
      t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
  from tblTable t
  where t.ID = @FromTableID

  select @FromTableName = TableName
  from tblTable
  where ID = @FromTableID

  select @ToTableName = TableName,
         @SalesID = OrderNum,
         @OnlineOrderCompanyID = OnlineOrderCompanyID,
         @TakeOutOrder = TakeOut
  from tblTable
  where ID = @ToTableID

  update tblSales
  set TakeOutOrder = @TakeOutOrder,
      TableID = @ToTableID
  where ID = @SalesID

  delete o
  from tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o
    inner join tblTable t on o.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where t.ID = @ToTableID

  if (exists (select *
              from tblTable
              where ID = @ToTableID
                and TakeOut = 1
                and (Delivery = 1 or [Online] = 1)
                and OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0)) begin

    select @OnlineOrderNumber = OnlineOrderNumber,
           @OnlineOrderCustomerName = PickupPerson
    from tblTable
    where ID = @ToTableID

    exec sp_InsertSalesOfOnlineOrders @SalesID, @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OnlineOrderNumber, @OnlineOrderCustomerName, 0

  end

  set @TableMoveNotificationMessage = char(13) + char(10) + char(13) + char(10) + 
                                      char(13) + char(10) + char(13) + char(10) +
                                      ''Table MOVED!'' + char(13) + char(10) + char(13) + char(10) + 
                                      @FromTableName + '' --> '' + @ToTableName + 
                                      char(13) + char(10) + char(13) + char(10) +
                                      char(13) + char(10) + char(13) + char(10) +
                                      ''_''
  
  select @TableMoveNotificationMessage as TableMoveNotificationMessage

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RecordNoSaleTransaction]
  @CashierID int,
  @StationID smallint,
  @UseSpecialOrderNumberSequence bit,
  @LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction record_no_sale

  declare @DailyOrderNumber int

  exec sp_GetDailyOrderNumber @UseSpecialOrderNumberSequence, @LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence, @DailyOrderNumber output

  insert into tblSales (CashierID, SaleDateTime, SubTotal, DSCAmt, GSTAmt, PSTAmt, TransType, OriginalTransType, Guests,
                        CustomerID, DailyOrderNumber, GSTRate, PSTRate, TakeOutOrder, TableID, StationID, AlcoholDSCAmt, CustomerTypeID, CustomerGroupID)
  values (@CashierID, getdate(), 0, 0, 0, 0, 2, 2, 1, 1, @DailyOrderNumber, 0, 0, 0, 0, @StationID, 0, 1, 1)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction record_no_sale
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction record_no_sale
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteCheckedOrders]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction delete_checked_orders

  delete
  from tblCheckedOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction delete_checked_orders
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction delete_checked_orders
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPendingOrdersBackup]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblPendingOrders
             where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

    delete
    from tblPendingOrdersBackup
    where SalesID = @SalesID

    insert into tblPendingOrdersBackup
    select *
    from tblPendingOrders
    where SalesID = @SalesID

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCheckedOrders]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ItemID smallint, @SizeID tinyint, @Qty smallint, @DeletedQty tinyint, @Tastes varchar(200), 
          @ItemName varchar(30), @SizeName varchar(30), @PersonIndex tinyint

  declare @tmpCheckedOrders table
  (
    [ID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [SalesID] [int] NOT NULL,
    [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
    [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
    [Qty] [smallint] NULL,
    [DeletedQty] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
    [Tastes] [varchar](2000) NOT NULL,
    [ItemName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
    [SizeName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
    [PersonIndex] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
    [Status] [bit] NOT NULL
  )

  insert into @tmpCheckedOrders
  select *
  from tblCheckedOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID  

  delete
  from tblCheckedOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  insert into tblCheckedOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, DeletedQty, Tastes, ItemName, SizeName, PersonIndex, [Status])
  select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, 0, Tastes, ItemName,
--         case when ltrim(rtrim(isnull(ItemName2, ''''))) = '''' then ItemName else ItemName2 end, 
         SizeName, PersonIndex, 0
  from tblPendingOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and ExtraChargeItem = 0

  declare curs_checked_orders cursor for
    select ItemID, SizeID, DeletedQty, Tastes, PersonIndex
    from @tmpCheckedOrders
    where [Status] = 1

    open curs_checked_orders 
    fetch next from curs_checked_orders into @ItemID, @SizeID, @DeletedQty, @Tastes, @PersonIndex
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      while (@DeletedQty > 0) begin
      
        update c
        set c.DeletedQty = c.DeletedQty + 1
        from tblCheckedOrders c
        where c.SalesID = @SalesID
          and c.ItemID = @ItemID
          and c.SizeID = @SizeID
          and c.Tastes = @Tastes
          and c.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
          and exists (select 1
                      from tblCheckedOrders c2
                      where c2.SalesID = c.SalesID
                        and c2.ItemID = c.ItemID
                        and c2.SizeID = c.SizeID
                        and c2.Tastes = c.Tastes
                        and c2.PersonIndex = c.PersonIndex
                        and c2.DeletedQty < c2.Qty
                      group by c2.SalesID, c2.ItemID, c2.SizeID, c2.Tastes, c2.PersonIndex
                      having min(c2.ID) = c.ID)
  
        set @DeletedQty = @DeletedQty - 1

      end

      fetch next from curs_checked_orders into @ItemID, @SizeID, @DeletedQty, @Tastes, @PersonIndex
    end
    close curs_checked_orders
  deallocate curs_checked_orders

  update c
  set c.Status = case when c.Qty = c.DeletedQty then 1 else 0 end
  from tblCheckedOrders c
  where c.SalesID = @SalesID


  /*
  insert into tblCheckedOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, DeletedQty, Tastes, ItemName, SizeName, PersonIndex, [Status])
  select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, 0, Tastes, ItemName,
--         case when ltrim(rtrim(isnull(ItemName2, ''''))) = '''' then ItemName else ItemName2 end, 
         SizeName, PersonIndex, 0
  from tblPendingOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and ExtraChargeItem = 0

  update c
  set c.Status = 1
  from tblCheckedOrders c
    inner join @tmpCheckedOrders t on c.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                  and c.ItemID = t.ItemID
                                  and c.SizeID = t.SizeID
                                  and c.Tastes = t.Tastes
                                  and c.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
  where t.Status = 1  
  */

  /*
  insert into tblCheckedOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, DeletedQty, Tastes, ItemName, SizeName, PersonIndex, [Status])
  select SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, 0, Tastes, ItemName,
--         case when ltrim(rtrim(isnull(ItemName2, ''''))) = '''' then ItemName else ItemName2 end, 
         SizeName, PersonIndex, 0
  from tblPendingOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and ExtraChargeItem = 0

  update c
  set c.DeletedQty = t.Qty
  from tblCheckedOrders c
    inner join @tmpCheckedOrders t on c.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                  and c.ItemID = t.ItemID
                                  and c.SizeID = t.SizeID
                                  and c.Tastes = t.Tastes
                                  and c.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
  where t.Status = 1  

  update c
  set c.DeletedQty = case when t.DeletedQty > c.Qty then c.Qty else t.DeletedQty end,
      c.Status = case when c.Qty = t.DeletedQty then 1 else 0 end
  from tblCheckedOrders c
    inner join @tmpCheckedOrders t on c.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                  and c.ItemID = t.ItemID
                                  and c.SizeID = t.SizeID
                                  and c.Tastes = t.Tastes
                                  and c.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
  where t.Status = 0
    and t.DeletedQty > 0
  */

  /*
--  declare curs_checked_orders cursor for
--    select ItemID, SizeID, Qty, Tastes, ItemName, SizeName, PersonIndex
--    from tblPendingOrders
--    where SalesID = @SalesID
--      and ExtraChargeItem = 0
--    order by PersonIndex
--
--    open curs_checked_orders 
--    fetch next from curs_checked_orders into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @ItemName, @SizeName, @PersonIndex
--    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
--
--      while (@Qty > 0) begin
--
--        insert into tblCheckedOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, DeletedQty, Tastes, ItemName, SizeName, PersonIndex, [Status])
--        values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, 1, 0, @Tastes, @ItemName, @SizeName, @PersonIndex, 0)  
--
--        set @Qty = @Qty - 1
--
--      end
--
--      fetch next from curs_checked_orders into @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @Tastes, @ItemName, @SizeName, @PersonIndex
--    end
--    close curs_checked_orders
--  deallocate curs_checked_orders
--
--  declare curs_checked_qty cursor for
--    select ItemID, SizeID, Tastes, PersonIndex

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPendingOrderNumbers]
  @TakeOut bit,
  @DisplayType tinyint,
  @FrontKitchen bit,
  @BackKitchen bit,
  @ExtraKitchen bit,
  @Bar bit, 
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@DisplayType = 1) begin

    select t.DailyOrdNum, t.TableName, t.PickupTime, t.PhoneNum, t.PickupPerson,
           convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, getdate()) / 60)) + '' hrs '' +
           convert(varchar(5), (datediff(n, t.TimeIn, getdate()) % 60)) + '' min  '' as ElapsedTime,
           isnull(u.FName, '''') + '' '' + isnull(u.LName, '''') + ''  '' as ServerName
    from tblTable t left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
    where t.OrderNum > 0 
      and t.TakeOut = @TakeOut
    order by t.DailyOrdNum

  end
  else if (@DisplayType = 2) begin

    select distinct k.DailyOrderNumber, 
                    isnull(k.PickupTime, ''Now'') + '' '' as PickupTime,
--                    case isnull(t.TakeOut, s.TakeOutOrder) 
--                      when 1 then 
--                        case when isnull(t.PickupTime, ''Now'') like ''00:00%'' then 
--                                replace(substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, s.SaleDateTime), 100), 13, 5), '' '', ''0'') + '' '' +
--                                substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, s.SaleDateTime), 100), 18, 2)
--                             else isnull(t.PickupTime, ''Now'')
--                        end                                
--                      else replace(substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, s.SaleDateTime), 100), 13, 5), '' '', ''0'') + '' '' +
--                           substring(convert(varchar, isnull(t.TimeIn, s.SaleDateTime), 100), 18, 2) 
--                    end + '' '' as PickupTime,
                    case when s.TakeOutOrder = 0 then isnull(t.TakeOut, s.TakeOutOrder) else s.TakeOutOrder end as TakeOut
    from tblKitchenOrders k left join tblTable t on k.SalesID = t.OrderNum, tblSales s
    where k.SalesID = s.ID
      and k.SalesID > 0
      and k.Status = 1
      and k.StationID = @StationID
      and s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112)
      and ((case when (@FrontKitchen = 1) then
                   case KitchenF when 1 then 1 else 0 end
                 else 0
            end = 1)
           or
           (case when (@BackKitchen = 1) then
                   case KitchenB when 1 then 1 else 0 end
                 else 0
            end = 1)
           or
           (case when (@ExtraKitchen = 1) then
                   case KitchenE when 1 then 1 else 0 end
                 else 0
            end = 1)
           or
           (case when (@Bar = 1) then
                   case Bar when 1 then 1 else 0 end
                 else 0
            end = 1))
    order by k.DailyOrderNumber

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetDailyOrderNumber]
  @UseSpecialOrderNumberSequence bit,
  @LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence int,
  @DailyOrderNumber int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction get_daily_order_number

  select @DailyOrderNumber = convert(int, [Value])
  from tblMisc
  where Code = ''DON''

  set @DailyOrderNumber = isnull(@DailyOrderNumber, 0)

  if (@UseSpecialOrderNumberSequence = 1) and (@LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence > 0) begin

    update tblMisc
    set [Value] = convert(varchar, case when case when (@DailyOrderNumber % 10) = @LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence then 
                                                    (((@DailyOrderNumber + 1) / 10) + case when (@LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence = 9) then 0 else 1 end) * 10
                                                  else @DailyOrderNumber
                                             end >= 9999 then 0 
                                        else case when (@DailyOrderNumber % 10) = @LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence then 
                                                    (((@DailyOrderNumber + 1) / 10) + case when (@LastDigitOfOrderNumberSequence = 9) then 0 else 1 end) * 10
                                                  else @DailyOrderNumber
                                             end
                                   end + 1)
    where Code = ''DON''

  end
  else begin

    update tblMisc
    set [Value] = convert(varchar, case when @DailyOrderNumber >= 9999 then 0 else @DailyOrderNumber end + 1)
    where Code = ''DON''

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction get_daily_order_number
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction get_daily_order_number
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertSale]
  @CashierID smallint,
  @SubTotal smallmoney,
  @GSTAmt smallmoney,
  @PSTAmt smallmoney,
  @PST2Amt smallmoney,
  @TransType tinyint,
  @CustomerID int,
  @DailyOrderNumber int,
  @GSTRate decimal(5, 4),
  @PSTRate decimal(5, 4),
  @PST2Rate decimal(5, 4),
  @TakeOutOrder bit,
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @CustomerTypeID tinyint,
  @CustomerGroupID tinyint,
  @NewSalesID int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_sale

  insert into tblSales (CashierID, SaleDateTime, SubTotal, DSCAmt, GSTAmt, PSTAmt, PST2Amt, TransType, OriginalTransType, 
                        Guests, CustomerID, DailyOrderNumber, GSTRate, PSTRate, PST2Rate, TakeOutOrder, TableID, StationID, 
                        CustomerTypeID, CustomerGroupID)
  values (@CashierID, getdate(), @SubTotal, 0, @GSTAmt, @PSTAmt, @PST2Amt, @TransType, @TransType, 1, 
          @CustomerID, @DailyOrderNumber, @GSTRate, @PSTRate, @PST2Rate, @TakeOutOrder, @TableID, @StationID, 
          @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_sale
    set @NewSalesID = scope_identity()

    if (exists (select *
                from tblTable
                where ID = @TableID
                  and TakeOut = 1
                  and (Delivery = 1 or [Online] = 1)
                  and OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0)) begin

      declare @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint, @OnlineOrderNumber varchar(20), @OnlineOrderCustomerName varchar(100)

      select @OnlineOrderCompanyID = OnlineOrderCompanyID,
             @OnlineOrderNumber = OnlineOrderNumber,
             @OnlineOrderCustomerName = PickupPerson
      from tblTable
      where ID = @TableID
      
      exec sp_InsertSalesOfOnlineOrders @NewSalesID, @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OnlineOrderNumber, @OnlineOrderCustomerName, 0

    end

    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_sale
    set @NewSalesID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPendingOrders]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Qty smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @Tastes varchar(2000),
  @SideDishes varchar(200),
  @ItemName varchar(100),
  @SizeName varchar(30),
  @ApplyGST bit,
  @ApplyPST bit,
  @DSCAmt smallmoney,
  @KitchenB bit,
  @KitchenF bit,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @SeparateBillPrint bit,
  @Bar bit,
  @ApplyNoDSC bit,
  @OpenItem bit,
  @ItemName2 varchar(30),
  @ExtraChargeItem bit,
  @ApplyPST2 bit,
  @KitchenE bit,
  @DSCAmtEmployee smallmoney,
  @DSCAmtType1 smallmoney,
  @DSCAmtType2 smallmoney,
  @DayHourDiscountRate float,
  @PricePerWeightUnit smallmoney,
  @MeasuredWeight float,
  @DecimalPlaces tinyint,
  @DiscountPercent float,
  @Kitchen5 bit,
  @Kitchen6 bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_pending_orders

  insert into tblPendingOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, Tastes,  SideDishes, ItemName, SizeName, 
                                ApplyGST, ApplyPST, DSCAmt, KitchenB, KitchenF, PersonIndex, SeparateBillPrint, 
                                Bar, ApplyNoDSC, OpenItem, ItemName2, ExtraChargeItem, ApplyPST2, KitchenE,  
                                DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, DayHourDiscountRate, PricePerWeightUnit, 
                                MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, DiscountPercent, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
  values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @UnitPrice, @Tastes, @SideDishes, @ItemName, @SizeName, 
          @ApplyGST, @ApplyPST, @DSCAmt, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @PersonIndex, @SeparateBillPrint, 
          @Bar, @ApplyNoDSC, @OpenItem, @ItemName2, @ExtraChargeItem, @ApplyPST2, @KitchenE,  
          @DSCAmtEmployee, @DSCAmtType1, @DSCAmtType2, @DayHourDiscountRate, @PricePerWeightUnit, 
          round(@MeasuredWeight, @DecimalPlaces), @DecimalPlaces, round(@DiscountPercent, 3), @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_pending_orders
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_pending_orders
    return 0
  end
    
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_ResetDailyOrderNumber]
  @DailyOrderNumber int
  --@Reset bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction reset_daily_order_number

  update tblmisc 
  set [Value] = convert(varchar, @DailyOrderNumber)
  where Code = ''DON''

  truncate table tblOrderNumber
  truncate table tblReadyOrderNumber
  truncate table tblKitchenOrders
  truncate table tblCheckedOrders

  delete tib
  from tblTipAmountInBill tib
    left join tblTable t on tib.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where t.OrderNum is null

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction reset_daily_order_number
    --set @Reset = 1
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction reset_daily_order_number
    --set @Reset = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertDeletedItems]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Qty smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @UserID smallint,
  @DeleteReason varchar(200)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblDeletedItems (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, DeletedDateTime, UserID, DeleteReason)  
  select top 1 @SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @UnitPrice, getdate(), @UserID, @DeleteReason  
  from tblPendingOrders  
  where SalesID = @SalesID  
    and ItemID = @ItemID  
    and SizeID = @SizeID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPeripheralSettings]
  @StationName varchar(20),
  @Code varchar(5),
  @Value varchar(255)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_peripheral_setting

  insert into tblPeripherals (StationName, Code, [Value])
  select top 1 upper(@StationName), @Code, @Value
  from tblPeripherals p1
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblPeripherals p2
                    where upper(p2.StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                      and p2.Code = @Code)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_peripheral_setting
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_peripheral_setting
    return 0
  end 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdatePeripheralSettings]
  @StationName varchar(20),
  @Code varchar(5),
  @Value varchar(255),
  @CopyToAllOtherStations bit
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_peripheral_setting

  update tblPeripherals
  set [Value] = @Value
  where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
    and Code = @Code

  if (@CopyToAllOtherStations = 1) begin
  
    update p
    set p.Value = @Value
    from (select *
          from tblPeripherals
          where upper(StationName) <> upper(@StationName)
            and Code = @Code) p

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_peripheral_setting
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_peripheral_setting
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTableOpenStatus]
  @Opened bit,
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationIDInUse smallint
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction update_table_open_status

    update tblTable
    set Opened = case when isnull(@Opened, 0) = 0 then 0 else 1 end,
        StationIDInUse = case when isnull(@Opened, 0) = 0 then 0 else @StationIDInUse end
    where ID = @TableID

    commit transaction update_table_open_status
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_table_open_status
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_ResetTables]
  @TableID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction reset_tables

  update tblTable
  set Opened = 0 
  where Opened = 1
    and case when @TableID > 0 then
               case when ID = @TableID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

  update t
  set t.OrderNum = 0,
      t.ServerID = 0,
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.CallType = 255,
      t.PickupDate = null,
      t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
  from tblTable t
  where t.OrderNum > 0
    and not exists (select *
                    from tblPendingOrders p
                    where p.SalesID = t.OrderNum)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction reset_tables
    return 1 
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction reset_tables
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateSale]
  @SubTotal smallmoney,
  @DSCAmt smallmoney,
  @AlcoholDSCAmt smallmoney,
  @GSTAmt smallmoney,
  @PSTAmt smallmoney,
  @PST2Amt smallmoney,
  --@TransType tinyint,
  @Guests tinyint,
  @CustomerID int,
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @SalesID int,
  @ChargeOnAccountTrans bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_sale

  declare @GiftCardChargeAmt smallmoney

  select @GiftCardChargeAmt = sum(isnull(Qty, 0) * isnull(UnitPrice, 0))
  from tblPendingOrders
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    /* If this SalesID is for the separate payment, unless it is the last part of separate payement, 
       (if it is the last separate payment, it uses the original SalesID. so, it should be fine but...) 
       new SalesID does not exist in tblPendingOrders. So, the below items will not be deducted from subtotal. */
    and (upper(ltrim(rtrim(ItemName))) like ''GIFT CARD CHARGE%''
         or
         upper(ltrim(rtrim(ItemName))) like ''CASH BACK%''
         or
         upper(ltrim(rtrim(ItemName))) like ''DELIVERY CHARGE%'')

  set @SubTotal = @SubTotal - isnull(@GiftCardChargeAmt, 0)

  update tblSales  
  set SubTotal = round(@SubTotal, 2),  
      DSCAmt = round(@DSCAmt, 2),  
      AlcoholDSCAmt = round(@AlcoholDSCAmt, 2),
      GSTAmt = round(@GSTAmt, 2),  
      PSTAmt = round(@PSTAmt, 2),  
      PST2Amt = round(@PST2Amt, 2),
      TransType = case when @ChargeOnAccountTrans = 1 then 9 else TransType end,
      OriginalTransType = case when @ChargeOnAccountTrans = 1 then 9 else TransType end,
      Guests = @Guests,
      SaleDateTime = getdate(),  
      CustomerID = @CustomerID,  
      TableID = @TableID,
      StationID = @StationID      
  where ID = @SalesID

  --exec sp_UpdateStationLockStatus @TableID, 0, 1

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_sale
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_sale
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
