EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTableInfoBySalesID]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select t.*, u.FName, u.LName, 
         isnull(c.PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, cast(0 as bit)) as PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, 
         isnull(c.PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder, cast(0 as bit)) as PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder,
         isnull(c.PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, cast(0 as bit)) as PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber,
         isnull(ta.IncludedTipAmt, 0) as IncludedTipAmt,
         isnull(soo.DineInOrder, 0) as IsSelfDineInOrder,
         isnull(c.Integrated, 0) as IntegratedOnlineOrder,
         isnull(soo.ReservedTipAmt, 0) as ReservedTipAmt,
         isnull(soo.DeliveryChargeAmt, 0) as DeliveryChargeAmt
  from tblTable t 
    left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID 
    left join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
    left join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders soo on soo.SalesID = t.OrderNum
    left join (select *
               from tblTipAmountInBill
               where PersonIndex = 0
                 and SalesID = @SalesID) ta on ta.SalesID = t.OrderNum /* The join with tblTipAmountInBill is for the delivery charge amount in online ordering */
  where t.OrderNum = @SalesID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MergeOrders]
  @FromTableID smallint,
  @ToTableID smallint,
  @MergePersonIndex smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @OldSalesID int, @NewSalesID int, @ItemID smallint, @ToDailyOrderNumber int, @NextPersonIndex tinyint /*, @MergeTotalAmt smallmoney*/

  select @OldSalesID = max(p.SalesID)
  from tblTable t
    inner join tblPendingOrders p on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
  where t.ID = @FromTableID

  select @NewSalesID = max(p.SalesID),
         @NextPersonIndex = max(p.PersonIndex) + 1
  from tblTable t
    inner join tblPendingOrders p on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where t.ID = @ToTableID

  if (@NextPersonIndex < 254) begin

    if (@MergePersonIndex >= 0) begin

      if exists (select *
                 from tblPendingOrders p
                   inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
                   inner join tblTable t on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
                 where t.ID = @FromTableID
                   and p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex
                   and isnull(p.SideDishes, '''') not like ''SPLIT_%''
                   and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1) begin

        declare curs_time_charged_items cursor for      
          select p.SalesID, p.ItemID
          from tblPendingOrders p
            inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
            inner join tblTable t on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          where t.ID = @FromTableID
            and p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex
            and isnull(p.SideDishes, '''') not like ''SPLIT_%''
            and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1

          open curs_time_charged_items
          fetch next from curs_time_charged_items into @OldSalesID, @ItemID
          while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

            update tblTimeStartEnd
            set SalesID = @NewSalesID,
                PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
            where SalesID = @OldSalesID
              and ItemID = @ItemID
    
            fetch next from curs_time_charged_items into @OldSalesID, @ItemID
          end
          close curs_time_charged_items
        deallocate curs_time_charged_items

      end

      --select @MergeTotalAmt = 
      --from tblPendingOrders p
      --  inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
      --where t.ID = @FromTableID
      --  and p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex
      --  and isnull(p.SideDishes, '''') not like ''SPLIT_%''

      --update t
      --set t.TotalAmt = t.TotalAmt + @MergeTotalAmt
      --from tblTable t
      --where t.ID = @ToTableID

      --update t
      --set t.TotalAmt = t.TotalAmt - @MergeTotalAmt
      --from tblTable t
      --where t.ID = @FromTableID

      update pb
      set pb.SalesID = @NewSalesID,
          pb.PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
      from tblTable t
        inner join tblPendingOrdersBackup pb on t.OrderNum = pb.SalesID
      where t.ID = @FromTableID
        and pb.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex
        and isnull(pb.SideDishes, '''') not like ''SPLIT_%''

      update p
      set p.SalesID = @NewSalesID,
          p.PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
      from tblTable t
        inner join tblPendingOrders p on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
      where t.ID = @FromTableID
        and p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex
        and isnull(p.SideDishes, '''') not like ''SPLIT_%''

      if not exists (select *
                     from tblTable t
                       inner join tblPendingOrders p on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
                     where t.ID = @FromTableID) begin

        select @ToDailyOrderNumber = s.DailyOrderNumber
        from tblSales s
          inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
        where t.ID = @ToTableID

        --update s
        --set s.DailyOrderNumber = convert(int, convert(varchar, s.DailyOrderNumber) + ''0'' + convert(varchar, @ToDailyOrderNumber))
        --from tblSales s
        --  inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
        --where t.ID = @FromTableID

        update s
        set s.TransType = 2,
            s.OriginalTransType = 2,
            s.Guests = 0,
            s.CustomerID = 1,
            s.DailyOrderNumber = convert(int, convert(varchar, s.DailyOrderNumber) + ''0'' + convert(varchar, @ToDailyOrderNumber))
        from tblSales s
          inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
        where t.ID = @FromTableID
    
        update t
        set t.OrderNum = 0,
            t.ServerID = 0,
            t.NumOfGuests = 0,
            t.Opened = 0,
            t.PickupTime = '''',
            t.PhoneNum = '''',
            t.PickupPerson = '''',
            t.BillPrinted = 0,
            t.Attention = 0,
            t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
            t.TotalAmt = 0,
            t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
        from tblTable t
        where t.ID = @FromTableID

      end
      else begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from tblTable t
                         inner join tblPendingOrders p on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
                       where t.ID = @FromTableID
                         and p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex) begin

          update p
          set p.PersonIndex = p.PersonIndex - 1
          from tblTable t
            inner join tblPendingOrders p on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          where t.ID = @FromTableID
            and p.PersonIndex > @MergePersonIndex

          update pb
          set pb.PersonIndex = pb.PersonIndex - 1
          from tblTable t
            inner join tblPendingOrdersBackup pb on pb.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          where t.ID = @FromTableID
            and pb.PersonIndex > @MergePersonIndex

        end

      end

    end
    else begin    

      if exists (select *
                 from tblPendingOrders p
                   inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
                   inner join tblTable t on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
                 where t.ID = @FromTableID
                   and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1) begin

        update tblTimeStartEnd
        set SalesID = @NewSalesID,
            PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
        where SalesID = @OldSalesID

      end

      update pb
      set pb.SalesID = @NewSalesID,
          pb.PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
      from tblTable t
        inner join tblPendingOrdersBackup pb on t.OrderNum = pb.SalesID
      where t.ID = @FromTableID

      update p
      set p.SalesID = @NewSalesID,
          p.PersonIndex = @NextPersonIndex
      from tblTable t
        inner join tblPendingOrders p on t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
      where t.ID = @FromTableID

      select @ToDailyOrderNumber = s.DailyOrderNumber
      from tblSales s
        inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
      where t.ID = @ToTableID

      --update s
      --set s.DailyOrderNumber = convert(int, convert(varchar, s.DailyOrderNumber) + ''0'' + convert(varchar, @ToDailyOrderNumber))
      --from tblSales s
      --  inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
      --where t.ID = @FromTableID

      update s
      set s.TransType = 2,
          s.OriginalTransType = 2,
          s.Guests = 0,
          s.CustomerID = 1,
          s.DailyOrderNumber = convert(int, convert(varchar, s.DailyOrderNumber) + ''0'' + convert(varchar, @ToDailyOrderNumber))
      from tblSales s
        inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
      where t.ID = @FromTableID

      update t
      set t.TotalAmt = t.TotalAmt + (select TotalAmt
                                     from tblTable
                                     where ID = @FromTableID)
      from tblTable t
      where t.ID = @ToTableID

      update t
      set t.OrderNum = 0,
          t.ServerID = 0,
          t.NumOfGuests = 0,
          t.Opened = 0,
          t.PickupTime = '''',
          t.PhoneNum = '''',
          t.PickupPerson = '''',
          t.BillPrinted = 0,
          t.Attention = 0,
          t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
          t.TotalAmt = 0,
          t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
      from tblTable t
      where t.ID = @FromTableID

    end

    return 1

  end
  else begin
    
    return 0 

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertStation]
  @StationName varchar(30),
  @KitchenDisplay bit,
  @NewStationID smallint = -1 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_station

  insert into tblStation (StationName, [Status], KitchenDisplay)
  select @StationName, 1, @KitchenDisplay
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblStation
                    where upper(ltrim(rtrim(StationName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@StationName))))

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_station
    set @NewStationID = isnull(scope_identity(), -1)
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_station
    set @NewStationID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateStation]
  @StationName varchar(30),
  @Status bit,
  @KitchenDisplay bit,
  @StationID smallint = -1 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_station

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblStation
                 where upper(ltrim(rtrim(StationName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@StationName)))
                   and ID <> @StationID) begin

    update tblStation
    set StationName = @StationName,
        [Status] = @Status,
        KitchenDisplay = @KitchenDisplay
    where ID = @StationID

  end
  else begin
    
    set @StationID = -1

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_station
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_station
    set @StationID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetStation]
  @Status tinyint,
  @OrderBy varchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(500)

  set @script = ''select ID, StationName, [Status], KitchenDisplay '' +
                ''from tblStation ''

  if (@Status = 1) begin
    set @script = @script + 
                ''where [Status] = 1 ''
  end
  else if (@Status = 2) begin
    set @script = @script + 
                ''where [Status] = 0 ''
  end

  if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderBy)) = '''')
    set @script = @script + 
                ''order by ID''
  else
    set @script = @script + 
                ''order by '' + @OrderBy

  exec sp_executesql @script

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertClockInTimeStamp]
  @EmployeeID int
AS
BEGIN
  -- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @DateTimeIn smalldatetime

  set @DateTimeIn = getdate()

  if not exists (select 1
                 from tblTimeStamp
                 where EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
                   and DateTimeIn >= dateadd(n, 1, @DateTimeIn)) begin

    insert into tblTimeStamp (EmployeeID, DateTimeIn, DateTimeOut, [State])
    values (@EmployeeID, @DateTimeIn, @DateTimeIn, 0)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateClockOutState]
  @TimeStampID int,
  @ClockOut bit,
  @TimeExceeded bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblTimeStamp
  set [State] = @ClockOut,
      DateTimeOut = case @TimeExceeded when 1 then DateTimeOut else getdate() end
  where ID = @TimeStampID      

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfClockedInTimeExceeded]
  @TimeStampID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ClockedInTimeExceeded bit

  if exists (select *
             from tblTimeStamp
             where ID = @TimeStampID
               and [State] = 0
               and datediff(n, DateTimeIn, getdate()) > 1200)
    
    set @ClockedInTimeExceeded = 1

  else
    
    set @ClockedInTimeExceeded = 0

  select @ClockedInTimeExceeded as ClockedInTimeExceeded

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetClockedInEmployees]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as EmployeeName, ts.*
  from tblTimeStamp ts, tblUser u
  where ts.EmployeeID = u.ID
    and ts.State = 0
  order by ts.DateTimeIn

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetAvailableItemDetail]
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Barcode varchar(15),
  @ApplySpecialPricing bit,
  @SpecialPricingRate smallint,
  @UnitPriceType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select i.ID as ItemID, i.IName, i.IName2, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.ApplyPST2,
         i.KitchenB, i.KitchenF, i.KitchenE, i.Bar, i.Kitchen5, i.Kitchen6, i.Alcohol, i.RewardItem, 
         i.HourlyChargedItem, i.GroupItem, i.OpenItem, i.SideDish, i.Taste, i.ScaleItem, 
         isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) as ApplyNoDSC,
         case when @ApplySpecialPricing = 1 then
                dbo.GetSpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice(case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then isnull(case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                                                              when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                                                              when 3 then a.UnitPrice3 
                                                                                                          end, 0)
                                                           else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                                                                    when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                                                                    when 3 then a.UnitPrice3 
                                                                                                                end) 
                                                      end, @SpecialPricingRate)
              else
                case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then isnull(case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                        when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                        when 3 then a.UnitPrice3 
                                                                    end, 0)
                     else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                              when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                              when 3 then a.UnitPrice3 
                                                                          end) 
                end
         end as UnitPrice,
         isnull(a.SizeID, 0) as SizeID, 
         isnull(s.SizeName, '''') as SizeName, 
         isnull(s.ShortName, '''') as ShortName,
         case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then 0 
              else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountRate(a.ItemID, a.SizeID) 
         end as DayHourDiscountRate
  from tblItem i left join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
                 left join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
  where (case when @Barcode <> '''' then 
           case when i.BarCode = @Barcode then 1 else 0 end
         else 
           case when (@SizeID > 0) and (isnull(a.ItemID, 0) = @ItemID) then
             case when i.ID = @ItemID and isnull(s.ID, 0) = @SizeID then 1 else 0 end
           else
             case when i.ID = @ItemID then 1 else 0 end
           end
         end = 1)
  order by isnull(s.DisplayOrder, 0), IName, SizeName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSurchargeItemInfo]
AS
BEGIN

  from tblItem i, tblAvailableSize a
  where a.ItemID = i.ID
    and a.SizeID = 1
    and upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = ''SURCHARGE''

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByYearMonth]
  @SelectedYear int,
  @Stations varchar(500)
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /*==============================================================================================*/
  /* Convert string format station list into the temporary table */

  select cast(0 as smallint) as StationID
  into #tmp_station 

  while (charindex('','', @Stations) > 0) begin
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    values (cast(substring(@Stations, 1, charindex('','', @Stations) - 1) as smallint))

    set @Stations = substring(@Stations, charindex('','', @Stations) + 1, len(@Stations))
  end

  insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
  values (cast(@Stations as smallint))

  if not exists (select *
                 from #tmp_station t
                   inner join tblStation s on t.StationID = s.ID) begin
    truncate table #tmp_station
    insert into #tmp_station (StationID)
    select ID
    from tblStation
  end

  /*==============================================================================================*/

  /*==============================================================================================*/
  /* Create temp table */

  declare @i tinyint, @Year1 int, @Year2 int, @Year3 int

  select cast(0 as smallint) as YearIndex, cast(0 as tinyint) as MonthIndex, 
         cast(0 as int) as TransCount, cast(0 as money) as TotalAmt
  into #tmp_summary

  truncate table #tmp_summary
  
  set @Year1 = @SelectedYear
  set @Year2 = @SelectedYear - 1
  set @Year3 = @SelectedYear - 2  
  set @i = 1
  while (@i <= 12) begin

    insert into #tmp_summary (YearIndex, MonthIndex, TransCount, TotalAmt)
    values (@Year1, @i, 0, 0)

    insert into #tmp_summary (YearIndex, MonthIndex, TransCount, TotalAmt)
    values (@Year2, @i, 0, 0)

    insert into #tmp_summary (YearIndex, MonthIndex, TransCount, TotalAmt)
    values (@Year3, @i, 0, 0)

    set @i = @i + 1
  end

  /*==============================================================================================*/

  /*==============================================================================================*/
  /* Get Sales Summary */

  update t1
  set t1.TransCount = isnull(t2.TransCount, 0),
      t1.TotalAmt = isnull(t2.TotalAmt, 0)
  from #tmp_summary t1 left join (select year(s.SaleDateTime) as YearIndex,
                                         month(s.SaleDateTime) as MonthIndex,            
                                         count(s.ID) as TransCount, 
                                         isnull(round(sum(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt),2),0) as TotalAmt
                                  from tblSales s
                                    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
                                  where s.TransType in (0, 1, 5)
                                    and year(s.SaleDateTime) >= @Year3
                                    and year(s.SaleDateTime) <= @Year1
                                  group by year(s.SaleDateTime), month(s.SaleDateTime)) t2 on t1.YearIndex = t2.YearIndex 
                                                                                          and t1.MonthIndex = t2.MonthIndex

  /*==============================================================================================*/

  select *
  from #tmp_summary
  order by YearIndex, MonthIndex

  drop table #tmp_summary
  drop table #tmp_station

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByHourItem]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @CategoryID tinyint, @ItemID smallint, @SizeID tinyint, 
          @SaleHour tinyint, @SoldQty int, @SoldAmt money

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  IF  EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem]'') AND type in (N''U''))
    DROP TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem]

  CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem](
	  [CategoryID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [CatName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [IName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [IName2] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [SizeName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [Qty10AM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty10AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty11AM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty11AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty12PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty12PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty1PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty1PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty2PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty2PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty3PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty3PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty4PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty4PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty5PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty5PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty6PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty6PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty7PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty7PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty8PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty8PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty9PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty9PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty10PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty10PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty11PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Qty11PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt10AM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt10AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt11AM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt11AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt12PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt12PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt1PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt1PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt2PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt2PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt3PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt3PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt4PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt4PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt5PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt5PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt6PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt6PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt7PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt7PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt8PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt8PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt9PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt9PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt10PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt10PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt11PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem_Amt11PM]  DEFAULT ((0))
  ) ON [PRIMARY]

  insert into tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem (CategoryID, ItemID, SizeID, CatName, IName, IName2, SizeName)
  select c.ID, i.ID, z.ID, c.CatName, i.IName, i.IName2, case when z.ID = 1 then '''' else z.SizeName end as SizeName
  from tblSales s, tblSalesDetail sd, tblItem i, tblSize z, tblCategory c
  where sd.SalesID = s.ID
    and sd.ItemID = i.ID
    and sd.SizeID = z.ID
    and i.CategoryID = c.ID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
    and sd.Voided = 0
  group by c.ID, i.ID, z.ID, c.CatName, i.IName, i.IName2, case when z.ID = 1 then '''' else z.SizeName end
  order by c.CatName, i.IName, i.IName2, SizeName

  if convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAORB'')) = 1 begin
      
    declare curs_sales cursor for
      select i.CategoryID, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, 
              case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23 
                  else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
              end as SaleHour, 
              sum(sd.Qty) as SoldQty, 
              sum((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) +
                  ((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) * (case when i.ApplyGST = 1 then s.GSTRate else 0 end +
                                              case when i.ApplyPST = 1 then s.PSTRate else 0 end +
                                              case when i.ApplyPST2 = 1 then s.PST2Rate else 0 end))) as SoldAmt
      from tblSales s
        inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
      where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        and s.TransType = 1
        and sd.Voided = 0
      group by i.CategoryID, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, 
                case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23
                    else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
                end

  end
  else begin

    declare curs_sales cursor for
      select i.CategoryID, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, 
              case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23 
                  else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
              end as SaleHour, 
              sum(sd.Qty) as SoldQty, sum(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice) as SoldAmt
      from tblSales s
        inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
      where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        and s.TransType = 1
        and sd.Voided = 0
      group by i.CategoryID, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, 
                case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23
                    else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
                end

  end
  
      open curs_sales 
      fetch next from curs_sales into @CategoryID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @SaleHour, @SoldQty, @SoldAmt
      while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

        if (@SaleHour = 10) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty10AM = @SoldQty,
              Amt10AM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end
        else if (@SaleHour = 11) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty11AM = @SoldQty,
              Amt11AM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 12) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty12PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt12PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 13) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty1PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt1PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 14) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty2PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt2PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 15) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty3PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt3PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 16) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty4PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt4PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 17) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty5PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt5PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 18) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty6PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt6PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 19) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty7PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt7PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 20) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty8PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt8PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 21) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty9PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt9PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 22) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty10PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt10PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  
        else if (@SaleHour = 23) begin
          update tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
          set Qty11PM = @SoldQty,
              Amt11PM = @SoldAmt
          where CategoryID = @CategoryID
            and ItemID = @ItemID
            and SizeID = @SizeID
        end  

        fetch next from curs_sales into @CategoryID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @SaleHour, @SoldQty, @SoldAmt
      end
      close curs_sales
    deallocate curs_sales
    
  select *
  from tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem
  order by CatName, IName, SizeName

  drop table tmpSalesSummaryByHourItem

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByHourCustomer]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @CustomerTypeID tinyint, @CustomerGroupID tinyint,
          @SaleHour tinyint, @NumOfGuests int, @SalesAmt money

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  IF  EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer]'') AND type in (N''U''))
    DROP TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer]

  CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer](
	  [CustomerTypeID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerGroupID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerType] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerGroup] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
	  [Qty10AM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty10AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty11AM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty11AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty12PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty12PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty1PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty1PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty2PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty2PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty3PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty3PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty4PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty4PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty5PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty5PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty6PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty6PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty7PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty7PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty8PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty8PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty9PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty9PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty10PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty10PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Qty11PM] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Qty11PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt10AM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt10AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt11AM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt11AM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt12PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt12PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt1PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt1PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt2PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt2PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt3PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt3PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt4PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt4PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt5PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt5PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt6PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt6PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt7PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt7PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt8PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt8PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt9PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt9PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt10PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt10PM]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [Amt11PM] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer_Amt11PM]  DEFAULT ((0))
  ) ON [PRIMARY]

  insert into tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer (CustomerTypeID, CustomerGroupID, CustomerType, CustomerGroup)
  select ct.ID, cg.ID, ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup
  from tblSales s, tblCustomerType ct, tblCustomerGroup cg
  where s.CustomerTypeID = ct.ID
    and s.CustomerGroupID = cg.ID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
  group by ct.ID, cg.ID, ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup
  order by ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup

  declare curs_sales cursor for
    select s.CustomerTypeID, s.CustomerGroupID, 
           case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23 
                else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
           end as SaleHour, 
           sum(s.Guests) as NumOfGuests, sum(s.SubTotal) as SalesAmt
    from tblSales s
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
    group by s.CustomerTypeID, s.CustomerGroupID,
             case when (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) > 0 and datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) < 10) then 23
                  else datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) 
             end

    open curs_sales 
    fetch next from curs_sales into @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID, @SaleHour, @NumOfGuests, @SalesAmt
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      if (@SaleHour = 10) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty10AM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt10AM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end
      else if (@SaleHour = 11) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty11AM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt11AM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 12) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty12PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt12PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 13) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty1PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt1PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 14) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty2PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt2PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 15) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty3PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt3PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 16) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty4PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt4PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 17) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty5PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt5PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 18) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty6PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt6PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 19) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty7PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt7PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 20) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty8PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt8PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 21) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty9PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt9PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 22) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty10PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt10PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleHour = 23) begin
        update tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
        set Qty11PM = @NumOfGuests,
            Amt11PM = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  

      fetch next from curs_sales into @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID, @SaleHour, @NumOfGuests, @SalesAmt
    end
    close curs_sales
  deallocate curs_sales
    
  select *
  from tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer
  order by case when CustomerTypeID = 1 then ''ZZZZZ'' + CustomerType else CustomerType end, 
           case when CustomerGroupID = 1 then ''ZZZZZ'' + CustomerGroup else CustomerGroup end

  drop table tmpSalesSummaryByHourCustomer

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertWageHistory]
  @EmployeeID smallint,  
  @EffectiveDate varchar(8),
  @Wage smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblEmployeeWageHistory (EmployeeID, EffectiveDate, Wage)
  values (@EmployeeID, @EffectiveDate, @Wage)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateWageHistory]
  @WageHistoryID int,
  @EffectiveDate varchar(8),
  @Wage smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblEmployeeWageHistory
  set EffectiveDate = @EffectiveDate,
      Wage = @Wage
  where ID = @WageHistoryID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetEmployeeWageHistory]
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select ID, EmployeeID, EffectiveDate, Wage,
         convert(varchar, EffectiveDate, 107) as StrEffectiveDate
  from tblEmployeeWageHistory
  where EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
  order by EffectiveDate desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByDayCustomer]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  declare @CustomerTypeID tinyint, @CustomerGroupID tinyint,
          @SaleDayIndex tinyint, @NumOfGuests int, @SalesAmt money

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  IF  EXISTS (SELECT * FROM sys.objects WHERE object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer]'') AND type in (N''U''))
    DROP TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer]

  CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer](
	  [CustomerTypeID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerGroupID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerType] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerGroup] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
    [QtySun] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtySun]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtyMon] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtyMon]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtyTue] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtyTue]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtyWed] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtyWed]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtyThu] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtyThu]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtyFri] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtyFri]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [QtySat] [int] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_QtySat]  DEFAULT ((0)),	  
	  [AmtSun] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtSun]  DEFAULT ((0)),
    [AmtMon] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtMon]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [AmtTue] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtTue]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [AmtWed] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtWed]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [AmtThu] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtThu]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [AmtFri] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtFri]  DEFAULT ((0)),
	  [AmtSat] [money] NOT NULL CONSTRAINT [DF_tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer_AmtSat]  DEFAULT ((0))	  
  ) ON [PRIMARY]

  insert into tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer (CustomerTypeID, CustomerGroupID, CustomerType, CustomerGroup)
  select ct.ID, cg.ID, ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup
  from tblSales s, tblCustomerType ct, tblCustomerGroup cg
  where s.CustomerTypeID = ct.ID
    and s.CustomerGroupID = cg.ID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
  group by ct.ID, cg.ID, ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup
  order by ct.CustomerType, cg.CustomerGroup

  declare curs_sales cursor for
    select s.CustomerTypeID, s.CustomerGroupID, datepart(dw, s.SaleDateTime) as SaleDayIndex, 
           sum(s.Guests) as NumOfGuests, sum(s.SubTotal) as SalesAmt
    from tblSales s
    where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and s.TransType = 1
      group by s.CustomerTypeID, s.CustomerGroupID, datepart(dw, s.SaleDateTime)

    open curs_sales 
    fetch next from curs_sales into @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID, @SaleDayIndex, @NumOfGuests, @SalesAmt
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      if (@SaleDayIndex = 1) begin /* Sunday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtySun = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtSun = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 2) begin /* Monday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtyMon = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtMon = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 3) begin /* Tuesday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtyTue = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtTue = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 4) begin /* Wednesday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtyWed = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtWed = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 5) begin /* Thursday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtyThu = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtThu = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 6) begin /* Friday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtyFri = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtFri = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end  
      else if (@SaleDayIndex = 7) begin /* Saturday */
        update tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
        set QtySat = @NumOfGuests,
            AmtSat = @SalesAmt
        where CustomerTypeID = @CustomerTypeID
          and CustomerGroupID = @CustomerGroupID
      end

      fetch next from curs_sales into @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID, @SaleDayIndex, @NumOfGuests, @SalesAmt
    end
    close curs_sales
  deallocate curs_sales
    
  select *
  from tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer
  order by case when CustomerTypeID = 1 then ''ZZZZZ'' + CustomerType else CustomerType end, 
           case when CustomerGroupID = 1 then ''ZZZZZ'' + CustomerGroup else CustomerGroup end

  drop table tmpSalesSummaryByDayCustomer

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCustomerByCustomerNumber]
  @CustomerNum varchar(20),
  @LookupPhoneNum bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblCustomer
  where ID > 1
    and ((CustomerNum = @CustomerNum)
         or
         (case when @LookupPhoneNum = 1 then
                 case when Phone = @CustomerNum then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 0
          end = 1))

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTimeStamps]
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @FromDate varchar(8),
  @ToDate varchar(8)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  into #tmpWageHistory
  from tblEmployeeWageHistory h1
  where h1.EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
    and h1.EffectiveDate <= @ToDate
    and case when (not exists (select *
                               from tblEmployeeWageHistory h2
                               where h2.EmployeeID = h1.EmployeeID
                                 and h2.EffectiveDate <= @FromDate)) or
                  (h1.EffectiveDate >= (select max(h2.EffectiveDate)
                                        from tblEmployeeWageHistory h2
                                        where h2.EmployeeID = h1.EmployeeID
                                          and h2.EffectiveDate <= @FromDate)) then 1
             else 0
        end = 1

  set @ToDate = convert(varchar, dateadd(d, 1, @ToDate), 112)

  select t.ID, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut,
         case t.State when 0 then ''IN'' else ''OUT'' end as [Status],
         case t.State when 0 then ''00:00''
                      else replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, datediff(n, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut) / 60))) +
                           convert(varchar, datediff(n, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut) / 60) + '':'' +
                           replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, datediff(n, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut) % 60))) +
                           convert(varchar, datediff(n, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut) % 60) end as WorkedHours,
         case t.State when 0 then 0 else datediff(n, t.DateTimeIn, t.DateTimeOut) end as HoursInMinutes,
         (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as EmployeeName, isnull(h.Wage, 0) as Wage
  from tblUser u, tblTimeStamp t left join #tmpWageHistory h 
                                  on h.EmployeeID = t.EmployeeID 
                                 and exists (select max(w.EffectiveDate)
                                             from #tmpWageHistory w
                                             where w.EmployeeID = h.EmployeeID
                                               and w.EffectiveDate <= t.DateTimeIn
                                             having max(w.EffectiveDate) = h.EffectiveDate)
  where t.EmployeeID = u.ID
    and t.EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
    and t.DateTimeIn >= @FromDate
    and t.DateTimeIn < @ToDate
  order by DateTimeIn desc

  drop table #tmpWageHistory

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetApplicableWageHistory]
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @FromDate varchar(8),
  @ToDate varchar(8)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblEmployeeWageHistory h1
  where h1.EmployeeID = @EmployeeID
    and h1.EffectiveDate <= @ToDate
    and case when (not exists (select *
                               from tblEmployeeWageHistory h2
                               where h2.EmployeeID = h1.EmployeeID
                                 and h2.EffectiveDate <= @FromDate)) or
                  (h1.EffectiveDate >= (select max(h2.EffectiveDate)
                                        from tblEmployeeWageHistory h2
                                        where h2.EmployeeID = h1.EmployeeID
                                          and h2.EffectiveDate <= @FromDate)) then 1
             else 0
        end = 1
  order by h1.EffectiveDate

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCheckedOrdersMissed]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @SalesID int

  declare curs_checked_orders_missed cursor for
    select distinct SalesID
    from tblPendingOrders p
    where p.SalesID > 0
      and exists (select *
                  from tblTable t
                  where t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
                    and t.OrderNum > 0)
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblCheckedOrders c
                      where c.SalesID = p.SalesID)

    open curs_checked_orders_missed
    fetch next from curs_checked_orders_missed into @SalesID 
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
      
      exec sp_InsertCheckedOrders @SalesID

      fetch next from curs_checked_orders_missed into @SalesID
    end
    close curs_checked_orders_missed
  deallocate curs_checked_orders_missed

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteKitchenOrders]
  @SalesID int,
  @FrontKitchen bit,
  @BackKitchen bit,
  @ExtraKitchen bit,
  @Bar bit,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblKitchenOrders
  set [Status] = 3
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and [Status] = 1
    and StationID = @StationID
    and ((case when (@FrontKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenF when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@BackKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenB when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@ExtraKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenE when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@Bar = 1) then
                 case Bar when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)) 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetDeletedOrderNumbers]
  @FrontKitchen bit,
  @BackKitchen bit,
  @ExtraKitchen bit,
  @Bar bit, 
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select distinct top 32 k.DailyOrderNumber, isnull(k.PickupTime, ''Now'') + '' '' as PickupTime,  
                  case when s.TakeOutOrder = 0 then isnull(t.TakeOut, s.TakeOutOrder) else s.TakeOutOrder end as TakeOut
  from tblKitchenOrders k left join tblTable t on k.SalesID = t.OrderNum, tblSales s
  where k.SalesID = s.ID
    and k.SalesID > 0
    and k.Status = 3 /* 3 - Deleted */
    and k.StationID = @StationID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112)
    and ((case when (@FrontKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenF when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@BackKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenB when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@ExtraKitchen = 1) then
                 case KitchenE when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1)
         or
         (case when (@Bar = 1) then
                 case Bar when 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 0
          end = 1))
  order by k.DailyOrderNumber desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetDeletedKitchenOrders]
  @FrontKitchen bit,
  @BackKitchen bit,
  @ExtraKitchen bit,
  @Bar bit,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(max)

  if ((@FrontKitchen = 1) or (@BackKitchen = 1) or (@ExtraKitchen = 1) or (@Bar = 1)) begin 

    set @script = ''select k.ID, k.SalesID, k.ItemID, k.SizeID, k.Qty, k.Tastes, k.SideDishes, '' +
                  ''       replicate('''' '''', 4 - len(convert(varchar, k.Qty))) + convert(varchar, k.Qty) + ''''   '''' + k.ItemName as ItemName, '' +
                  ''       replicate('''' '''', 4 - len(convert(varchar, k.Qty))) + convert(varchar, k.Qty) + ''''   '''' + '' + 
                  ''       case when isnull(ltrim(rtrim(k.ItemName2)), '''''''') = '''''''' then k.ItemName else k.ItemName2 end as ItemName2, '' +
                  ''       k.SizeName, k.ItemNumber, k.KitchenB, k.KitchenF, k.KitchenE, k.Bar, k.PersonIndex, k.DailyOrderNumber, '' +
                  ''       k.Status, isnull(t.TableName, '''''''') as TableName '' +
                  ''from tblKitchenOrders k '' +
                  ''  inner join tblSales s on k.SalesID = s.ID '' +
                  ''  left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID '' +
                  ''where k.Status = 3 '' +
                  ''  and s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar(8), getdate(), 112) '' +
                  ''  and k.StationID = '' + convert(varchar, @StationID)                  

    set @script = @script + ''  and (''

    if (@FrontKitchen = 1) 
      set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenF = 1 or ''
    if (@BackKitchen = 1)
      set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenB = 1 or ''
    if (@ExtraKitchen = 1)
      set @script = @script + ''k.KitchenE = 1 or ''
    if (@Bar = 1)
      set @script = @script + ''k.Bar = 1 or ''
      
    set @script = substring(@script, 1, len(@script) - 3) + '')''   

    set @script = @script + '' order by k.SalesID, k.PersonIndex, k.ItemID, k.SizeID''

  end
  else begin
    select @script = ''select * '' +
                     ''from tblKitchenOrders '' +
                     ''where ID = 0''  
  end 

  exec sp_executesql @script

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[IsStoreClosedAfterMidnight]
(
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN

  declare @ClosedAfterMidnight bit

  select @ClosedAfterMidnight = case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(dbo.GetMiscValue(''CLAMN'')))) = ''TRUE'' then 1 else 0 end

  return isnull(@ClosedAfterMidnight, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetFromDateTime]
(
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
)
RETURNS datetime
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @DateTime datetime, @HoursAfterMidnight tinyint

  set @HoursAfterMidnight = 6

  set @DateTime = case when @ByTime = 1 then @FromDateTime
                       else case when dbo.IsStoreClosedAfterMidnight() = 1 then
                                   case when getdate() >= dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, convert(varchar(8), @FromDateTime, 112))) then
                                          dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, convert(varchar(8), @FromDateTime, 112)))
                                        else dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, dateadd(d, -1, convert(varchar(8), @FromDateTime, 112))))
                                   end
                                 else convert(varchar(8), @FromDateTime, 112) 
                            end
                  end

  return @DateTime

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetToDateTime]
(
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
)
RETURNS datetime
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @DateTime datetime, @HoursAfterMidnight tinyint

  set @HoursAfterMidnight = 6

  set @DateTime = case when @ByTime = 1 then dateadd(s, 1, @ToDateTime)
                       else case when dbo.IsStoreClosedAfterMidnight() = 1 then
                                   case when getdate() >= dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, convert(varchar(8), @ToDateTime /*getdate()*/, 112))) then
                                          dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar(8), @ToDateTime, 112))))
                                        else dateadd(s, 1, dateadd(hh, @HoursAfterMidnight, convert(varchar(8), @ToDateTime, 112)))
                                   end
                                 else dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar(8), @ToDateTime, 112))
                            end
                  end

  return @DateTime

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[CheckIfLinkedServerExists]
(
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100)
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Exists bit

  if exists (select srv.name 
             from sys.servers srv 
             where srv.server_id != 0 
               and srv.name = @LinkedServerName)
 
    set @Exists = 1

  else
 
    set @Exists = 0

  return @Exists

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertStore]
  @StoreName varchar(50),
  @StoreCode varchar(20),
  @Status bit,
  @MerchantNumber varchar(20),
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100),
  @NewStoreID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_store

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblStore) begin
    truncate table tblStore
  end

  insert into tblStore (StoreName, StoreCode, [Status], MerchantNumber, LinkedServerName)
  values (@StoreName, @StoreCode, 1, @MerchantNumber, upper(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName))))    

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_store
    set @NewStoreID = isnull(scope_identity(), 0)
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_store
    set @NewStoreID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateStore]
  @StoreName varchar(50),
  @StoreCode varchar(20),
  @Status bit,
  @MerchantNumber varchar(20),
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100),
  @StoreID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_store

  update tblStore
  set StoreName = @StoreName,
      StoreCode = @StoreCode,
      [Status] = @Status,
      MerchantNumber = @MerchantNumber,
      LinkedServerName = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)))
  where ID = @StoreID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_store
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_store
    set @StoreID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetStore]
  @ActiveOnly bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *, dbo.CheckIfLinkedServerExists(LinkedServerName) as LinkedServerExists
  from tblStore
  where case when @ActiveOnly = 1 then 
               case when [Status] = 1 then 1
                    else 0
               end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by ID

END'
GO

  @StoreID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete
  from tblStore
  where ID = @StoreID

END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSalesSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @PartialClosing bit = 0,
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  if (len(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName))) > 0) begin
    
    declare @script nvarchar(500)

    set @script = ''exec ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].TPPro.dbo.spr_SalesSummary '''''' + 
                  convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112) + '''''', '''''' + convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112) + '''''', 0, 0, 0, 0''

    exec sp_executesql @script

  end
  else begin

    exec spr_SalesSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @ByTime, @EmployeeID, @StationID, @PartialClosing
  
  end  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_AddStoreLinkedServer]
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100),
  @LoginName varchar(20),
  @Password varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @LinkedServerName = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)))

  begin try
    exec sp_DeleteStoreLinkedServer @LinkedServerName
  end try
  begin catch
  end catch

  begin try
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_addlinkedserver @server = @LinkedServerName, @srvproduct=N''SQL Server''
    /* For security reasons the linked server remote logins password is changed with ######## */
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_addlinkedsrvlogin @rmtsrvname=@LinkedServerName,@useself=N''False'',@locallogin=NULL,@rmtuser=@LoginName,@rmtpassword=@Password   

    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''collation compatible'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''data access'', @optvalue=N''true''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''dist'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''pub'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''rpc'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''rpc out'', @optvalue=N''true''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''sub'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''connect timeout'', @optvalue=N''0''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''collation name'', @optvalue=null
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''lazy schema validation'', @optvalue=N''false''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''query timeout'', @optvalue=N''0''
    EXEC master.dbo.sp_serveroption @server=@LinkedServerName, @optname=N''use remote collation'', @optvalue=N''true''
  end try
  begin catch
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RemoveUnusedLinkedServers]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @LinkedServerName varchar(100)

  declare curs_linked_servers cursor for
    select srv.name 
    from sys.servers srv 
    where srv.server_id != 0 
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblStore s
                      where s.LinkedServerName collate database_default = srv.name collate database_default)
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblMisc m
                      where m.Code = ''ORLSN''
                        and upper(m.Value collate database_default) = upper(srv.name collate database_default))
  
    open curs_linked_servers
    fetch next from curs_linked_servers into @LinkedServerName
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      exec sp_DeleteStoreLinkedServer @LinkedServerName

      fetch next from curs_linked_servers into @LinkedServerName
    end
    close curs_linked_servers
  deallocate curs_linked_servers

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteStoreLinkedServer]
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select srv.name 
             from sys.servers srv 
             where srv.server_id != 0 
               and srv.name = @LinkedServerName)

    exec master.dbo.sp_dropserver @server=@LinkedServerName, @droplogins=''droplogins''

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetDailySalesSummaryByType]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @NoGroupByType bit = 0,
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (len(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName))) > 0) begin
    
    declare @script nvarchar(500)

    set @script = ''exec ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].TPPro.dbo.spr_DailySalesSummaryByType '''''' + 
                  convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112) + '''''', '''''' + convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112) + '''''', 0, '' +
                  convert(varchar, @NoGroupByType)

    exec sp_executesql @script

  end
  else begin

    exec spr_DailySalesSummaryByType @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, @ByTime, @NoGroupByType
  
  end  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateStoreLinkedServer]
  @MerchantNumber varchar(20),
  @LinkedServerName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @LinkedServerName = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)))

  update tblStore
  set LinkedServerName = @LinkedServerName
  where upper(ltrim(rtrim(MerchantNumber))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@MerchantNumber)))

  if exists (select *
             from tblStore
             where LinkedServerName = @LinkedServerName) begin

    exec sp_AddStoreLinkedServer @LinkedServerName

  end
  
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetInventory]
  @CategoryID tinyint,
  @Status tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @GrandTotal money

  select @GrandTotal = sum(round(case when a.OnHandQty < 0 then 0 else a.OnHandQty end * cast(a.UnitPrice as money), 2))
  from tblItem i
    inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
  where i.ManageInv = 1
    and case when @Status = 1 then 
               case when i.Status = 1 then 1 end
             when @Status = 2 then
               case when i.Status = 0 then 1 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

  select c.ID as CategoryID, c.CatName, i.IName, i.IName2, s.SizeName, a.OnHandQty, a.SizeID, i.BarCode, 
         a.UnitPrice, round(case when a.OnHandQty < 0 then 0 else a.OnHandQty end * cast(a.UnitPrice as money), 2) as ExtTotal, 
         cast(0 as money) as CategoryTotal
  into #tmp_inventory
  from tblItem i
    inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
  where i.ManageInv = 1
    and case when @CategoryID > 0 then 
               case when i.CategoryID = @CategoryID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @Status = 1 then 
               case when i.Status = 1 then 1 end
             when @Status = 2 then
               case when i.Status = 0 then 1 end
             else
               1
        end = 1  

  update t
  set t.CategoryTotal = isnull(ct.CategoryTotal, 0)
  from #tmp_inventory t
    inner join (select CategoryID, sum(ExtTotal) as CategoryTotal
                from #tmp_inventory
                group by CategoryID) ct on t.CategoryID = ct.CategoryID
  
  select *, @GrandTotal as GrandTotal
  from #tmp_inventory
  order by CatName, CategoryID, IName, SizeName

  drop table #tmp_inventory

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfSameTimeChargeItemExists]
  @FromTableID smallint,
  @ToTableID smallint,
  @MergePersonIndex smallint
  --@Exists bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblTable t, tblPendingOrders p, tblItem i
             where t.OrderNum = p.SalesID
               and p.ItemID = i.ID
               and case when (@MergePersonIndex >= 0) then 
                          case when p.PersonIndex = @MergePersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
                        else 1
                   end = 1
               and t.ID = @FromTableID
               and i.HourlyChargedItem = 1
               and exists (select *
                           from tblTable t2, tblPendingOrders p2
                           where t2.OrderNum = p2.SalesID                              
                             and t2.ID = @ToTableID
                             and p2.ItemID = i.ID)) begin
    
    --set @Exists = 1
    return 1

  end
  else begin

    --set @Exists = 0
    return 0

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckDuplicateBarcode]
  @ItemID smallint,
  @Barcode varchar(15),
  @New bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@New = 1) begin
    if exists (select *
               from tblItem
               where upper(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(BarCode, '''')))) = upper(@Barcode)
                 and upper(ltrim(rtrim(@Barcode))) <> '''')
      return 1
    else
      return 0
  end
  else begin
    if exists (select *
               from tblItem
               where ID <> @ItemID
                 and upper(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(BarCode, '''')))) = upper(@Barcode)
                 and upper(ltrim(rtrim(@Barcode))) <> '''')
      return 1
    else
      return 0
  end
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSize]
  @SizeGroupID tinyint,
  @AllSizes bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select 0 as OrderIndex, ID, ID as SizeID, SizeName, ShortName, isnull(DisplayOrder, 0) as DisplayOrder, '''' as SizeGroupName --, cast(0 as bit) as ApplyNoDSC
  from tblSize
  where ID = 1
    and SizeGroupID = @SizeGroupID

  union all

  select 1 as OrderIndex, s.ID, s.ID as SizeID, s.SizeName, s.ShortName, isnull(s.DisplayOrder, 0) as DisplayOrder, isnull(sg.SizeGroupName, '''') as SizeGroupName --, cast(0 as bit) as ApplyNoDSC
  from tblSize s left join tblSizeGroup sg on s.SizeGroupID = sg.ID
  where s.ID > 1
    and case when (@SizeGroupID > -1) and (@AllSizes = 0) then 
               case when s.SizeGroupID = @SizeGroupID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

  order by OrderIndex, SizeGroupName, DisplayOrder, SizeName, ID

END'
GO

  where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
    and ItemID = @ItemID
    and case when @SizeID > 0 then
               case when SizeID = @SizeID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

END'
