EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateAvailableSize]
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @ApplyQty smallint,
  @UserID smallint,
  @StationName varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select 1
              from tblAvailableSizeTemp
              where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                and ItemID = @ItemID
                and SizeID = @SizeID) begin

    update tblAvailableSizeTemp
    set UnitPrice = @UnitPrice, --case when @ApplyQty = 0 then @UnitPrice else UnitPrice end,
        ApplyQty = @ApplyQty --case when @ApplyQty <> 0 then @ApplyQty else ApplyQty end
    where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
      and ItemID = @ItemID
      and SizeID = @SizeID

  end
  else begin

    if (@ItemID = 0) begin

      insert into tblAvailableSizeTemp (StationName, ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3) 
      values (upper(@StationName), @ItemID, @SizeID, @UnitPrice, 0, 0, 0 /*General discount will be applied for the new items*/, 0, 0)

    end
    else begin

      insert into tblAvailableSizeTemp (StationName, ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3) 
      select top 1 upper(@StationName), isnull(ich.ItemID, @ItemID), isnull(ich.SizeID, @SizeID), @UnitPrice, 
                   isnull(ich.OnHandQty, 0) + isnull(ich.AppliedQty, 0), 0, 0 /*General discount will be applied for the new items*/, 0, 0 
      from tblItem i
        left join tblInventoryChangeHistory ich on ich.ItemID = i.ID
                                               and ich.SizeID = @SizeID
      where i.ID = @ItemID      
      order by ich.ID desc

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateItem]
  @IName varchar(30), 
  @CategoryID tinyint, 
  @ApplyGST bit, 
  @ApplyPST bit, 
  @Status bit, 
  @OpenItem bit, 
  @KitchenB bit, 
  @KitchenF bit, 
  @Bar bit,
  @SideDish bit, 
  @Taste bit, 
  @IName2 varchar(30), 
  @ApplyPST2 bit, 
  @BarCode varchar(15), 
  @KitchenE bit, 
  @Alcohol bit, 
  @HourlyChargedItem bit, 
  @ScaleItem bit, 
  @OnlineItem bit, 
  @ItemDescription varchar(2000), 
  @ImageFilePath varchar(200),
  @RewardItem bit,
  @GroupItem bit,
  @Kitchen5 bit,
  @Kitchen6 bit,
  @ItemImage image,
  @ItemImageFileType varchar(5),
  @ManageInv bit,
  @NonAlcohol bit,
  @StationName varchar(30),
  @UserID smallint,
  @ItemID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_item

  update tblItem
  set IName = @IName, 
      CategoryID = @CategoryID, 
      ApplyGST = @ApplyGST, 
      ApplyPST = @ApplyPST, 
      [Status] = @Status, 
      OpenItem = @OpenItem, 
      KitchenB = @KitchenB, 
      KitchenF = @KitchenF, 
      Bar = @Bar,
      SideDish = @SideDish, 
      Taste = @Taste, 
      IName2 = @IName2, 
      ApplyPST2 = @ApplyPST2, 
      BarCode = @BarCode, 
      KitchenE = @KitchenE, 
      Alcohol = @Alcohol, 
      HourlyChargedItem = @HourlyChargedItem, 
      ScaleItem = @ScaleItem, 
      OnlineItem = @OnlineItem, 
      ItemDescription = @ItemDescription, 
      ImageFilePath = @ImageFilePath,
      RewardItem = @RewardItem,
      GroupItem = @GroupItem,
      Kitchen5 = @Kitchen5,
      Kitchen6 = @Kitchen6,
      ItemImage = @ItemImage,
      ItemImageFileType = @ItemImageFileType,
      ManageInv = @ManageInv,
      NonAlcohol = @NonAlcohol
  where ID = @ItemID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_item

    if (@StationName <> '''') begin
    
      delete 
      from tblAvailableSize
      where ItemID = @ItemID

      if exists (select 1
                 from tblAvailableSizeTemp
                 where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                   and ItemID = @ItemID) begin

        insert into tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3)
        select ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3
        from tblAvailableSizeTemp
        where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
          and ItemID = @ItemID

      end
      else begin

        insert into tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3)
        values (@ItemID, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)

      end

      declare @SizeID smallint, @ApplyQty smallint

      declare curs_inventory cursor for 
        select SizeID, ApplyQty
        from tblAvailableSizeTemp
        where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
          and ItemID = @ItemID

        open curs_inventory
        fetch next from curs_inventory into @SizeID, @ApplyQty
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          exec sp_RecordInventoryChange 0, @ItemID, @SizeID, @ApplyQty, @UserID

          fetch next from curs_inventory into @SizeID, @ApplyQty
        end
        close curs_inventory
      deallocate curs_inventory

    end

    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_item
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertItem]
  @IName varchar(30), 
  @CategoryID tinyint, 
  @ApplyGST bit, 
  @ApplyPST bit, 
  @Status bit, 
  @OpenItem bit, 
  @KitchenB bit, 
  @KitchenF bit, 
  @Bar bit,
  @SideDish bit, 
  @Taste bit, 
  @IName2 varchar(30), 
  @ApplyPST2 bit, 
  @BarCode varchar(15), 
  @KitchenE bit, 
  @Alcohol bit, 
  @HourlyChargedItem bit, 
  @ScaleItem bit, 
  @OnlineItem bit, 
  @ItemDescription varchar(2000), 
  @ImageFilePath varchar(200),
  @RewardItem bit,
  @GroupItem bit,
  @Kitchen5 bit,
  @Kitchen6 bit,
  @ItemImage image,
  @ItemImageFileType varchar(5),
  @ManageInv bit,
  @NonAlcohol bit,
  @StationName varchar(30),
  @NewItemID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_item

  insert into tblItem (IName, CategoryID, ApplyGST, ApplyPST, [Status], OpenItem, KitchenB, KitchenF, Bar,
                       SideDish, Taste, IName2, ApplyPST2, BarCode, KitchenE, Alcohol, HourlyChargedItem, 
                       ScaleItem, OnlineItem, ItemDescription, ImageFilePath, RewardItem, GroupItem,
                       Kitchen5, Kitchen6, ItemImage, ItemImageFileType, ManageInv, NonAlcohol)
  values (@IName, @CategoryID, @ApplyGST, @ApplyPST, @Status, @OpenItem, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @Bar,
          @SideDish, @Taste, @IName2, @ApplyPST2, @BarCode, @KitchenE, @Alcohol, @HourlyChargedItem, 
          @ScaleItem, @OnlineItem, @ItemDescription, @ImageFilePath, @RewardItem, @GroupItem,
          @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6, @ItemImage, @ItemImageFileType, @ManageInv, @NonAlcohol)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_item
    set @NewItemID = scope_identity()

    if (@StationName <> '''') begin
    
      if exists (select 1
                 from tblAvailableSizeTemp
                 where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
                   and ItemID = 0) begin
      
        insert into tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3)
        select @NewItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, 
               0, /*OnHandQty*/
               0, /*ApplyNoDSC*/ /*0 means that general discount will be applied for the new items*/
               UnitPrice2, 
               UnitPrice3
        from tblAvailableSizeTemp
        where upper(StationName) = upper(@StationName)
          and ItemID = 0

      end
      else begin

        insert into tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3)
        values (@NewItemID, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)

      end

    end

    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_item
    set @NewItemID = 0 
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertBillCollectHistory]
  @SalesID int, 
  @StationID smallint, 
  @CashierID int, 
  @CustomerID int,
  @CreditSalesID int,
  @BillCollectAmt smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
  -- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
  -- interfering with SELECT statements.
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_billcollect_history

  insert into tblBillCollectHistory (SalesID, StationID, CashierID, CustomerID, BillCollectDate, BillCollectAmt)
  values (@SalesID, @StationID, @CashierID, @CustomerID, getdate(), @BillCollectAmt)

  /* This part is not needed in Restaurant version, only needed in Retail version */
--  update tblSales
--  set SubTotal = SubTotal - @BillCollectAmt
--  where ID = @SalesID

  declare @ReceivedPaymentTypeID tinyint

  select @ReceivedPaymentTypeID = PaymentTypeID
  from tblPayment
  where SalesID = @SalesID

  set @ReceivedPaymentTypeID = isnull(@ReceivedPaymentTypeID, 0)

  exec sp_InsertCredit @CreditSalesID, @BillCollectAmt, 1, @CustomerID, @ReceivedPaymentTypeID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_billcollect_history
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_billcollect_history
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_CreditSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @EmployeeID int,
  @CustomerID int,
  @GivenCreditAmt money = 0 output,
  @ReceivedCreditAmt money = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @GivenCreditAmt = sum(round(c.CreditValue, 2))
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblCredit c on c.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join #tmp_station t on s.StationID = t.StationID
  where s.TransType in (1, 9)
    and c.Received = 0
    and c.DateRecorded >= @FromDateTime
    and c.DateRecorded <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then 
               case when s.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1
    and case when (@CustomerID > 0) then
               case when s.CustomerID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1
               
  select @ReceivedCreditAmt = sum(round(b.BillCollectAmt, 2))
  from tblBillCollectHistory b
    inner join #tmp_station t on b.StationID = t.StationID
  where b.BillCollectDate >= @FromDateTime
    and b.BillCollectDate <  @ToDateTime
    and case when (@EmployeeID > 0) then 
               case when b.CashierID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1
    and case when (@CustomerID > 0) then
               case when b.CustomerID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1

/*
  declare @Received bit, @CreditAmt money

  if (@EmployeeID = 0) begin
  
    if (@CustomerID = 0) begin
      declare curs_credit_summary cursor for
        select c.Received, sum(round(c.CreditValue, 2))
        from tblSales s, tblCredit c, #tmp_station t
        where c.SalesID = s.ID
          and s.StationID = t.StationID
          and s.TransType = 1
          and c.DateRecorded >= @FromDateTime
          and c.DateRecorded <  @ToDateTime
--          and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
--          and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        group by c.Received
    end
    else begin
      declare curs_credit_summary cursor for
        select c.Received, sum(round(c.CreditValue, 2))
        from tblSales s, tblCredit c, #tmp_station t
        where c.SalesID = s.ID
          and s.StationID = t.StationID
          and s.TransType = 1
          and c.DateRecorded >= @FromDateTime
          and c.DateRecorded <  @ToDateTime
--          and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
--          and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
          and s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
        group by c.Received
    end
  end
  else begin

    declare curs_credit_summary cursor for
      select c.Received, sum(round(c.CreditValue, 2))
      from tblSales s, tblCredit c, #tmp_station t
      where c.SalesID = s.ID
        and s.StationID = t.StationID
        and s.TransType = 1
        and c.DateRecorded >= @FromDateTime
        and c.DateRecorded <  @ToDateTime
--        and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
--        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        and s.CashierID = @EmployeeID
      group by c.Received

  end  

    open curs_credit_summary
    fetch next from curs_credit_summary into @Received, @CreditAmt
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      if (@Received = 1) set @ReceivedCreditAmt = @CreditAmt
      else if (@Received = 0) set @GivenCreditAmt = @CreditAmt

      fetch next from curs_credit_summary into @Received, @CreditAmt
    end
    close curs_credit_summary
  deallocate curs_credit_summary
*/

  set @ReceivedCreditAmt = isnull(@ReceivedCreditAmt, 0)
  set @GivenCreditAmt = isnull(@GivenCreditAmt, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCredit]
  @ByCustomer bit,
  @CustomerID int,
  @ShowEachTrans bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  if (@ByCustomer = 1) begin
    select c.CustomerID, t.CustomerNum, (t.FName + '' '' + t.LName) as CustomerName, t.CreditBalance, c.CreditValue
    from (select CustomerID, sum(round(CreditValue, 2)) as CreditValue
          from tblCredit
          group by CustomerID
          having sum(round(CreditValue, 2)) < 0) c, tblCustomer t
    where c.CustomerID = t.ID
    order by CustomerName
  end
  else begin
    if (@ShowEachTrans = 1) begin
      
      declare @OldestUnpaidSalesID int

      select @OldestUnpaidSalesID = min(c1.SalesID)
      from tblCredit c1
      where exists (select c2.SalesID
                    from tblCredit c2
                    where c2.SalesID = c1.SalesID
                    group by c2.SalesID
                    having sum(round(c2.CreditValue, 2)) < 0)
        and case when (@CustomerID > 0) then
                   case when (c1.CustomerID = @CustomerID) then 1
                        else 0
                   end
                 else 1
            end = 1

      if (isnull(@OldestUnpaidSalesID, 0) > 0) begin

        select c.SalesID, dbo.FormatDate(c.DateRecorded) as DateRecorded, c.CreditValue,
               (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as CashierName, (t.FName + '' '' + t.LName) as CustomerName, s.CustomerID
        from tblCredit c, tblSales s, tblUser u, tblCustomer t
        where c.SalesID = s.ID
          and s.CashierID = u.ID
          and s.CustomerID = t.ID
          and case when (@CustomerID > 0) then
                     case when (t.ID = @CustomerID) then 1
                          else 0
                     end
                   else 1
              end = 1
          and c.SalesID >= @OldestUnpaidSalesID
        order by DateRecorded desc, c.SalesID desc

      end
      else begin
        
        select c.SalesID, dbo.FormatDate(c.DateRecorded) as DateRecorded, c.CreditValue,
               (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as CashierName, (t.FName + '' '' + t.LName) as CustomerName, s.CustomerID
        from tblCredit c, tblSales s, tblUser u, tblCustomer t
        where c.SalesID = s.ID
          and s.CashierID = u.ID
          and s.CustomerID = t.ID
          and c.SalesID = 0

      end
    end
    else begin

      select c.SalesID, dbo.FormatDate(s.SaleDateTime) as DateRecorded, c.CreditValue,
             (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as CashierName, (t.FName + '' '' + t.LName) as CustomerName, s.CustomerID
      from (select SalesID, sum(round(CreditValue, 2)) as CreditValue
            from tblCredit
            group by SalesID
            having sum(round(CreditValue, 2)) < 0) c, tblSales s, tblUser u, tblCustomer t
      where c.SalesID = s.ID
        and s.CashierID = u.ID
        and s.CustomerID = t.ID
        and case when (@CustomerID > 0) then
                   case when (t.ID = @CustomerID) then 1
                        else 0
                   end
                 else 1
            end = 1
      order by DateRecorded desc, c.SalesID desc

    end
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetBillCollectHistory]
  @CustomerID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select b.ID, b.SalesID, b.StationID, b.CashierID, b.CustomerID,
         dbo.FormatDate(b.BillCollectDate) as BillCollectDate, b.BillCollectAmt,
         (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as CashierName, (c.FName + '' '' + c.LName) as CustomerName
  from tblBillCollectHistory b, tblUser u, tblCustomer c
  where b.CashierID = u.ID
    and b.CustomerID = c.ID
    and b.CustomerID = @CustomerID
  order by b.ID desc

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCredit]
  @SalesID int,
  @CreditValue smallmoney,
  @Received bit,
  @CustomerID int,
  @ReceivedPaymentTypeID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_credit

  if (@Received = 0)  begin
  
    insert into tblCredit (SalesID, CreditValue, Received, DateRecorded, CustomerID)
    values (@SalesID, @CreditValue, @Received, getdate(), @CustomerID)

  end
  else begin
    
    if (@CreditValue > 0) begin

      if (@SalesID > 0) begin /* @SalesID > 0 means two cases below */
        
        if exists (select *
                   from tblMisc
                   where Code = ''HTCOA''
                     and upper(ltrim(rtrim(Value))) = ''TRUE'') begin

          /* all the credit is paid for transactions ID less than or equal to @SalesID */
          insert into tblCredit (SalesID, CreditValue, Received, DateRecorded, CustomerID)
          --values (@SalesID, @CreditValue, 1, getdate(), @CustomerID)
          select SalesID, abs(round(CreditValue, 2)), 1, getdate(), c.CustomerID
          from tblCredit c
            inner join tblSales s on c.SalesID = s.ID
          where c.SalesID <= @SalesID
            and c.CustomerID = @CustomerID
            and c.Received = 0
            and s.TransType = 9
          
          /* update charge on account sales back to regular sales so they can be included in sales report */
          update p
          set p.PaymentTypeID = @ReceivedPaymentTypeID
          from tblSales s
            inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
          where s.ID <= @SalesID
            and s.TransType = 9
            and s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
            and p.PaymentTypeID = 11

          update tblSales
          set TransType = 1,
              OriginalTransType = 1,
              SaleDateTime = getdate()
          where ID <= @SalesID
            and TransType = 9
            and CustomerID = @CustomerID

        end
        else begin 

          /* the credit is paid by selecting a single transaction */
          insert into tblCredit (SalesID, CreditValue, Received, DateRecorded, CustomerID)
          values (@SalesID, @CreditValue, @Received, getdate(), @CustomerID)

        end

      end
      else begin 

        /* the credit is paid by the amount that customer paid - applies the amount to the oldest transactions first */

        declare @ApplicableSalesID int, @CreditBalance smallmoney, @CreditValueToApply smallmoney

        set @CreditValueToApply = @CreditValue

        declare curs_credit cursor for
          select SalesID, abs(sum(round(CreditValue, 2)))
          from tblCredit
          where CustomerID = @CustomerID
          group by SalesID
          having sum(round(CreditValue, 2)) < 0
          order by SalesID

          open curs_credit
          fetch next from curs_credit into @ApplicableSalesID, @CreditBalance
          while (@@fetch_status) = 0 begin
            
            if (@CreditValueToApply > 0) begin

              if (@CreditValueToApply < @CreditBalance)
                set @CreditBalance = @CreditValueToApply
               
              insert into tblCredit (SalesID, CreditValue, Received, DateRecorded, CustomerID)
              values (@ApplicableSalesID, @CreditBalance, @Received, getdate(), @CustomerID)
              
              set @CreditValueToApply = @CreditValueToApply - @CreditBalance

            end
            else
              break

            fetch next from curs_credit into @ApplicableSalesID, @CreditBalance
          end
          close curs_credit
        deallocate curs_credit

      end

    end

  end  

  update tblCustomer
  set CreditBalance = isnull(CreditBalance, 0) + @CreditValue
  where ID = @CustomerID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_credit
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_credit
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetDayHourDiscountPrice] 
(
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney
)
RETURNS smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @DiscountPrice smallmoney, @CurrentTime smallint

  set @CurrentTime = (datepart(hh, getdate())*100) + datepart(n, getdate())

  select @DiscountPrice = case when (isnull(ApplyHour, 0) = 1) then
                                 case when (((@CurrentTime >= HourFrom) and (@CurrentTime < HourTo)) or
                                            ((@CurrentTime + 2400 >= HourFrom) and (@CurrentTime + 2400 < HourTo))) then
                                        case when (isnull(ApplyHourPrice, 0) = 1) then
                                               isnull(HourPrice, -1)
                                             else
                                               -1
                                        end
                                      else
                                        case when (isnull(ApplyDay, 0) = 1) and (isnull(ApplyDayPrice, 0) = 1) then
                                               isnull(DayPrice, -1)
                                             else
                                               -1
                                        end
                                 end                              
                               else 
                                 case when (isnull(ApplyDay, 0) = 1) and (isnull(ApplyDayPrice, 0) = 1) then
                                        isnull(DayPrice, -1)
                                      else
                                        -1
                                 end
                          end
  from tblDayHourDiscount
  where ItemID = @ItemID
    and SizeID = @SizeID
    and WeekDayIndex = datepart(dw, getdate())
  
  return case when isnull(@DiscountPrice, -1) >= 0 then @DiscountPrice else @UnitPrice end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetDayHourDiscountRate] 
(
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint
)
RETURNS float
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @DiscountRate float, @CurrentTime smallint

  set @CurrentTime = (datepart(hh, getdate())*100) + datepart(n, getdate())

  select @DiscountRate = case when (isnull(ApplyHour, 0) = 1) then
                                case when (((@CurrentTime >= HourFrom) and (@CurrentTime < HourTo)) or
                                           ((@CurrentTime + 2400 >= HourFrom) and (@CurrentTime + 2400 < HourTo))) then
                                       case when (isnull(ApplyHourRate, 0) = 1) then
                                              isnull(HourRate, 0)
                                            else 
                                              0
                                       end
                                     else                     
                                       case when (isnull(ApplyDay, 0) = 1) and (isnull(ApplyDayRate, 0) = 1) then
                                              isnull(DayRate, 0)
                                            else
                                              0
                                       end
                                end
                              else 
                                case when (isnull(ApplyDay, 0) = 1) and (isnull(ApplyDayRate, 0) = 1) then
                                       isnull(DayRate, 0)
                                     else
                                       0
                                end
                         end
  from tblDayHourDiscount
  where ItemID = @ItemID
    and SizeID = @SizeID
    and WeekDayIndex = datepart(dw, getdate())
  
  return isnull(@DiscountRate, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertIncludedTip]
  @SalesID int,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @IncludedTipAmt smallmoney,
  @Inserted bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_included_tip_amount

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblTipAmountInBill
                 where SalesID = @SalesID
                   and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex) begin

    insert into tblTipAmountInBill (SalesID, PersonIndex, IncludedTipAmt)
    values (@SalesID, @PersonIndex, @IncludedTipAmt)

  end
  else begin

    update tblTipAmountInBill
    set IncludedTipAmt = @IncludedTipAmt
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_included_tip_amount
    set @Inserted = 1
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_included_tip_amount
    set @Inserted = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetCurrentDateTime]
(	
  @DateFormatType tinyint,
  @TimeFormatType tinyint,
  @GetDate bit,
  @GetTime bit
)
RETURNS varchar(25)
AS
BEGIN

  declare @Now datetime, @CurrentDate varchar(11), @CurrentTime varchar(11), @CurrentDateTime varchar(25)  

  set @Now = getdate()

  if (@DateFormatType = 1) /* dd-mmm-yyyy */
    set @CurrentDate = replace(substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'')
  else if (@DateFormatType = 2) /* ddmmmyyyy */
    set @CurrentDate = replace(substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 113), 1, 11), '' '', '''')
  else if (@DateFormatType = 3) /* mmm-dd */
    set @CurrentDate = substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 1, 3) + ''-'' + 
                       ltrim(substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 5, 2))
  else if (@DateFormatType = 4) /* mm/dd/yyyy */ 
    set @CurrentDate = convert(varchar, @Now, 101)
  else if (@DateFormatType = 5) /* yyyymmdd */
    set @CurrentDate = convert(varchar, @Now, 112)
  else if (@DateFormatType = 6) /* DDD.  mmm-dd */
    set @CurrentDate = substring(datename(dw, @Now), 1, 3) + ''.  '' + 
                       substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 1, 3) + ''-'' + 
                       ltrim(substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 5, 2))
  else if (@DateFormatType = 7) /* yyyy-mm-dd */
    set @CurrentDate = substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 120), 1, 10)
  else
    set @CurrentDate = ''''

  if (@TimeFormatType = 1) /* hh:nn:ss AMPM */
    set @CurrentTime = substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 13, 8) + '' '' + 
                       substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 25, 2)
  else if (@TimeFormatType = 2) /* hh:nn AMPM */
    set @CurrentTime = substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' +
                       substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 109), 25, 2)
  else if (@TimeFormatType = 3) /* hhnnss */
    set @CurrentTime = replace(substring(convert(varchar, @Now, 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')
  else if (@TimeFormatType = 4) /* hh:nn:ss */
    set @CurrentTime = convert(varchar, getdate(), 108)
  else 
    set @CurrentTime = ''''

  if (@GetDate = 1) begin
    if (@GetTime = 1)
      set @CurrentDateTime = @CurrentDate + case @TimeFormatType when 2 then ''  ''
                                                                 when 3 then ''_'' 
                                                                 else '' '' 
                                            end + @CurrentTime
    else
      set @CurrentDateTime = @CurrentDate
  end
  else
    set @CurrentDateTime = @CurrentTime

  return @CurrentDateTime

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSalesIDsInBillPrintQueue]
  @StationName varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmpBillPrintQueue table (SalesID int, PrinterName varchar(200))

  delete bpq
  from tblBillPrintQueue bpq
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblPendingOrders po
                    where po.SalesID = bpq.SalesID)

  insert into @tmpBillPrintQueue (SalesID, PrinterName)
  select SalesID, PrinterName
  from tblBillPrintQueue  
  where upper(ltrim(rtrim(StationName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@StationName)))

  delete bpq
  from tblBillPrintQueue bpq
    inner join @tmpBillPrintQueue t on t.SalesID = bpq.SalesID
  where upper(ltrim(rtrim(bpq.StationName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@StationName)))

  select b.*, t.TableName, t.DailyOrdNum, t.NumOfGuests, t.PickupTime, 
         t.PhoneNum, t.PickupPerson, t.PickupDate, u.FName as WaitressName
  from @tmpBillPrintQueue b
    inner join tblTable t on b.SalesID = t.OrderNum
    inner join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
  order by SalesID

END'
GO

                from tblItem i

  where p.SalesID = @SalesID

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdatePrepaidCardBalance]
  @SalesID int,
  @AmtUsed money,
  @Barcode varchar(30),
  @IsToAdjust bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@IsToAdjust = 1) begin
  
    declare @PaidAmount money, @TipAmount money, @PrepaidCardUsedAmount money

    select @PaidAmount = sum(p.PaidAmount),
           @TipAmount = sum(p.TipAmount)
    from tblPayment p
    where p.PaymentTypeID = 9
      and p.SalesID = @SalesID

    select @PrepaidCardUsedAmount = sum(AmtUsed)
    from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
    where SalesID = @SalesID

    if (@PaidAmount <= (@PrepaidCardUsedAmount + @AmtUsed)) and
       ((@PaidAmount + @TipAmount) >= (@PrepaidCardUsedAmount + @AmtUsed)) begin

      update tblPrepaidCards 
      set Balance = Balance - @AmtUsed
      where Barcode = @Barcode

      update tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
      set AmtUsed = AmtUsed + @AmtUsed,
          Balance = Balance - @AmtUsed
      where SalesID = @SalesID
        and Barcode = @Barcode

    end
  
  end
  else begin

    update tblPrepaidCards 
    set Balance = Balance - @AmtUsed
    where Barcode = @Barcode

    if exists (select 1
               from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
               where SalesID = @SalesID
                 and Barcode = @Barcode) begin

      update tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
      set AmtUsed = AmtUsed + @AmtUsed,
          Balance = Balance - @AmtUsed
      where SalesID = @SalesID
        and Barcode = @Barcode

    end
    else begin

      insert into tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory (SalesID, Barcode, DateTimeUsed, AmtUsed, Balance)
      select top 1 @SalesID, Barcode, getdate(), @AmtUsed, Balance
      from tblPrepaidCards
      where Barcode = @Barcode

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetCardTransactions]
  @FromDate datetime,
  @ToDate datetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select p.StationName,
         convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 112)) as SaleDate,
         s.SaleDateTime as SaleDateTime,
         p.SalesID,
         p.PaymentTypeID,
         isnull(pt.PaymentType, '''') as PaymentType, 
         p.PaidAmount, 
         isnull(p.TipAmount, 0) as TipAmount,
         p.PaidAmount + isnull(p.TipAmount, 0) as TotalPaidAmount,
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' 
              else ''****'' + reverse(substring(reverse(dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber)), 1, 4)) 
         end as CardNumber, 
         --dbo.DecryptString(p.CardExpiryDate) as CreditCardExpiryDate,
         isnull(p.AuthorizationNo, '''') as AuthorizationNo, 
         isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''') as TransactionIdentifier,
         case p.Voided when 1 then ''Voided'' else '''' end [Status],
         isnull(p.BatchNo, '''') as BatchNo,
         isnull(p.ItemNo, '''') as ItemNo,
         isnull(p.RevisionNo, '''') as RevisionNo,
         --dbo.DecryptString(p.TrackData) as TrackData,
         isnull(p.TipAdjusted, 0) as TipAdjusted,
         case isnull(p.BatchClosed, 0) when 1 then ''Y'' else ''N'' end as Settled
  from tblPayment p left join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID, 
       (select *
        from tblSales
        where SaleDateTime >= @FromDate
          and SaleDateTime <  dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDate, 112))) s
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and p.SalesID = s.ID
  order by p.StationName, s.SaleDateTime, p.ID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfCardPaymentExists]
  @SalesID int,
  @CardPaymentExists bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    -- Insert statements for procedure here
  
  if exists (select *
             from tblPayment
             where SalesID = @SalesID
               and PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
               and (isnull(AuthorizationNo, '''') <> ''''
                    or
                    isnull(SequenceNo, '''') <> '''' 
                    or
                    isnull(CardReceipt, '''') <> '''')) begin

    set @CardPaymentExists = 1
    return 1

  end
  else begin
  
    set @CardPaymentExists = 0
    return 0

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSummarizedPendingOrders]
  @SalesID int,
  @PersonIndex smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.DiscountPercent, p.Qty, round(p.Qty * p.UnitPrice, 2) as UnitPrice,
         isnull(DSCAmt, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0) as DiscountAmt, 
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.PricePerWeightUnit else 0 end as PricePerWeightUnit, 
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.MeasuredWeight else 0 end as MeasuredWeight,
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.DecimalPlaces else 0 end as DecimalPlaces,   
         --case when (p.ExtraChargeItem = 1) then p.ItemName else p.Tastes end as Tastes
         p.Tastes, p.ItemName, p.ItemName2, p.SizeName, row_number() over(order by p.SalesID) as SequenceNo
  from tblPendingOrders p
    inner join tblItem i on p.ItemID = i.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
    and case when (@PersonIndex >= 0) then
               case when p.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

/*
  select p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.DiscountPercent, sum(p.Qty) as Qty, round(sum(p.Qty * p.UnitPrice), 2) as UnitPrice,
         sum(isnull(DSCAmt, 0)) + sum(isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0)) + sum(isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0)) + sum(isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0)) as DiscountAmt, 
         0 as PricePerWeightUnit, 0 as MeasuredWeight, 0 as DecimalPlaces
  from tblPendingOrders p, tblItem i
  where p.ItemID = i.ID
    and p.SalesID = @SalesID
    and case when (@PersonIndex >= 0) then
               case when p.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and i.ScaleItem = 0
    and i.OpenItem = 0
  group by p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.DiscountPercent

  union all

  select p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.DiscountPercent, p.Qty, round(p.Qty * p.UnitPrice, 2) as UnitPrice,
         isnull(DSCAmt, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtEmployee, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType1, 0) + isnull(DSCAmtType2, 0) as DiscountAmt, 
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.PricePerWeightUnit else 0 end as PricePerWeightUnit, 
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.MeasuredWeight else 0 end as MeasuredWeight,
         case when (i.ScaleItem = 1) then p.DecimalPlaces else 0 end as DecimalPlaces
  from tblPendingOrders p, tblItem i
  where p.ItemID = i.ID
    and p.SalesID = @SalesID
    and case when (@PersonIndex >= 0) then
               case when p.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and (i.OpenItem = 1 or i.ScaleItem = 1)
*/

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertMemo]
  @Memo text,
  @MemoDate varchar(8),
  @BulletinBoardMemo bit,
  @LimitExceededNote varchar(200) output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @MemoID int, @MemoCount int, @MemoCountLimit int

  set @MemoCountLimit = case when @BulletinBoardMemo = 1 then 100 else 999 end
  set @LimitExceededNote = ''''

  select @MemoID = isnull(max(ID), 0),
         @MemoCount = count(*)
  from tblMemo
  where BulletinBoardMemo = @BulletinBoardMemo

  if (@MemoID < 10000) and (@MemoCount < @MemoCountLimit) begin

    insert into tblMemo (Memo, MemoDate, BulletinBoardMemo, MemoRecordedDateTime)
    values (@Memo, @MemoDate, @BulletinBoardMemo, getdate())

  end
  else begin
 
    if (@MemoCount < @MemoCountLimit) begin

      if exists (select *
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMemo]'') 
                   and type in (N''U''))

        drop table tmpMemo

      select *
      into tmpMemo
      from tblMemo

      if exists (select *
                 from tmpMemo) begin

        truncate table tblMemo

        insert into tblMemo (Memo, MemoDate, BulletinBoardMemo, MemoRecordedDateTime)
        select Memo, MemoDate, BulletinBoardMemo, MemoRecordedDateTime
        from tmpMemo
        order by ID

        if exists (select *
                   from tblMemo) begin

          insert into tblMemo (Memo, MemoDate, BulletinBoardMemo, MemoRecordedDateTime)
          values (@Memo, @MemoDate, @BulletinBoardMemo, getdate())

        end

      end

      if exists (select *
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMemo]'') 
                   and type in (N''U''))

        drop table tmpMemo

    end
    else begin
    
      if @BulletinBoardMemo = 1 begin
      
        set @LimitExceededNote = ''Maximum bulletin board memo count is 100.'' + char(13) + char(10) +
                                 ''Please delete some old memos...'' 

      end
      else begin

        set @LimitExceededNote = ''Maximum daily memo count is 999.'' + char(13) + char(10) +
                                 ''100 oldest memos will be deleted!'' + char(13) + char(10) +
                                 ''Continue?''

      end

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetMemo]
  @MemoFromDate smalldatetime,
  @MemoToDate smalldatetime,
  @BulletinBoardMemo bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblMemo
  where case when @BulletinBoardMemo = 1 then
               case when BulletinBoardMemo = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             else
               case when BulletinBoardMemo = 0
                     and MemoDate >= @MemoFromDate
                     and MemoDate <  dateadd(d, 1, @MemoToDate) then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
  order by MemoDate desc, ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ImportItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(1000), @item_file varchar(150), @dos_cmd_str varchar(500) 

  set @item_file = ''C:\TopPos\ItemImport.txt''

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemImport]'')
               and type in (N''U''))
    drop table tmpItemImport

  create table [dbo].[tmpItemImport](
    [CategoryName] [varchar](30) NULL,
    [ItemName] [varchar](30) NULL,
    [ItemName2] [varchar](30) NULL,
    [UnitPrice] [varchar](10) NULL,
    [Tax1] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Tax2] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Tax3] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Back] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Front] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Front2] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Bar] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Taste] [varchar](1) NULL,
    [Alcohol] [varchar](1) NULL
  )

  create table #tmpItemFile
  (
    item_file_name nvarchar(100)
  )

  set @dos_cmd_str = ''dir '' + @item_file + '' /b''
  insert #tmpItemFile
  exec xp_cmdshell @dos_cmd_str

  if exists (select *
             from #tmpItemFile) begin    

    set @script = 
        ''bulk insert tmpItemImport '' +
        ''from '''''' + @item_file + '''''' '' +
        ''with (fieldterminator = ''''\t'''', '' +
              ''firstrow = 2, '' +
              ''rowterminator = ''''\n'''')''

    exec sp_executesql @script

  end

  drop table #tmpItemFile


  update tmpItemImport
  set CategoryName = isnull(dbo.CleanupInvalidChars(CategoryName), ''Unknown''),
      ItemName = isnull(dbo.CleanupInvalidChars(ItemName), ''Unknown''),
      ItemName2 = isnull(dbo.CleanupInvalidChars(ItemName2), ''''),
      Tax1 =      case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Tax1)))     = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end,
      Tax2 =      case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Tax2)))     = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Tax3 =      case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Tax3)))     = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Back =      case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Back)))     = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Front =     case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Front)))    = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Front2 =    case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Front2)))   = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Bar =       case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Bar)))      = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Taste =     case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Taste)))    = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end, 
      Alcohol =   case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(Alcohol)))  = ''Y'' then ''Y'' else '''' end

  /* "Print to" location cannot be specified for tastes with extra charge amount */
  update tmpItemImport
  set Back = '''',
      Front = '''',
      Front2 = '''',
      Bar = ''''
  where Taste = ''Y''
    and convert(smallmoney, UnitPrice) > 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_GetImportedItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemImport]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin
    
    create table [dbo].[tmpItemImport](
      [CategoryName] [varchar](30) NULL,
      [ItemName] [varchar](30) NULL,
      [ItemName2] [varchar](30) NULL,
      [UnitPrice] [varchar](10) NULL,
      [Tax1] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Tax2] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Tax3] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Back] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Front] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Front2] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Bar] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Taste] [varchar](1) NULL,
      [Alcohol] [varchar](1) NULL
    )

  end

  select t.CategoryName, t.ItemName, t.ItemName2, 
          isnull(convert(smallmoney, t.UnitPrice), 0) as UnitPrice, 
          t.Tax1, t.Tax2, t.Tax3, t.Back, t.Front, t.Front2, t.Bar, t.Taste, t.Alcohol,
          convert(bit, case when isnull(i.ID, 0) > 0 then 1 else 0 end) as ItemExists
  from tmpItemImport t 
        left join tblCategory c on upper(ltrim(rtrim(c.CatName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.CategoryName)))
        left join tblItem i on upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.ItemName)))
                          and i.CategoryID = isnull(c.ID, 0)    

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_InsertImportedItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblCategory (CatName, PrintOrder, CategoryImageFilePath)
  select distinct t.CategoryName, 0, null
  from tmpItemImport t
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblCategory c
                    where upper(ltrim(rtrim(c.CatName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.CategoryName))))


  declare @CategoryName varchar(30), @CategoryID tinyint, @ItemName varchar(30), @ItemName2 varchar(30),
          @UnitPrice smallmoney, @Tax1 bit, @Tax2 bit, @Tax3 bit, @Back bit, @Front bit, @Front2 bit, @Bar bit,
          @Taste bit, @Alcohol bit, @ItemID smallint

  declare curs_existing_item cursor for
    select i.ID, isnull(convert(smallmoney, t.UnitPrice), 0)
    from tmpItemImport t 
      inner join tblCategory c on upper(ltrim(rtrim(c.CatName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.CategoryName)))
      inner join tblItem i on i.CategoryID = c.ID
                          and upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.ItemName)))

    open curs_existing_item
    fetch next from curs_existing_item into @ItemID, @UnitPrice
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update a
      set a.UnitPrice = @UnitPrice
      from tblAvailableSize a
      where a.ItemID = @ItemID
        and a.SizeID = 1

      fetch next from curs_existing_item into @ItemID, @UnitPrice
    end
    close curs_existing_item
  deallocate curs_existing_item

  declare curs_item cursor for
    select isnull(c.ID, 1), /*t.CategoryName,*/ t.ItemName, t.ItemName2, 
           isnull(convert(smallmoney, t.UnitPrice), 0), 
           case when t.Tax1     = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Tax2     = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Tax3     = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Back     = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Front    = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Front2   = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Bar      = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Taste    = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end,
           case when t.Alcohol  = ''Y'' then 1 else 0 end
    from tmpItemImport t left join tblCategory c on upper(ltrim(rtrim(c.CatName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.CategoryName)))
    where not exists (select *
                      from tblItem i
                      where upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.ItemName)))
                        and i.CategoryID = isnull(c.ID, 1))

    open curs_item
    fetch next from curs_item into @CategoryID, @ItemName, @ItemName2, @UnitPrice, @Tax1, @Tax2, @Tax3, 
                                   @Back, @Front, @Front2, @Bar, @Taste, @Alcohol
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      set @ItemID = 0

      exec sp_CopyAvailableSizeForEdit @ItemID, ''SYSTEM''

      if (@Taste = 0) or ((@Taste = 1) and (@UnitPrice > 0)) begin
 
        exec sp_UpdateAvailableSize @ItemID, 1, @UnitPrice, 0, 1, ''SYSTEM''

      end

      exec sp_InsertItem @ItemName, @CategoryID, @Tax1, @Tax2, 1, 0, @Back, @Front, @Bar, 0, @Taste, 
                         @ItemName2, @Tax3, '''', @Front2, @Alcohol, 0, 0, 0, null, null, 0, 0, 0, 0, null, null, 1, 0, ''SYSTEM'', @ItemID output

      exec sp_DeleteAvailableSize 0, 0, ''SYSTEM''

      fetch next from curs_item into @CategoryID, @ItemName, @ItemName2, @UnitPrice, @Tax1, @Tax2, @Tax3, 
                                     @Back, @Front, @Front2, @Bar, @Taste, @Alcohol
    end
    close curs_item
  deallocate curs_item  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_GetItemsToExport]
  @Preview bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@Preview = 0) begin

    select i.ID as ItemID, a.SizeID, c.CatName, i.IName, i.IName2, 
           case when a.SizeID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName, 
           a.UnitPrice
    from tblItem i 
         inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
         inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
         inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where i.Status = 1
    order by c.CatName, i.IName

  end
  else begin

--    declare @script nvarchar(2000), @export_file_nm varchar(500), 
--            @file_creation_str varchar(1000), @bcp_parameter varchar(1000)

--    set @export_file_nm = ''Item_List_Exported_'' + convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) + ''.csv''

    if exists (select * 
               from sys.objects 
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListExport]'')
                 and type in (N''U''))
      drop table tmpItemListExport

    select 0 as ID, cast('''' as varchar(1000)) as ItemInfo
    into tmpItemListExport

    truncate table tmpItemListExport
    
    insert into tmpItemListExport (ID, ItemInfo)
    select 0, 
           ''Item ID'' + char(44) + ''Size ID'' + char(44) +
           ''Category Name'' + char(44) + ''Item Name'' + char(44) +
           ''Alternative Name'' + char(44) +
           ''Size Name'' + char(44) + ''Unit Price''

    insert into tmpItemListExport (ID, ItemInfo)
    select cast(1 as int) as ID,
           convert(varchar, i.ID) + char(44) +
           convert(varchar, a.SizeID) + char(44) +
           ltrim(rtrim(c.CatName)) + char(44) +
           ltrim(rtrim(i.IName)) + char(44) +
           ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2)) + char(44) +
           case when a.SizeID = 1 then '''' else ltrim(rtrim(s.SizeName)) end + char(44) +
           convert(varchar, a.UnitPrice)
    from tblItem i 
         inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
         inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
         inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
    where i.Status = 1
    order by c.CatName, i.IName

    select *
    from tmpItemListExport
    order by ID

--    set @script = ''select ItemInfo '' +
--                  ''from tmpItemListExport '' +
--                  ''order by ID''
--
--    set @file_creation_str = ''echo '''''''' > C:\TopPos\Reports\'' + @export_file_nm
--    set @bcp_parameter = ''bcp "'' + @script + ''" queryout "C:\TopPos\Reports\'' + @export_file_nm + ''" -c -T -x'' 
--
--    exec master..xp_cmdshell @file_creation_str
--    exec master..xp_cmdshell @bcp_parameter
--
--    drop table tmpItemListExport

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPayout]
  @PayDate varchar(8),
  @AccountID tinyint,
  @SubTotalAmt smallmoney,
  @Tax1Amt smallmoney,
  @Tax2Amt smallmoney,
  @Tax3Amt smallmoney,
  @UserID smallint,
  @PayType varchar(5),
  @ChequeNo varchar(20),
  @Memo varchar(255),
  @BankID tinyint,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @PayoutDate smalldatetime

  if (isdate(@PayDate) = 1) begin
    set @PayoutDate = convert(smalldatetime, @PayDate) 
--    if (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) >= 0) and 
--       (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) < 60000)
      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, 59, dateadd(hh, 23, convert(varchar, @PayoutDate, 112)))
--    else
--      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, datepart(n, getdate()), dateadd(hh, datepart(hh, getdate()), convert(varchar, @PayoutDate, 112)))
  end
  else begin
--    if (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) >= 0) and 
--       (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) < 60000)
--      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, 59, dateadd(hh, 23, convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -1, getdate()), 112)))
--    else
      set @PayoutDate = getdate()
  end

  begin try
    begin transaction insert_payout
 
    insert into tblPayout (PayDate, AccountID, SubTotalAmt, GSTAmt, PSTAmt, UserID, PayType, ChequeNo, Memo, BankID, StationID)
    values (@PayoutDate, @AccountID, @SubTotalAmt, @Tax1Amt, @Tax2Amt, @UserID, @PayType, @ChequeNo, @Memo, @BankID, @StationID)

    commit transaction insert_payout
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction insert_payout
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdatePayout]
  @PayoutID int,
  @PayDate varchar(8),
  @AccountID tinyint,
  @SubTotalAmt smallmoney,
  @Tax1Amt smallmoney,
  @Tax2Amt smallmoney,
  @Tax3Amt smallmoney,
  @UserID smallint,
  @PayType varchar(5),
  @ChequeNo varchar(20),
  @Memo varchar(255),
  @BankID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @PayoutDate smalldatetime

  if (isdate(@PayDate) = 1) begin
    set @PayoutDate = convert(smalldatetime, @PayDate) 
--    if (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) >= 0) and 
--       (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) < 60000)
      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, 59, dateadd(hh, 23, convert(varchar, @PayoutDate, 112)))
--    else
--      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, datepart(n, getdate()), dateadd(hh, datepart(hh, getdate()), convert(varchar, @PayoutDate, 112)))
  end
  else begin
--    if (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) >= 0) and 
--       (convert(int, replace(substring(convert(varchar, getdate(), 114), 1, 8), '':'', '''')) < 60000)
--      set @PayoutDate = dateadd(n, 59, dateadd(hh, 23, convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -1, getdate()), 112)))
--    else
      set @PayoutDate = getdate()
  end

  begin try
    begin transaction update_payout
 
    update tblPayout
    set PayDate = @PayoutDate, 
        AccountID = @AccountID, 
        SubTotalAmt = @SubTotalAmt, 
        GSTAmt = @Tax1Amt, 
        PSTAmt = @Tax2Amt, 
        UserID = @UserID, 
        PayType = @PayType, 
        ChequeNo = @ChequeNo, 
        Memo = @Memo, 
        BankID = @BankID
        /* StationID = @StationID  -- Do not update first time recorded station ID */
    where ID = @PayoutID

    commit transaction update_payout
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_payout

    declare @ErrorMsg varchar(3000), @StoredProcedureName varchar(50)
    set @ErrorMsg = isnull(error_message(), '''')
    set @StoredProcedureName = error_procedure()
    exec sp_InsertErrorLog @ErrorMsg, @StoredProcedureName

    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

  select distinct BusinessCategory
  from tmpMasterItemList
  order by BusinessCategory
  
END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_GetMatchingItemList]
  @BusinessCategory varchar(50),
  @SearchFieldIndex tinyint,
  @SearchKey varchar(30),
  @BeginWith bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
  
  set @SearchKey = ltrim(rtrim(@SearchKey))

  if (@SearchKey <> '''') begin

    select *
    from tmpMasterItemList
    where BusinessCategory = @BusinessCategory
      and case when @BeginWith = 1 then
                 case when upper(ItemName) like upper(@SearchKey) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 case when upper(ItemName) like ''%'' + upper(@SearchKey) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1

  end
  else begin

    select *
    from tmpMasterItemList
    where BusinessCategory = ''''

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_InsertItemsFromInsertList]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @CategoryName varchar(30), @CategoryID tinyint, @ItemName varchar(30), @ItemName2 varchar(30),
          @UnitPrice smallmoney, @Tax1 bit, @Tax2 bit, @Tax3 bit, @Back bit, @Front bit, @Front2 bit, @Bar bit,
          @Taste bit, @Alcohol bit, @OpenItem bit, @ItemID smallint

  declare curs_item cursor for
    select t.CategoryID, t.ItemName, t.ItemName2, t.UnitPrice, t.Tax1, t.Tax2, t.Tax3, 
           t.Back, t.Front, t.Front2, t.Bar, t.Taste, t.Alcohol, t.OpenItem
    from tmpItemListToInsert t
    where not exists (select *
                      from tblItem i
                      where upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.ItemName)))
                        and i.CategoryID = t.CategoryID)

    open curs_item
    fetch next from curs_item into @CategoryID, @ItemName, @ItemName2, @UnitPrice, @Tax1, @Tax2, @Tax3, 
                                   @Back, @Front, @Front2, @Bar, @Taste, @Alcohol, @OpenItem
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      set @ItemID = 0

      exec sp_CopyAvailableSizeForEdit @ItemID, ''SYSTEM''

      if (@Taste = 0) or ((@Taste = 1) and (@UnitPrice > 0)) begin
 
        exec sp_UpdateAvailableSize @ItemID, 1, @UnitPrice, 0, 1, ''SYSTEM''

      end

      exec sp_InsertItem @ItemName, @CategoryID, @Tax1, @Tax2, 1, @OpenItem, @Back, @Front, @Bar, 0, @Taste, 
                         @ItemName2, @Tax3, '''', @Front2, @Alcohol, 0, 0, 0, null, null, 0, 0, 0, 0, null, null, 1, 0, ''SYSTEM'', @ItemID output

      exec sp_DeleteAvailableSize 0, 0, ''SYSTEM''

      fetch next from curs_item into @CategoryID, @ItemName, @ItemName2, @UnitPrice, @Tax1, @Tax2, @Tax3, 
                                     @Back, @Front, @Front2, @Bar, @Taste, @Alcohol, @OpenItem
    end
    close curs_item
  deallocate curs_item  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_GetItemListToInsert]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListToInsert]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin
    
    CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmpItemListToInsert](
      [CategoryID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
      [ItemName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
      [ItemName2] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
      [UnitPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
      [Tax1] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Tax2] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Tax3] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Back] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Front] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Front2] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Bar] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Taste] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [Alcohol] [bit] NOT NULL,
      [OpenItem] [bit] NOT NULL
    ) ON [PRIMARY]

  end

  select t.CategoryID, c.CatName as CategoryName, t.ItemName, t.ItemName2, t.UnitPrice,
         t.Tax1, t.Tax2, t.Tax3, t.Back, t.Front, t.Front2, t.Bar, t.Taste, t.Alcohol, t.OpenItem       
  from tmpItemListToInsert t left join tblCategory c on t.CategoryID = c.ID

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTablesWithOrders]
  @TakeOut bit,
  @QueryType tinyint,
  @SearchString varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select t.ID,
         case when t.TakeOut = 0 and ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson)) <> '''' then 
                ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson)) 
              else t.TableName 
         end as TableName, 
         t.PickupTime, t.PhoneNum, t.PickupPerson, 
         case when (t.TakeOut = 1) and (t.Delivery = 1 or t.Online = 1) and (t.OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0) then t.OnlineOrderNumber else t.DailyOrdNum end as DailyOrdNum,
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber) end as CardNumber,
         p.PreAuthorizedAmount
  from tblTable t
    left join tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans p on p.TableID = t.ID 
                                         and p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
  where t.OrderNum > 0
    and case when @TakeOut = 1 then
               case when t.TakeOut = 1 then 1 else 0 end                 
             else
               case when t.TakeOut = 0 then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and case @QueryType 
          when 1 then
            case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(case when t.TakeOut = 0 and ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson)) <> '''' then 
                                               ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson)) 
                                             else t.TableName 
                                        end))) like ''%'' + upper(ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString))) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end
          when 2 then
            case when reverse(substring(ltrim(rtrim(reverse(isnull(dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber), '''')))), 1, 4)) = ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString)) then 1 else 0 end
          when 3 then
            case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.PhoneNum))) like ''%'' + upper(ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString))) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end           
          when 4 then
            case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(t.PickupPerson))) like ''%'' + upper(ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString))) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end
          else 1
        end = 1

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_AssignUnlinkedOrdersToEmptyTables]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @SalesID int, @TakeOutOrder bit, @DailyOrderNumber int, @TableID smallint

  declare curs_unlinked_orders cursor for
    select distinct po1.SalesID, s1.TakeOutOrder, s1.DailyOrderNumber, s1.TableID
    from tblPendingOrders po1 
         left join tblTable t1 on isnull(t1.OrderNum, 0) = po1.SalesID
         inner join (select * 
                     from tblSales
                     where SubTotal = 0
                       and TableID > 0
                       and TransType = 1 /* This is important - if not stated, causes voided or merged orders to be relinked to table */
                       and SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)) s1 on po1.SalesID = s1.ID
    where isnull(t1.OrderNum, 0) = 0

    union

    select distinct po2.SalesID, s2.TakeOutOrder, s2.DailyOrderNumber, s2.TableID
    from tblPendingOrdersBackup po2 
         left join tblTable t2 on isnull(t2.OrderNum, 0) = po2.SalesID
         inner join (select * 
                     from tblSales
                     where SubTotal = 0
                       and TableID > 0
                       and TransType = 1 /* This is important - if not stated, causes voided or merged orders to be relinked to table */
                       and SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)) s2 on po2.SalesID = s2.ID
    where isnull(t2.OrderNum, 0) = 0
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblSalesDetail sd
                      where sd.SalesID = s2.ID)
      /* This condition is to allow finishing separated transaction with $0 payment for the last unpaid transaction */
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblSales s
                      where s.ID > s2.ID
                        and s.DailyOrderNumber = s2.DailyOrderNumber)

    order by SalesID

    open curs_unlinked_orders
    fetch next from curs_unlinked_orders into @SalesID, @TakeOutOrder, @DailyOrderNumber, @TableID
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update tblTable
      set OrderNum = @SalesID,
          DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrderNumber
      where ID = @TableID
        and Opened = 0
        and OrderNum = 0
        and Linked = 1

      fetch next from curs_unlinked_orders into @SalesID, @TakeOutOrder, @DailyOrderNumber, @TableID
    end
    close curs_unlinked_orders
  deallocate curs_unlinked_orders


--  declare @SalesID int, @TakeOutOrder bit, @DailyOrderNumber int, @TableID smallint
--
--  declare curs_unlinked_orders cursor for
--    select distinct po.SalesID, s.TakeOutOrder, s.DailyOrderNumber
--    from tblPendingOrders po 
--         left join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = po.SalesID
--         inner join (select * 
--                     from tblSales
--                     where SubTotal = 0
--                       and SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)) s on po.SalesID = s.ID
--    where t.OrderNum is null
--    order by po.SalesID
--
--    open curs_unlinked_orders
--    fetch next from curs_unlinked_orders into @SalesID, @TakeOutOrder, @DailyOrderNumber
--    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin
--
--      select top 1 @TableID = ID
--      from tblTable 
--      where Linked = 1
--        and TakeOut = @TakeOutOrder
--        and Opened = 0
--        and OrderNum = 0      
--      order by ID
--
--      update tblTable
--      set OrderNum = @SalesID,
--          DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrderNumber
--      where ID = @TableID
--
--      fetch next from curs_unlinked_orders into @SalesID, @TakeOutOrder, @DailyOrderNumber
--    end
--    close curs_unlinked_orders
--  deallocate curs_unlinked_orders

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTableOpenStatus]
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationIDInUse smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction get_table_open_status

    declare @Opened bit, @OrderNum int, @DailyOrdNum int, @ServerID smallint, 
            @NumOfGuests tinyint, @PickupTime varchar(8), @PhoneNum varchar(10),
            @PickupPerson varchar(20), @FName varchar(30), @LName varchar(30), @PickupDate smalldatetime
            --@Updated bit

    select @Opened = t.Opened --,
           --@OrderNum = t.OrderNum,
           --@DailyOrdNum = t.DailyOrdNum,
           --@ServerID = t.ServerID,
           --@NumOfGuests = t.NumOfGuests,
           --@PickupTime = t.PickupTime,
           --@PhoneNum = t.PhoneNum,
           --@PickupPerson = t.PickupPerson,
           --@FName = u.FName,
           --@LName = u.LName,
           --@PickupDate = t.PickupDate
    from tblTable t with (ROWLOCK) --left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
    where t.ID = @TableID

    if (isnull(@Opened, 1) = 0) begin

      exec sp_UpdateTableOpenStatus 1, @TableID, @StationIDInUse --, @Updated output

      /* This script will continue with @Opened as 0 and return @Opened with the value of 0 to show the user "table is in use" message */
    end

    /* if Opened = 1 then user will see "table is in use" message */
    --select @Opened as Opened, @OrderNum as OrderNum, @DailyOrdNum as DailyOrdNum, @ServerID as ServerID, 
    --       @NumOfGuests as NumOfGuests, @PickupTime as PickupTime, @PhoneNum as PhoneNum, 
    --       @PickupPerson as PickupPerson, @FName as FName, @LName as LName, @PickupDate as PickupDate

    update tblTable
    set ServerID = case when ServerID = 0 then 1 else ServerID end,
        NumOfGuests = case when NumOfGuests = 0 then 1 else NumOfGuests end
    where ID = @TableID 
      and (ServerID = 0 or NumOfGuests = 0)

    select isnull(@Opened, 1) as Opened,
           t.OrderNum,
           t.DailyOrdNum,
           t.ServerID,
           t.NumOfGuests,
           t.PickupTime,
           t.PhoneNum,
           t.PickupPerson,
           isnull(u.FName, '''') as FName,
           isnull(u.LName, '''') as LName,
           t.PickupDate,
           t.StationIDInUse,
           t.OnlineOrderNumber,
           isnull(s.StationName, '''') as StationName,
           --cast(case when (t.TakeOut = 0) and (isnull(soo.OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0) > 0) then 1 else 0 end as bit) as IsSelfDineInOrder
           isnull(soo.DineInOrder, 0) as IsSelfDineInOrder
    from tblTable t 
      left join tblUser u on t.ServerID = u.ID
      left join tblStation s on t.StationIDInUse = s.ID
      left join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders soo on soo.SalesID = t.OrderNum
    where t.ID = @TableID

    commit transaction get_table_open_status
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction get_table_open_status
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetAvailableItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;  

  select c.ID as CategoryID, c.CatName, i.ID as ItemID, s.ID as SizeID,
         i.IName, i.IName2, case when a.SizeID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName
  from tblAvailableSize a
    inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
  where i.OpenItem = 0
    and i.GroupItem = 0 
    and i.Status = 1
  order by CatName, IName, SizeName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CopyDiscountSetting]
  @CopyItemID int,
  @CopySizeID smallint,
  @Food bit,
  @Alcohol bit,
  @ApplyItemID int,
  @ApplySizeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ApplyNoDSC bit, @ItemID int, @SizeID smallint

  select @ApplyNoDSC = ApplyNoDSC
  from tblAvailableSize
  where ItemID = @CopyItemID
    and SizeID = @CopySizeID

  if ((@Food = 1) or (@Alcohol = 1)) begin

    update a
    set a.ApplyNoDSC = isnull(@ApplyNoDSC, 0)
    from tblAvailableSize a
      inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
    where case when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 1 then 1
               when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 0 then
                 case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 0 else 1 end
               when @Food = 0 and @Alcohol = 1 then
                 case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 
                 0
          end = 1
      and i.OpenItem = 0
      and i.GroupItem = 0 
      and i.Status = 1
      and (a.ItemID <> @CopyItemID or a.SizeID <> @CopySizeID)
    
    delete d
    from tblDayHourDiscount d
      inner join tblItem i on d.ItemID = i.ID
    where case when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 1 then 1
               when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 0 then
                 case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 0 else 1 end
               when @Food = 0 and @Alcohol = 1 then
                 case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 1 else 0 end
               else 
                 0
          end = 1
      and (d.ItemID <> @CopyItemID or d.SizeID <> @CopySizeID)

    if (isnull(@ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 0) and
       exists (select *
               from tblDayHourDiscount
               where ItemID = @CopyItemID
                 and SizeID = @CopySizeID
                 and (ApplyDay = 1 or ApplyHour = 1)) begin

      declare curs_item cursor for
        
        select a.ItemID, a.SizeID
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
        where case when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 1 then 1
                   when @Food = 1 and @Alcohol = 0 then
                     case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 0 else 1 end
                   when @Food = 0 and @Alcohol = 1 then
                     case when i.Alcohol = 1 then 1 else 0 end
                   else 
                     0
              end = 1
          and i.OpenItem = 0
          and i.GroupItem = 0 
          and i.Status = 1
          and (a.ItemID <> @CopyItemID or a.SizeID <> @CopySizeID)

        open curs_item
        fetch next from curs_item into @ItemID, @SizeID
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          insert into tblDayHourDiscount (ItemID, SizeID, WeekDayIndex, 
                                          ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice, 
                                          ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, 
                                          DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice)
          select @ItemID, @SizeID, WeekDayIndex, 
                 ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice, 
                 ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, 
                 DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice
          from tblDayHourDiscount
          where ItemID = @CopyItemID
            and SizeID = @CopySizeID

          fetch next from curs_item into @ItemID, @SizeID

        end
        close curs_item
      deallocate curs_item

    end

  end
  else begin

    update a
    set a.ApplyNoDSC = isnull(@ApplyNoDSC, 0)
    from tblAvailableSize a
    where a.ItemID = @ApplyItemID
      and a.SizeID = @ApplySizeID

    delete d
    from tblDayHourDiscount d
    where d.ItemID = @ApplyItemID
      and d.SizeID = @ApplySizeID

    insert into tblDayHourDiscount (ItemID, SizeID, WeekDayIndex, 
                                    ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice, 
                                    ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, 
                                    DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice)
    select @ApplyItemID, @ApplySizeID, WeekDayIndex, 
           ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice, 
           ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, 
           DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice
    from tblDayHourDiscount
    where ItemID = @CopyItemID
      and SizeID = @CopySizeID

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetHistoryOrderDetailBySalesID]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select cast(0 as bit) as OldItemExists, sd.ItemID, sd.SizeID, sd.Qty, 
         case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then 
                case when i.OpenItem = 1 then sd.UnitPrice
                     else isnull(a.UnitPrice, 0)
                end
              else
                case when i.OpenItem = 1 then 
                       dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, sd.UnitPrice) 
                     else
                       dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, a.UnitPrice)
                end
         end as UnitPrice,
         isnull(sd.Tastes, '''') as Tastes, '''' as SideDishes, 0 as DSCAmt, 
         0 as PersonIndex, cast(0 as bit) as SeparateBillPrint, isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) as ApplyNoDSC,
         cast(case when i.Taste = 1 then 1 else 0 end as bit) as ExtraChargeItem,
         0 as DSCAmtEmployee, 0 as DSCAmtType1, 0 as DSCAmtType2, 
         case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then 0 
              else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountRate(a.ItemID, a.SizeID) 
         end as DayHourDiscountRate,
         round(0, 2) as PricePerWeightUnit, 0 as MeasuredWeight, 0 as DecimalPlaces, 
         round(0, 3) as DiscountPercent,
         case when sd.ItemName <> '''' then sd.ItemName else i.IName end as IName, 
         case when sd.ItemName2 <> '''' then sd.ItemName2 else i.IName2 end as IName2,
         case when sd.SizeID > 1 then 
                case when sd.SizeName <> '''' then sd.SizeName else isnull(s.SizeName, '''') end
              else '''' 
         end as SizeName,
         i.ID, i.CategoryID, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, i.Status, i.OpenItem, i.KitchenB, i.KitchenF, i.Bar, i.SideDish,
         i.Taste, i.ApplyPST2, i.BarCode, i.KitchenE, i.Alcohol, i.HourlyChargedItem, i.ScaleItem, i.OnlineItem,
         i.ItemDescription, i.ImageFilePath, i.RewardItem, i.GroupItem, i.Kitchen5, i.Kitchen6, i.ItemImage,
         i.ItemImageFileType, i.ManageInv,i.NonAlcohol
  into #tmp_history_order_detail
  from tblSalesDetail sd
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize s on sd.SizeID = s.ID
    left join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
                                and a.SizeID = s.ID
  where sd.SalesID = @SalesID

  if exists (select *
             from #tmp_history_order_detail t
             where not exists (select *
                               from tblMenuLayout ml
                               where ml.LayoutModeType = 1
                                 and ml.ItemID = t.ItemID)) begin

    update #tmp_history_order_detail
    set OldItemExists = 1

  end

  select *
  from #tmp_history_order_detail

END'
GO
