EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPrepaidCardBalance]
  @Barcode varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select p.*, c.FName, c.LName, c.CustomerNum, c.Phone
  from tblPrepaidCards p
    inner join tblCustomer c on p.CustomerID = c.ID
  where case when (@Barcode <> '''') then
               case when p.Barcode = @Barcode then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1
  order by p.Barcode

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail]
  @Barcode varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT staterments.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ID int

  declare @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 table
  (
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    TransDateTime varchar(20),
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int,
    DiscountAmt smallmoney
  )

  declare @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 table
  (
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    TransDateTime varchar(20),
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int,
    DiscountAmt smallmoney
  )

  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 (TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, DiscountAmt)
  select convert(varchar, ChargeDate, 120) as TransDateTime, Amount as Credit, null as Debit, null as Balance, SalesID, DiscountAmt
  from tblPrepaidCardChargeHistory
  where Barcode = @Barcode
  order by TransDateTime

  /* Didn''t use "union all" to make sure the charge records are inserted before use records for the case that the time is the same */
  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 (TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, DiscountAmt)
  select convert(varchar, DateTimeUsed, 120) as TransDateTime, null as Credit, AmtUsed as Debit, Balance, SalesID, 0 as DiscountAmt
  from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
  where Barcode = @Barcode 
  order by TransDateTime

  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 (TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, DiscountAmt)
  select TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, DiscountAmt
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1
  order by TransDateTime, ID

  declare curs_detail cursor for
    select ID
    from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2
    order by ID

    open curs_detail
    fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update t
      set t.Balance = isnull(t.Credit, 0) - isnull(t.Debit, 0)
                      + isnull((select t2.Balance
                                from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t2
                                where t2.ID = case when t.ID > 1 then t.ID - 1
                                                   else 0
                                              end), 0)
      from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t
      where t.ID = @ID
      
      fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    end
    close curs_detail
  deallocate curs_detail

  select *
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2
  order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCashInOutHistory]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @SalesCashAmt money, @ActualCashAmt money, @NonCashTipOutAmt money

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select @SalesCashAmt = sum(round(isnull(dbo.GetPaymentTotal(ID, 1), 0), 2))
  from tblSales
  where SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and TransType in (0, 1)

  select @ActualCashAmt = sum(round(EndCash - StartCash, 2)),
         @NonCashTipOutAmt = sum(NonCashTipOut)
  from tblCashInDrawer
  where StartDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and StartDateTime <  @ToDateTime

  select @SalesCashAmt as SalesCashAmt, 
         @ActualCashAmt as ActualCashAmt, 
         @NonCashTipOutAmt as NonCashTipOutAmt,
         c.StartDateTime, 
         c.EndDateTime, 
         round(c.StartCash, 2) as StartCash,
         round(c.EndCash, 2) as EndCash, 
         round(c.NonCashTipOut, 2) as NonCashTipOut,
         round(c.DiscrepancyAmt, 2) as DiscrepancyAmt,
         case c.Status when 1 then ''Open'' else ''Closed'' end as DrawerStatus,
         u1.FName as StartCashier, 
         u2.FName as EndCashier, 
         c.DiscrepancyNote
  from tblCashInDrawer c 
    inner join tblUser u1 on c.StartCashierID = u1.ID
    inner join tblUser u2 on c.EndCashierID = u2.ID
  where c.StartDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and c.StartDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  order by c.ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTransactionsWithDeletedItems]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @TotalOfDeletedUnsavedItems money

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select @TotalOfDeletedUnsavedItems = sum(isnull(Qty * UnitPrice, 0)) 
  from tblDeletedUnsavedItems
  where DeletedDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and DeletedDateTime <  @ToDateTime

  select s.ID, s.DailyOrderNumber, s.SaleDateTime, (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as Server,
         case s.TransType when 1 then ''SALE''
                          when 3 then ''VOID''
                          when 4 then ''S.VOID''
                          else '''' 
         end as TransType,
         round(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt, 2) as Total
  from tblSales s
    inner join (select distinct SalesID
                from tblDeletedItems) d on d.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID    
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime  
    and case when @StationID > 0 then
               case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

  union all

  select 0 as ID, 0 as DailyOrderNumber, null as SaleDateTime, '''' as Server, '''' as TransType, @TotalOfDeletedUnsavedItems as Total

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertDeletedUnsavedItems]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Qty smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @UserID smallint,
  @DeleteReason varchar(200),
  @LastSalesID int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@SalesID = 0) begin
    select @LastSalesID = max(ID)
    from tblSales

    set @LastSalesID = isnull(@LastSalesID, 0)
    set @SalesID = @LastSalesID
  end

  insert into tblDeletedUnsavedItems (LastSalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, DeletedDateTime, UserID, DeleteReason)  
  values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @UnitPrice, getdate(), @UserID, @DeleteReason)

  set @LastSalesID = @SalesID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetDeletedUnsavedItems]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime 
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select case when (d.Qty = 0) and (d.UnitPrice = 0) then '''' else i.IName end as IName,
         case when (d.Qty = 0) and (d.UnitPrice = 0) then '''' else z.SizeName end as SizeName,
         d.Qty, d.UnitPrice, d.DeletedDateTime, (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as Server, 
         ltrim(rtrim(DeleteReason)) + '': '' + convert(varchar, d.LastSalesID) + '' was the last sales ID'' as DeleteReason
  from tblDeletedUnsavedItems d
    inner join tblItem i on d.ItemID = i.ID
    inner join tblSize z on d.SizeID = z.ID
    inner join tblUser u on d.UserID = u.ID
  where d.DeletedDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and d.DeletedDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  order by d.DeletedDateTime, i.IName, z.SizeName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCustomersWithUnpaidTransactions]
  @CustomerID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblCustomer c
    inner join (select distinct CustomerID
                from tblSales 
                where TransType = 9
                  and CustomerID > 1) s on s.CustomerID = c.ID
  where case when @CustomerID > 1 then
               case when c.ID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetUnpaidTransactions]
  @CustomerID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select s.ID, cast(0 as smallmoney) as PaidAmount, cast(0 as smallmoney) as PaidTipAmount,
               sum(p.PaidAmount) as UnpaidAmount, sum(p.TipAmount) as UnpaidTipAmount
  into #tmpUnpaidTransactions
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.TransType = 9
    and p.PaymentTypeID = 11
    and s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
  group by s.ID

  select t.ID, sum(p.PaidAmount) as PaidAmount, sum(p.TipAmount) as PaidTipAmount
  into #tmpPartiallyPaidAmount 
  from #tmpUnpaidTransactions t
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = t.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID <> 11
  group by t.ID

  update t1
  set t1.PaidAmount = t2.PaidAmount,
      t1.PaidTipAmount = t2.PaidTipAmount
  from #tmpUnpaidTransactions t1
    inner join #tmpPartiallyPaidAmount t2 on t2.ID = t1.ID

  select s.ID, s.CustomerID, s.SaleDateTime, s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt as TotalAmount, 
         t.PaidAmount, t.PaidTipAmount, t.UnpaidAmount, t.UnpaidTipAmount
  from #tmpUnpaidTransactions t
    inner join tblSales s on s.ID = t.ID
  order by s.ID

  drop table #tmpPartiallyPaidAmount
  drop table #tmpUnpaidTransactions

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateItemPrice]
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @UnitPriceType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_item_price

  update tblAvailableSize
  set UnitPrice = case @UnitPriceType when 1 then @UnitPrice else UnitPrice end,
      UnitPrice2 = case @UnitPriceType when 2 then @UnitPrice else UnitPrice2 end,
      UnitPrice3 = case @UnitPriceType when 3 then @UnitPrice else UnitPrice3 end   
  where ItemID = @ItemID
    and SizeID = @SizeID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_item_price
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_item_price
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

    declare @FileType varchar(5)

    if (upper(@FileType) in (''PNG'', ''JPG'', ''JPEG'', ''GIF'', ''BMP'')) begin
      insert into tblAdImages (AdImageFileName, AdImage, AdImageFileType, [Status])
      values (@AdImageFileName, @AdImage, @FileType, @Status)
    end
  end  

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetRewardPointsSaved]
(
	@SalesID int
)
RETURNS int
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @RewardPointSubTotal smallmoney, @RewardPointsSaved int, @SaveRewardPointOnApplicableItemsOnly bit, 
          @RewardSavePointValue int, @RewardPurchaseAmtValue smallmoney, @PaidAmountByRewardPoints smallmoney,
          @IsRefund bit

  select @SaveRewardPointOnApplicableItemsOnly = case when upper(Value) = ''TRUE'' then 1 else 0 end
  from tblMisc
  where Code = ''ORPAI''

  select @RewardSavePointValue = convert(int, substring(Value, 1, charindex(''@'', Value) - 1)),
         @RewardPurchaseAmtValue = convert(smallmoney, substring(Value, charindex(''@'', Value) + 1, 4))
  from tblMisc
  where Code = ''SRPR''

  select @PaidAmountByRewardPoints = sum(PaidAmount)
  from tblPayment
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and PaymentTypeID = 10 /* Reward Point Payment Type ID */

	select @RewardPointSubTotal = round(sum(round(sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice, 2)) - sum(sd.DiscountAmt), 2)
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
  where s.ID = @SalesID
    and case when @SaveRewardPointOnApplicableItemsOnly = 1 then 
               case when i.RewardItem = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

  select @IsRefund = case when TransType = 0 then 1 else 0 end
  from tblSales
  where ID = @SalesID

  if (round(isnull(@RewardPointSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@PaidAmountByRewardPoints, 0), 0, 1) > 0)
    set @RewardPointsSaved = @RewardSavePointValue * (round(isnull(@RewardPointSubTotal, 0) - isnull(@PaidAmountByRewardPoints, 0), 0, 1) / @RewardPurchaseAmtValue)
  else
    set @RewardPointsSaved = 0

  return case when @IsRefund = 1 then -1 else 1 end * isnull(@RewardPointsSaved, 0)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_LinkTransactionToCustomer]
  @SalesID int,
  @CustomerID int
AS
BEGIN
  -- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
  -- interfering with SELECT statements.
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction link_to_customer

    if exists (select *
               from tblSales
               where TransType in (0, 1)
                 and ID = @SalesID
                 and CustomerID <> @CustomerID) begin

      declare @OldCustomerID int, @RewardPointsSaved int

      select @OldCustomerID = CustomerID
      from tblSales 
      where ID = @SalesID

      update tblSales
      set CustomerID = @CustomerID
      where ID = @SalesID

      if exists (select *
                 from tblPointsDetail
                 where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

        select @RewardPointsSaved = isnull(PointSaved - PointUsed, 0)
        from tblPointsDetail
        where SalesID = @SalesID

        update tblCustomer
        set EarnedPoints = EarnedPoints - @RewardPointsSaved
        where case when @OldCustomerID > 1 then
                     case when ID = @OldCustomerID then 1 else 0 end
                   else 0
              end = 1

        if (@CustomerID > 1) begin
    
          update tblCustomer
          set EarnedPoints = EarnedPoints + @RewardPointsSaved
          where ID = @CustomerID      

        end
        else begin

          delete
          from tblPointsDetail
          where SalesID = @SalesID

        end

      end
      else begin

        /* this would be always for saved points. if there were any used points, then the record should exist.
           which means it would not come to this else condition */
        set @RewardPointsSaved = dbo.GetRewardPointsSaved(@SalesID) 

        exec sp_InsertUpdateRewardPointsDetail @SalesID, @CustomerID, 0, @RewardPointsSaved

      end

    end
        
    commit transaction link_to_customer
    return 1
  end try
 
  begin catch
    rollback transaction link_to_customer
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCustomer]
  @FName varchar(30),
  @LName varchar(30),
  @CustomerNum varchar(20), 
  @DateEntered varchar(20), 
  @Gender bit,
  @Phone varchar(20),
  @Address varchar(200), 
  @CardValue smallmoney,
  @Savings smallmoney,
  @LastVisit varchar(20),
  @EarnedPoints int,  
  @CustomerNote varchar(255),
  --@CreditBalance smallmoney,
  @NewCustomerID int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction insert_customer

    insert into tblCustomer (FName, LName, CustomerNum, DateEntered, Gender, Phone, [Address], 
                             CardValue, Savings, LastVisit, EarnedPoints, CustomerNote /*, CreditBalance*/)
    values (@FName, @LName, @CustomerNum, @DateEntered, @Gender, @Phone, @Address, 
            @CardValue, @Savings, @LastVisit, @EarnedPoints, @CustomerNote /*, @CreditBalance*/)

    commit transaction insert_customer
    set @NewCustomerID = scope_identity()
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction insert_customer
    set @NewCustomerID = 0
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateCustomer]
  @FName varchar(30),
  @LName varchar(30), 
  @DateEntered varchar(20), 
  @Gender bit,
  @Phone varchar(20),
  @Address varchar(200), 
  @CardValue smallmoney,
  @Savings smallmoney,
  @LastVisit varchar(20),
  @EarnedPoints int, 
  @CustomerNote varchar(255),
  --@CreditBalance smallmoney,
  @CustomerNum varchar(20),
  @CustomerID int,
  @ByCustomerID bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction update_customer

    update tblCustomer
    set FName = @FName, 
        LName = case when @LName = ''-1'' then LName else @LName end, 
        DateEntered = case when @DateEntered = ''-1'' then DateEntered else @DateEntered end, 
        Gender = case when @DateEntered = ''-1'' then Gender else @Gender end, --Assume Gender is updated when DateEntered is updated as well. 
        Phone = case when @Phone = ''-1'' then Phone else @Phone end, 
        [Address] = case when @Address = ''-1'' then [Address] else @Address end, 
        CardValue = case when @CardValue = -1 then CardValue else @CardValue end, 
        Savings = case when @Savings = -1 then Savings else @Savings end,
        LastVisit = case when @LastVisit = ''-1'' then getdate() else @LastVisit end, 
        EarnedPoints = case when @EarnedPoints = -1 then EarnedPoints else @EarnedPoints end,
        CustomerNote = case when @CustomerNote = ''-1'' then CustomerNote else @CustomerNote end,
        --CreditBalance = case when @CreditBalance = -1 then CreditBalance else @CreditBalance end,
        CustomerNum = case when @ByCustomerID = 1 then @CustomerNum else CustomerNum end
    where case when @ByCustomerID = 1 then 
                 case when ID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
               else
                 case when CustomerNum = @CustomerNum then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1

    commit transaction update_customer
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_customer
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetSalesCustomerInfo]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @CustomerID int

  select @CustomerID = isnull(CustomerID, 1)
  from tblSales
  where ID = @SalesID  

  if (isnull(@CustomerID, 1) = 1) begin

    select @CustomerID = isnull(c.ID, 1)
    from tblTable t
      left join tblCustomer c on t.PhoneNum = c.CustomerNum
    where t.OrderNum = @SalesID   

  end  

  select *
  from tblCustomer
  where ID = isnull(@CustomerID, 1)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetModifiersForOnlineOrder] 
(
  @OrderID int,  
  @ItemIndex smallint,
  @ItemType bit
)
RETURNS varchar(2000)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @ItemModifiers varchar(2000)

  set @ItemModifiers = ''''

  if (@ItemType = 1) begin

    declare @Modifier varchar(100)    

    declare curs_modifier cursor for
      select case when (d.ItemType = 0 and d.ItemPrice <> 0 and d.ItemName <> '''') then 
                    --ltrim(rtrim(d.ItemSizeName)) + ''_$'' + convert(varchar, d.ItemPrice) + ''_#'' + d.ItemName
                    case when isnull(s.ID, 0) > 1 then isnull(s.SizeName, '''')
                         else ltrim(rtrim(d.ItemSizeName)) 
                    end + ''_$'' + convert(varchar, d.ItemPrice) + ''_#'' + d.ItemName
                  else /* _# could be added in "else" part as well */
                    case when (d.ItemSizeID > 1) and (ltrim(rtrim(d.ItemSizeName)) = '''') then isnull(s.SizeName, '''')
                         else ltrim(rtrim(d.ItemSizeName))
                    end                  
             end
      from tblOnlineOrderDetail d
        left join tblSize s on d.ItemSizeID = s.ID
      where ((d.ItemType = 0 and d.ItemID > 0)
             or 
             (d.ItemType = 1 and d.ItemSizeID > 1))
        and d.OrderID = @OrderID
        and d.ItemIndex = @ItemIndex

      open curs_modifier
      fetch next from curs_modifier into @Modifier
      while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

        set @ItemModifiers = @ItemModifiers + @Modifier + ''|''
    
        fetch next from curs_modifier into @Modifier
	    end
      close curs_modifier
    deallocate curs_modifier

    select @ItemModifiers = isnull(@ItemModifiers, '''') + 
                            case when isnull(ItemComments, '''') <> '''' then ''@'' + ItemComments + ''|'' else '''' end
    from tblOnlineOrderDetail
    where OrderID = @OrderID
      and ItemIndex = @ItemIndex
      and ItemType = 1

    set @ItemModifiers = ltrim(rtrim(substring(isnull(@ItemModifiers, ''''), 1, 2000)))

    if (len(@ItemModifiers) <> '''') begin

      set @ItemModifiers = substring(@ItemModifiers, 1, len(@ItemModifiers) - 1) + ''|''

    end

  end  

  return @ItemModifiers

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetCustomerSales]
  @CustomerID int,
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, 0)

  select c.FName, c.LName, c.CustomerNum, s.ID, s.SaleDateTime,
         round(s.SubTotal,2) as SubTotalAmt,
         round(s.DSCAmt,2) as DSCAmt,
         round(s.GSTAmt,2) as GSTAmt,
         round(s.PSTAmt,2) as PSTAmt,
         round(s.PST2Amt,2) as PST2Amt,
         round(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt, 2) as TotalAmt,
         --pt.PaymentType,          
         --case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' 
         --     else replicate(''*'', len(p.CardNumber) - 4) + reverse(substring(reverse(p.CardNumber), 1, 4)) 
         --end as CardNumber,
         --p.PaidAmount,
         '''' as PaymentType,
         '''' as CardNumber,
         0 as PaidAmount,
         cast(case S.TransType when 0 then ''Refund''
                               when 1 then ''Sale''
                               when 2 then ''NoSale''
                               when 3 then ''Void''
                               when 4 then ''SalesVoid''
                               when 5 then ''Training''
                               when 9 then ''Unpaid''
                               else '''' 
              end as varchar(10)) as TransType,
         dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX1'') as Tax1Name, 
         dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX2'') as Tax2Name, 
         dbo.GetMiscValue(''TAX3'') as Tax3Name
  from tblSales s
    --inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    --inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
    inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
  where s.CustomerID = @CustomerID
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    --and p.Voided = 0
  order by s.ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPaymentDetailBySalesID]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select pt.PaymentType, 
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' 
              else replicate(''*'', len(dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber)) - 4) + reverse(substring(reverse(dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber)), 1, 4)) 
         end as CardNumber,
         p.PaidAmount,
         case when p.Voided = 1 then ''Voided'' else '''' end as Voided,
         p.PaidDateTime, p.StationName
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
    and p.Voided = 0
  order by p.ID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertPendingOrdersTemp]
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Qty smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @Tastes varchar(2000),
  @SideDishes varchar(200),
  @ItemName varchar(100),
  @SizeName varchar(30),
  @ApplyGST bit,
  @ApplyPST bit,
  @DSCAmt smallmoney,
  @KitchenB bit,
  @KitchenF bit,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @SeparateBillPrint bit,
  @Bar bit,
  @ApplyNoDSC bit,
  @OpenItem bit,
  @ItemName2 varchar(30),
  @ExtraChargeItem bit,
  @ApplyPST2 bit,
  @KitchenE bit,
  @DSCAmtEmployee smallmoney,
  @DSCAmtType1 smallmoney,
  @DSCAmtType2 smallmoney,
  @DayHourDiscountRate float,
  @PricePerWeightUnit smallmoney,
  @MeasuredWeight float,
  @DecimalPlaces tinyint,
  @DiscountPercent float,
  @Kitchen5 bit,
  @Kitchen6 bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_pending_orders_temp

  insert into tblPendingOrdersTemp (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, Tastes,  SideDishes, ItemName, SizeName, 
                                    ApplyGST, ApplyPST, DSCAmt, KitchenB, KitchenF, PersonIndex, SeparateBillPrint, 
                                    Bar, ApplyNoDSC, OpenItem, ItemName2, ExtraChargeItem, ApplyPST2, KitchenE,  
                                    DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, DayHourDiscountRate, PricePerWeightUnit, 
                                    MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, DiscountPercent, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
  values (@SalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @UnitPrice, @Tastes, @SideDishes, @ItemName, @SizeName, 
          @ApplyGST, @ApplyPST, @DSCAmt, @KitchenB, @KitchenF, @PersonIndex, @SeparateBillPrint, 
          @Bar, @ApplyNoDSC, @OpenItem, @ItemName2, @ExtraChargeItem, @ApplyPST2, @KitchenE,  
          @DSCAmtEmployee, @DSCAmtType1, @DSCAmtType2, @DayHourDiscountRate, @PricePerWeightUnit, 
          round(@MeasuredWeight, @DecimalPlaces), @DecimalPlaces, round(@DiscountPercent, 3), @Kitchen5, @Kitchen6)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_pending_orders_temp
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_pending_orders_temp
    return 0
  end
    
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertBillsToPrint]
  @SalesID int,
  @BillPrintType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try

    declare @StationName varchar(30), @PrinterName varchar(200)

    select top 1 @StationName = StationName
    from tblPeripherals
    where Code = ''PSO''
      and upper([Value]) = ''TRUE''

    select @PrinterName = [Value]
    from tblPeripherals
    where StationName = @StationName
      and Code = ''CPN''

    insert into tblBillPrintQueue (StationName, SalesID, PrinterName, BillPrintType)
    values (@StationName, @SalesID, @PrinterName, @BillPrintType)

    return cast(1 as bit)

  end try

  begin catch

    return cast(0 as bit)

  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTableInfo1]
  @TableID smallint,
  @OrderNum int,
  @DailyOrdNum int,
  @BillPrinted bit,
  @TotalAmtUpdated bit,
  @TotalAmt smallmoney
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction update_table_info1

    if (@TotalAmtUpdated = 1) begin

      update tblTable 
      set TotalAmt = @TotalAmt
      where ID = @TableID

    end
    else begin

      declare @DateTimeIn smalldatetime

      set @DateTimeIn = getdate()

      update tblTable 
      set OrderNum = @OrderNum, 
          TimeIn = @DateTimeIn, 
          DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrdNum, 
          BillPrinted = case when isnull(@BillPrinted, 0) = 0 then 0 else 1 end,
          Attention = 0,
          TotalAmt = @TotalAmt
      where ID = @TableID

    end

    commit transaction update_table_info1
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_table_info1
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTableInfo2]
  @TableID smallint,
  @ServerID smallint,
  @NumOfGuests tinyint,
  @TableNickName varchar(20)
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction update_table_info2

    update tblTable
    set ServerID = case when isnull(@ServerID, 0) = 0 then 1 else @ServerID end,
        NumOfGuests = case when isnull(@NumOfGuests, 0) = 0 then 1 else @NumOfGuests end,
        PickupPerson = isnull(@TableNickName, '''')
    where ID = @TableID

    update s
    set s.CashierID = case when isnull(@ServerID, 0) = 0 then 1 else @ServerID end 
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblTable t on t.OrderNum = s.ID
    where t.ID = @TableID   

    commit transaction update_table_info2
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_table_info2
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTableInfo3]
  @TableID smallint
  --@Updated bit = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction update_table_info3

    delete po
    from tblPendingOrders po
      inner join tblTable t on po.SalesID = t.OrderNum
    where t.ID = @TableID
      and po.SalesID > 0
  
    update t  
    set t.OrderNum = 0, 
        t.ServerID = 0, 
        t.NumOfGuests = 0, 
        --t.Opened = 0,  
        t.PickupTime = '''', 
        t.PhoneNum = '''', 
        t.PickupPerson = '''',  
        t.DailyOrdNum = 0, 
        t.BillPrinted = 0,
        t.TotalAmt = 0,
        t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
    from tblTable t  
    where t.ID = @TableID  

    commit transaction update_table_info3
    --set @Updated = 1
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction update_table_info3
    --set @Updated = 0
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetTotalTimeCharged]
(
	@SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint
)
RETURNS varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @TotalTimeCharged varchar(20), @Hours smallint, @Minutes smallint, @TotalInMinutes int

  set @TotalTimeCharged = ''''

	select @TotalInMinutes = isnull(sum(datediff(n, StartDateTime, EndDateTime)), 0)
  from tblTimeStartEnd
  where SalesID = @SalesID
    and ItemID = @ItemID

  if (@TotalInMinutes > 0) begin

    set @Hours = @TotalInMinutes / 60.0
    set @Minutes = @TotalInMinutes % 60.0

    if (@Hours > 0) 
      set @TotalTimeCharged = convert(varchar, @Hours) + '' hr '' + convert(varchar, @Minutes) + '' min''
    else
      set @TotalTimeCharged = convert(varchar, @Minutes) + '' min''

  end
	
  return @TotalTimeCharged

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTotalMemoCount]
  @BulletinBoardMemo bit,

AS

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @MemoCount = count(*)
  from tblMemo
  where BulletinBoardMemo = @BulletinBoardMemo

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SyncDailySalesSummaryToOnlineReportServer]
  @refresh_data bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @today smalldatetime, @sale_date smalldatetime, @updated_datetime smalldatetime, 
          @store_id varchar(100), @LinkedServerName varchar(100), @script nvarchar(max),
          @last_updated_datetime smalldatetime

  set @today = convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)
  set @sale_date = convert(varchar, (year(getdate()) * 10000) + 101)
  set @updated_datetime = getdate()
  select @store_id = dbo.GetMiscValue(''ORSID'')
  select @LinkedServerName = dbo.GetMiscValue(''ORLSN'')

  if (@refresh_data = 1) begin

    --select *
    --into #tmp_rpt_sales_summary
    --from rpt_sales_summary

    --truncate table rpt_sales_summary
    --truncate table rpt_online_order_sales_summary

    --insert into rpt_sales_summary
    --select *
    --from #tmp_rpt_sales_summary
    --where SaleDate < @sale_date
    --order by SaleDate

    --drop table #tmp_rpt_sales_summary

    delete
    from rpt_sales_summary
    where SaleDate >= @sale_date

    delete
    from rpt_online_order_sales_summary
    where SaleDate >= @sale_date

  end

  select @last_updated_datetime = isnull(max(UpdatedDateTime), dateadd(n, -10, @updated_datetime))
  from rpt_sales_summary

  if (datediff(n, @last_updated_datetime, @updated_datetime) >= 10) begin

    while (@sale_date <= @today) begin      

      /* For each day sales summary, 
         "truncate" table "rpt_sales_summary_temp" everytime, before "exec spr_SalesSummary" is executed. 
         and then insert into "rpt_sales_summary" with "@sale_date" */
      truncate table rpt_sales_summary_temp 
      truncate table rpt_online_order_sales_summary_temp

      if (not exists (select *
                      from rpt_sales_summary
                      where SaleDate = @sale_date
                        and SaleDate < @today))
         or
         (@sale_date >= dateadd(d, -3, @today)) begin    

        delete 
        from rpt_sales_summary
        where SaleDate = @sale_date

        delete
        from rpt_online_order_sales_summary
        where SaleDate = @sale_date

        insert into rpt_sales_summary_temp (
          SubTotal, DSC, Tax1, Tax2, Tax3, Total,
          FoodSubTotal, FoodTax1Total, FoodTax2Total, FoodTax3Total,
          NonAlcoholSubTotal, NonAlcoholTax1Total, NonAlcoholTax2Total, NonAlcoholTax3Total,
          AlcoholSubTotal, AlcoholTax1Total, AlcoholTax2Total, AlcoholTax3Total,
          DineInTotal, DineInCount, TakeOutTotal, TakeOutCount, DeliveryTotal, DeliveryCount, OnlineTotal, OnlineCount,
          TotalSum, NetCash, NetDebit, NetCredit, NetVisa, NetMc, NetAmex, NetCoupon, NetDiscover, NetJcb, NetGiftCard, NetRewardPoint, NetChargeOnAccount,
          NetCashTip, NetDebitTip, NetCreditTip, NetVisaTip, NetMcTip, NetAmexTip, NetCouponTip, NetDiscoverTip, NetJcbTip, NetGiftCardTip, NetChargeOnAccountTip, NetTip,
          CashPaymentCount, DebitPaymentCount, VisaPaymentCount, McPaymentCount, AmexPaymentCount, CouponPaymentCount, DiscoverPaymentCount, JcbPaymentCount,
          GiftCardPaymentCount, RewardPointPaymentCount, ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount, 
          DailyChargeAmtOnPC, DailyUsedAmtOnPC, DailyDiscountAmtOnPC, TotalChargeAmtOnPC, TotalUsedAmtOnPC, TotalDiscountAmtOnPC, TotalBalanceOnPC, 
          RefundSubTotal, RefundTax1, RefundTax2, RefundTax3, RefundTotal, 
          PayoutSubTotal, PayoutTax1, PayoutTax2, PayoutTotal, 
          CashPayoutTotal, DebitPayoutTotal, CreditPayoutTotal, ChequePayoutTotal, GivenCreditAmt, ReceivedCreditAmt, NetCreditAmt,
          SalesCount, RefundCount, NoSaleCount, ChargeOnAccSalesCount, PayoutCount, VoidCount, TransCount, GuestCount,
          AverageSaleAmt, DSCAmtGeneral, DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, 
          DeletedItemsCount, DeletedAmount, PriceChangedItemsCount, PriceChangedAmount, SoldItemsCount, SoldAmount, 
          Tax1Name, Tax2Name, Tax3Name)
        exec spr_SalesSummary @sale_date, @sale_date, 0, 0, 0, 0        

        insert into rpt_sales_summary
        select convert(int, @store_id), @updated_datetime, @sale_date, *
        from rpt_sales_summary_temp

        insert into rpt_online_order_sales_summary_temp (
          OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, Integrated, TransType, TransTypeDescription, TransCount, 
          SubTotalAmt, DSCAmt, Tax1Amt, Tax2Amt, Tax3Amt, TotalAmt, GuestCount, PaymentLocation, PaymentTypeID, PaymentType, 
          PaymentCount, PaidAmount, TipAmount, CommissionSubTotal, CommissionTax1, CommissionTax2, 
          CommissionTax3, CommissionTotal, Tax1Rate, Tax2Rate, Tax3Rate)
        exec spr_SalesOfOnlineOrdersSummary @sale_date, @sale_date, 0

        insert into rpt_online_order_sales_summary
        select convert(int, @store_id), @updated_datetime, @sale_date, 
               OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, Integrated, TransType, TransTypeDescription, TransCount, 
               SubTotalAmt, DSCAmt, Tax1Amt, Tax2Amt, Tax3Amt, TotalAmt, GuestCount, 3 /*PaymentTypeID*/, ''Visa'' /*PaymentType*/, /* To get one row for a day, used default value otherwise, it will create multiple rows */
               sum(PaymentCount), sum(PaidAmount), sum(TipAmount), CommissionSubTotal, CommissionTax1, CommissionTax2, 
               CommissionTax3, CommissionTotal, Tax1Rate, Tax2Rate, Tax3Rate, ''Online'' /*PaymentLocation*/ /* To get one row for a day, used default value otherwise, it will create multiple rows */
        from rpt_online_order_sales_summary_temp
        group by OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, Integrated, TransType, TransTypeDescription, TransCount, 
                 SubTotalAmt, DSCAmt, Tax1Amt, Tax2Amt, Tax3Amt, TotalAmt, GuestCount, CommissionSubTotal, CommissionTax1, CommissionTax2, 
                 CommissionTax3, CommissionTotal, Tax1Rate, Tax2Rate, Tax3Rate
      end

      set @sale_date = dateadd(d, 1, @sale_date)

    end    

    if (len(ltrim(rtrim(@LinkedServerName))) > 0) begin   

      set @script = 
       ''insert into ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.SalesSummaries (
                    StoreID, TransCount, SubTotalAmt, DSCAmt, GSTAmt, PSTAmt, PST2Amt, TotalAmt, 
                    CashPaidAmt, DebitPaidAmt, VisaPaidAmt, McPaidAmt, AmexPaidAmt, CouponPaidAmt,
                    CashTipPaidAmt, DebitTipPaidAmt, CreditTipPaidAmt, TotalTipPaidAmt, TransGuestCount, Date)
        select r.StoreID, (r.SalesCount - r.RefundCount), r.SubTotal, r.DSC, r.Tax1, r.Tax2, r.Tax3, r.Total,
               r.NetCash, r.NetDebit, r.NetVisa, r.NetMc, r.NetAmex, r.NetCoupon,
               r.NetCashTip, r.NetDebitTip, r.NetCreditTip, r.NetTip, r.GuestCount, r.SaleDate
        from rpt_sales_summary r 
          left join (select *
                     from ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.SalesSummaries
                     where StoreID = '' + @store_id + '') s on s.StoreID = r.StoreID
                                                           and convert(varchar, s.[Date], 112) = convert(varchar, r.SaleDate, 112)
        where s.StoreID is null
        order by r.SaleDate

        update s
        set s.TransCount = (r.SalesCount - r.RefundCount), 
            s.SubTotalAmt = r.SubTotal, 
            s.DSCAmt = r.DSC, 
            s.GSTAmt = r.Tax1, 
            s.PSTAmt = r.Tax2, 
            s.PST2Amt = r.Tax3, 
            s.TotalAmt = r.Total, 
            s.CashPaidAmt = r.NetCash, 
            s.DebitPaidAmt = r.NetDebit, 
            s.VisaPaidAmt = r.NetVisa, 
            s.McPaidAmt = r.NetMc, 
            s.AmexPaidAmt = r.NetAmex, 
            s.CouponPaidAmt = r.NetCoupon,
            s.CashTipPaidAmt = r.NetCashTip, 
            s.DebitTipPaidAmt = r.NetDebitTip, 
            s.CreditTipPaidAmt = r.NetCreditTip, 
            s.TotalTipPaidAmt = r.NetTip, 
            s.TransGuestCount = r.GuestCount
        from (select *
              from ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.SalesSummaries
              where StoreID = '' + @store_id + '') s
          inner join rpt_sales_summary r on s.StoreID = r.StoreID
                                        and convert(varchar, s.[Date], 112) = convert(varchar, r.SaleDate, 112)
        where s.[Date] >= '''''' + convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -3, @today), 112) + ''''''
          and s.SubTotalAmt <> r.SubTotal''

      exec sp_executesql @script

      set @script = 
       ''insert into ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.OnlineOrderSalesSummaries (
                    StoreID, Date, OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, Integrated, TransType, TransTypeDescription,
                    TransCount, SubTotalAmt, DSCAmt, Tax1Amt, Tax2Amt, Tax3Amt, TotalAmt, GuestCount, PaymentTypeID,
                    PaymentType, PaymentCount, PaidAmount, TipAmount, CommissionSubTotal, CommissionTax1, 
                    CommissionTax2, CommissionTax3, CommissionTotal, Tax1Rate, Tax2Rate, Tax3Rate)
        select r.StoreID, r.SaleDate, r.OnlineOrderCompanyID, r.CompanyName, r.Integrated, r.TransType, r.TransTypeDescription,
               r.TransCount, r.SubTotalAmt, r.DSCAmt, r.Tax1Amt, r.Tax2Amt, r.Tax3Amt, r.TotalAmt, r.GuestCount, r.PaymentTypeID,
               r.PaymentType, r.PaymentCount, r.PaidAmount, r.TipAmount, r.CommissionSubTotal, r.CommissionTax1,
               r.CommissionTax2, r.CommissionTax3, r.CommissionTotal, r.Tax1Rate, r.Tax2Rate, r.Tax3Rate
        from rpt_online_order_sales_summary r 
          left join (select *
                     from ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.OnlineOrderSalesSummaries
                     where StoreID = '' + @store_id + '') s on s.StoreID = r.StoreID
                                                         and s.OnlineOrderCompanyID = r.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                         and convert(varchar, s.[Date], 112) = convert(varchar, r.SaleDate, 112)
        where s.StoreID is null
        order by r.SaleDate

        update s
        set s.OnlineOrderCompanyID = r.OnlineOrderCompanyID, 
            s.CompanyName = r.CompanyName, 
            s.Integrated = r.Integrated, 
            s.TransType = r.TransType, 
            s.TransTypeDescription = r.TransTypeDescription,
            s.TransCount = r.TransCount, 
            s.SubTotalAmt = r.SubTotalAmt, 
            s.DSCAmt = r.DSCAmt, 
            s.Tax1Amt = r.Tax1Amt, 
            s.Tax2Amt = r.Tax2Amt, 
            s.Tax3Amt = r.Tax3Amt, 
            s.TotalAmt = r.TotalAmt, 
            s.GuestCount = r.GuestCount, 
            s.PaymentTypeID = r.PaymentTypeID,
            s.PaymentType = r.PaymentType, 
            s.PaymentCount = r.PaymentCount, 
            s.PaidAmount = r.PaidAmount, 
            s.TipAmount = r.TipAmount, 
            s.CommissionSubTotal = r.CommissionSubTotal,
            s.CommissionTax1 = r.CommissionTax1,
            s.CommissionTax2 = r.CommissionTax2,
            s.CommissionTax3 = r.CommissionTax3,
            s.CommissionTotal = r.CommissionTotal,
            s.Tax1Rate = r.Tax1Rate,
            s.Tax2Rate = r.Tax2Rate,
            s.Tax3Rate = r.Tax3Rate
        from (select *
              from ['' + upper(rtrim(@LinkedServerName)) + ''].INISolutionsDataBase.dbo.OnlineOrderSalesSummaries
              where StoreID = '' + @store_id + '') s
          inner join rpt_online_order_sales_summary r on s.StoreID = r.StoreID
                                                     and s.OnlineOrderCompanyID = r.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                     and convert(varchar, s.[Date], 112) = convert(varchar, r.SaleDate, 112)
        where s.[Date] >= '''''' + convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -3, @today), 112) + ''''''
          and s.SubTotalAmt <> r.SubTotalAmt''

      exec sp_executesql @script

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spcrm_SyncPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail]
  @StoreID int, 
  @SyncNumberOfDays tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT staterments.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ID int

  declare @tmpSyncPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail table
  (
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    CardNum varchar(30),
    TransDateTime varchar(20),
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int
  )

  if exists (select *
             from sys.objects
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail]'')
               and [type] in (N''U''))
    drop table rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail

  create table rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail(
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    StoreID int,
    CardNum varchar(30),
    TransDateTime varchar(20),
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int
  )

  insert into @tmpSyncPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail (CardNum, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID)
  select Barcode, convert(varchar, ChargeDate, 120) as TransDateTime, Amount as Credit, null as Debit, null as Balance, SalesID
  from tblPrepaidCardChargeHistory
  where ChargeDate >= convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -@SyncNumberOfDays, getdate()), 112)
    --and isnull(SalesID, 0) > 0
  order by TransDateTime

  /* Didn''t use "union all" to make sure the charge records are inserted before use records for the case that the time is the same */
  insert into @tmpSyncPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail (CardNum, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID)
  select Barcode, convert(varchar, DateTimeUsed, 120) as TransDateTime, null as Credit, AmtUsed as Debit, Balance, SalesID
  from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
  where DateTimeUsed >= convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -@SyncNumberOfDays, getdate()), 112)
    --and isnull(SalesID, 0) > 0
  order by TransDateTime

  insert into rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail (StoreID, CardNum, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID)
  select @StoreID, CardNum, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID
  from @tmpSyncPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail
  order by TransDateTime, ID

  declare curs_detail cursor for
    select ID
    from rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail
    order by ID

    open curs_detail
    fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update t
      set t.Balance = isnull(t.Credit, 0) - isnull(t.Debit, 0)
                      + isnull((select t2.Balance
                                from rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail t2
                                where t2.CardNum = t.CardNum
                                  and exists (select 1
                                              from rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail t3
                                              where t3.CardNum = t2.CardNum
                                                and t3.ID < t.ID
                                              group by CardNum
                                              having max(t3.ID) = t2.ID)), 0)
      from rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail t
      where t.ID = @ID
      
      fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    end
    close curs_detail
  deallocate curs_detail

  --select *
  --from rpt_PrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail
  --order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetSpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice]
(
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
	@SpecialPricingRate smallint
)
RETURNS smallmoney
AS
BEGIN  

  declare @SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice smallmoney, @tempValue smallint

  if (@SpecialPricingRate <> 0) begin

    set @SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice = @UnitPrice + round(@UnitPrice * (@SpecialPricingRate / 100.0), 2)

    set @tempValue = round(@SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice * 100.0, 0)

    if ((@tempValue % 10) in (1,2,6,7)) 
      set @tempValue = @tempValue - ((@tempValue % 10) % 5)
    else if ((@tempValue % 10) in (3,4,8,9)) 
      set @tempValue = @tempValue + (5 - ((@tempValue % 10) % 5));

    set @SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice = round(@tempValue / 100.0, 2);

  end
  else

    set @SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice = @UnitPrice

  return isnull(@SpecialPricingAppliedUnitPrice, isnull(@UnitPrice, 0))

END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_AssignStationNumberToTable]
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationID smallint

  where StationID = @StationID

  update tblTable
  set StationID = @StationID
  where ID = @TableID  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateStationLockStatus]
  @TableID smallint,
  @StationID smallint,
  @Locked bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_station_lock

  if (@TableID > 0) begin
  
    update s
    set s.Locked = @Locked
    from tblTable t
      inner join tblStation s on t.StationID = s.ID
    where t.ID = @TableID

  end
  else begin

    update tblStation
    set Locked = case when exists (select *
                                   from tblTable
                                   where StationID = @StationID
                                     and OrderNum = 0) and (@TableID = -1) then Locked 
                      else @Locked 
                 end
    where ID = @StationID

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_station_lock
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_station_lock
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetLoyaltyStampCards]
  @CustomerID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select row_number() over (order by ID) as StampNo,
         ID, CustomerID, StampCount,
         replace(substring(convert(varchar, c.CreatedDateTime, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'') + ''  '' +
         substring(convert(varchar, c.CreatedDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, c.CreatedDateTime, 109), 25, 2) as CreatedDateTime,
         cast(case when exists (select 1
                                from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d
                                where d.LoyaltyStampCardID = c.ID
                                  and d.StampedStatus = 0) then 1 else 0 end as bit) as StampAvailable
  from tblLoyaltyStampCard c
  where c.CustomerID = @CustomerID
  order by c.CreatedDateTime desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetLoyaltyStampCardDetail]
  @LoyaltyStampCardID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select LoyaltyStampCardID, StampSequenceNo, StampedStatus,
         case when StampedStatus = 1 then ''X'' else '''' end as Stamped,
         case when StampedStatus = 1 then
                replace(substring(convert(varchar, StampedDateTime, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'') + ''  '' +
                substring(convert(varchar, StampedDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' + substring(convert(varchar, StampedDateTime, 109), 25, 2)
              else ''''
         end as StampedDateTime
  from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail
  where LoyaltyStampCardID = @LoyaltyStampCardID
  order by StampSequenceNo

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertLoyaltyStampCard]
  @CustomerID int,
  @StampCount smallint,
  @NewStampCardID int = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select 1
                 from tblLoyaltyStampCard c
                 where c.CustomerID = @CustomerID
                   and exists (select 1
                               from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d
                               where d.LoyaltyStampCardID = c.ID
                                 and d.StampedStatus = 0)) begin

    if (@StampCount > 0) begin

      declare @StampSequenceNo smallint

      begin transaction insert_stamp_card

      insert into tblLoyaltyStampCard (CustomerID, StampCount, CreatedDateTime)
      values (@CustomerID, @StampCount, getdate())

      set @NewStampCardID = scope_identity()
      set @StampSequenceNo = 1

      while (@StampCount > 0) begin

        insert into tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail (LoyaltyStampCardID, StampSequenceNo, StampedStatus, StampedDateTime)
        values (@NewStampCardID, @StampSequenceNo, 0, getdate())

        set @StampSequenceNo = @StampSequenceNo + 1
        set @StampCount = @StampCount - 1

      end

      if (@@error = 0) begin
        commit transaction insert_stamp_card
        return 1
      end
      else begin
        rollback transaction insert_stamp_card
        set @NewStampCardID = 0
        return 0
      end

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateLoyaltyStampCardStampedStatus]
  @LoyaltyStampCardID int,
  @DoStamp bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_stamped_status

  if (@DoStamp = 1) begin
    if exists (select 1
               from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail
               where LoyaltyStampCardID = @LoyaltyStampCardID
                 and StampedStatus = 0) begin

      update d
      set d.StampedStatus = 1,
          d.StampedDateTime = getdate()
      from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d
      where d.LoyaltyStampCardID = @LoyaltyStampCardID
        and d.StampSequenceNo = (select min(d2.StampSequenceNo)
                                 from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d2
                                 where d2.LoyaltyStampCardID = d.LoyaltyStampCardID
                                   and d2.StampedStatus = 0)

    end
  end
  else begin
    if exists (select 1
               from tblLoyaltyStampCard c
               where c.ID = @LoyaltyStampCardID
                 and c.StampCount > (select max(StampSequenceNo)
                                     from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d
                                     where d.LoyaltyStampCardID = c.ID
                                       and d.StampedStatus = 1)) begin

      update d
      set d.StampedStatus = 0
      from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d
      where d.LoyaltyStampCardID = @LoyaltyStampCardID
        and d.StampSequenceNo = (select max(d2.StampSequenceNo)
                                 from tblLoyaltyStampCardDetail d2
                                 where d2.LoyaltyStampCardID = d.LoyaltyStampCardID
                                   and d2.StampedStatus = 1)

    end
  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_stamped_status
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_stamped_status
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetAllOpenCardTransactions]
  @StationID smallint,
  @CashierID smallint = 0
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select p.ID, 
         p.SalesID, 
         p.PaymentTypeID, p.PaidAmount, p.TipAmount,
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' else ''****'' + dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber) end as CardNumber, 
         case when p.CardExpiryDate is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardExpiryDate) end as CardExpiryDate,
         isnull(p.AuthorizationNo, '''') as CardTransAuthNo, 
         case when charindex(''['', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, 1, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransPaymentID,
         case when charindex('']'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransOrderID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransReferenceID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, 32) else '''' end as CardTransExternalPaymentID,
         case p.Voided when 1 then ''Voided'' 
                       else case when isnull(p.ItemNo, '''') in (''A'', ''P'') then ''Open'' else '''' end 
         end as CardTransStatus,
         case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(p.ItemNo, ''''))) when ''S'' then ''Sale'' 
                                                   when ''A'' then ''Auth'' 
                                                   when ''P'' then ''PreAuth'' 
                                                   when ''R'' then ''Refund''
                                                   else '''' 
         end as CardTransType,
         isnull(p.TipAdjusted, 0) as TipAdjusted
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and case when @StationID = 0 then 1
             else case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and case when @CashierID = 0 then 1
             else case when s.CashierID = @CashierID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and p.BatchClosed = 0
    and p.CardNumber is not null
  order by CardTransReferenceID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO


EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetOpenCardTransCount]
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select count(*) as OpenCardTransCount
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and case when @StationID = 0 then 1
             else case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1 
    and p.BatchClosed = 0
    and p.Voided = 0
    and ((isnull(p.ItemNo, '''') = ''A'' and p.TipAdjusted = 0)
         or
         isnull(p.ItemNo, '''') = ''P'')
    and p.CardNumber is not null

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_UpdateBatchClosedStatus]
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @AutoCloseout bit

  select @AutoCloseout = case when upper(Value) = ''TRUE'' then 1 else 0 end
  from tblMisc
  where Code = ''ABCO''

  if (isnull(@AutoCloseout, 0) = 1) begin

    update p
    set p.BatchClosed = 1
    from tblPayment p
      inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
    where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
      /* @StationID would be always -1 if @AutoCloseout is True. So commented out the following clause */ 
      --and case when @StationID in (0, -1) then 1
      --         else case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
      --    end = 1 
      and p.BatchClosed = 0
      and p.CardNumber is not null
      and (p.ItemNo <> ''P'' or p.Voided = 1)
      and s.SaleDateTime < convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)

  end
  else begin

    update p
    set p.BatchClosed = 1
    from tblPayment p
      inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
    where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
      and case when @StationID = 0 then 1
               else case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
          end = 1 
      and p.BatchClosed = 0
      and p.CardNumber is not null
      and (p.ItemNo <> ''P'' or p.Voided = 1)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[ConvertUnixTimeStampToLocalDateTime]
(
  @UnixTimeStamp bigint
)
RETURNS datetime
AS
BEGIN
	                      
  if (@UnixTimeStamp > 2147483647) /* if @UnixTimeStamp is greater than 2147483647 (max number for int type), it means the number is in milliseconds */ 
    set @UnixTimeStamp = @UnixTimeStamp / 1000 /* dateadd function takes int type value not bigint type value so reduce it to seconds */

  declare @LocalTimeOffset bigint --, @AdjustedLocalDateTime bigint

  set @LocalTimeOffset = datediff(s, getdate(), getutcdate())
  --set @AdjustedLocalDateTime = (@UnixTimeStamp - @LocalTimeOffset)
  --return dateadd(s, @AdjustedLocalDateTime - 1262304000 /* difference in seconds between 1970-01-01 and 2010-01-01 */, cast(''20100101'' as datetime))
  return dateadd(s, @UnixTimeStamp - @LocalTimeOffset - 1262304000 /* difference in seconds between 1970-01-01 and 2010-01-01 */, cast(''20100101'' as datetime))
                                             
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[ExtractCloverTransactionDateTime]
(
  @ResponseString varchar(3000)
)
RETURNS varchar(25)
AS
BEGIN	

  if (isnull(@ResponseString, '''') <> '''') and (charindex(''"createdTime":'', @ResponseString) > 0) begin

    declare @UnixTimeStamp bigint, @TransactionDateTime datetime, @DateTimeString varchar(25)

    set @ResponseString = substring(@ResponseString, charindex(''"createdTime":'', @ResponseString) + 14, 15)
    
    if (charindex('','', @ResponseString) > 0)
      set @ResponseString = substring(@ResponseString, 1, charindex('','', @ResponseString) - 1)

    if (isnumeric(@ResponseString) = 1) begin
    
      set @UnixTimeStamp = convert(bigint, @ResponseString)

      set @TransactionDateTime = dbo.ConvertUnixTimeStampToLocalDateTime(@UnixTimeStamp)

      set @DateTimeString = replace(substring(convert(varchar, @TransactionDateTime, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'') + '' '' + 
                                    substring(convert(varchar, @TransactionDateTime, 109), 13, 8) + '' '' + 
                                    substring(convert(varchar, @TransactionDateTime, 109), 25, 2)

    end
    else

      set @DateTimeString = ''''

  end
  else

    set @DateTimeString = ''''

  return @DateTimeString

END'
GO
