EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetPreAuthorizedCardTrans]
  @QueryType tinyint,
  @TableID smallint,
  @SalesID int,
  @SearchString varchar(100),
  @PreAuthorizedCardTransID int
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select pa.ID, pa.TableID, pa.SalesID, pa.PaymentTypeID, 
         isnull(pt.PaymentType, '''') as PaymentType, 
         pa.PreAuthorizedAmount,
         case when pa.CardNumber is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(pa.CardNumber) end as CardNumber, 
         case when pa.CardExpiryDate is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(pa.CardExpiryDate) end as CardExpiryDate,
         isnull(pa.AuthorizationNo, '''') as AuthorizationNo,
         case when charindex(''['', isnull(pa.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(pa.SequenceNo, 1, charindex(''['', pa.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransPaymentID,
         case when charindex('']'', isnull(pa.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(pa.SequenceNo, charindex(''['', pa.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex('']'', pa.SequenceNo) - charindex(''['', pa.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransOrderID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(pa.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(pa.SequenceNo, charindex('']'', pa.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex(''|'', pa.SequenceNo) - charindex('']'', pa.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransReferenceID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(pa.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(pa.SequenceNo, charindex(''|'', pa.SequenceNo) + 1, 32) else '''' end as CardTransExternalPaymentID,
         isnull(pa.CardReceipt, '''') as CardReceipt,
         case pa.Voided when 1 then ''Voided'' else '''' end [Status],
         pa.StationName,
         pa.BatchClosed,
         dbo.ExtractCloverTransactionDateTime(pa.CardReceipt) as CardTransDateTime,
         dbo.DecryptString(pa.TrackData) as TrackData,
         pa.CardholderName
  from tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans pa 
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on pa.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
  where case @QueryType 
          when 1 then
            case when pa.TableID = @TableID and pa.SalesID = @SalesID then 1 else 0 end
          when 2 then
            case when upper(ltrim(rtrim(pa.CardholderName))) like ''%'' + upper(ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString))) + ''%'' then 1 else 0 end
          when 3 then
            case when reverse(substring(ltrim(rtrim(reverse(isnull(dbo.DecryptString(pa.CardNumber), '''')))), 1, 4)) = ltrim(rtrim(@SearchString)) then 1 else 0 end
          when 4 then
            case when pa.ID = @PreAuthorizedCardTransID then 1 else 0 end
          else 1
        end = 1
  order by pa.CardholderName, pa.ID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_InsertPreAuthorizedCardTrans]
  @TableID smallint,
  @SalesID int,
  @PaymentTypeID tinyint,
  @PreAuthorizedAmount smallmoney,
  @CardNumber varchar(20),
  @CardExpiryDate varchar(10),
  @AuthorizationNo varchar(20),
  @SequenceNo varchar(100),
  @CardReceipt nvarchar(4000),
  @StationName varchar(20),
  @TrackData varchar(100),
  @CardholderName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  insert into tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans (TableID, SalesID, PaymentTypeID, PreAuthorizedAmount, CardNumber, CardExpiryDate, 
                                         AuthorizationNo, SequenceNo, CardReceipt, StationName, TrackData, CardholderName)
  values (@TableID, @SalesID, @PaymentTypeID, @PreAuthorizedAmount, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardNumber, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@CardNumber) end, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardExpiryDate, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@CardExpiryDate) end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@AuthorizationNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @AuthorizationNo end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@SequenceNo, ''''))) when '''' then null else @SequenceNo end,
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@CardReceipt, ''''))) when '''' then null else @CardReceipt end,
          @StationName, 
          case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(@TrackData, ''''))) when '''' then null else dbo.EncryptString(@TrackData) end,
          @CardholderName)

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateItemProperties]  
  @PropertyUpdateType tinyint,
  @PropertyIndex tinyint,
  @ItemID smallint,

  @ApplyTax1 bit, 
  @ApplyTax2 bit, 
  @ApplyTax3 bit, 
  
  @OpenItem bit, 
  @Alcohol bit, 
  @NonAlcohol bit,
  @Taste bit, 
  @ScaleItem bit, 
  @HourlyChargedItem bit, 
  @GroupItem bit,
  @RewardItem bit,
  @OnlineItem bit,
  @ManageInv bit,

  @Kitchen1 bit, 
  @Kitchen2 bit, 
  @Kitchen3 bit, 
  @Kitchen4 bit,
  @Kitchen5 bit,
  @Kitchen6 bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_item_properties

  if (@PropertyUpdateType = 1) begin
  
    update tblItem
    set ApplyGST  = case when @PropertyIndex = 1 then @ApplyTax1 else ApplyGST  end, 
        ApplyPST  = case when @PropertyIndex = 2 then @ApplyTax2 else ApplyPST  end, 
        ApplyPST2 = case when @PropertyIndex = 3 then @ApplyTax3 else ApplyPST2 end
    where ID = @ItemID

  end
  else if (@PropertyUpdateType = 2) begin

    update tblItem
    set --OpenItem          = case when @PropertyIndex = 1  then @OpenItem          else OpenItem          end, 
        Alcohol           = case when @PropertyIndex = 2  then @Alcohol           
                                 else case when @PropertyIndex = 3 and @NonAlcohol = 1 then 0 else Alcohol end 
                            end, 
        NonAlcohol        = case when @PropertyIndex = 3  then @NonAlcohol        
                                 else case when @PropertyIndex = 2 and @Alcohol = 1 then 0 else NonAlcohol end    
                            end,
        --Taste             = case when @PropertyIndex = 4  then @Taste             else Taste             end, 
        ScaleItem         = case when @PropertyIndex = 5  then @ScaleItem         else ScaleItem         end, 
        HourlyChargedItem = case when @PropertyIndex = 6  then @HourlyChargedItem else HourlyChargedItem end, 
        --GroupItem         = case when @PropertyIndex = 7  then @GroupItem         else GroupItem         end,
        RewardItem        = case when @PropertyIndex = 8  then @RewardItem        else RewardItem        end, 
        OnlineItem        = case when @PropertyIndex = 9  then @OnlineItem        else OnlineItem        end, 
        ManageInv         = case when @PropertyIndex = 10 then @ManageInv         else ManageInv         end
    where ID = @ItemID

  end
  else if (@PropertyUpdateType = 3) begin

    update tblItem
    set KitchenB = case when @PropertyIndex = 1 then @Kitchen1 else KitchenB end, 
        KitchenF = case when @PropertyIndex = 2 then @Kitchen2 else KitchenF end,
        KitchenE = case when @PropertyIndex = 3 then @Kitchen3 else KitchenE end, 
        Bar      = case when @PropertyIndex = 4 then @Kitchen4 else Bar      end,
        Kitchen5 = case when @PropertyIndex = 5 then @Kitchen5 else Kitchen5 end,
        Kitchen6 = case when @PropertyIndex = 6 then @Kitchen6 else Kitchen6 end
    where ID = @ItemID

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_item_properties
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_item_properties
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetItemByItemName]
  @ItemName varchar(50),
  @SearchType tinyint,
  @ActiveOnly bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(1000)

  set @ItemName = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@ItemName)))

  select c.CatName, i.CategoryID, i.ID, i.IName, i.IName2
  from tblItem i
    inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
  where case when @ActiveOnly = 1 then
               case when i.[Status] = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @SearchType = 2 then
               case when (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) like @ItemName + ''%'') or
                         (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2))) like @ItemName + ''%'') then 1 else 0 end
             when @SearchType = 3 then
               case when (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) like ''%'' + @ItemName) or
                         (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2))) like ''%'' + @ItemName) then 1 else 0 end
             when @SearchType = 4 then
               case when (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) = @ItemName) or
                         (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2))) = @ItemName) then 1 else 0 end
             else
               case when (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName))) like ''%'' + @ItemName + ''%'') or
                         (upper(ltrim(rtrim(i.IName2))) like ''%'' + @ItemName + ''%'') then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
  order by c.CatName, i.IName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetBatchSummary]
  @StationID smallint,
  @IncludePreAuthTrans bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select sum(p.PaidAmount) as PaidAmount, sum(p.TipAmount) as TipAmount, 
         sum(p.PaidAmount + p.TipAmount) as TotalAmount, count(p.ID) as TransCount
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and case when @StationID = 0 then 1
             else case when s.StationID = @StationID then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1 
    and p.BatchClosed = 0
    and p.Voided = 0
    and p.CardNumber is not null
    and case when @IncludePreAuthTrans = 0 then 
               case when p.ItemNo <> ''P'' then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetCardPayment]
  @SalesID int,
  @AuthorizationNo varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN

  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  open symmetric key EncryptionKey decryption by certificate EncryptionCert with password = ''dkdldosdkdlthffntustmektzja-1n1$0lut10n$.c0m''

  select p.ID, p.SalesID, p.PaymentTypeID, p.PaidAmount, p.TipAmount,
         case when p.CardNumber is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardNumber) end as CardNumber, 
         case when p.CardExpiryDate is null then '''' else dbo.DecryptString(p.CardExpiryDate) end as CardExpiryDate,
         isnull(p.AuthorizationNo, '''') as AuthorizationNo, 
         --isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''') as SequenceNo,
         case when charindex(''['', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, 1, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransPaymentID,
         case when charindex('']'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex(''['', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransOrderID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) - charindex('']'', p.SequenceNo) - 1) else '''' end as CardTransReferenceID,
         case when charindex(''|'', isnull(p.SequenceNo, '''')) > 0 then substring(p.SequenceNo, charindex(''|'', p.SequenceNo) + 1, 32) else '''' end as CardTransExternalPaymentID,
         isnull(p.CardReceipt, '''') as CardReceipt,
         pt.PaymentType,
         case p.Voided when 1 then ''Voided'' else '''' end as [Status],
         --p.BatchNo, 
         case ltrim(rtrim(isnull(p.ItemNo, ''''))) when ''S'' then ''Sale'' 
                                                   when ''A'' then ''Auth'' 
                                                   when ''P'' then ''PreAuth'' 
                                                   when ''R'' then ''Refund''
                                                   else '''' 
         end as CardTransType, 
         --p.RevisionNo, 
         p.StationName, p.BatchClosed,   
         dbo.ExtractCloverTransactionDateTime(p.CardReceipt) as CardTransDateTime,     
         replace(substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 113), 1, 11), '' '', ''-'') + '' '' + 
           substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 109), 13, 8) + '' '' + 
           substring(convert(varchar, p.PaidDateTime, 109), 25, 2) as PaidDateTime,
         ltrim(rtrim(u.FName)) as CashierName
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
  where p.SalesID = @SalesID
    and case when @AuthorizationNo <> '''' then 
               case when p.AuthorizationNo = @AuthorizationNo then 1 else 0 end
             else
               1
        end = 1
  order by p.ID

  close symmetric key EncryptionKey

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertStoreCredit]
  @CustomerID int,
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @Qty smallint,
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @DiscountAmt smallmoney,
  @StoreCreditMemo text,
  @StoreCreditUserID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_store_credit

  declare @RefundSalesID int, @SubTotal smallmoney, @ExtDiscountAmt smallmoney, @Tax1Amt smallmoney, @Tax2Amt smallmoney, @Tax3Amt smallmoney, 
          @DailyOrderNumber int, @TakeOutOrder bit, @TableID smallint, @StationID smallint, @CustomerTypeID tinyint, @CustomerGroupID tinyint,
          @Tax1Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax2Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax3Rate decimal(5, 4), @StoreCreditAmount smallmoney --, @PaidDateTime datetime

  if (@ItemID = 0) and (@SizeID = 0) and (@Qty = 0) and (@UnitPrice = 0) and (@DiscountAmt = 0) begin /* Store credit for the entire transaction */

    select @SubTotal = SubTotal,
           @ExtDiscountAmt = DSCAmt,
           @Tax1Amt = GSTAmt,
           @Tax2Amt = PSTAmt,
           @Tax3Amt = PST2Amt,
           @Tax1Rate = GSTRate,
           @Tax2Rate = PSTRate,
           @Tax3Rate = PST2Rate,
           @TakeOutOrder = TakeOutOrder,
           @TableID = TableID,
           @StationID = StationID,
           @CustomerTypeID = CustomerTypeID,
           @CustomerGroupID = CustomerGroupID
    from tblSales
    where ID = @SalesID

  end
  else begin

    set @SubTotal = round(@Qty * @UnitPrice, 2) 
    set @ExtDiscountAmt = round(@Qty * @DiscountAmt, 2) /* @DiscountAmt is for the single quantity, so @Qty must be multiplied to get the total discount amount */

    select @Tax1Rate = GSTRate,
           @Tax2Rate = PSTRate,
           @Tax3Rate = PST2Rate,
           @TakeOutOrder = TakeOutOrder,
           @TableID = TableID,
           @StationID = StationID,
           @CustomerTypeID = CustomerTypeID,
           @CustomerGroupID = CustomerGroupID
    from tblSales
    where ID = @SalesID

    select @Tax1Amt = case when ApplyGST = 1 then round((@SubTotal - @ExtDiscountAmt) * @Tax1Rate, 2) else 0 end,
           @Tax2Amt = case when ApplyPST = 1 then round((@SubTotal - @ExtDiscountAmt) * @Tax2Rate, 2) else 0 end,
           @Tax3Amt = case when ApplyPST2 = 1 then round((@SubTotal - @ExtDiscountAmt) * @Tax3Rate, 2) else 0 end
    from tblItem
    where ID = @ItemID 

  end

  set @SubTotal = -1 * @SubTotal 
  set @ExtDiscountAmt = -1 * @ExtDiscountAmt
  set @Tax1Amt = -1 * @Tax1Amt
  set @Tax2Amt = -1 * @Tax2Amt
  set @Tax3Amt = -1 * @Tax3Amt

  set @StoreCreditAmount = @SubTotal - @ExtDiscountAmt + @Tax1Amt + @Tax2Amt + @Tax3Amt

  set @DailyOrderNumber = 0
  exec sp_GetDailyOrderNumber 0, 0, @DailyOrderNumber output

  exec sp_InsertSale @StoreCreditUserID, @SubTotal, @Tax1Amt, @Tax2Amt, @Tax3Amt, 0, @CustomerID, @DailyOrderNumber, 
                     @Tax1Rate, @Tax2Rate, @Tax3Rate, @TakeOutOrder, @TableID, @StationID, @CustomerTypeID, @CustomerGroupID,
                     @RefundSalesID output

  if (@ItemID = 0) and (@SizeID = 0) and (@Qty = 0) and (@UnitPrice = 0) and (@DiscountAmt = 0) begin /* Store credit for the entire transaction */

    insert into tblSalesDetail (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, PricePerWeightUnit, MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, 
                                DiscountAmt, DiscountPercent, Tastes)
    select @RefundSalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, PricePerWeightUnit, MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, 
           DiscountAmt, DiscountPercent, Tastes
    from tblSalesDetail
    where SalesID = @SalesID

  end
  else begin

    exec sp_InsertSalesDetail @RefundSalesID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @Qty, @UnitPrice, 0, 0, 0, @ExtDiscountAmt, 0, '''', '''', '''', ''''

  end  

  exec sp_UpdateSale @SubTotal, @ExtDiscountAmt, 0, @Tax1Amt, @Tax2Amt, @Tax3Amt, 1, @CustomerID, @TableID, @StationID, @RefundSalesID, 0
  
  --set @PaidDateTime = getdate()

  exec sp_InsertPayment @RefundSalesID, 6 /* Coupon */, @StoreCreditAmount, 0, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null /* @PaidDateTime - if null then getdate() will be used in the stored procedure "sp_InsertPayment" */

  insert into tblStoreCredit (CustomerID, StoreCreditSalesID, StoreCreditRefundSalesID, StoreCreditAmount, StoreCreditDate, StoreCreditMemo, 
                              StoreCreditUserID, StoreCreditUsed, StoreCreditUsedSalesID, StoreCreditUsedDate, StoreCreditUsedUserID, StoreCreditVoided)
  values (@CustomerID, @SalesID, @RefundSalesID, abs(@StoreCreditAmount), getdate(), @StoreCreditMemo, @StoreCreditUserID, 0, 0, null, 0, 0)  

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_store_credit
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction insert_store_credit
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_VoidStoreCredit]
  @StoreCreditID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction void_store_credit

  update s
  set s.TransType = 3
  from tblSales s 
    inner join tblStoreCredit sc on sc.StoreCreditRefundSalesID = s.ID
  where s.TransType = 0
    and sc.ID = @StoreCreditID

  update tblStoreCredit
  set StoreCreditVoided = 1
  where ID = @StoreCreditID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction void_store_credit
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction void_store_credit
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetStoreCreditTotal]
  @CustomerID int,
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ByTime bit,
  @EmployeeID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditVoided = 0 and (case when @EmployeeID > 0 then case when StoreCreditUserID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end else 1 end = 1) then 1 else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditCount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditVoided = 0 and (case when @EmployeeID > 0 then case when StoreCreditUserID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end else 1 end = 1) then StoreCreditAmount else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditAmount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 0 and StoreCreditVoided = 0 then 1 else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditAvailableCount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 0 and StoreCreditVoided = 0 then StoreCreditAmount else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditAvailableAmount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 1 and StoreCreditVoided = 0 and (case when @EmployeeID > 0 then case when StoreCreditUsedUserID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end else 1 end = 1) then 1 else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditUsedCount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 1 and StoreCreditVoided = 0 and (case when @EmployeeID > 0 then case when StoreCreditUsedUserID = @EmployeeID then 1 else 0 end else 1 end = 1) then StoreCreditAmount else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditUsedAmount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 0 and StoreCreditVoided = 1 then 1 else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditVoidedCount,
         isnull(sum(case when StoreCreditUsed = 0 and StoreCreditVoided = 1 then StoreCreditAmount else 0 end), 0) as StoreCreditVoidedAmount
  from tblStoreCredit 
  where case when @CustomerID > 1 then 
               case when CustomerID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @FromDateTime is not null then
               case when (StoreCreditDate >= case when @ByTime = 1 then @FromDateTime else convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112) end) and
                         (StoreCreditDate <  case when @ByTime = 1 then dateadd(s, 1, @ToDateTime) else dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112)) end) 
                      then 1 
                    else 0 
               end                      
             else 1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetStoreCreditDetail]
  @CustomerID int,
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime,
  @OnlyAvailableCredit bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select sc.*, 
         ltrim(rtrim(c.FName + '' '' + c.LName)) as CustomerName, 
         c.CustomerNum,
         ltrim(rtrim(u.FName + '' '' + u.LName)) as StoreCreditUserName, 
         ltrim(rtrim(isnull(u2.FName, '''') + '' '' + isnull(u2.LName, ''''))) as StoreCreditUsedUserName,
         case when sc.StoreCreditUsed = 1 then ''Used''
              when sc.StoreCreditVoided = 1 then ''Voided''
              else ''Available'' 
         end as StoreCreditStatus
  from tblStoreCredit sc
    inner join tblCustomer c on sc.CustomerID = c.ID
    inner join tblUser u on sc.StoreCreditUserID = u.ID
    left join tblUser u2 on sc.StoreCreditUsedUserID = u2.ID
  where case when @CustomerID > 1 then 
               case when sc.CustomerID = @CustomerID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @FromDateTime is not null then
               case when (sc.StoreCreditDate >= convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112)) and
                         (sc.StoreCreditDate <  dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112))) then 1 else 0 end                    
             else 1
        end = 1
    and case when @OnlyAvailableCredit = 1 then
               case when sc.StoreCreditUsed = 0 and sc.StoreCreditVoided = 0 then 1 else 0 end 
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by sc.ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_ApplyStoreCreditToPayment] 
  @StoreCreditID int,
  @SalesID int,
  @StoreCreditAmount smallmoney,
  @UserID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON

  if exists (select *
             from tblStoreCredit
             where ID = @StoreCreditID
               and StoreCreditUsed = 0
               and StoreCreditVoided = 0) begin

    declare @PaidDateTime datetime 

    set @PaidDateTime = getdate()

    --exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, 6 /* Use "Coupon" method as a store credit payment */, @StoreCreditAmount, 0, 
    --                      null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @PaidDateTime

    update tblStoreCredit
    set StoreCreditUsed = 1,
        StoreCreditUsedSalesID = @SalesID,
        StoreCreditUsedDate = @PaidDateTime,
        StoreCreditUsedUserID = @UserID
    where ID = @StoreCreditID

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetPayoutTransactions]
  @FromDateTime smalldatetime,
  @ToDateTime smalldatetime,
  @OrderBy varchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(500)

  if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderBy)) = '''') set @OrderBy = ''ID desc''

  select p.ID, 
         p.PayDate, 
         p.AccountID, 
         round(p.SubTotalAmt, 2) as SubTotalAmt, 
         round(p.GSTAmt, 2) as GSTAmt, 
         round(p.PSTAmt, 2) as PSTAmt,
         round(p.SubTotalAmt + p.GSTAmt + p.PSTAmt, 2) as Total, 
         (u.FName + '' '' + u.LName) as UserName, 
         p.ChequeNo,
         case PayType when ''C'' then ''Cash'' 
                      when ''Q'' then ''Cheque'' 
                      when ''D'' then ''Debit'' 
         end as PayType,
         a1.AccountName as Accounts, 
         a2.AccountName as AccType, 
         p.BankID, 
         case p.BankID when 0 then '''' 
                       else b.BankName 
         end as BankName,
         p.Memo
  into #tmp_payout_transactions
  from tblPayout p
    inner join tblAccount a1 on p.AccountID = a1.ID
    inner join tblAccount a2 on a1.PID = a2.ID
    inner join tblUser u on p.UserID = u.ID
    left join tblBank b on p.BankID = b.ID
  where p.PayDate >= @FromDateTime
    and p.PayDate <  dateadd(d, 1, @ToDateTime)

  set @script = ''select * from #tmp_payout_transactions order by '' + @OrderBy
  exec sp_executesql @script

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetTare]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *, case DefaultTare when 1 then ''Y'' else '''' end as IsDefaultTare
  from tblTare
  order by TareDescription

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertTare]
  @TareDescription varchar(50),
  @TareWeight float,
  @DefaultTare bit,
  @NewTareID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_tare

  if @DefaultTare = 1 begin
    
    update tblTare
    set DefaultTare = 0

  end 

  insert into tblTare (TareDescription, TareWeight, DefaultTare)
  values (@TareDescription, @TareWeight, @DefaultTare)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_tare
    set @NewTareID = isnull(scope_identity(), 0)
    return 1
  end
  else begin  
    rollback transaction insert_tare
    set @NewTareID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateTare]
  @TareDescription varchar(50),
  @TareWeight float,
  @DefaultTare bit,
  @TareID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_tare

  if @DefaultTare = 1 begin
    
    update tblTare
    set DefaultTare = 0

  end

  update tblTare
  set TareDescription = @TareDescription,
      TareWeight = @TareWeight,
      DefaultTare = @DefaultTare
  where ID = @TareID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_tare
    return 1
  end
  else begin  
    rollback transaction update_tare
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteTare]
  @TareID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction delete_tare

  delete 
  from tblTare
  where ID = @TareID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction delete_tare
    return 1
  end
  else begin  
    rollback transaction delete_tare
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MoveTableForSelfOrder]
  @SelfOrderTableID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ToTableID int, @ToTableName varchar(20)

  select @ToTableID = t1.ID,
         @ToTableName = t1.TableName
  from tblTable t1
    inner join (select Min(ID) as ID
                from tblTable 
                where ID >= 151
                  and ID <= 200
                  and Linked = 1
                  and OrderNum = 0) t2 on t2.ID = t1.ID
    
  update t1
  set t1.OrderNum = t2.OrderNum,
      t1.TimeIn = t2.TimeIn,
      t1.ServerID = t2.ServerID,
      t1.NumOfGuests = t2.NumOfGuests,
      t1.Opened = 0,
      t1.PickupTime = t2.PickupTime,
      t1.PhoneNum = t2.PhoneNum,
      t1.PickupPerson = t2.PickupPerson,
      t1.BillPrinted = t2.BillPrinted,
      t1.Attention = t2.Attention,
      t1.DailyOrdNum = t2.DailyOrdNum,
      t1.TotalAmt = t2.TotalAmt,
      t1.OnlineOrderNumber = t2.OnlineOrderNumber
  from tblTable t1
    inner join (select *
                from tblTable
                where ID = @SelfOrderTableID) t2 on 1 = 1
  where t1.ID = @ToTableID

  update t
  set t.OrderNum = 0,
      t.ServerID = 0,
      t.NumOfGuests = 0,
      t.Opened = 0,
      t.PickupTime = '''',
      t.PhoneNum = '''',
      t.PickupPerson = '''',
      t.BillPrinted = 0,
      t.Attention = 0,
      t.DailyOrdNum = 0,
      t.TotalAmt = 0,
      t.OnlineOrderNumber = ''''
  from tblTable t
  where t.ID = @SelfOrderTableID

  select @ToTableName as ToTableName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
