  update tblSales
  set CashierID = @CashierID
  where ID = @SalesID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSalesTransactionsForCashTip]
  @SaleDate smalldatetime
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @MaxShiftIndex tinyint, @FromDateTime datetime, @ToDateTime datetime, @TotalCashTipAmount smallmoney

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@SaleDate, 0)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@SaleDate, 0)

  select s.ID, 
         s.SaleDateTime,
         substring(convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' +
         substring(convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 109), 25, 2) as SaleTime, 
         round(s.SubTotal-s.DSCAmt+s.GSTAmt+s.PSTAmt+s.PST2Amt, 2) as TotalAmt,       
         s.DailyOrderNumber,
         isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName
  into #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip
  from tblSales s 
    left join tblTable t on s.TableID = t.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
    and s.SubTotal > 0

  select @MaxShiftIndex = max(isnull(ct.ShiftIndex, 0))
  from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t
    left join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = t.ID
  where t.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and t.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime

  if (@ToDateTime <= dbo.GetFromDateTime(getdate(), 0)) begin

    update ct
    set ct.ShiftIndex = @MaxShiftIndex + 1
    from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t
      inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = t.ID
    where t.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and t.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and ct.ShiftIndex = 0

    delete t
    from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t
    where t.SaleDateTime < dbo.GetFromDateTime(getdate(), 0)
      and not exists (select *
                      from tblCashTip ct2
                      where ct2.SalesID = t.ID)

  end
  else begin

    if (@MaxShiftIndex > 0) begin

      delete t
      from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t
      where t.SaleDateTime < (select max(t2.SaleDateTime)
                              from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t2
                                inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = t2.ID
                              where ct.ShiftIndex = @MaxShiftIndex)
        and not exists (select *
                        from tblCashTip ct2
                        where ct2.SalesID = t.ID)

    end

  end

  select s.ID, 
         sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount, 
         sum(case when p.PaymentTypeID = 1 then round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2) else 0 end) as PaidCashTipAmount,
         sum(case when p.PaymentTypeID > 1 then round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2) else 0 end) as PaidNonCashTipAmount
  into #tmp_payment_for_cash_tip
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and s.TransType = 1
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by s.ID

  select t.*, p.PaidAmount, p.PaidNonCashTipAmount,
         /*p.PaidCashTipAmount +*/ isnull(ct.CashTipAmount, 0) as CashTipAmount,
         isnull(ct.ShiftIndex, 0) as ShiftIndex, 
         cast(0 as smallmoney) as TotalCashTipByShift
  into #tmp_trans_list_for_cash_tip
  from #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip t
    inner join #tmp_payment_for_cash_tip p on p.ID = t.ID
    left join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = t.ID
  order by t.SaleDateTime desc  

  update tl
  set tl.TotalCashTipByShift = t2.TotalCashTipByShift
  from #tmp_trans_list_for_cash_tip tl
    inner join (select ct.ShiftIndex, sum(/*p.PaidCashTipAmount +*/ ct.CashTipAmount) as TotalCashTipByShift
                from #tmp_payment_for_cash_tip p
                  inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = p.ID
                group by ct.ShiftIndex) t2 on t2.ShiftIndex = tl.ShiftIndex  

  select *
  from #tmp_trans_list_for_cash_tip
  order by SaleDateTime desc

  drop table #tmp_trans_for_cash_tip
  drop table #tmp_payment_for_cash_tip
  drop table #tmp_trans_list_for_cash_tip

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_RecordCashTip]
  @SalesID int,
  @CashTipAmount smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --exec sp_UpdateTipAmount @SalesID, @CashTipAmount, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblCashTip
                 where SalesID = @SalesID) begin

    insert into tblCashTip (SalesID, CashTipAmount)
    values (@SalesID, @CashTipAmount)
 
  end
  else begin

    update tblCashTip
    set CashTipAmount = @CashTipAmount
    where SalesID = @SalesID

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_SplitCashTipByShift]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @MaxShiftIndex tinyint

  select @MaxShiftIndex = max(ct.ShiftIndex)
  from tblSales s 
    inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= dbo.GetFromDateTime(getdate(), 0)
    and s.SaleDateTime <  dbo.GetToDateTime(getdate(), 0)

  update ct
  set ct.ShiftIndex = @MaxShiftIndex + 1
  from tblSales s 
    inner join tblCashTip ct on ct.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= dbo.GetFromDateTime(getdate(), 0)
    and s.SaleDateTime <  dbo.GetToDateTime(getdate(), 0)
    and ct.ShiftIndex = 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spws_ProcessOnlineOrder]
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint,
  @OrderID int, 
  @StationName varchar(20),
  @OrderProcessMsg varchar(100) = '''' output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try  
    begin transaction process_online_order

    if exists (select *
               from tblOnlineOrders o
                 inner join tblOnlineOrderDetail od on od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = o.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                   and od.OrderID = o.OrderID
               where o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                 and o.OrderID = @OrderID
                 and o.[Status] = 1
                 and od.ItemType = 1
                 --and od.ItemPrice <> 0
               /*order by od.ItemIndex*/) begin

      declare @OrderEntered tinyint, @OrderType varchar(100), @BlankTableID smallint, @AltOrderID varchar(20), @TableID int, @SalesID int, 
              @AdditionalOrder bit, @PaymentType varchar(100), @PaymentTypeID tinyint, @TotalAmtPaid smallmoney, @TipAmt smallmoney, 
              @TipInserted bit, @PaymentStatus varchar(100), @OrderPaid bit, @IsTakeOutOrder bit

      set @OrderEntered = 0
      set @AdditionalOrder = 0

      /* Get Order Type */
      select @OrderType = upper(OrderType),
             @AltOrderID = AltOrderID,
             --@SalesID = SalesID,
             @TableID = TableID
      from tblOnlineOrders
      where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
        and OrderID = @OrderID

      if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''TAKEOUT'') or (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DELIVERY'')
        set @IsTakeOutOrder = 1
      else
        set @IsTakeOutOrder = 0

      if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') or (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''PAYMENT'') begin /* DINEIN or PAYMENT */

        select @BlankTableID = ID,
               @SalesID = OrderNum
        from tblTable
        where ID = @TableID
          and Opened = 0

        if (isnull(@BlankTableID, 0) > 0) begin
          
          update tblTable
          set Opened = 1
          where ID = @BlankTableID    

        end                  

        if (isnull(@BlankTableID, 0) > 0) and (isnull(@SalesID, 0) > 0) begin

          if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') begin /* DINEIN */

            if not exists (select *
                           from tblOrderPrintCue
                           where SalesID = @SalesID
                             and PrintedStatus in (0, 1)) begin

              set @AdditionalOrder = 1

              insert into tblPendingOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, SizeName, 
                                            ApplyGST, ApplyPST, DSCAmt, KitchenB, KitchenF, PersonIndex, SeparateBillPrint, 
                                            Bar, ApplyNoDSC, OpenItem, ItemName2, ExtraChargeItem, ApplyPST2, KitchenE,  
                                            DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, DayHourDiscountRate, PricePerWeightUnit, 
                                            MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, DiscountPercent, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
              select @SalesID, a.ItemID, a.SizeID, od.ItemQty, 
                     case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                          else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                     end as UnitPrice,
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then
                            dbo.GetModifiersForOnlineOrder(od.OrderID, od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType)
                          when (od.ItemType = 0 and od.ItemPrice <> 0) then
                            od.ItemName
                          else
                            ''''                      
                     end as ItemModifiers, 
                     '''' as SideDishes, 
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then i.IName 
                          else case when s.ID > 1 then s.SizeName else ltrim(rtrim(od.ItemSizeName)) end -- + ''_$'' + convert(varchar, od.ItemPrice)
                     end as ItemName,
                     s.SizeName, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, 
                     case when o.DiscountPercent > 0 then
                            round(case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then 0 --isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                                       else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                                  end * od.ItemQty * (o.DiscountPercent / 100.0), 3)
                          else 0
                     end as DSCAmt,
                     i.KitchenB, i.KitchenF, 0, 0, i.Bar, isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0), i.OpenItem, i.IName2, 
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then 0 else 1 end as ExtraChargeItem,
                     i.ApplyPST2, i.KitchenE, 0, 0, 0, 
                     case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then 0
                          else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountRate(a.ItemID, a.SizeID)
                     end as DayHourDiscountRate, 
                     0, round(0, 0), 0, round(o.DiscountPercent / 100.0, 3) /*round(0, 3)*/, i.Kitchen5, i.Kitchen6 
              from tblOnlineOrders o
                inner join tblOnlineOrderDetail od on od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = o.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                  and od.OrderID = o.OrderID
                inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = od.ItemID
                                             and a.SizeID = od.ItemSizeID
                inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
                inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
              where od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                and od.OrderID = @OrderID
                --and od.ItemPrice <> 0
              order by od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType desc      

              insert into tblPendingOrdersTemp (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, SizeName, 
                                                ApplyGST, ApplyPST, DSCAmt, KitchenB, KitchenF, PersonIndex, SeparateBillPrint, 
                                                Bar, ApplyNoDSC, OpenItem, ItemName2, ExtraChargeItem, ApplyPST2, KitchenE,  
                                                DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, DayHourDiscountRate, PricePerWeightUnit, 
                                                MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, DiscountPercent, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
              select @SalesID, a.ItemID, a.SizeID, od.ItemQty, 
                     case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                          else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                     end as UnitPrice,
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then
                            dbo.GetModifiersForOnlineOrder(od.OrderID, od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType)
                          when (od.ItemType = 0 and od.ItemPrice <> 0) then
                            od.ItemName
                          else
                            ''''                      
                     end as ItemModifiers, 
                     '''' as SideDishes, 
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then i.IName 
                          else case when s.ID > 1 then s.SizeName else ltrim(rtrim(od.ItemSizeName)) end -- + ''_$'' + convert(varchar, od.ItemPrice)
                     end as ItemName,
                     s.SizeName, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, 
                     case when o.DiscountPercent > 0 then
                            round(case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then 0 --isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                                       else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                                  end * od.ItemQty * (o.DiscountPercent / 100.0), 3)
                          else 0
                     end as DSCAmt,
                     i.KitchenB, i.KitchenF, 0, 0, i.Bar, isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0), i.OpenItem, i.IName2, 
                     case when od.ItemType = 1 then 0 else 1 end as ExtraChargeItem,
                     i.ApplyPST2, i.KitchenE, 0, 0, 0, 
                     case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) then 0
                          else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountRate(a.ItemID, a.SizeID)
                     end as DayHourDiscountRate, 
                     0, round(0, 0), 0, round(o.DiscountPercent / 100.0, 3) /*round(0, 3)*/, i.Kitchen5, i.Kitchen6 
              from tblOnlineOrders o
                inner join tblOnlineOrderDetail od on od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = o.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                  and od.OrderID = o.OrderID
                inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = od.ItemID
                                             and a.SizeID = od.ItemSizeID
                inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
                inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
              where od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                and od.OrderID = @OrderID
                --and od.ItemPrice <> 0
              order by od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType desc 

              /* Insert additional payment if every order is prepaid */
              select @TotalAmtPaid = o.Total, 
                     @TipAmt = o.Tip, 
                     @PaymentType = upper(ltrim(rtrim(o.PaymentType))),
                     @PaymentStatus = upper(o.PaymentStatus)
              from tblOnlineOrders o
              where o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID 
                and o.OrderID = @OrderID

              if (@PaymentStatus = ''PAID'') set @OrderPaid = 1 else set @OrderPaid = 0
          
              if (@OrderPaid = 1) begin

                set @PaymentTypeID = case when @PaymentType = ''VISA''     then 3
                                          when @PaymentType = ''MC''       then 4
                                          when @PaymentType = ''AMEX''     then 5
                                          when @PaymentType = ''DISCOVER'' then 7
                                          when @PaymentType = ''JCB''      then 8
                                          else 3 /* ''VISA'' */
                                      end
                exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, @PaymentTypeID, @TotalAmtPaid, @TipAmt, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @StationName, null, null
                if (@TipAmt > 0)
                  exec sp_UpdateIncludedTipForAdditionalOnlineOrder @SalesID, 0, @TipAmt

              end
              else begin
                update tblSalesOfOnlineOrders
                set ReservedTipAmt = ReservedTipAmt + @TipAmt
                where SalesID = @SalesID
                  and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
              end
            
              set @OrderEntered = 1 

            end
            else begin

              set @OrderEntered = 2 /* set to 2 so that no order entry and no printing schedule happen */

            end

          end
          else if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''PAYMENT'') begin /* PAYMENT */

            select @TotalAmtPaid = o.Total, 
                   @TipAmt = o.Tip, 
                   @PaymentType = upper(ltrim(rtrim(o.PaymentType))),
                   @PaymentStatus = upper(o.PaymentStatus)
            from tblOnlineOrders o
            where o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID 
              and o.OrderID = @OrderID

            if (@PaymentStatus = ''PAID'') set @OrderPaid = 1 else set @OrderPaid = 0
          
            if (@OrderPaid = 1) begin

              set @PaymentTypeID = case when @PaymentType = ''VISA''     then 3
                                        when @PaymentType = ''MC''       then 4
                                        when @PaymentType = ''AMEX''     then 5
                                        when @PaymentType = ''DISCOVER'' then 7
                                        when @PaymentType = ''JCB''      then 8
                                        else 3 /* ''VISA'' */
                                    end
              exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, @PaymentTypeID, @TotalAmtPaid, @TipAmt, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @StationName, null, null
              if (@TipAmt > 0)
                --exec sp_InsertIncludedTip @SalesID, 0, @TipAmt, @TipInserted output
                exec sp_UpdateIncludedTipForAdditionalOnlineOrder @SalesID, 0, @TipAmt

              /* update status */
              update tblOnlineOrders 
              set [Status] = 0
              where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                and OrderID = @OrderID
            
              set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Payment successfully applied!''

            end
            else
              set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Payment NOT applied!''

            set @OrderEntered = 2 /* set to 2 so that no order entry and no printing schedule happen */

          end

        end

      end
      else begin /* TAKEOUT (PICKUP) or DELIVERY */

        /* Get blank table ID */
        select top 1 @BlankTableID = t.ID
        from tblTable t
          --inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
        where t.Linked = 1
          and t.TakeOut = 1
          and t.OrderNum = 0
          and t.Opened = 0
          and t.Attention = 0 /* used this additional condition to prevent reserving the same BlankTableID by multiple simultaneous calls to this stored procedure */
          and case when isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''TAKEOUT'' then
                     case when t.[Online] = 1 then 1 else 0 end
                   else
                     case when t.Delivery = 1 then 1 else 0 end
              end = 1
          and t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          --and upper(ltrim(rtrim(c.CompanyName))) = upper(''ePOS'')
        order by t.ID

        /* Update reserved table so that other calls cannot reserve the same table */
        /* Attention value will be back to 0 below - just earn some time to reserve the table */
        update tblTable
        set Opened = 1,
            Attention = 1
        where ID = @BlankTableID

      end

      if (@OrderEntered = 0) begin

        if (isnull(@BlankTableID, 0) > 0) begin
       
          declare @CashierID smallint, @GSTRate decimal(5, 4), @PSTRate decimal(5, 4), @PST2Rate decimal(5, 4), @CustomerID int, 
                  @DailyOrderNumber int, @FName varchar(30), @LName varchar(30), @Phone varchar(20), @Today varchar(20), 
                  @CustomerNote varchar(255), @Address varchar(200), @PickUpDateTime smalldatetime, @PrintDateTime varchar(20), 
                  @DeliveryCharge smallmoney, @CustomerName varchar(20), @OnlineOrderNumber varchar(20), @DoNotApplyHappyHourOnTakeOutAndDelivery bit

          /* Get Cashier ID */
          select top 1 @CashierID = ID
          from tblUser
          where upper(LName) like ''WEBORDER%''
          order by ID

          if (isnull(@CashierID, 0) = 0) begin
            exec sp_InsertUser ''OnlineOrder9999'', ''WebOrder'', ''_'', 3, 1, '''', 0, '''', 0, 0, 0, @CashierID output
          end

          select @GSTRate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''GST''))
          select @PSTRate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''PST''))
          select @PST2Rate = convert(decimal(5, 4), dbo.GetMiscValue(''PST2''))
          select @DoNotApplyHappyHourOnTakeOutAndDelivery = cast(case when upper(dbo.GetMiscValue(''NWHDT'')) = ''TRUE'' then 1 else 0 end as bit)
          select @Today = dbo.GetCurrentDateTime(7, 4, 1, 1)

          set @CustomerName = ''''
          set @OnlineOrderNumber = ''''

          select @CustomerID = isnull(c.ID, 0),
                 @FName = substring(o.FirstName, 1, 30),
                 @LName = substring(o.LastName, 1, 30),
                 @CustomerName = ltrim(rtrim(substring(ltrim(rtrim(o.FirstName)) + '' '' + ltrim(rtrim(o.LastName)), 1, 20))),
                 @OnlineOrderNumber = isnull(@AltOrderID, ''''),
                 @Phone = substring(o.PhoneNum, 1, 20),
                 @CustomerNote = substring(ltrim(rtrim(
                                           --''OnlineOrder# '' + convert(varchar, @OrderID) + char(13) + char(10) +
                                           --o.EmailAddress + char(13) + char(10) +
                                           ltrim(rtrim(o.UserComments)) + case when ltrim(rtrim(o.UserComments)) <> '''' then char(13) + char(10) else '''' end
                                           --o.DeliveryComments
                                           )), 1, 255),
                 @Address = substring(ltrim(rtrim(
                                      o.DeliveryLine1 + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryLine2 + char(13) + char(10) +
                                      o.DeliveryCity + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryState + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryZipCode)), 1, 200),
                 @TotalAmtPaid = o.Total, 
                 @DeliveryCharge = isnull(o.DeliveryCharge, 0),
                 @TipAmt = o.Tip, 
                 @PaymentType = upper(ltrim(rtrim(o.PaymentType))),
                 @PaymentStatus = upper(o.PaymentStatus),
                 @PickUpDateTime = o.RequestedDateTime
          from tblOnlineOrders o
            left join tblCustomer c on o.PhoneNum = c.CustomerNum --(o.PhoneNum = c.CustomerNum or o.PhoneNum = c.Phone) /* Should look at only "CustomerNum"? */
          where o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID 
            and o.OrderID = @OrderID

          if (@CustomerID = 0) /* Insert New Customer Info */

            if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') 
              set @CustomerID = 1 /* Assign 1 instead of creating a new customer with a blank customer number */
            else
              exec sp_InsertCustomer @FName, @LName, @Phone, @Today, 1, @Phone, @Address, 0, 0, @Today, 0, @CustomerNote, @CustomerID output

          else/* Update Customer Info */

            exec sp_UpdateCustomer @FName, @LName, ''-1'', 1, @Phone, @Address, -1, -1, @Today, -1, @CustomerNote, @Phone, 0, 0

          set @CustomerID = case when isnull(@CustomerID, 0) = 0 then 1 else @CustomerID end

          /* Get Order No. */
          exec sp_GetDailyOrderNumber 0, 0, @DailyOrderNumber output

          exec sp_InsertSale @CashierID,
                             0, /* SubTotal */
                             0, /* GSTAmt */
                             0, /* PSTAmt */
                             0, /* PST2Amt*/
                             1, /* TransType */
                             @CustomerID, 
                             @DailyOrderNumber,  
                             @GSTRate, 
                             @PSTRate,
                             @PST2Rate, 
                             @IsTakeOutOrder,
                             @BlankTableID, 
                             1, /* StationID */
                             1, /* CustomerTypeID */
                             1,  /* CustomerGroupID */
                             @SalesID output

          if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') 
            /* Normally, this was done in "sp_InsertSale". but Dine-In tables are not linked to an online order company. So, this is done separately here */
            exec sp_InsertSalesOfOnlineOrders @SalesID, @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OnlineOrderNumber, @CustomerName, 1

          --update tblOnlineOrders
          --set SalesID = @SalesID
          --where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          --  and OrderID = @OrderID
          --  and SalesID = 0

          if (@PaymentStatus = ''PAID'') set @OrderPaid = 1 else set @OrderPaid = 0

          set @TipAmt = @TipAmt + @DeliveryCharge
          --set @TotalAmtPaid = @TotalAmtPaid - @TipAmt

          if (@OrderPaid = 1) begin
            set @PaymentTypeID = case when @PaymentType = ''VISA''     then 3
                                      when @PaymentType = ''MC''       then 4
                                      when @PaymentType = ''AMEX''     then 5
                                      when @PaymentType = ''DISCOVER'' then 7
                                      when @PaymentType = ''JCB''      then 8
                                      else 3 /* ''VISA'' */
                                 end
            exec sp_InsertPayment @SalesID, @PaymentTypeID, @TotalAmtPaid, @TipAmt, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, @StationName, null, null
            if (@TipAmt > 0)
              exec sp_InsertIncludedTip @SalesID, 0, @TipAmt, @TipInserted output

            if ((isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DELIVERY'') and (@DeliveryCharge > 0)) begin 
              /* record delivery charge to print on bill as a separate description */
              update tblSalesOfOnlineOrders
              set DeliveryChargeAmt = @DeliveryCharge
              where SalesID = @SalesID
                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
            end
          end
          else begin
            /* the tip for pickup order will not be included in total since the tip amount could be changed at the time of payment on pickup. 
               So, instead, record the intended tip payment amount separately to print on bill */
            update tblSalesOfOnlineOrders
            set ReservedTipAmt = ReservedTipAmt + (@TipAmt - @DeliveryCharge),
                DeliveryChargeAmt = @DeliveryCharge /* record delivery charge to print on bill as a separate description */
            where SalesID = @SalesID
              and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID

            if ((isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DELIVERY'') and (@DeliveryCharge > 0)) 
              exec sp_InsertIncludedTip @SalesID, 0, @DeliveryCharge, @TipInserted output /* delivery charge is considered as paid tip */
          end

          update tblTable
          set OrderNum = @SalesID,
              TimeIn = getdate(),
              ServerID = @CashierID,
              NumOfGuests = 1,
              DailyOrdNum = @DailyOrderNumber,
              --BillPrinted = @OrderPaid, /* Disabled since a special color for the paid table has been added. Instead of using bill printed color */
              Attention = 0,
              PhoneNum = ltrim(rtrim(substring(@Phone, 1, 10))),
              PickupPerson = case when (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') then '''' else @CustomerName end,
                             --case when (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') then TableName + '' ('' + @CustomerName + '')''
                             --                                                  else @CustomerName
                             --end,
              PickupDate = convert(varchar(8), @PickUpDateTime, 112), /* "yyyymmdd" converted automatically back to smalldatetime */
              PickupTime = substring(convert(varchar, @PickUpDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' + 
                           substring(convert(varchar, @PickUpDateTime, 109), 25, 2),
              TotalAmt = @TotalAmtPaid,
              OnlineOrderNumber = @OnlineOrderNumber
          where ID = @BlankTableID       
        
          exec sp_UpdateSalesOfOnlineOrders @SalesID, @OnlineOrderNumber, @CustomerName

          insert into tblPendingOrders (SalesID, ItemID, SizeID, Qty, UnitPrice, Tastes, SideDishes, ItemName, SizeName, 
                                        ApplyGST, ApplyPST, DSCAmt, KitchenB, KitchenF, PersonIndex, SeparateBillPrint, 
                                        Bar, ApplyNoDSC, OpenItem, ItemName2, ExtraChargeItem, ApplyPST2, KitchenE,  
                                        DSCAmtEmployee, DSCAmtType1, DSCAmtType2, DayHourDiscountRate, PricePerWeightUnit, 
                                        MeasuredWeight, DecimalPlaces, DiscountPercent, Kitchen5, Kitchen6)
          select @SalesID, a.ItemID, a.SizeID, od.ItemQty, 
                 case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                      else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                 end as UnitPrice,
                 case when od.ItemType = 1 then
                        dbo.GetModifiersForOnlineOrder(od.OrderID, od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType)
                      when (od.ItemType = 0 and od.ItemPrice <> 0) then
                        od.ItemName
                      else
                        ''''                      
                 end as ItemModifiers, 
                 '''' as SideDishes, 
                 case when od.ItemType = 1 then i.IName 
                      --else ltrim(rtrim(od.ItemSizeName)) -- + ''''_$'''' + convert(varchar, od.ItemPrice)
                      else case when s.ID > 1 then s.SizeName else ltrim(rtrim(od.ItemSizeName)) end -- + ''_$'' + convert(varchar, od.ItemPrice)
                 end as ItemName,
                 s.SizeName, i.ApplyGST, i.ApplyPST, 
                 case when o.DiscountPercent > 0 then
                        round(case when isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1 then 0 --isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0)
                                   else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountPrice(a.ItemID, a.SizeID, convert(smallmoney, isnull(od.ItemPrice, 0))) 
                              end * od.ItemQty * (o.DiscountPercent / 100.0), 3)
                      else 0
                 end as DSCAmt,
                 i.KitchenB, i.KitchenF, 0, 0, i.Bar, isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0), i.OpenItem, i.IName2, 
                 case when od.ItemType = 1 then 0 else 1 end as ExtraChargeItem,
                 i.ApplyPST2, i.KitchenE, 0, 0, 0, 
                 case when (isnull(a.ApplyNoDSC, 0) = 1) or ((@DoNotApplyHappyHourOnTakeOutAndDelivery = 1) and (@IsTakeOutOrder = 1)) then 0
                      else dbo.GetDayHourDiscountRate(a.ItemID, a.SizeID)
                 end as DayHourDiscountRate, 
                 0, round(0, 0), 0, round(o.DiscountPercent / 100.0, 3) /*round(0, 3)*/, i.Kitchen5, i.Kitchen6 
          from tblOnlineOrders o
            inner join tblOnlineOrderDetail od on od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = o.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                              and od.OrderID = o.OrderID
            inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = od.ItemID
                                         and a.SizeID = od.ItemSizeID
            inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
            inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
          where od.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
            and od.OrderID = @OrderID
            --and od.ItemPrice <> 0
          order by od.ItemIndex, od.ItemType desc      

          --if exists (select *
          --           from tblOnlineOrders
          --           where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          --             and OrderID = @OrderID
          --             and Discount > 0) begin
          
          --  declare @DollarDiscountAmt smallmoney, @DSC_SalesID int, @DSC_ItemID smallint, @DSC_SizeID smallint, @DSC_UnitPrice smallmoney, @DSC_Qty smallint

          --  select @DollarDiscountAmt = Discount
          --  from tblOnlineOrders
          --  where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          --    and OrderID = @OrderID
          --    and Discount > 0

          --  declare curs_ordered_items cursor for
          --    select p.SalesID, p.ItemID, p.SizeID, p.UnitPrice, p.Qty
          --    from tblPendingOrders p
          --      inner join tblOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = p.SalesID
          --    where o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          --      and o.OrderID = @OrderID
          --      and p.UnitPrice > 0

          --    open curs_ordered_items
          --    fetch next from curs_ordered_items into @DSC_SalesID, @DSC_ItemID, @DSC_SizeID, @DSC_UnitPrice, @DSC_Qty
          --    while (@@fetch_status = 0) and (@DollarDiscountAmt > 0) begin

          --      if (round(@DSC_UnitPrice * @DSC_Qty, 2) >= @DollarDiscountAmt) begin

          --        update tblPendingOrders
          --        set DSCAmt = @DollarDiscountAmt
          --        where SalesID = @DSC_SalesID
          --          and ItemID = @DSC_ItemID
          --          and SizeID = @DSC_SizeID

          --        set @DollarDiscountAmt = 0

          --      end
          --      else begin

          --        update tblPendingOrders
          --        set DSCAmt = round(UnitPrice * Qty, 2)
          --        where SalesID = @DSC_SalesID
          --          and ItemID = @DSC_ItemID
          --          and SizeID = @DSC_SizeID

          --        set @DollarDiscountAmt = @DollarDiscountAmt - round(@DSC_UnitPrice * @DSC_Qty, 2)

          --      end      

          --      fetch next from curs_ordered_items into @DSC_SalesID, @DSC_ItemID, @DSC_SizeID, @DSC_UnitPrice, @DSC_Qty
          --    end
          --    close curs_ordered_items
          --  deallocate curs_ordered_items
          
          --end  

          set @OrderEntered = 1 

        end
        else begin 
          if (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''DINEIN'') or (isnull(@OrderType, '''') = ''PAYMENT'')
            set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Table is in use!''
          else
            set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Online order tables are full!''
        end

      end

      if (@OrderEntered = 1) and (isnull(@OrderType, '''') <> ''PAYMENT'') begin

        /*Start Printing */                     
        set @PrintDateTime = convert(varchar(20), dateadd(ss, -10, getdate()), 120)
        exec sp_InsertOrdersToBePrinted @SalesID, @PrintDateTime, 0

        /* update status */
        update tblOnlineOrders 
        set [Status] = 0,
            SalesID = @SalesID
        where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
          and OrderID = @OrderID

        --update tblOnlineOrders
        --set SalesID = @SalesID
        --where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
        --  and OrderID = @OrderID
        --  and SalesID = 0

        if (@AdditionalOrder = 1) begin

          update t
          set t.TotalAmt = t.TotalAmt + o.Total
          from tblTable t
            inner join tblOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = t.OrderNum
          where t.ID = @BlankTableID
            and o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
            and o.OrderID = @OrderID

        end

        set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Order placed in the printing queue!''

      end

      update tblTable
      set Opened = 0
      where ID = isnull(@BlankTableID, 0) 

    end
    else
      set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Order ID '' + convert(varchar, @OrderID) + '' does not exist!''

    commit transaction process_online_order
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction process_online_order
    set @OrderProcessMsg = ''There was an error while processing the order! (Order ID: '' + convert(varchar, @OrderID) + '')''
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spws_InsertOnlineOrders]
  @OrderID int,
  @xmlString varchar(max),
  @OrderProcessed bit = 0 output,
  @OrderProcessMsg varchar(100) = '''' output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @StationName varchar(20), @IntegrationCode varchar(50), @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint, 
          @OrderType varchar(100), @DineInSelfOrderCode varchar(1000), @TableID smallint

  select top 1 @StationName = p.StationName
  from tblPeripherals p
    inner join tblStation s on upper(p.StationName) = upper(s.StationName)
  where p.Code = ''PSO'' /*Print Scheduled Order*/
    and upper(p.Value) = ''TRUE''
    and s.[Status] = 1

  /* This can be called for the ones not processed because of full online order tables.
  exec spws_InsertOnlineOrders 0, '''', 0, ''''
  */
		
  begin try
  
    begin transaction insert_online_orders

    set @OrderProcessed = 0
    set @OrderProcessMsg = ''''
    set @OnlineOrderCompanyID = 0

    /*========================== Extract XML data into tables =================================================================*/

    if (@OrderID > 0) and (ltrim(rtrim(@xmlString)) <> '''') begin

      declare @xml xml

      set @xml = @xmlString
  		
      if not exists (select * 
                     from sys.objects 
                     where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTestXML]'')
                       and type in (N''U'')) begin

        CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmpTestXML](
          [ID] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
          [xmlString] [xml] NULL
        ) ON [PRIMARY]

      end

      insert into tmpTestXML (xmlString) values (@xml)

      select @IntegrationCode = ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''integration_code[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))),
             @OrderType = ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''type[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))),
             @DineInSelfOrderCode = ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''dine_in_self_order_code[1]'', ''varchar(1000)''), '''')))
      from @xml.nodes(''/ticket'') as tbl(tickets)

      if (ltrim(rtrim(@IntegrationCode)) = '''') set @IntegrationCode = ''EPOS''

      select @OnlineOrderCompanyID = ID
      from tblOnlineOrderCompany
      where [Integrated] = 1
        and ltrim(rtrim(IntegrationCode)) <> ''''
        and ltrim(rtrim(IntegrationCode)) = @IntegrationCode

      if (isnull(@OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0) > 0) begin

        set @TableID = 0

        if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderType)) = ''DINEIN'') or (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderType)) = ''PAYMENT'') begin
          
          set @TableID = dbo.GetDineInSelfOrderTableID(@DineInSelfOrderCode)

        end

        if (@TableID >= 0) begin

          if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderType)) in (''TAKEOUT'', ''DELIVERY'', ''DINEIN'')) begin
  		
            /* Insert Order Info */
            insert into tblOnlineOrders (OrderID, OrderType, FirstName, LastName, PhoneNum, EmailAddress, UserComments,
                                         DeliveryCompanyName, DeliveryLocationName, DeliveryLine1, DeliveryLine2, DeliveryCity,
                                         DeliveryState, DeliveryZipCode, DeliveryComments, SubTotal, Tax, CouponName, Discount,
                                         DeliveryCharge, Total, PaymentType, PaymentStatus, CreateDateTime, RequestedDateTime,
                                         [Status], DiscountPercent, Tip, SalesID, AltOrderID, TableID, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select tickets.value(''order_id[1]'', ''int'') as OrderID,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''type[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as OrderType,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/firstname/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as FirstName,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/lastname/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as LastName,
                   --replace(replace(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/phone/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))), ''-'', ''''), '' '', '''') as PhoneNum,    
                   right(replace(replace(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/phone/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))), ''-'', ''''), '' '', ''''), 10) as PhoneNum,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/email/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as EmailAddress,    
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''comments[1]'', ''varchar(4000)''), ''''))) as UserComments,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/company_name/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as DeliveryCompanyName,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/location_name/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as DeliveryLocationName,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/line1/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as DeliveryLine1,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/line2/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as DeliveryLine2,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/city/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))) as DeliveryCity,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/state/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))) as DeliveryState,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/zip/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))) as DeliveryZipCode,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(delivery_address/comments/text())[1]'', ''varchar(4000)''), ''''))) as DeliveryComments,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''subtotal[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as SubTotal,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''tax[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Tax,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''coupon_name[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as CouponName,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''discount[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Discount,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''deliverycharges[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as DeliveryCharge,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''total[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Total,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''PaymentType[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as PaymentType,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''PaymentStatus[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as PaymentStatus,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''created_timestamp[1]'', ''smalldatetime''), getdate()) as CreatedDateTime,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''requested_timestamp[1]'', ''smalldatetime''), getdate()) as RequestedDateTime,
                   1 as OrderStatus,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''discount_percent[1]'', ''float''), 0) as DiscountPercent,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''tip[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Tip,
                   0 as SalesID,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''alt_order_id[1]'', ''varchar(20)''), 0) as AltOrderID,
                   isnull(@TableID, 0) as TableID,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            from @xml.nodes(''/ticket'') as tbl(tickets)
            where isnull(tickets.value(''order_id[1]'', ''int''), 0) = @OrderID
              and not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrders
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID)

            /* Insert Order Detail */
            insert into tblOnlineOrderDetail (OrderID, ItemType, ItemIndex, ItemID, ItemSizeID, ItemName, ItemSizeName, ItemQty, ItemPrice, ItemModifiers, ItemComments, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select @OrderID as OrderID,
                   cast(1 as bit) as ItemType,       
                   dense_rank() over (order by items) as ItemIndex,
                   isnull(convert(smallint, 
                                  case when charindex(''|'', items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) = 0 then items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')
                                       else substring(items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 1, charindex(''|'', items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) - 1)
                                  end), 0) as ItemID,
                   isnull(case convert(smallint, isnull(items.value(''@pos_name[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), '''')) when 0 then 1
                               else convert(smallint, isnull(items.value(''@pos_name[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))
                          end, 1) as ItemSizeID,    
        --           isnull(convert(smallint,
        --                          case when charindex(''|'', items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) = 0 then ''1''
        --                               else substring(items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), charindex(''|'', items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')) + 1, len(items.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')))
        --                          end), 0) as ItemSizeID,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(items.value(''(name/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as ItemName,    
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(items.value(''(size/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as ItemSizeName,   
                   isnull(items.value(''(quantity/text())[1]'', ''smallint''), 0) as ItemQty,
                   isnull(items.value(''(price/text())[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as ItemPrice,
                   '''' as ItemModifers,
                   ltrim(rtrim(replace(isnull(items.value(''(comments/text())[1]'', ''varchar(255)''), ''''), ''$'', ''''))) as ItemComments,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            from @xml.nodes(''/ticket/items/item'') as tbl(items)
            where not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrderDetail
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                and ItemType = 1)

            /* Insert Item Modifiers  */
            insert into tblOnlineOrderDetail (OrderID, ItemType, ItemIndex, ItemID, ItemSizeID, ItemName, ItemSizeName, ItemQty, ItemPrice, ItemModifiers, ItemComments, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select @OrderID as OrderID,
                   cast(0 as bit) as ItemType,
                   dense_rank() over (order by items) as ItemIndex,
                   isnull(convert(smallint, 
                                  case when charindex(''|'', modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) = 0 then modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')
                                       else substring(modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 1, charindex(''|'', modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) - 1)
                                  end), 0) as ItemModifierID,
                   isnull(case convert(smallint, isnull(modifiers.value(''@pos_name[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), '''')) when 0 then 1
                               else convert(smallint, isnull(modifiers.value(''@pos_name[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))
                          end, 1) as ItemSizeID,    
        --           isnull(convert(smallint,
        --                          case when charindex(''|'', modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), 0) = 0 then ''1''
        --                               else substring(modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), charindex(''|'', modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')) + 1, len(modifiers.value(''@pos_id[1]'', ''varchar(100)'')))
        --                          end), 0) as ItemSizeID,
                   case when isnull(modifiers.value(''(price/text())[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) <> 0 then
                          convert(varchar, abs(convert(int, convert(varbinary, newid()))))
                        else
                          ''''
                   end as ItemName,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(modifiers.value(''(name/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as ItemSizeName,
                   isnull(modifiers.value(''(quantity/text())[1]'', ''smallint''), 0) as ItemQty,
                   isnull(modifiers.value(''(price/text())[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as ItemPrice,
                   '''' as ItemModifers,
                   '''' as ItemComments,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            from @xml.nodes(''/ticket/items/item'') as tbl(items)
              outer apply items.nodes(''modifiers/modifier'') as tbl2(modifiers)
            where not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrderDetail
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                and ItemType = 0)
      --        and exists (select *
      --                    from items.nodes(''modifiers/modifier'') as tbl3(modifiers2))

            /* Update extracted modifier ItemIndex to -1, for the ones that are duplicate to the size selection of menu */
            update d1
            set d1.ItemIndex = -1
            from tblOnlineOrderDetail d1
            where d1.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
              and d1.OrderID = @OrderID
              and d1.ItemType = 0
              and d1.ItemPrice = 0
              and exists (select *
                          from tblOnlineOrderDetail d2
                          where d2.OnlineOrderCompanyID = d1.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                            and d2.OrderID = d1.OrderID
                            and d2.ItemType = 1
                            and d2.ItemID = d1.ItemID
                            and d2.ItemSizeID = d1.ItemSizeID)
                            
          end
          else if (ltrim(rtrim(@OrderType)) = ''PAYMENT'') begin

            /* Insert Payment Info */
            insert into tblOnlineOrders (OrderID, OrderType, FirstName, LastName, PhoneNum, EmailAddress, UserComments,
                                         DeliveryCompanyName, DeliveryLocationName, DeliveryLine1, DeliveryLine2, DeliveryCity,
                                         DeliveryState, DeliveryZipCode, DeliveryComments, SubTotal, Tax, CouponName, Discount,
                                         DeliveryCharge, Total, PaymentType, PaymentStatus, CreateDateTime, RequestedDateTime,
                                         [Status], DiscountPercent, Tip, SalesID, AltOrderID, TableID, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select tickets.value(''order_id[1]'', ''int'') as OrderID,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''type[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as OrderType,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/firstname/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as FirstName,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/lastname/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as LastName,
                   right(replace(replace(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/phone/text())[1]'', ''varchar(50)''), ''''))), ''-'', ''''), '' '', ''''), 10) as PhoneNum,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''(customer/email/text())[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as EmailAddress,    
                   '''' as UserComments,
                   '''' as DeliveryCompanyName,
                   '''' as DeliveryLocationName,
                   '''' as DeliveryLine1,
                   '''' as DeliveryLine2,
                   '''' as DeliveryCity,
                   '''' as DeliveryState,
                   '''' as DeliveryZipCode,
                   '''' as DeliveryComments,
                   0 as SubTotal,
                   0 as Tax,
                   '''' as CouponName,
                   0 as Discount,
                   0 as DeliveryCharge,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''total[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Total,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''PaymentType[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as PaymentType,
                   ltrim(rtrim(isnull(tickets.value(''PaymentStatus[1]'', ''varchar(100)''), ''''))) as PaymentStatus,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''created_timestamp[1]'', ''smalldatetime''), getdate()) as CreatedDateTime,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''requested_timestamp[1]'', ''smalldatetime''), getdate()) as RequestedDateTime,
                   1 as OrderStatus,
                   0 as DiscountPercent,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''tip[1]'', ''smallmoney''), 0) as Tip,
                   0 as SalesID,
                   isnull(tickets.value(''alt_order_id[1]'', ''varchar(20)''), 0) as AltOrderID,
                   isnull(@TableID, 0) as TableID,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            from @xml.nodes(''/ticket'') as tbl(tickets)
            where isnull(tickets.value(''order_id[1]'', ''int''), 0) = @OrderID
              and not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrders
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID)

            /* Insert Blank Detail for Payment */
            insert into tblOnlineOrderDetail (OrderID, ItemType, ItemIndex, ItemID, ItemSizeID, ItemName, ItemSizeName, ItemQty, ItemPrice, ItemModifiers, ItemComments, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select @OrderID as OrderID,
                   cast(1 as bit) as ItemType,
                   1 as ItemIndex,
                   0 as ItemID,
                   0 as ItemSizeID,
                   '''' as ItemName,
                   '''' as ItemSizeName,
                   0 as ItemQty,
                   0 as ItemPrice,
                   '''' as ItemModifers,
                   '''' as ItemComments,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            where not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrderDetail
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                and ItemType = 1)

            insert into tblOnlineOrderDetail (OrderID, ItemType, ItemIndex, ItemID, ItemSizeID, ItemName, ItemSizeName, ItemQty, ItemPrice, ItemModifiers, ItemComments, OnlineOrderCompanyID)
            select @OrderID as OrderID,
                   cast(0 as bit) as ItemType,
                   1 as ItemIndex,
                   0 as ItemID,
                   0 as ItemSizeID,
                   '''' as ItemName,
                   '''' as ItemSizeName,
                   0 as ItemQty,
                   0 as ItemPrice,
                   '''' as ItemModifers,
                   '''' as ItemComments,
                   @OnlineOrderCompanyID as OnlineOrderCompanyID
            where not exists (select *
                              from tblOnlineOrderDetail
                              where OrderID = @OrderID
                                and OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                and ItemType = 0)            

          end

          set @OrderProcessed = 1

          /*===================== Process Order ===========================================================*/
          exec spws_ProcessOnlineOrder @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OrderID, @StationName, @OrderProcessMsg output
          /*===============================================================================================*/

        end
        else begin

          set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Self-Order Dine-In Table not Found!''

        end

      end
      else begin

        set @OrderProcessMsg = ''Integration code missing or wrong!''

      end

    end
    else begin

      declare curs_pending_online_orders cursor for
        select OnlineOrderCompanyID, OrderID
        from tblOnlineOrders
        where RequestedDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) -- dateadd(d, -1, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))
          and [Status] = 1
        order by RequestedDateTime, OrderID

        open curs_pending_online_orders
        fetch next from curs_pending_online_orders into @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OrderID
        while @@fetch_status = 0 begin

          /*===================== Process Order ===========================================================*/
          exec spws_ProcessOnlineOrder @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OrderID, @StationName, @OrderProcessMsg output
          /*===============================================================================================*/

          fetch next from curs_pending_online_orders into @OnlineOrderCompanyID, @OrderID
        end
        close curs_pending_online_orders
      deallocate curs_pending_online_orders

    end

    commit transaction insert_online_orders
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction insert_online_orders
    set @OrderProcessed = 0
    return 0
  end catch
		
END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_VoidOrUndoVoidRewardPoint]
  @SalesID int,
  @Void bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction void_or_undo_void_reward_point

    update c
    set c.EarnedPoints = c.EarnedPoints + (case when @Void = 1 then -1 else 1 end * (pd.PointSaved - pd.PointUsed))
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
      inner join tblPointsDetail pd on pd.SalesID = s.ID
    where c.ID > 1
      and s.ID = @SalesID     

    commit transaction void_or_undo_void_reward_point
    return 1
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction void_or_undo_void_reward_point
    return 0
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_GetCardTransactionCashiers]  
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select distinct u.ID, u.FName, u.LName, ltrim(rtrim(u.FName)) + '' '' + ltrim(rtrim(u.LName)) as CashierName
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblUser u on s.CashierID = u.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and p.BatchClosed = 0
    and p.CardNumber is not null
  order by CashierName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spfd_CheckIfTransactionsWithoutTipAdjustmentExist]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select count(p.ID) as PaymentCount
  from tblPayment p
    inner join tblSales s on p.SalesID = s.ID
  where p.PaymentTypeID in (2, 3, 4, 5, 7, 8)
    and p.BatchClosed = 0
    and p.CardNumber is not null
    and p.TipAdjusted = 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetOnlineOrderCompany]
  @ActiveCompanyOnly bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany
  where ID = 0

  select *, case when ShowNameOnButton = 1 then ''Yes'' else ''No'' end as StrShowNameOnButton,
         case when [Status] = 1 then ''Active'' else '''' end as StrStatus
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany
  where case when @ActiveCompanyOnly = 1 then
               case when [Status] = 1 then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1
  order by CompanyName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertOnlineOrderCompany]
  @CompanyName varchar(50),
  @CompanyColor int,
  @ShowNameOnButton bit,
  @CommissionPercentage decimal(4, 2),
  @PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder bit,
  @PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder bit,
  @PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber bit,
  @Integrated bit,
  @IntegrationCode varchar(50),
  @APITransactionKey varchar(100),
  @CommissionCalculationType char(1),
  @ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL varchar(1000),
  @NewOnlineOrderCompanyID smallint = 0 output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction insert_online_order_company

  insert into tblOnlineOrderCompany (CompanyName, CompanyColor, ShowNameOnButton, [Status], CommissionPercentage,
                                     PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder, 
                                     PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, [Integrated], IntegrationCode, APITransactionKey, 
                                     /*DineInSelfOrderURL,*/ CommissionCalculationType, ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL)
  values (@CompanyName, @CompanyColor, @ShowNameOnButton, 1, @CommissionPercentage, 
          @PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder, @PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder, 
          @PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber, @Integrated, @IntegrationCode, @APITransactionKey, 
          /*null,*/ @CommissionCalculationType, @ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL)

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction insert_online_order_company
    set @NewOnlineOrderCompanyID = isnull(scope_identity(), 0)
    return 1
  end
  else begin  
    rollback transaction insert_online_order_company
    set @NewOnlineOrderCompanyID = 0
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateOnlineOrderCompany]
  @CompanyName varchar(50),
  @CompanyColor int,
  @ShowNameOnButton bit,
  @Status bit,
  @CommissionPercentage decimal(4, 2),
  @PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder bit,
  @PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder bit,
  @PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber bit,
  @Integrated bit,
  @IntegrationCode varchar(50),
  @APITransactionKey varchar(100),
  @CommissionCalculationType char(1),
  @ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL varchar(1000),
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_online_order_company

  update tblOnlineOrderCompany 
  set CompanyName = @CompanyName,
      CompanyColor = @CompanyColor,
      ShowNameOnButton = @ShowNameOnButton,
      [Status] = @Status,
      CommissionPercentage = @CommissionPercentage,
      PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder = @PrintWaitressCopyForPickupOrder,
      PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder = @PrintWaitressCopyForDeliveryOrder,
      PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber = @PromptToEnterOnlineOrderNumber,
      [Integrated] = @Integrated,
      IntegrationCode = @IntegrationCode,
      APITransactionKey = @APITransactionKey,
      /*DineInSelfOrderURL = null,*/
      CommissionCalculationType = @CommissionCalculationType,
      ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL = @ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL
  where ID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_online_order_company
    return 1
  end
  else begin  
    rollback transaction update_online_order_company
    return 0
  end

END'
GO
