EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesOfOnlineOrdersSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation bit, @Tax1Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax2Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax3Rate decimal(5, 4)

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation = convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''IDOCC''))
  
  select distinct top 1 @Tax1Rate = GSTRate, 
                        @Tax2Rate = PSTRate, 
                        @Tax3Rate = PST2Rate
  from tblSales
  where SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Sales Summary                                                                                     */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/

  select o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ooc.CompanyName, ooc.[Integrated], 
         isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A'') as CommissionCalculationType, 
         ((year(s.SaleDateTime) * 100) + month(s.SaleDateTime)) as SaleYearMonth, --s.TransType, 
         --case --when s.TransType = 0 then ''Refund''
         --     when s.TransType = 1 then ''Sale''
         --     --when s.TransType = 2 then ''NoSale''
         --     --when s.TransType = 3 then ''Void''
         --     --when s.TransType = 4 then ''SalesVoid''
         --     --when s.TransType = 5 then ''Training''
         --     --when s.TransType = 9 then ''Unpaid''
         --     else '''' 
         --end as TransTypeDescription,
         '''' as TransTypeDescription,
         isnull(count(s.TransType),0) as TransCount,
         sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.GSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax1Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.PSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax2Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as Tax3Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt,
         sum(isnull(s.Guests,0)) as GuestCount
  into #tmp_online_order_sales
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and case when @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation = 1 then 1
             else case when o.DineInOrder = 0 then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  group by o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ooc.CompanyName, ooc.[Integrated], 
           isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A''),
           ((year(s.SaleDateTime) * 100) + month(s.SaleDateTime)) --, s.TransType

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/

  select o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType, 
         case when isnull(ord.PaymentStatus, ''UNPAID'') = ''PAID'' then ''Online'' else ''In Store'' end as PaymentLocation,
         count(p.PaymentTypeID) as PaymentCount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount
  into #tmp_online_order_payments
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    left join tblOnlineOrders ord on ord.SalesID = s.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and case when @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation = 1 then 1
             else case when o.DineInOrder = 0 then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    --and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    --and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType,
           case when isnull(ord.PaymentStatus, ''UNPAID'') = ''PAID'' then ''Online'' else ''In Store'' end

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Commission Summary                                                                                */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  
  select os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
         sum(case when os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) then 
                    round((os.SubTotalAmt - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)
                  else 
                    case when os.SubTotalAmt > isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) then 
                           round((isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2) 
                         else 0 
                    end
             end) as CommissionSubTotal,
         sum(round(os.Tax1Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax1,
         sum(round(os.Tax2Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax2,
         sum(round(os.Tax3Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax3
  into #tmp_online_order_commission
  from #tmp_online_order_sales os    
    left join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''A''
  group by os.OnlineOrderCompanyID

  insert into #tmp_online_order_commission
  select os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
         sum(round(os.SubTotalAmt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionSubTotal,
         sum(round(os.Tax1Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax1,
         sum(round(os.Tax2Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax2,
         sum(round(os.Tax3Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax3
  from #tmp_online_order_sales os    
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                     and os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) 
                                                     and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt)
  where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''B''
  group by os.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Summary                                                                                           */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/  

  select OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, [Integrated], CommissionCalculationType, TransTypeDescription,
         sum(TransCount) as TransCount,
         sum(SubTotalAmt) as SubTotalAmt,
         sum(DSCAmt) as DSCAmt,
         sum(Tax1Amt) as Tax1Amt,
         sum(Tax2Amt) as Tax2Amt,
         sum(Tax3Amt) as Tax3Amt,
         sum(TotalAmt) as TotalAmt,
         sum(GuestCount) as GuestCount
  into #tmp_online_order_sales_summary
  from #tmp_online_order_sales
  group by OnlineOrderCompanyID, CompanyName, [Integrated], CommissionCalculationType, TransTypeDescription

  select ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ts.CompanyName, ts.[Integrated],   
         1 as TransType, /*ts.TransType, just in case of separating sales by transaction type, save the column for TransType */ 
         ts.TransTypeDescription, ts.TransCount, ts.SubTotalAmt, ts.DSCAmt,
         ts.Tax1Amt, ts.Tax2Amt, ts.Tax3Amt, ts.TotalAmt, ts.GuestCount, isnull(tp.PaymentLocation, ''In Store'') as PaymentLocation,
         isnull(tp.PaymentTypeID, 0) as PaymentTypeID, 
         isnull(tp.PaymentType, ''N/A'') as PaymentType, 
         isnull(tp.PaymentCount, 0) as PaymentCount, 
         isnull(tp.PaidAmount, 0) as PaidAmount, 
         isnull(tp.TipAmount, 0) as TipAmount, 
         isnull(tc.CommissionSubTotal, 0) as CommissionSubTotal,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax1, 0) as CommissionTax1,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax2, 0) as CommissionTax2,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax3, 0) as CommissionTax3,
         isnull(tc.CommissionSubTotal, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax1, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax2, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax3, 0) as CommissionTotal,
         @Tax1Rate as Tax1Rate,
         @Tax2Rate as Tax2Rate,
         @Tax3Rate as Tax3Rate
  from #tmp_online_order_sales_summary ts
    left join #tmp_online_order_commission tc on tc.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID
    left join #tmp_online_order_payments tp on tp.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  order by ts.CompanyName, tp.PaymentLocation, tp.PaymentType
  
  drop table #tmp_online_order_sales
  drop table #tmp_online_order_sales_summary
  drop table #tmp_online_order_payments
  drop table #tmp_online_order_commission

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_PaymentsSummaryExcludingOnlineOrders]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @CashPaidAmt money, @DebitPaidAmt money, @CreditCardPaidAmt money, @VisaPaidAmt money, @McPaidAmt money, @AmexPaidAmt money, 
          @CouponPaidAmt money, @DiscoverPaidAmt money, @JcbPaidAmt money, @GiftCardPaidAmt money, @RewardPointPaidAmt money,
          @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt money, @TotalPaidAmt money,

          @CashTipPaidAmt money, @DebitTipPaidAmt money, @CreditTipPaidAmt money, @VisaTipPaidAmt money, @McTipPaidAmt money, 
          @AmexTipPaidAmt money, @CouponTipPaidAmt money, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt money, @JcbTipPaidAmt money, 
          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt money, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt money, @TotalTipPaidAmt money, 
          
          @CashPaymentCount int, @DebitPaymentCount int, @CreditCardPaymentCount int, @VisaPaymentCount int, @McPaymentCount int, 
          @AmexPaymentCount int, @CouponPaymentCount int, @DiscoverPaymentCount int, @JcbPaymentCount int, @GiftCardPaymentCount int, 
          @RewardPointPaymentCount int, @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount int

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/

  exec spr_PaymentSummary @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, 0 /*@EmployeeID*/,
                          @CashPaidAmt output, @DebitPaidAmt output, @VisaPaidAmt output, 
                          @McPaidAmt output, @AmexPaidAmt output, @CouponPaidAmt output,
                          @DiscoverPaidAmt output, @JcbPaidAmt output, @GiftCardPaidAmt output, 
                          @RewardPointPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt output,
                          @CashTipPaidAmt output, @DebitTipPaidAmt output, @CreditTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @VisaTipPaidAmt output, @McTipPaidAmt output, @AmexTipPaidAmt output,
                          @CouponTipPaidAmt output, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt output, @JcbTipPaidAmt output, 
                          @GiftCardTipPaidAmt output, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt output,
                          @TotalTipPaidAmt output, @CashPaymentCount output, @DebitPaymentCount output, 
                          @VisaPaymentCount output, @McPaymentCount output, @AmexPaymentCount output, 
                          @CouponPaymentCount output, @DiscoverPaymentCount output, @JcbPaymentCount output, 
                          @GiftCardPaymentCount output, @RewardPointPaymentCount output, 
                          @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount output

  /* Get the payments for Non-Integrated online order company tables */
  select p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType,
         --count(p.PaymentTypeID) as PaymentCount,
         sum(case when p.PaidAmount <> 0 then 1 else 0 end) as PaymentCount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount
  into #tmp_payments_for_online_orders 
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and ooc.[Integrated] = 0  /* Orders paid through delivery online ordering system assuming all orders paid online */
    --and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    --and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType

  /* Get the payments paid online for Integrated online order company tables */
  insert into #tmp_payments_for_online_orders 
  select p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType,
         --count(p.PaymentTypeID) as PaymentCount,
         sum(case when p.PaidAmount <> 0 then 1 else 0 end) as PaymentCount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount,
         sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount  
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblOnlineOrders ord on ord.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and ooc.[Integrated] = 1
    and isnull(ord.PaymentStatus, ''UNPAID'') = ''PAID''  /* Orders paid through integrated online ordering system for all TAKEOUT/DELIVERY/DINEIN */
    and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    and p.Voided = 0
  group by p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType

  select PaymentTypeID, PaymentType, 
         sum(PaymentCount) as PaymentCount,
         sum(PaidAmount) as PaidAmount,
         sum(TipAmount) as TipAmount
  into #tmp_online_order_payments
  from #tmp_payments_for_online_orders
  group by PaymentTypeID, PaymentType

  select @CashPaidAmt = @CashPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @CashPaymentCount = @CashPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @CashTipPaidAmt = @CashTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 1

  select @DebitPaidAmt = @DebitPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @DebitPaymentCount = @DebitPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @DebitTipPaidAmt = @DebitTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 2

  select @VisaPaidAmt = @VisaPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @VisaPaymentCount = @VisaPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @VisaTipPaidAmt = @VisaTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 3

  select @McPaidAmt = @McPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @McPaymentCount = @McPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @McTipPaidAmt = @McTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 4

  select @AmexPaidAmt = @AmexPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @AmexPaymentCount = @AmexPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @AmexTipPaidAmt = @AmexTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 5

  select @CouponPaidAmt = @CouponPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @CouponPaymentCount = @CouponPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @CouponTipPaidAmt = @CouponTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 6

  select @DiscoverPaidAmt = @DiscoverPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @DiscoverPaymentCount = @DiscoverPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @DiscoverTipPaidAmt = @DiscoverTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 7

  select @JcbPaidAmt = @JcbPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @JcbPaymentCount = @JcbPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @JcbTipPaidAmt = @JcbTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 8

  select @GiftCardPaidAmt = @GiftCardPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @GiftCardPaymentCount = @GiftCardPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @GiftCardTipPaidAmt = @GiftCardTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 9

  select @RewardPointPaidAmt = @RewardPointPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @RewardPointPaymentCount = @RewardPointPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 10

  select @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt - t.PaidAmount,
         @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount = @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount - t.PaymentCount,
         @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt - t.TipAmount
  from #tmp_online_order_payments t
  where t.PaymentTypeID = 11

  set @CreditCardPaidAmt = @VisaPaidAmt + @McPaidAmt + @AmexPaidAmt + @DiscoverPaidAmt + @JcbPaidAmt
  set @CreditCardPaymentCount = @VisaPaymentCount + @McPaymentCount + @AmexPaymentCount + @DiscoverPaymentCount + @JcbPaymentCount
  set @TotalPaidAmt = @CashPaidAmt + @DebitPaidAmt + @CreditCardPaidAmt + @CouponPaidAmt + @GiftCardPaidAmt + @RewardPointPaidAmt + @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt

  set @CreditTipPaidAmt = @VisaTipPaidAmt + @McTipPaidAmt + @AmexTipPaidAmt + @DiscoverTipPaidAmt + @JcbTipPaidAmt
  set @TotalTipPaidAmt = @CashTipPaidAmt + @DebitTipPaidAmt + @CreditTipPaidAmt + @CouponTipPaidAmt + @GiftCardTipPaidAmt + @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt

  drop table #tmp_online_order_payments 
  drop table #tmp_payments_for_online_orders

  select @CashPaidAmt as CashPaidAmt, @DebitPaidAmt as DebitPaidAmt, @CreditCardPaidAmt as CreditCardPaidAmt,
         @VisaPaidAmt as VisaPaidAmt, @McPaidAmt as McPaidAmt, @AmexPaidAmt as AmexPaidAmt, @CouponPaidAmt as CouponPaidAmt,
         @DiscoverPaidAmt as DiscoverPaidAmt, @JcbPaidAmt as JcbPaidAmt, @GiftCardPaidAmt as GiftCardPaidAmt, 
         @RewardPointPaidAmt as RewardPointPaidAmt, @ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt as ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt, @TotalPaidAmt as TotalPaidAmt,

         @CashTipPaidAmt as CashTipPaidAmt, @DebitTipPaidAmt as DebitTipPaidAmt, @CreditTipPaidAmt as CreditTipPaidAmt, 
         @VisaTipPaidAmt as VisaTipPaidAmt, @McTipPaidAmt as McTipPaidAmt, @AmexTipPaidAmt as AmexTipPaidAmt,
         @CouponTipPaidAmt as CouponTipPaidAmt, @DiscoverTipPaidAmt as DiscoverTipPaidAmt, @JcbTipPaidAmt as JcbTipPaidAmt, 
         @GiftCardTipPaidAmt as GiftCardTipPaidAmt, @ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt as ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt,
         @TotalTipPaidAmt as TotalTipPaidAmt, 

         @CashPaymentCount as CashPaymentCount, @DebitPaymentCount as DebitPaymentCount, @CreditCardPaymentCount as CreditCardPaymentCount,
         @VisaPaymentCount as VisaPaymentCount, @McPaymentCount as McPaymentCount, @AmexPaymentCount as AmexPaymentCount, 
         @CouponPaymentCount as CouponPaymentCount, @DiscoverPaymentCount as DiscoverPaymentCount, @JcbPaymentCount as JcbPaymentCount, 
         @GiftCardPaymentCount as GiftCardPaymentCount, @RewardPointPaymentCount as RewardPointPaymentCount, 
         @ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount as ChargeOnAccountPaymentCount
  
END'
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ExportMenuItems]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --declare @script nvarchar(2000), @export_file_nm varchar(500), 
  --        @file_creation_str varchar(1000), @bcp_parameter varchar(1000)

  --set @export_file_nm = ''Menu_Item_Exported_'' + convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) + ''.txt''

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsExport]'')
               and type in (N''U''))
    drop table tmpMenuItemsExport

  select cast(0 as tinyint) as ID, cast('''' as varchar(50)) as TableName, cast('''' as varchar(1000)) as MenuItem
  into tmpMenuItemsExport

  truncate table tmpMenuItemsExport

  /*=======================================================================*/
  /* tblCategory                                                           */
  /*=======================================================================*/

  insert into tmpMenuItemsExport (ID, TableName, MenuItem)
  select 0, 
         ''Category'',
         ''ID'' + char(9) +
         ''CatName'' + char(9) +
         ''PrintOrder'' + char(9) +
         ''CategoryImageFilePath''

  insert into tmpMenuItemsExport (ID, TableName, MenuItem)
  select 1,
         ''Category'',

  from TPPro.dbo.tblCategory
  order by ID

  /*=======================================================================*/

  /*=======================================================================*/

         ''ManageInv'' + char(9) +
         ''NonAlcohol''

--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @bcp_parameter

  drop table tmpMenuItemsExport

END'

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ExportMenuLayout]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --declare @script nvarchar(2000), @export_file_nm varchar(500), 
  --        @file_creation_str varchar(1000), @bcp_parameter varchar(1000)

  --set @export_file_nm = ''Menu_Layout_Exported_'' + convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) + ''.txt''

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuLayoutExport]'')
               and type in (N''U''))
    drop table tmpMenuLayoutExport

  select cast(0 as tinyint) as ID, cast('''' as varchar(1000)) as MenuLayout
  into tmpMenuLayoutExport

  truncate table tmpMenuLayoutExport
  
  insert into tmpMenuLayoutExport (ID, MenuLayout)
  select 0, 
         ''Level'' + char(9) +

         ''ControlIndex'' + char(9) +

         ''Caption'' + char(9) +

         ''AlignLeft'' + char(9) +
         ''Height'' + char(9) +
         ''Width'' + char(9) +
         ''FontName'' + char(9) +
         ''FontSize'' + char(9) +
         ''FontBold'' + char(9) +
         ''FontItalic'' + char(9) +
         ''FontColor'' + char(9) +
         ''Color'' + char(9) +
         ''ImageFileName'' + char(9) +
         ''ScaleItem'' + char(9) +
         ''TasteModifier'' + char(9) +
         ''NextItemID'' + char(9) +
         ''NextItemName'' + char(9) +
         ''GroupItem'' + char(9) +
         ''ItemImage'' + char(9) +
         ''ItemImageFileType'' + char(9) +
         ''SoldOut'' + char(9) +
         ''LayoutModeType''

  insert into tmpMenuLayoutExport (ID, MenuLayout)
  select 1,
         convert(varchar, [Level]) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, TabIndex) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, ControlIndex) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, ItemID) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, OpenItem) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, SideDish) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, Taste) + char(9) +
         isnull(ItemName, '''') + char(9) +
         isnull(Caption, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, AlignTop) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, AlignLeft) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, Height) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, Width) + char(9) +
         isnull(FontName, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, FontSize) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, FontBold) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, FontItalic) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, FontColor) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, Color) + char(9) +
         isnull(ImageFileName, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, ScaleItem) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, TasteModifier) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, NextItemID) + char(9) +
         isnull(NextItemName, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, GroupItem) + char(9) +
         char(9) + --ItemImage
         isnull(ItemImageFileType, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, SoldOut) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, LayoutModeType)
  from TPPro.dbo.tblMenuLayout
  order by LayoutModeType, [Level], TabIndex, ControlIndex

  select *
  from tmpMenuLayoutExport
  order by ID

--  set @script = ''select MenuLayout '' +
--                ''from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuLayoutExport '' +
--                ''order by ID''
--
--  set @file_creation_str = ''echo '''''''' > C:\TopPos\Reports\MenuLayout\'' + @export_file_nm
--  set @bcp_parameter = ''bcp "'' + @script + ''" queryout "C:\TopPos\Reports\MenuLayout\'' + @export_file_nm + ''" -c -T -x'' 
--
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @file_creation_str
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @bcp_parameter

  drop table tmpMenuLayoutExport

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ExportTableLayout]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  --declare @script nvarchar(2000), @export_file_nm varchar(500), 
  --        @file_creation_str varchar(1000), @bcp_parameter varchar(1000)

  --set @export_file_nm = ''Table_Layout_Exported_'' + convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) + ''.txt''

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTableLayoutExport]'')
               and type in (N''U''))
    drop table tmpTableLayoutExport

  select cast(0 as tinyint) as ID, cast('''' as varchar(1000)) as TableLayout
  into tmpTableLayoutExport

  truncate table tmpTableLayoutExport
  
  insert into tmpTableLayoutExport (ID, TableLayout)
  select 0, 
         ''Level'' + char(9) +
         ''TabIndex'' + char(9) +
         ''ControlIndex'' + char(9) +
         ''TableID'' + char(9) +
         ''Caption'' + char(9) +
         ''AlignTop'' + char(9) +
         ''AlignLeft'' + char(9) +
         ''Height'' + char(9) +
         ''Width'' + char(9) +
         ''FontName'' + char(9) +
         ''FontSize'' + char(9) +
         ''FontBold'' + char(9) +
         ''FontItalic'' + char(9) +
         ''FontColor'' + char(9) +
         ''Color'' + char(9) +
         ''ImageFileName'' + char(9) +
         ''TableImage'' + char(9) +
         ''TableImageFileType'' + char(9) +
         ''LayoutModeType'' + char(9) +
         ''TableName'' + char(9) +
         ''TakeOut'' + char(9) +
         ''Delivery'' + char(9) +
         ''Online'' + char(9) +
         ''StayOn'' + char(9) +
         ''ApplySpecialPricing'' + char(9) +
         ''SpecialPricingRate'' + char(9) +
         ''BellNumber'' + char(9) +
         ''StationID'' + char(9) +
         ''OnlineOrderCompanyID'' + char(9) +
         ''AccessPermissionRequired'' + char(9) +
         ''AppliedUnitPriceType''

  insert into tmpTableLayoutExport (ID, TableLayout)
  select 1,
         convert(varchar, tl.[Level]) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.TabIndex) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.ControlIndex) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.TableID) + char(9) +
         isnull(tl.Caption, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.AlignTop) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.AlignLeft) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.Height) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.Width) + char(9) +
         isnull(tl.FontName, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.FontSize) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.FontBold) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.FontItalic) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.FontColor) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.Color) + char(9) +
         isnull(tl.ImageFileName, '''') + char(9) +
         char(9) + --TableImage
         isnull(tl.TableImageFileType, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, tl.LayoutModeType) + char(9) +
         isnull(t.TableName, '''') + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.TakeOut, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.Delivery, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.[Online], 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.StayOn, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.ApplySpecialPricing, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.SpecialPricingRate, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.BellNumber, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.StationID, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.AccessPermissionRequired, 0)) + char(9) +
         convert(varchar, isnull(t.AppliedUnitPriceType, 1))
  from tblTableLayout tl
    left join tblTable t on tl.TableID = t.ID
  order by tl.LayoutModeType, tl.TabIndex, tl.Level, tl.ControlIndex

  select *
  from tmpTableLayoutExport
  order by ID

--  set @script = ''select TableLayout '' +
--                ''from TPPro.dbo.tmpTableLayoutExport '' +
--                ''order by ID''
--
--  set @file_creation_str = ''echo '''''''' > C:\TopPos\Reports\TableLayout\'' + @export_file_nm
--  set @bcp_parameter = ''bcp "'' + @script + ''" queryout "C:\TopPos\Reports\TableLayout\'' + @export_file_nm + ''" -c -T -x'' 
--
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @file_creation_str
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @bcp_parameter

  drop table tmpTableLayoutExport

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ImportMenuItems]
  @MenuItemsFileName varchar(100),
  @ProcessInsertUpdate bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(max), @tmp_table_name varchar(50)

  if (@ProcessInsertUpdate = 0) begin

    declare @data_file varchar(150), @tbl_table_name varchar(50), 
            @column_nm varchar(50), @data_type varchar(20), @character_maximum_length varchar(6)
  
    set @data_file = @MenuItemsFileName
    set @MenuItemsFileName = reverse(substring(reverse(@MenuItemsFileName), 1, charindex(''\'', reverse(@MenuItemsFileName)) - 1))
    set @MenuItemsFileName = substring(@MenuItemsFileName, 1, charindex(''_'', @MenuItemsFileName) - 1)

    create table #tmp_file_exists 
    (
      file_exists int,
      file_is_a_directory int,
      parent_directory_exists int
    )

    insert into #tmp_file_exists
    exec master.dbo.xp_fileexist @data_file

    if exists (select *
               from #tmp_file_exists
               where file_exists = 1) begin

      select @tbl_table_name = name,
             @tmp_table_name = replace(name, ''tbl'', ''tmpMenuItemsImport_'')
      from sys.objects 
      where type in (N''U'')
        and is_ms_shipped = 0
        and upper(name) = upper(''tbl'' + @MenuItemsFileName)

      if exists (select * 
                  from sys.objects 
                  where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].['' + @tmp_table_name + '']'')
                    and type in (N''U'')) begin

        set @script = ''drop table '' + @tmp_table_name
        exec sp_executesql @script

      end

      --set @script = ''select * '' +
      --              ''into '' + @tmp_table_name + '' '' +
      --              ''from '' + @tbl_table_name
      --exec sp_executesql @script
        
      --set @script = ''truncate table '' + @tmp_table_name
      --exec sp_executesql @script

      set @script = ''create table '' + @tmp_table_name + ''(''

      declare curs_columns cursor for
        select column_name, data_type, 
               case when character_maximum_length is not null then
                      case when character_maximum_length > 8000 then ''''
                           else ''('' + convert(varchar, character_maximum_length) + '')'' 
                      end
                    else '''' 
               end
        from information_schema.columns
        where table_name = @tbl_table_name
        order by ordinal_position

        open curs_columns
        fetch next from curs_columns into @column_nm, @data_type, @character_maximum_length
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          set @script = @script + char(13) + char(10) +
                        @column_nm + '' '' + @data_type + @character_maximum_length + '',''

          fetch next from curs_columns into @column_nm, @data_type, @character_maximum_length
        end
        close curs_columns
      deallocate curs_columns

      set @script =  substring(@script, 1, len(@script) - 1) + '')''

      exec sp_executesql @script
  
      /* Import Menu Items Data */
      set @script = ''bulk insert '' + @tmp_table_name + '' '' +
                    ''from '''''' + @data_file + '''''' '' +
                    ''with (fieldterminator = ''''\t'''', '' +
                          ''firstrow = 2, '' +
                          ''rowterminator = ''''\n'''')''
      exec sp_executesql @script

      drop table #tmp_file_exists

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].['' + @tmp_table_name + '']'')
                   and type in (N''U''))

        return 1

      else
        
        return -1

    end
    else begin

      return 0

    end

  end
  else begin

    begin try
      begin transaction apply_updated_item_info

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblCategory                                                                 */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_Category]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        update c1
        set c1.CatName = isnull(c2.CatName, ''n/a''),
            c1.PrintOrder = isnull(c2.PrintOrder, 0),
            c1.CategoryImageFilePath = c2.CategoryImageFilePath
        from TPPro.dbo.tblCategory c1
          inner join TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Category c2 on c2.ID = c1.ID

        /*---------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

        set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblCategory on

        insert into TPPro.dbo.tblCategory (ID, CatName, PrintOrder, CategoryImageFilePath)
        select c2.ID, isnull(c2.CatName, ''n/a''), isnull(c2.PrintOrder, 0), c2.CategoryImageFilePath
        from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Category c2
        where not exists (select *
                          from TPPro.dbo.tblCategory c1
                          where c1.ID = c2.ID) 
        order by c2.ID

        set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblCategory off

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblItem                                                                     */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_Item]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Item t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblCategory c
                                         where c.ID = t.CategoryID)) begin

          update i1
          set i1.IName = isnull(i2.IName, ''n/a''),
              i1.CategoryID = i2.CategoryID,
              i1.ApplyGST = i2.ApplyGST,
              i1.ApplyPST = i2.ApplyPST,
              i1.[Status] = i2.[Status],
              i1.OpenItem = i2.OpenItem,
              i1.KitchenB = i2.KitchenB,
              i1.KitchenF = i2.KitchenF,
              i1.Bar = i2.Bar,
              i1.SideDish = i2.SideDish,
              i1.Taste = i2.Taste,
              i1.IName2 = isnull(i2.IName2, ''''),
              i1.ApplyPST2 = i2.ApplyPST2,
              i1.BarCode = isnull(i2.BarCode, ''''),
              i1.KitchenE = i2.KitchenE,
              i1.Alcohol = i2.Alcohol,
              i1.HourlyChargedItem = i2.HourlyChargedItem,
              i1.ScaleItem = i2.ScaleItem,
              i1.OnlineItem = i2.OnlineItem,
              i1.ItemDescription = i2.ItemDescription,
              i1.ImageFilePath = i2.ImageFilePath,
              i1.RewardItem = i2.RewardItem,
              i1.GroupItem = i2.GroupItem,
              i1.Kitchen5 = i2.Kitchen5,
              i1.Kitchen6 = i2.Kitchen6,
              i1.ItemImage = i2.ItemImage,
              i1.ItemImageFileType = i2.ItemImageFileType,
              i1.ManageInv = i2.ManageInv,
              i1.NonAlcohol = i2.NonAlcohol
          from TPPro.dbo.tblItem i1
            inner join TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Item i2 on i2.ID = i1.ID

          /*-------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

          set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblItem on

          insert into TPPro.dbo.tblItem (ID, IName, CategoryID, ApplyGST, ApplyPST, [Status], OpenItem, KitchenB, KitchenF, Bar, SideDish, Taste, IName2,
                                         ApplyPST2, BarCode, KitchenE, Alcohol, HourlyChargedItem, ScaleItem, OnlineItem, ItemDescription, ImageFilePath,
                                         RewardItem, GroupItem, Kitchen5, Kitchen6, ItemImage, ItemImageFileType, ManageInv, NonAlcohol)
          select i2.ID, isnull(i2.IName, ''n/a''), i2.CategoryID, i2.ApplyGST, i2.ApplyPST, i2.[Status], i2.OpenItem, i2.KitchenB, i2.KitchenF, i2.Bar, i2.SideDish, i2.Taste, 
                 isnull(i2.IName2, ''''), i2.ApplyPST2, isnull(i2.BarCode, ''''), i2.KitchenE, i2.Alcohol, i2.HourlyChargedItem, i2.ScaleItem, i2.OnlineItem, i2.ItemDescription, 
                 i2.ImageFilePath, i2.RewardItem, i2.GroupItem, i2.Kitchen5, i2.Kitchen6, i2.ItemImage, i2.ItemImageFileType, i2.ManageInv, i2.NonAlcohol
          from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Item i2
          where not exists (select *
                            from TPPro.dbo.tblItem i1
                            where i1.ID = i2.ID)
          order by i2.ID

          set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblItem off

        end

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblSizeGroup                                                                */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_SizeGroup]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        update sg1
        set sg1.SizeGroupName = isnull(sg2.SizeGroupName, ''n/a'')
        from TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup sg1
          inner join TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_SizeGroup sg2 on sg2.ID = sg1.ID

        /*---------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

        set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup on

        insert into TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup (ID, SizeGroupName)
        select sg2.ID, isnull(sg2.SizeGroupName, ''n/a'')
        from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_SizeGroup sg2
        where not exists (select *
                          from TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup sg1
                          where sg1.ID = sg2.ID)
        order by sg2.ID

        set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup off

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblSize                                                                     */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_Size]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Size t
                       where t.SizeGroupID > 0
                         and not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblSizeGroup sg
                                         where sg.ID = t.SizeGroupID)) begin

          update s1
          set s1.SizeName = isnull(s2.SizeName, ''n/a''),
              s1.ShortName = s2.ShortName,
              s1.DisplayOrder = s2.DisplayOrder,
              s1.SizeGroupID = isnull(s2.SizeGroupID, 0)
          from TPPro.dbo.tblSize s1
            inner join TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Size s2 on s2.ID = s1.ID

          /*-------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

          set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblSize on

          insert into TPPro.dbo.tblSize (ID, SizeName, ShortName, DisplayOrder, SizeGroupID)
          select s2.ID, isnull(s2.SizeName, ''n/a''), s2.ShortName, s2.DisplayOrder, isnull(s2.SizeGroupID, 0)
          from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_Size s2
          where not exists (select *
                            from TPPro.dbo.tblSize s1
                            where s1.ID = s2.ID)
          order by s2.ID

          set identity_insert TPPro.dbo.tblSize off

        end

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblAvailableSize                                                            */
      /*=============================================================================*/
     
      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblItem i
                                         where i.ID = t.ItemID)) 
           and
           not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblSize s
                                         where s.ID = t.SizeID)) begin

          --truncate table TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize

          --insert into TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC)
          --select ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC
          --from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize

          /* To exclude "OnHandQty", the delete/update/insert are done instead of truncate the table and insert */
          delete a
          from TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize a
          where not exists (select *
                            from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize t
                            where t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                              and t.SizeID = a.SizeID)        
        
          update a
          set a.UnitPrice = t.UnitPrice,
              a.ApplyNoDSC = t.ApplyNoDSC,
              a.UnitPrice2 = t.UnitPrice2,
              a.UnitPrice3 = t.UnitPrice3
          from TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize a
            inner join TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                                   and t.SizeID = a.SizeID        

          insert into TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize (ItemID, SizeID, UnitPrice, OnHandQty, ApplyNoDSC, UnitPrice2, UnitPrice3)
          select t.ItemID, t.SizeID, t.UnitPrice, t.OnHandQty, t.ApplyNoDSC, t.UnitPrice2, t.UnitPrice3
          from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_AvailableSize t
          where not exists (select *
                            from TPPro.dbo.tblAvailableSize a
                            where a.ItemID = t.ItemID
                              and a.SizeID = t.SizeID)

        end

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblDayHourDiscount                                                          */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_DayHourDiscount]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_DayHourDiscount t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblItem i
                                         where i.ID = t.ItemID)) 
           and
           not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_DayHourDiscount t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblSize s
                                         where s.ID = t.SizeID)) begin

          truncate table TPPro.dbo.tblDayHourDiscount

          insert into TPPro.dbo.tblDayHourDiscount (ItemID, SizeID, WeekDayIndex, ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice,
                                                    ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, 
                                                    HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice)
          select ItemID, SizeID, WeekDayIndex, ApplyDay, ApplyDayRate, ApplyDayPrice,
                 ApplyHour, ApplyHourRate, ApplyHourPrice, DayRate, DayPrice, HourFrom, 
                 HourTo, HourRate, HourPrice
          from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_DayHourDiscount

        end

      end

      /*=============================================================================*/
      /* tblSubItem                                                                  */
      /*=============================================================================*/

      if exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuItemsImport_SubItem]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

        if not exists (select *
                       from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_SubItem t
                       where not exists (select *
                                         from TPPro.dbo.tblItem i
                                         where i.ID = t.ItemID)) begin

          truncate table TPPro.dbo.tblSubItem

          insert into TPPro.dbo.tblSubItem (ItemID, SubItemDescription, PrintToKitchenIndex)
          select ItemID, isnull(SubItemDescription, ''n/a''), PrintToKitchenIndex
          from TPPro.dbo.tmpMenuItemsImport_SubItem
          order by ID

        end

      end

      /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

      declare curs_tmp_tables cursor for 
        select name
        from sys.objects 
        where type in (N''U'')
          and is_ms_shipped = 0
          and upper(name) like ''tmpMenuItemsImport_%''

        open curs_tmp_tables
        fetch next from curs_tmp_tables into @tmp_table_name
        while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

          set @script = ''drop table '' + @tmp_table_name
          exec sp_executesql @script

          fetch next from curs_tmp_tables into @tmp_table_name
        end
        close curs_tmp_tables
      deallocate curs_tmp_tables

      commit transaction apply_updated_item_info
      return 1
    end try

    begin catch
      rollback transaction apply_updated_item_info
      return 0
    end catch

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ImportMenuLayout]
  @MenuLayoutFileName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(1000), @data_file varchar(150) 

  set @data_file = @MenuLayoutFileName

  create table #tmp_file_exists 
  (
    file_exists int,
    file_is_a_directory int,
    parent_directory_exists int
  )

  insert into #tmp_file_exists
  exec master.dbo.xp_fileexist @data_file
  
  if exists (select *
             from #tmp_file_exists
             where file_exists = 1) begin

    if exists (select * 
               from sys.objects 
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpMenuLayoutImport]'')
                 and type in (N''U''))
      drop table tmpMenuLayoutImport 

    select *
    into tmpMenuLayoutImport
    from tblMenuLayout

    truncate table tmpMenuLayoutImport

    /* Import Menu Layout Data */
    set @script = ''bulk insert tmpMenuLayoutImport '' +
                  ''from '''''' + @data_file + '''''' '' +
                  ''with (fieldterminator = ''''\t'''', '' +
                        ''firstrow = 2, '' +
                        ''rowterminator = ''''\n'''')''
    exec sp_executesql @script
  
    drop table #tmp_file_exists

    if exists (select *
               from tmpMenuLayoutImport) begin

      delete
      from tblMenuLayout

      insert into tblMenuLayout
      select *
      from tmpMenuLayoutImport

    end

    drop table tmpMenuLayoutImport

    return 1

  end
  else begin

    return 0

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ImportTableLayout]
  @TableLayoutFileName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(1000), @data_file varchar(150) 

  set @data_file = @TableLayoutFileName
  
  create table #tmp_file_exists 
  (
    file_exists int,
    file_is_a_directory int,
    parent_directory_exists int
  )

  insert into #tmp_file_exists
  exec master.dbo.xp_fileexist @data_file

  if exists (select *
             from #tmp_file_exists
             where file_exists = 1) begin

    if exists (select * 
               from sys.objects 
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTableLayoutImport]'')
                 and type in (N''U''))
      drop table tmpTableLayoutImport 

    select tl.*, isnull(t.TableName, '''') as TableName, t.TakeOut, t.Delivery, t.[Online], t.StayOn, t.ApplySpecialPricing,  
           t.SpecialPricingRate, t.BellNumber, t.StationID, t.OnlineOrderCompanyID, t.AccessPermissionRequired, t.AppliedUnitPriceType
    into tmpTableLayoutImport
    from tblTableLayout tl
      left join tblTable t on tl.TableID = t.ID

    truncate table tmpTableLayoutImport

    /* Import Table Layout Data */
    set @script = ''bulk insert tmpTableLayoutImport '' +
                  ''from '''''' + @data_file + '''''' '' +
                  ''with (fieldterminator = ''''\t'''', '' +
                        ''firstrow = 2, '' +
                        ''rowterminator = ''''\n'''')''
    exec sp_executesql @script
  
    drop table #tmp_file_exists

    if exists (select *
               from tmpTableLayoutImport) begin

      delete 
      from tblTableLayout
      
      insert into tblTableLayout
      select [Level], TabIndex, ControlIndex, TableID, Caption, AlignTop, AlignLeft, Height, Width, FontName, FontSize, 
             FontBold, FontItalic, FontColor, Color, ImageFileName, TableImage, TableImageFileType, LayoutModeType
      from tmpTableLayoutImport

      update t
      set t.Linked = 1,
          t.TableName = tl.TableName,
          t.TakeOut = tl.TakeOut,
          t.Delivery = tl.Delivery,
          t.[Online] = tl.[Online],
          t.StayOn = tl.StayOn,
          t.ApplySpecialPricing = tl.ApplySpecialPricing,
          t.SpecialPricingRate = tl.SpecialPricingRate,
          t.BellNumber = tl.BellNumber,
          t.StationID = tl.StationID,
          t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = tl.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
          t.AccessPermissionRequired = tl.AccessPermissionRequired,
          t.AppliedUnitPriceType = tl.AppliedUnitPriceType
      from tblTable t
        inner join tmpTableLayoutImport tl on tl.TableID = t.ID

    end

    drop table tmpTableLayoutImport

    return 1

  end
  else begin

    return 0

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ResetForNewBranch]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  exec sp_ClearDatabase 0

  delete
  from tblCustomer
  where ID > 1  

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblCustomer'', RESEED, 1)

  update tblCustomer
  set FName = ''General'',
      LName = ''Customer'',
      CustomerNum = ''0'',
      DateEntered = getdate(),
      Gender = 1,
      Phone = '''',
      [Address] = '''',
      CardValue = 0,
      Savings = 0,
      LastVisit = getdate(),
      EarnedPoints = 0
  where ID = 1

  delete
  from tblCustomerGroup
  where ID > 1

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblCustomerGroup'', RESEED, 1)

  delete
  from tblCustomerType
  where ID > 1

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblCustomerType'', RESEED, 1)

  truncate table tblEmployeeWageHistory

  delete
  from tblUser
  where ID > 1

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblUser'', RESEED, 1)

  update tblUser
  set UserAccessCode = ''1'',
      LName = ''Admin'',
      FName = ''Admin'',
      GroupID = 1,
      [Status] = 1,
      [Address] = '''',
      Wage = 0,
      Memo = '''',
      LastClosingTime = getdate(),
      TipOutPercentage = 0
  where ID = 1

  delete
  from tblStation
  where ID > 1

  DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblStation'', RESEED, 1)

  update tblStation
  set StationName = ''POS1'',
      [Status] = 1,
      LastClosingTime = null,
      KitchenDisplay = 0
  where ID = 1

  delete
  from tblPeripherals
  where StationName <> ''POS1''

  update tblAvailableSize
  set OnHandQty = 0

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[ExtractTasteStringSeparatedByDelimiter]
(
	@TastesString varchar(2000),
  @Delimiter char(1)
)
RETURNS varchar(2000)
AS
BEGIN

  if (charindex(''|'', @TastesString) > 0) begin

    declare @strPart varchar(100), @ReturnString varchar(2000)

    set @ReturnString = ''''

    while (charindex(''|'', @TastesString) > 0) and (ltrim(rtrim(@TastesString)) <> ''|'') begin
      set @strPart = substring(@TastesString, 1, charindex(''|'', @TastesString) - 1)
      set @TastesString = substring(@TastesString, charindex(''|'', @TastesString) + 1, len(@TastesString) - len(@strPart) - 1)
      if (@ReturnString <> '''')
        set @ReturnString = @ReturnString + @Delimiter

      if (charindex(''_$'', @strPart) > 0) or (charindex(''_-$'', @strPart) > 0) or (charindex(''_($'', @strPart) > 0) begin
        if (charindex(''_-$'', @strPart) > 0)
          set @strPart = substring(@strPart, 1, charindex(''_-$'', @strPart) - 1)
        else if (charindex(''_($'', @strPart) > 0)
          set @strPart = substring(@strPart, 1, charindex(''_($'', @strPart) - 1)
        else
          set @strPart = substring(@strPart, 1, charindex(''_$'', @strPart) - 1)
      end
      else if (charindex(''_#'', @strPart) > 0)
        set @strPart = substring(@strPart, 1, charindex(''_#'', @strPart) - 1)

      set @ReturnString = @ReturnString + @strPart
    end 

    --if @ReturnString <> '''' 
    --  set @ReturnString = ''('' + @ReturnString + '')''
  end

  return @ReturnString

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_PriceUpdateGetItemList]
  @UnitPriceType tinyint,
  @RefreshList bit,
  @CopyOtherUnitPrice bit,
  @CopyUnitPriceType tinyint,
  @ApplyPercentage float
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate table (
	  [DisplayCategoryName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [CatName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryRank] [bigint] NULL,
	  [DisplayItemName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [IName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [ItemRank] [bigint] NULL,
	  [SizeName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [OldPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [CurrentPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [NewPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryGroupNo] [bigint] NULL,
	  [ItemGroupNo] [bigint] NULL
  )

  declare @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate table (
	  [DisplayCategoryName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [CatName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryID] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryRank] [bigint] NULL,
	  [DisplayItemName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [IName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [ItemID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [ItemRank] [bigint] NULL,
	  [SizeName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [SizeID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [OldPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [CurrentPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [NewPrice] [smallmoney] NOT NULL,
	  [CategoryGroupNo] [bigint] NULL,
	  [ItemGroupNo] [bigint] NULL
  )

  if (@UnitPriceType = 1) begin

    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice1Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      insert into @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate
      select *
      from tmpItemListForPrice1Update

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 2) begin

    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice2Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      insert into @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate
      select *
      from tmpItemListForPrice2Update

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 3) begin

    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice3Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      insert into @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate
      select *
      from tmpItemListForPrice3Update

    end

  end 

  if (@RefreshList = 1) begin

    insert into @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate (DisplayCategoryName, CatName, CategoryID, CategoryRank, 
                                            DisplayItemName, IName, ItemID, ItemRank, 
                                            SizeName, SizeID, OldPrice, CurrentPrice, NewPrice, CategoryGroupNo, ItemGroupNo)
    select case when CategoryRank = 1 then CatName else '''' end as DisplayCategoryName, CatName, CategoryID, CategoryRank,
           case when ItemRank = 1 then IName else '''' end as DisplayItemName, IName, ItemID, ItemRank,
           SizeName, SizeID, OldPrice, CurrentPrice, NewPrice, CategoryGroupNo, ItemGroupNo
    from (select c.CatName, c.ID as CategoryID, 
                 row_number() over(partition by c.CatName order by i.IName, s.SizeName) as CategoryRank,
                 i.IName, i.ID as ItemID, 
                 row_number() over(partition by c.CatName, i.IName, i.ID order by s.SizeName) as ItemRank,
                 case when s.ID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName, s.ID as SizeID, 
                 case @UnitPriceType when 1 then isnull(l.OldPrice, a.UnitPrice) 
                                     when 2 then isnull(l.OldPrice, a.UnitPrice2)
                                     when 3 then isnull(l.OldPrice, a.UnitPrice3)
                                     else isnull(l.OldPrice, a.UnitPrice) 
                 end as OldPrice,
                 case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice 
                                     when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                     when 3 then a.UnitPrice3
                                     else a.UnitPrice
                 end as CurrentPrice, 
                 case @UnitPriceType when 1 then case when @CopyOtherUnitPrice = 1 then
                                                        case @CopyUnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                when 3 then a.UnitPrice3
                                                                                else a.UnitPrice
                                                        end
                                                      else a.UnitPrice
                                                 end
                                     when 2 then case when @CopyOtherUnitPrice = 1 then
                                                        case @CopyUnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                when 3 then a.UnitPrice3
                                                                                else a.UnitPrice2
                                                        end
                                                      else a.UnitPrice2
                                                 end
                                     when 3 then case when @CopyOtherUnitPrice = 1 then
                                                        case @CopyUnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice
                                                                                when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                                                                when 3 then a.UnitPrice3
                                                                                else a.UnitPrice3
                                                        end
                                                      else a.UnitPrice3
                                                 end
                                     else a.UnitPrice
                 end as NewPrice,
                 dense_rank() over(order by c.CatName) as CategoryGroupNo,
                 dense_rank() over(partition by c.ID order by i.IName, i.ID) as ItemGroupNo
          from tblCategory c
            inner join tblItem i on i.CategoryID = c.ID
            inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
            inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
            left join @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate l on l.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                       and l.SizeID = a.SizeID 
          where i.[Status] = 1
            and exists (select 1
                        from tblMenuLayout ml 
                        where ml.ItemID = i.ID)) t

  end
  else begin

    insert into @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate (DisplayCategoryName, CatName, CategoryID, CategoryRank, 
                                            DisplayItemName, IName, ItemID, ItemRank, 
                                            SizeName, SizeID, OldPrice, CurrentPrice, NewPrice, CategoryGroupNo, ItemGroupNo)
    select case when CategoryRank = 1 then CatName else '''' end as DisplayCategoryName, CatName, CategoryID, CategoryRank,
           case when ItemRank = 1 then IName else '''' end as DisplayItemName, IName, ItemID, ItemRank,
           SizeName, SizeID, OldPrice, CurrentPrice, NewPrice, CategoryGroupNo, ItemGroupNo
    from (select c.CatName, c.ID as CategoryID, 
                 row_number() over(partition by c.CatName order by i.IName, s.SizeName) as CategoryRank,
                 i.IName, i.ID as ItemID, 
                 row_number() over(partition by c.CatName, i.IName, i.ID order by s.SizeName) as ItemRank,
                 case when s.ID = 1 then '''' else s.SizeName end as SizeName, s.ID as SizeID,
                 isnull(l.OldPrice, a.UnitPrice) as OldPrice, 
                 case @UnitPriceType when 1 then a.UnitPrice 
                                     when 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                                     when 3 then a.UnitPrice3
                                     else a.UnitPrice
                 end as CurrentPrice, 
                 isnull(l.NewPrice, a.UnitPrice) * case when @ApplyPercentage <> 0 then (1.0 + (@ApplyPercentage/100.0)) 
                                                        else 1 
                                                   end as NewPrice,
                 dense_rank() over(order by c.CatName) as CategoryGroupNo,
                 dense_rank() over(partition by c.ID order by i.IName, i.ID) as ItemGroupNo
          from tblCategory c
            inner join tblItem i on i.CategoryID = c.ID
            inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
            inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
            left join @tmpSavedItemListForPriceUpdate l on l.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                       and l.SizeID = a.SizeID 
          where i.[Status] = 1
            and exists (select 1
                        from tblMenuLayout ml 
                        where ml.ItemID = i.ID)) t

  end


  declare @CatName varchar(30), @CategoryID tinyint, @ItemGroupNo int, @AddValue int

  set @AddValue = 0
   
  declare curs_item_list cursor for 
    select CatName, CategoryID, max(ItemGroupNo) 
    from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate
    group by CatName, CategoryID
    order by CatName, CategoryID

    open curs_item_list
    fetch next from curs_item_list into @CatName, @CategoryID, @ItemGroupNo
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update t
      set t.ItemGroupNo = t.ItemGroupNo + @AddValue
      from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate t
      where t.CategoryID = @CategoryID

      set @AddValue = @AddValue + @ItemGroupNo
      
      fetch next from curs_item_list into @CatName, @CategoryID, @ItemGroupNo
    end
    close curs_item_list
  deallocate curs_item_list



  if (@UnitPriceType = 1) begin
      
    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice1Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U''))

      drop table tmpItemListForPrice1Update

    select *
    into tmpItemListForPrice1Update
    from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 2) begin
      
    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice2Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U'')) 

      drop table tmpItemListForPrice2Update

    select *
    into tmpItemListForPrice2Update
    from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate
      
  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 3) begin
      
    if exists (select *
                from sys.objects
                where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice3Update]'')
                  and [type] in (N''U'')) 

      drop table tmpItemListForPrice3Update

    select *
    into tmpItemListForPrice3Update
    from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate
      
  end

  select *
  from @tmpItemListForPriceUpdate
  order by CatName, CategoryRank, IName, ItemRank, SizeName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_PriceUpdateUpdateNewPrice]
  @UnitPriceType tinyint,
  @ItemID int,
  @SizeID int,
  @NewPrice smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@UnitPriceType = 1) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice1Update]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      update tmpItemListForPrice1Update
      set NewPrice = @NewPrice
      where ItemID = @ItemID
        and SizeID = @SizeID

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 2) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects

                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      update tmpItemListForPrice2Update
      set NewPrice = @NewPrice
      where ItemID = @ItemID
        and SizeID = @SizeID

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 3) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice3Update]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      update tmpItemListForPrice3Update
      set NewPrice = @NewPrice
      where ItemID = @ItemID
        and SizeID = @SizeID

    end

  end

END'
