EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_PriceUpdateApplyNewPrice]
  @UnitPriceType tinyint,
  @Reverse bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@UnitPriceType = 1) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice1Update]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      if (@Reverse = 1) begin
      
        update a
        set a.UnitPrice = t.OldPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice1Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice <> t.OldPrice

        update t
        set t.NewPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice1Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.OldPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice1Update t

      end
      else begin

        update a
        set a.UnitPrice = t.NewPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice1Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice <> t.NewPrice

        update t
        set t.OldPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice1Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.NewPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice1Update t

      end

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 2) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice2Update]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      if (@Reverse = 1) begin
      
        update a
        set a.UnitPrice2 = t.OldPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice2Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice2 <> t.OldPrice

        update t
        set t.NewPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice2Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.OldPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice2Update t

      end
      else begin

        update a
        set a.UnitPrice2 = t.NewPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice2Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice2 <> t.NewPrice

        update t
        set t.OldPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice2Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.NewPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice2Update t

      end

    end

  end
  else if (@UnitPriceType = 3) begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemListForPrice3Update]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      if (@Reverse = 1) begin
      
        update a
        set a.UnitPrice3 = t.OldPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice3Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice3 <> t.OldPrice

        update t
        set t.NewPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice3Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.OldPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice3Update t

      end
      else begin

        update a
        set a.UnitPrice3 = t.NewPrice
        from tblAvailableSize a
          inner join tmpItemListForPrice3Update t on t.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                                 and t.SizeID = a.SizeID
        where a.UnitPrice3 <> t.NewPrice

        update t
        set t.OldPrice = t.CurrentPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice3Update t

        update t
        set t.CurrentPrice = t.NewPrice
        from tmpItemListForPrice3Update t

      end

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetailBySelectedDates]
  @BySelectedDates bit,
  @FromDate smalldatetime,
  @ToDate smalldatetime,
  @Barcode varchar(30)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT staterments.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ID int

  declare @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 table
  (
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    Barcode varchar(30),
    TransDateTime smalldatetime,
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int
  )

  declare @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 table
  (
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    Barcode varchar(30),
    TransDateTime smalldatetime,
    Credit smallmoney,
    Debit smallmoney,
    Balance smallmoney,
    SalesID int,
    RemainingBalance smallmoney
  )

  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 (Barcode, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID)
  select Barcode, ChargeDate as TransDateTime, Amount as Credit, null as Debit, null as Balance, SalesID
  from tblPrepaidCardChargeHistory
  where case when @Barcode <> '''' then 
               case when Barcode = @Barcode then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by Barcode, TransDateTime

  /* Didn''t use "union all" to make sure the charge records are inserted before use records for the case that the time is the same */
  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1 (Barcode, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID)
  select Barcode, DateTimeUsed as TransDateTime, null as Credit, AmtUsed as Debit, Balance, SalesID
  from tblPrepaidCardUsageHistory
  where case when @Barcode <> '''' then 
               case when Barcode = @Barcode then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by Barcode, TransDateTime

  insert into @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 (Barcode, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, RemainingBalance)
  select Barcode, TransDateTime, Credit, Debit, Balance, SalesID, 0
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail1
  order by Barcode, TransDateTime, ID

  declare curs_detail cursor for
    select Barcode, ID
    from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2
    order by Barcode, ID

    open curs_detail
    fetch next from curs_detail into @Barcode, @ID
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update t
      set t.Balance = isnull(t.Credit, 0) - isnull(t.Debit, 0)
                      + isnull((select t2.Balance
                                from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t2
                                where t2.Barcode = t.Barcode 
                                  and t2.ID = case when t.ID > 1 then t.ID - 1
                                                   else 0
                                              end), 0)
      from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t
      where t.Barcode = @Barcode
        and t.ID = @ID
      
      fetch next from curs_detail into @Barcode, @ID
    end
    close curs_detail
  deallocate curs_detail

  update t
  set t.RemainingBalance = isnull(t.Balance, 0)
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t
  where exists (select max(t2.ID)
                from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t2
                where t2.Barcode = t.Barcode
                  and case when @BySelectedDates = 1 then
                             case when t2.TransDateTime >= convert(varchar, @FromDate, 112) and
                                       t2.TransDateTime <  dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDate, 112)) then 1 else 0 end
                           else 1
                      end = 1
                group by t2.Barcode
                having max(t2.ID) = t.ID)

  update t
  set t.RemainingBalance = t2.RemainingBalance
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t
    inner join (select Barcode, sum(RemainingBalance) as RemainingBalance
                from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 
                group by Barcode) t2 on t2. Barcode = t.Barcode

  select t.*, c.ID as CustomerID, c.FName, c.LName, c.CustomerNum, c.Phone
  from @tmpPrepaidCardCreditDebitDetail2 t
    inner join tblPrepaidCards p on t.Barcode = p.Barcode
    inner join tblCustomer c on p.CustomerID = c.ID
  where case when @BySelectedDates = 1 then
               case when t.TransDateTime >= convert(varchar, @FromDate, 112) and
                         t.TransDateTime <  dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, @ToDate, 112)) then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1
  order by t.Barcode, t.ID

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MaximizeNumberOfTables]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @NumberOfExtraDineInTables smallint, @NumberOfExtraTakeOutTables smallint, @TotalNumberOfExtraTables smallint

  set @TotalNumberOfExtraTables = 0

  select @NumberOfExtraDineInTables = 999 - count(*)
  from tblTable
  where ID <= 200
     or (ID > 300 and ID <= 1099)

  select @NumberOfExtraTakeOutTables = 999 - count(*)
  from tblTable
  where (ID > 200 and ID <= 300)
     or (ID > 1099 and ID <= 1998)

  set @TotalNumberOfExtraTables = @NumberOfExtraDineInTables + @NumberOfExtraTakeOutTables

  while (@TotalNumberOfExtraTables > 0) begin

    insert into tblTable (OrderNum, Linked, TimeIn, ServerID, NumOfGuests, Opened, TableName, PickupTime, PhoneNum, PickupPerson, 
                          TakeOut, BillPrinted, Attention, DailyOrdNum, BellNumber, CallType, Delivery, [Online], StayOn, PickupDate, 
                          TotalAmt, ApplySpecialPricing, SpecialPricingRate, StationID, StationIDInUse, OnlineOrderCompanyID, 
                          AccessPermissionRequired, AppliedUnitPriceType)
    values(0, 0, getdate(), 0, 0, 0, '''', '''', '''', '''', 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 255, 0, 0, 0, null, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1)

    set @TotalNumberOfExtraTables = @TotalNumberOfExtraTables - 1

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MinimizeNumberOfTables]
  @ExtraDineInTablesUsed bit output,
  @ExtraTakeOutTablesUsed bit output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @FromExtraTableID smallint, @ToExtraTableID smallint, @MaxTableID smallint

  set @ExtraDineInTablesUsed = 0
  set @ExtraTakeOutTablesUsed = 0
    
  set @FromExtraTableID = 1100
  set @ToExtraTableID = 1998

  if exists (select *
             from tblSales
             where TableID >= @FromExtraTableID
               and TableID <= @ToExtraTableID) or
     exists (select *
             from tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans
             where TableID >= @FromExtraTableID
               and TableID <= @ToExtraTableID) begin

    set @ExtraTakeOutTablesUsed = 1

  end
  else begin

    delete l
    from tblTableLayout l
      inner join tblTable t on l.TableID = t.ID
    where t.ID >= @FromExtraTableID
      and t.ID <= @ToExtraTableID

    delete t
    from tblTable t
    where t.ID >= @FromExtraTableID
      and t.ID <= @ToExtraTableID
   

    set @FromExtraTableID = 301
    set @ToExtraTableID = 1099

    if exists (select *
               from tblSales
               where TableID >= @FromExtraTableID
                 and TableID <= @ToExtraTableID) or
       exists (select *
               from tblPreAuthorizedCardTrans
               where TableID >= @FromExtraTableID
                 and TableID <= @ToExtraTableID) begin

      set @ExtraDineInTablesUsed = 1

    end
    else begin

      delete l
      from tblTableLayout l
        inner join tblTable t on l.TableID = t.ID
      where t.ID >= @FromExtraTableID
        and t.ID <= @ToExtraTableID

      delete t
      from tblTable t
      where t.ID >= @FromExtraTableID
        and t.ID <= @ToExtraTableID      

    end

    select @MaxTableID = max(ID)
    from tblTable 

    DBCC CHECKIDENT(''tblTable'', RESEED, @MaxTableID)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spcrm_SyncRewardPointsDetail]
  @StoreID int, 
  @SyncNumberOfDays tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT staterments.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @ID int

  if exists (select *
             from sys.objects
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[rpt_RewardPointsDetail]'')
               and [type] in (N''U''))
    drop table rpt_RewardPointsDetail

  create table rpt_RewardPointsDetail(
    ID int IDENTITY(1,1) NOT NULL,
    StoreID int,
    CustomerNum varchar(20),
    TransDateTime varchar(20),
    Earned int,
    Redeemed int,
    SumUp int,
    Balance int,
    CurrentBalance int,
    SalesID int
  )

  insert into rpt_RewardPointsDetail (StoreID, CustomerNum, TransDateTime, Earned, Redeemed, SumUp, Balance, CurrentBalance, SalesID)
  select @StoreID, c.CustomerNum, convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 120), d.PointSaved, d.PointUsed, d.PointSaved - d.PointUsed, null, c.EarnedPoints, d.SalesID
  from tblPointsDetail d
    inner join tblSales s on d.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblCustomer c on s.CustomerID = c.ID
  where s.SaleDateTime >= convert(varchar, dateadd(d, -@SyncNumberOfDays, getdate()), 112)
    and s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and c.ID > 1
  order by s.SaleDateTime

  update t
  set t.Balance = t.CurrentBalance
  from rpt_RewardPointsDetail t
  where exists (select 1
                from rpt_RewardPointsDetail t2
                where t2.CustomerNum = t.CustomerNum
                group by t2.CustomerNum
                having max(t2.ID) = t.ID)

  declare curs_detail cursor for
    select ID
    from rpt_RewardPointsDetail
    where Balance is null
    order by ID desc

    open curs_detail
    fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

      update t
      set t.Balance = (select isnull(t2.Balance, 0)
                       from rpt_RewardPointsDetail t2
                       where t2.CustomerNum = t.CustomerNum
                         and t2.Balance is not null
                         and exists (select 1
                                     from rpt_RewardPointsDetail t3 
                                     where t3.CustomerNum = t2.CustomerNum
                                       and t3.Balance is not null
                                       and t3.ID > t.ID
                                     group by t3.CustomerNum
                                     having min(t3.ID) = t2.ID)) - t.SumUp
      from rpt_RewardPointsDetail t
      where t.ID = @ID
      
      fetch next from curs_detail into @ID
    end
    close curs_detail
  deallocate curs_detail

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_ResetInventory]
  @CategoryID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblInventoryChangeHistory) begin

    insert into tblInventoryChangeHistory (ItemID, SizeID, OnHandQty, AppliedQty, SalesID, ChangedDateTime, UserID)
    select h.ItemID, h.SizeID, a.OnHandQty, case when a.OnHandQty < 0 then 1 else -1 end * abs(a.OnHandQty), 0, getdate(), 1
    from tblInventoryChangeHistory h
      inner join tblAvailableSize a on h.ItemID = a.ItemID
                                   and h.SizeID = a.SizeID
      inner join tblItem i on h.ItemID = i.ID
    where case when @CategoryID > 0 then 
                 case when i.CategoryID = @CategoryID then 1 else 0 end
               else 1
          end = 1
      and a.OnHandQty <> 0
      and exists (select h2.ItemID, h2.SizeID
                  from tblInventoryChangeHistory h2
                  group by h2.ItemID, h2.SizeID
                  having max(h2.ID) = h.ID)

  end

  update a
  set a.OnHandQty = 0
  from tblAvailableSize a
    inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
  where case when @CategoryID > 0 then 
               case when i.CategoryID = @CategoryID then 1 else 0 end
             else 1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_MoveUnlinkedItems]
  @FromCategoryID tinyint,
  @ToCategoryID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction move_unlinked_items
          
    update i
    set i.CategoryID = @ToCategoryID,
        i.Status = 0
    from tblItem i
    where i.CategoryID = @FromCategoryID
      and not exists (select 1
                      from tblMenuLayout ml
                      where ml.ItemID = i.ID)

    commit transaction move_unlinked_items
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction move_unlinked_items
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeactivateUnlinkedItems]
  @CategoryID tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin try
    begin transaction deactivate_unlinked_items
          
    update i
    set i.Status = 0
    from tblItem i
    where i.CategoryID = @CategoryID
      and not exists (select 1
                      from tblMenuLayout ml
                      where ml.ItemID = i.ID)

    commit transaction deactivate_unlinked_items
  end try

  begin catch
    rollback transaction deactivate_unlinked_items
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[CheckIfAnyTimeChargedItemStopped]
(
	@SalesID int
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Exists bit

  if exists (select t.* 
             from tblTimeStartEnd t
             where t.SalesID = @SalesID
               and not exists (select *
                               from tblTimeStartEnd t2
                               where t2.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                 and t2.ItemID = t.ItemID
                                 and t2.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
                                 and t2.Stopped = 0))

    set @Exists = 1

  else 

    set @Exists = 0

  return @Exists

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_SalesSummaryByItemInMinuteInterval]
  @FromDateTime datetime, 
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @BusinessHourFrom tinyint, 
  @BusinessHourTo tinyint,
  @MaxMinuteInterval tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @DateInterval smalldatetime, @HourInterval tinyint, @MinuteInterval tinyint,
          @SaleDate datetime, @NumOfMinutes tinyint, @IntervalDescription varchar(50)

  --set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  --set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  --set @BusinessHourFrom = 10 
  --set @BusinessHourTo = 22
  --set @MaxMinuteInterval = 4

  set @FromDateTime = convert(varchar, @FromDateTime, 112) 
  set @ToDateTime = convert(varchar, @ToDateTime, 112)   
  set @NumOfMinutes = 60 / @MaxMinuteInterval

  if (@BusinessHourFrom >= 0) and (@BusinessHourFrom <= 23) and (@BusinessHourTo >= 1) and (@BusinessHourTo <= 24) and (@MaxMinuteInterval > 0) begin

    if (@BusinessHourFrom < @BusinessHourTo) and (60 % @MaxMinuteInterval = 0) begin

      declare @DateIntervals table (
        SaleDate smalldatetime
      )

      declare @HourIntervals table (
        HourInterval tinyint,
        HourIn12h tinyint
      )

      declare @MinuteIntervals table (
        MinuteInterval tinyint,
        TimeIntervalFrom varchar(20),
        TimeIntervalTo varchar(20)
      )

      if exists (select *
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpDatesByTimeInterval]'') 
                   and type in (N''U''))
        drop table tmpDatesByTimeInterval

      create table tmpDatesByTimeInterval (
        SaleDate smalldatetime,
        HourInterval tinyint,
        HourIn12h tinyint,
        MinuteInterval tinyint,
        TimeIntervalFrom varchar(20),
        TimeIntervalTo varchar(20)
      )

      CREATE UNIQUE NONCLUSTERED INDEX [idx_interval] ON [dbo].[tmpDatesByTimeInterval] 
      (
        [SaleDate] ASC,
        [HourInterval] ASC,
        [MinuteInterval] ASC
      )WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, DROP_EXISTING = OFF, ONLINE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]

      if exists (select *
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpSalesByTimeInterval]'') 
                   and type in (N''U''))
        drop table tmpSalesByTimeInterval

      create table tmpSalesByTimeInterval (
        SaleDate smalldatetime,
        HourInterval tinyint,
        MinuteInterval tinyint,
        ItemName varchar(30),
        SizeName varchar(30),
        SoldQty int,
        ExtPrice money
      )

      CREATE CLUSTERED INDEX [idx_interval2] ON [dbo].[tmpSalesByTimeInterval] 
      (
        [SaleDate] ASC,
        [HourInterval] ASC,
        [MinuteInterval] ASC
      )WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, SORT_IN_TEMPDB = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, DROP_EXISTING = OFF, ONLINE = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]

      set @SaleDate = @FromDateTime
      while (@SaleDate >= @FromDateTime) and (@SaleDate < @ToDateTime) begin
        insert into @DateIntervals (SaleDate)
        values (@SaleDate)
        set @SaleDate = dateadd(d, 1, @SaleDate)
      end

      set @HourInterval = @BusinessHourFrom
      while (@HourInterval < @BusinessHourTo) begin
        insert into @HourIntervals (HourInterval, HourIn12h)
        values (@HourInterval, case when @HourInterval = 0 then 12 
                                    when @HourInterval > 12 then @HourInterval - 12 
                                    else @HourInterval
                               end) 
        set @HourInterval = @HourInterval + 1
      end

      set @MinuteInterval = 1
      while (@MinuteInterval <= @MaxMinuteInterval) begin
        insert into @MinuteIntervals (MinuteInterval, TimeIntervalFrom, TimeIntervalTo)
        values (@MinuteInterval,  
                case when @MinuteInterval = 1 then ''hh:00'' else ''hh:'' + convert(varchar, (@MinuteInterval - 1) * @NumOfMinutes) end,
                case when @MinuteInterval = @MaxMinuteInterval then ''hh:00'' else ''hh:'' + convert(varchar, @MinuteInterval * @NumOfMinutes) end)
        set @MinuteInterval = @MinuteInterval + 1
      end

      insert into tmpDatesByTimeInterval (SaleDate, HourInterval, HourIn12h, MinuteInterval, TimeIntervalFrom, TimeIntervalTo)
      select s.SaleDate, h.HourInterval, h.HourIn12h, m.MinuteInterval,      
             replace(m.TimeIntervalFrom, ''hh'', replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h))) + convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h)) + 
             case when (h.HourInterval < 12) then '' AM'' else '' PM'' end,
             case when m.MinuteInterval < @MaxMinuteInterval then 
                    replace(m.TimeIntervalTo, ''hh'', replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h))) + convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h)) 
                  else 
                    case when (h.HourInterval = 0 or h.HourInterval = 12) then
                           replace(m.TimeIntervalTo, ''hh'', ''01'')
                         else
                           replace(m.TimeIntervalTo, ''hh'', replicate(''0'', 2 - len(convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h + 1))) + convert(varchar, h.HourIn12h + 1))
                    end
             end + 
             case when h.HourInterval < 12 then
                    case when h.HourInterval = 11 and m.MinuteInterval = @MaxMinuteInterval then '' PM'' else '' AM'' end
                  else
                    case when h.HourInterval = 23 and m.MinuteInterval = @MaxMinuteInterval then '' AM'' else '' PM'' end
             end
      from @DateIntervals s
        inner join @HourIntervals h on 1 = 1
        inner join @MinuteIntervals m on 1 = 1

      insert into tmpSalesByTimeInterval (SaleDate, HourInterval, MinuteInterval, ItemName, SizeName, SoldQty, ExtPrice)
      select convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 112) as SaleDate, 
             (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) + 1) as SaleHour, 
             ((datepart(n, s.SaleDateTime) / @NumOfMinutes) + 1) as Interval, 
             i.IName, 
             case when z.ID > 1 then z.SizeName else '''' end as SizeName, 
             sum(sd.Qty) as SoldQty, 
             sum((sd.Qty * sd.UnitPrice)) as ExtPrice
      from tblSales s
        inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = s.ID
        inner join tblItem i on sd.ItemID = i.ID
        inner join tblSize z on sd.SizeID = z.ID
      where s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
        and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
        and sd.Voided = 0
      group by convert(varchar, s.SaleDateTime, 112), 
               (datepart(hh, s.SaleDateTime) + 1), 
               ((datepart(n, s.SaleDateTime) / @NumOfMinutes) + 1), 
               i.IName, 
               case when z.ID > 1 then z.SizeName else '''' end

      --select t.*, isnull(s.ItemName, '''') as ItemName, isnull(s.SizeName, '''') as SizeName, 
      --       isnull(s.SoldQty, 0) as SoldQty, isnull(s.ExtPrice, 0) as ExtPrice
      select t.SaleDate, t.HourInterval, t.TimeIntervalFrom + '' - '' + t.TimeIntervalTo, 
             isnull(s.ItemName, '''') as ItemName, isnull(s.SizeName, '''') as SizeName, 
             isnull(s.SoldQty, 0) as SoldQty, isnull(s.ExtPrice, 0) as ExtPrice
      from tmpDatesByTimeInterval t
        left join tmpSalesByTimeInterval s on s.SaleDate = t.SaleDate
                                          and s.HourInterval = t.HourInterval
                                          and s.MinuteInterval = t.MinuteInterval
      order by t.SaleDate, t.HourInterval, t.MinuteInterval, s.SoldQty, s.ExtPrice

      drop table tmpDatesByTimeInterval
      drop table tmpSalesByTimeInterval

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_BackupAndRestoreTablesWithOrderForTableLayout]
  @Step tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if @Step = 1 begin

    update tblTable
    set Opened = 1
    where Linked = 1

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTable_Backup]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U''))

      drop table tmpTable_Backup

    select *
    into tmpTable_Backup
    from tblTable
    where OrderNum > 0

    --select *
    --from tmpTable_Backup

    update tblTable
    set OrderNum = 0
    where OrderNum > 0

  end
  else if @Step = 2 begin

    if exists (select *
               from sys.objects
               where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpTable_Backup]'')
                 and [type] in (N''U'')) begin

      update t
      set t.OrderNum = b.OrderNum,
	      t.Linked = b.Linked,
	      t.TimeIn = b.TimeIn,
	      t.ServerID = b.ServerID,
	      t.NumOfGuests = b.NumOfGuests,
	      t.Opened = b.Opened,
	      t.TableName = b.TableName,
	      t.PickupTime = b.PickupTime,
	      t.PhoneNum = b.PhoneNum,
	      t.PickupPerson = b.PickupPerson,
	      t.TakeOut = b.TakeOut,
	      t.BillPrinted = b.BillPrinted,
	      t.Attention = b.Attention,
	      t.DailyOrdNum = b.DailyOrdNum,
	      t.BellNumber = b.BellNumber,
	      t.CallType = b.CallType,
	      t.Delivery = b.Delivery,
	      t.Online = b.Online,
	      t.StayOn = b.StayOn,
	      t.PickupDate = b.PickupDate,
	      t.TotalAmt = b.TotalAmt,
	      t.ApplySpecialPricing = b.ApplySpecialPricing,
	      t.SpecialPricingRate = b.SpecialPricingRate,
	      t.StationID = b.StationID,
	      t.StationIDInUse = b.StationIDInUse,
	      t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = b.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
	      t.AccessPermissionRequired = b.AccessPermissionRequired,
	      t.AppliedUnitPriceType = b.AppliedUnitPriceType
      from tblTable t
        inner join tmpTable_Backup b on b.ID = t.ID

      drop table tmpTable_Backup

    end

    update tblTable
    set Opened = 0 
    where Linked = 1

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule]
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint,
  @NewSaleTotalUpTo money,
  @NewCommissionPercentage decimal(4,2),
  @ResetCommissionRule bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @SaleTotalFrom money, @SaleTotalUpTo money, @CommissionPercentage decimal(4,2)
  
  if (@ResetCommissionRule = 1) or
     not exists (select *
                 from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
                 where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID) begin

    delete 
    from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
    where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID

    insert into tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule (OnlineOrderCompanyID, CommissionIndex, SaleTotalFrom, SaleTotalUpTo, CommissionPercentage)
    values (@OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0, 0, null, 0)

  end

  if (@NewSaleTotalUpTo > 0.01) begin

    select @SaleTotalFrom = SaleTotalFrom,
           @SaleTotalUpTo = SaleTotalUpTo,
           @CommissionPercentage = CommissionPercentage
    from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
    where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
      and SaleTotalFrom + 0.01 <= @NewSaleTotalUpTo
      and (SaleTotalUpTo is null
           or 
           SaleTotalUpTo - 0.01 > @NewSaleTotalUpTo)

    if (@SaleTotalFrom is not null) begin

      update tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
      set SaleTotalUpTo = @NewSaleTotalUpTo,
          CommissionPercentage = @NewCommissionPercentage       
      where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
        and SaleTotalFrom = @SaleTotalFrom
        and isnull(SaleTotalUpTo, -1) = isnull(@SaleTotalUpTo, -1)

      insert into tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule (OnlineOrderCompanyID, CommissionIndex, SaleTotalFrom, SaleTotalUpTo, CommissionPercentage)
      values (@OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0, @NewSaleTotalUpTo + 0.01, @SaleTotalUpTo, @CommissionPercentage)

      select *, rank() over(order by SaleTotalFrom) as OrderedCommissionIndex
      into #tmpCommissionOrdering
      from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
      where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID

      update c
      set c.CommissionIndex = t.OrderedCommissionIndex
      from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule c
        inner join #tmpCommissionOrdering t on c.SaleTotalFrom = t.SaleTotalFrom
      where c.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID

      drop table #tmpCommissionOrdering

    end

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule]
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select OnlineOrderCompanyID, 
         CommissionIndex, 
         convert(varchar, SaleTotalFrom, 1) as SaleTotalFrom, 
         case when SaleTotalUpTo is null then ''Max.''
              else convert(varchar, SaleTotalUpTo, 1) 
         end as SaleTotalUpTo, 
         CommissionPercentage
  from tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
  where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
  order by CommissionIndex

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'

  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint,
  @CommissionIndex tinyint,
  @CommissionPercentage decimal(4,2)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  update tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule
  set CommissionPercentage = @CommissionPercentage
  where OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
    and CommissionIndex = @CommissionIndex

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfScheduledOrderPrintingStationExists]
  @StationName varchar(20)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select *
  from tblPeripherals p
    inner join tblStation s on upper(p.StationName) = upper(s.StationName)
  where p.Code = ''PSO''
    and upper(p.Value) = ''TRUE''
    and upper(p.StationName) <> upper(@StationName)
    and s.Status = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_GetEncodedHashedKey]
  @key varchar(1000),
  @salt varchar(1000) output,
  @encoded_hashed_key varchar(1000) output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @seed int, @lcv tinyint, @cTime datetime, @hashed_key varbinary(max)

  set @cTime = getdate()
  set @seed = (datepart(hh, @cTime) * 10000000) + (datepart(n, @cTime) * 100000) + (datepart(s, @cTime) * 1000) + datepart(ms, @cTime)
  set @lcv = 1
  set @salt = char(round((rand(@seed) * 94.0) + 32, 3))

  while (@lcv < 25) begin
    set @salt = @salt + char(round((rand() * 94.0) + 32, 3))
    set @lcv = @lcv + 1
  end

  /* MD2 | MD4 | MD5 | SHA | SHA1 | SHA2_256 | SHA2_512 */
  set @hashed_key = HashBytes(''SHA1'', @key + @salt) /* authentication answer is "123456". it is hashed by SHA2_256 hash */
  --set @hashed_answer = HashBytes(''MD5'', ''123456'') /* authentication answer is "123456". it is hashed by MD5 hash */
  set @encoded_hashed_key = cast(N'''' as xml).value(''xs:base64Binary(xs:hexBinary(sql:variable("@hashed_key")))'', ''varchar(max)'') /* then hashed answer is encoded by Base64 */

  /*
  declare @decoded_hashed_key varchar(max)

  set @decoded_hashed_key = cast(cast(N'''' as xml).value(''xs:base64Binary(sql:variable("@encoded_hashed_key"))'', ''varbinary(max)'') as varchar(max))

  select @decoded_hashed_key
  */

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertCallHistory]
  @CallerNumber varchar(20),
  @CallerName varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblCallHistory (CallerNumber, CallerName, CalledDateTime)
  select @CallerNumber, @CallerName, getdate()
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblCallHistory
                    where CallerNumber = @CallerNumber
                      and datediff(s, CalledDateTime, getdate()) < 10)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetCallHistory]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select top 10 CallerNumber, CallerName,  
                substring(convert(varchar, CalledDateTime, 109), 13, 8) + '' '' + 
                substring(convert(varchar, CalledDateTime, 109), 25, 2) as CalledDateTime
  from tblCallHistory
  where CalledDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)
  order by ID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_ExportCustomers]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @script nvarchar(2000), @export_file_nm varchar(500), 
          @file_creation_str varchar(1000), @bcp_parameter varchar(1000)

  set @export_file_nm = ''Customers_List_Exported_'' + convert(varchar, getdate(), 112) + ''.csv''

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpCustomerListExport]'')
               and type in (N''U''))
    drop table tmpCustomerListExport

  select 0 as ID, cast('''' as varchar(2000)) as CustomerInfo
  into tmpCustomerListExport

  truncate table tmpCustomerListExport
  
  insert into tmpCustomerListExport (ID, CustomerInfo)
  select 0, 
         ''First Name'' + char(44) + ''Last Name'' + char(44) + ''Customer No.'' + char(44) +
         ''Created Date'' + char(44) + ''Phone'' + char(44) + 
         ''Address'' + char(44) + ''Note'' + char(44) + ''Last Visit''

  insert into tmpCustomerListExport (ID, CustomerInfo)
  select cast(1 as int) as ID,
         ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.FName, ''''))) collate database_default + char(44) +
         ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.LName, ''''))) collate database_default + char(44) + 
         ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.CustomerNum, ''''))) collate database_default + char(44) + 
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.DateEntered, ''''), 112), 5, 2) + ''/'' +
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.DateEntered, ''''), 112), 7, 2) + ''/'' +
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.DateEntered, ''''), 112), 1, 4) + char(44) +  
         ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.Phone, ''''))) collate database_default + char(44) +  
         replace(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.Address, ''''))), '','', '''') collate database_default + char(44) + 
         replace(ltrim(rtrim(isnull(c.CustomerNote, ''''))), '','', '''') collate database_default + char(44) + 
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.LastVisit, ''''), 112), 5, 2) + ''/'' +
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.LastVisit, ''''), 112), 7, 2) + ''/'' +
         substring(convert(varchar, isnull(c.LastVisit, ''''), 112), 1, 4) as CustomerInfo
  from TPPro.dbo.tblCustomer c
  where c.ID > 1
  order by c.FName, c.LName

  select *
  from tmpCustomerListExport
  order by ID

--  set @script = ''select CustomerInfo '' +
--                ''from TPPlus.dbo.tmpCustomerListExport '' +
--                ''order by ID''
--
--  set @file_creation_str = ''echo '''''''' > C:\TopPos\Reports\'' + @export_file_nm
--  set @bcp_parameter = ''bcp "'' + @script + ''" queryout "C:\TopPos\Reports\'' + @export_file_nm + ''" -c -T -x'' 
--
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @file_creation_str
--  exec master..xp_cmdshell @bcp_parameter

--  drop table tmpCustomerListExport

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetUnlinkedItems]
  @LayoutModeType tinyint,
  @TasteGroupItem bit,
  @TasteItemID smallint
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@TasteGroupItem = 1) begin

    select s.ID, i.CategoryID, s.SizeName as ItemName, cast(case when ml.ItemID is null then 0 else 1 end as bit) as LinkedStatus
    from tblItem i
      inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = i.ID
      inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
      left join (select *
                 from tblMenuLayout
                 where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
                   and [Level] = 3
                   and Taste = 1
                   and ItemID = @TasteItemID) ml on ml.ItemID = i.ID
                                                and ml.NextItemID = a.SizeID
    where i.ID = @TasteItemID
      and ml.ItemID is null
    order by s.SizeName

  end
  else begin

    select i.ID, i.CategoryID, case when isnull(i.IName2, '''') <> '''' then i.IName + '' ('' + i.IName2 + '')'' else i.IName end as ItemName,
           cast(case when ml.ItemID is null then 0 else 1 end as bit) as LinkedStatus
    from tblItem i
      left join (select ItemID
                 from tblMenuLayout
                 where LayoutModeType = @LayoutModeType
                 group by ItemID) ml on ml.ItemID = i.ID
    where i.[Status] = 1
      and ml.ItemID is null
    order by i.ID desc

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[CheckIfSplitTimeChargeItemExists]
(
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @PersonIndex tinyint
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Exists bit

  if exists (select 1
             from tblPendingOrders
             where SalesID = @SalesID
               and ItemID = @ItemID
               and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
               and SideDishes like ''SPLIT_[HT]_%'')
 
    set @Exists = 1

  else
 
    set @Exists = 0

  return @Exists

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[CheckIfTimeChargingStopped]
(
  @SalesID int,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @PersonIndex tinyint 
)
RETURNS bit
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @Stopped bit

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblPendingOrders po
                   inner join tblTimeStartEnd t on po.SalesID = t.SalesID
                                               and po.ItemID = t.ItemID
                                               and po.PersonIndex = t.PersonIndex
                 where po.SalesID = @SalesID
                   and case when @ItemID > 0 then
                              case when po.ItemID = @ItemID then 1 else 0 end
                            else 
                              1
                       end = 1
                   and po.PersonIndex = @PersonIndex
                   and t.Stopped = 0)
  
    set @Stopped = 1

  else
 
    set @Stopped = 0

  return @Stopped	

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CreateDineInSelfOrderCode]
  @TableID smallint,
  @DineInSelfOrderCode varchar(1000) output,
  @ExtendTime bit,
  @NewExpiryDateTime varchar(20) output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if (@ExtendTime = 0) begin

    declare @StrTableID varchar(20), @HashSalt varchar(1000), @ExpiryDateTime smalldatetime, @ExpirationType tinyint

    select @ExpirationType = case when isnull(convert(tinyint, Value), 0) = 0 then 1 else convert(tinyint, Value) end
    from tblMisc
    where Code = ''SOCET''

    if (@ExpirationType = 1) begin

      if exists (select *
                 from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
                 where TableID = @TableID) begin

        update tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
        set ExpiryDateTime = dateadd(yy, 20, getdate())
                 
      end 

    end
    else if (@ExpirationType = 2 and 
             exists (select *
                     from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
                     where TableID = @TableID
                       and ExpiryDateTime <> dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)))) 
            or
            (@ExpirationType = 3) begin
     
      delete
      from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
      where TableID = @TableID

    end
    
    if not exists (select *
                   from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
                   where TableID = @TableID) begin   
    
      set @StrTableID = convert(varchar, @TableID)

      exec spx_GetEncodedHashedKey @StrTableID, @HashSalt output, @DineInSelfOrderCode output

      set @ExpiryDateTime = case @ExpirationType when 1 then dateadd(yy, 20, getdate())
                                                 when 2 then dateadd(d, 1, convert(varchar, getdate(), 112))
                                                 when 3 then dateadd(hh, 2, getdate())
                            end

      insert into tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode (TableID, HashSalt, DineInSelfOrderCode, ExpiryDateTime)
      values (@TableID, @HashSalt, @DineInSelfOrderCode, @ExpiryDateTime)    

    end
    else begin

      select @DineInSelfOrderCode = DineInSelfOrderCode
      from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
      where TableID = @TableID

    end

  end
  else begin
    
    update tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
    set ExpiryDateTime = case @ExpirationType when 3 then
                                                case when dateadd(hh, 1, ExpiryDateTime) < dateadd(hh, 2, getdate()) then 
                                                       dateadd(hh, 1, ExpiryDateTime) 
                                                     else 
                                                       ExpiryDateTime
                                                end
                                              else ExpiryDateTime
                         end
    where TableID = @TableID

    select @NewExpiryDateTime = substring(convert(varchar, ExpiryDateTime, 109), 13, 5) + '' '' +
                                substring(convert(varchar, ExpiryDateTime, 109), 25, 2)
    from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
    where TableID = @TableID  

  end  

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[GetDineInSelfOrderTableID]
(
	@DineInSelfOrderCode varchar(1000)
)
RETURNS smallint
AS
BEGIN
	
  declare @TableID smallint

  select @TableID = TableID
  from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
  where DineInSelfOrderCode = @DineInSelfOrderCode
    and ExpiryDateTime >= getdate()
   
  return isnull(@TableID, -1)

END'
GO

	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.

  delete
  from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
  where TableID = @TableID

END'

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetDineInSelfOrderCode]
  @TableID smallint,
  @DineInSelfOrderCode varchar(1000) output
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select @DineInSelfOrderCode = DineInSelfOrderCode
  from tblTableDineInSelfOrderCode
  where TableID = @TableID
    and ExpiryDateTime >= getdate()

  set @DineInSelfOrderCode = isnull(@DineInSelfOrderCode, '''')

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_SalesOfOnlineOrdersSummary]
  @OnlineOrderCompanyName varchar(50),
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint

  select @OnlineOrderCompanyID = ID
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany
  where upper(ltrim(rtrim(CompanyName))) = upper(ltrim(rtrim(@OnlineOrderCompanyName)))

  if isnull(@OnlineOrderCompanyID, 0) > 0 begin

    set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
    set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  
    /*****************************************************************************************************/
    /* Sales Summary                                                                                     */
    /*****************************************************************************************************/

    select o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, c.CompanyName, c.[Integrated], s.TransType, 
           case when s.TransType = 0 then ''Refund''
                when s.TransType = 1 then ''Sale''
                --when s.TransType = 2 then ''NoSale''
                when s.TransType = 3 then ''Void''
                when s.TransType = 4 then ''SalesVoid''
                --when s.TransType = 5 then ''Training''
                --when s.TransType = 9 then ''Unpaid''
                else '''' 
           end as TransTypeDescription,
           isnull(count(s.TransType),0) as TransCount,
           sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt,
           sum(round(isnull(s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt,
           sum(round(isnull(s.GSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax1Amt,
           sum(round(isnull(s.PSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax2Amt,
           sum(round(isnull(s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as Tax3Amt,
           sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt,
           case s.TransType when 0 then -1 when 1 then 1 else 0 end * isnull(sum(s.Guests),0) as GuestCount
    into #tmp_online_order_sales
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
      inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany c on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
    where s.TransType in (0, 1, 3, 4)
      and o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
      and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    group by o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, c.CompanyName, c.[Integrated], s.TransType

    /*****************************************************************************************************/
    /* Payment Summary                                                                                   */
    /*****************************************************************************************************/

    select o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, s.TransType, p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType,
           count(p.PaymentTypeID) as PaymentCount,
           sum(round(isnull(p.PaidAmount,0),2)) as PaidAmount,
           sum(round(isnull(p.TipAmount,0),2)) as TipAmount
    into #tmp_online_order_payments
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
      inner join tblPaymentType pt on p.PaymentTypeID = pt.ID
      inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    where s.TransType in (0, 1, 3, 4)
      --and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      --and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      and p.Voided = 0
    group by o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, s.TransType, p.PaymentTypeID, pt.PaymentType

    /*****************************************************************************************************/
    /* Commission Summary                                                                                */
    /*****************************************************************************************************/

    select o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A'') as CommissionCalculationType,
           s.TransType, ((year(s.SaleDateTime) * 100) + month(s.SaleDateTime)) as SaleYearMonth,
           sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt         
    into #tmp_online_order_sales_subtotal
    from tblSales s
      inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
      inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
      --inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = s.ID
    where s.TransType in (0, 1)
      and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      --and p.PaidDateTime >= @FromDateTime
      --and p.PaidDateTime <  @ToDateTime
    group by o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A''), 
             s.TransType, ((year(s.SaleDateTime) * 100) + month(s.SaleDateTime))

    select os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
           sum(case when os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) then 
                      round((os.SubTotalAmt - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)
                    else 
                      case when os.SubTotalAmt > isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, 0) then 
                             round((isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, 0) - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2) 
                           else 0 
                      end
               end) as CommissionOnSubTotalAmt
    into #tmp_online_order_sales_for_commission
    from #tmp_online_order_sales_subtotal os    
      left join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
    where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''A''
    group by os.OnlineOrderCompanyID

    insert into #tmp_online_order_sales_for_commission
    select os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
           sum(round(os.SubTotalAmt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionOnSubTotalAmt
    from #tmp_online_order_sales_subtotal os    
      inner join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                       and os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) 
                                                       and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt)
    where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''B''
    group by os.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  
    /*****************************************************************************************************/
    /* Summary                                                                                           */
    /*****************************************************************************************************/  

    select ts.CompanyName, ts.TransTypeDescription, ts.TransCount, ts.SubTotalAmt, ts.DSCAmt, ts.Tax1Amt, ts.Tax2Amt, ts.Tax3Amt, ts.TotalAmt, 
           --isnull(tp.PaymentTypeID, 0) as PaymentTypeID, 
           isnull(tp.PaymentType, ''N/A'') as PaymentType, 
           isnull(tp.PaymentCount, 0) as PaymentCount, 
           isnull(tp.PaidAmount, 0) as PaidAmount, 
           isnull(tp.TipAmount, 0) as TipAmount, 
           isnull(tc.CommissionOnSubTotalAmt, 0) as CommissionOnSubTotalAmt
    from #tmp_online_order_sales ts
      left join #tmp_online_order_payments tp on tp.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                             and tp.TransType = ts.TransType
      left join #tmp_online_order_sales_for_commission tc on tc.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID
    order by ts.CompanyName, tp.PaymentType
  
    drop table #tmp_online_order_sales
    drop table #tmp_online_order_payments
    drop table #tmp_online_order_sales_subtotal
    drop table #tmp_online_order_sales_for_commission

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertUpdateNonIntegratedOnlineSelfPaymentURL]
  @SalesID int,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @SelfPaymentURL varchar(4000)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select *
                 from tblNonIntegratedOnlineSelfPaymentURL
                 where SalesID = @SalesID
                   and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex) begin

    insert into tblNonIntegratedOnlineSelfPaymentURL (SalesID, PersonIndex, SelfPaymentURL)
    values (@SalesID, @PersonIndex, @SelfPaymentURL)

  end
  else begin

    update tblNonIntegratedOnlineSelfPaymentURL
    set SelfPaymentURL = @SelfPaymentURL
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex

  end

END'

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_UpdateIncludedTipForAdditionalOnlineOrder]
	@SalesID int,
  @PersonIndex tinyint,
  @IncludedTipAmt smallmoney
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  begin transaction update_included_tip_amount

  if exists (select *
             from tblTipAmountInBill
             where SalesID = @SalesID
               and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex) begin

    update tblTipAmountInBill
    set IncludedTipAmt = IncludedTipAmt + @IncludedTipAmt
    where SalesID = @SalesID
      and PersonIndex = @PersonIndex

  end
  else begin

    insert into tblTipAmountInBill (SalesID, PersonIndex, IncludedTipAmt)
    values (@SalesID, @PersonIndex, @IncludedTipAmt)

  end

  if (@@error = 0) begin
    commit transaction update_included_tip_amount
    return 1
  end
  else begin
    rollback transaction update_included_tip_amount
    return 0
  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_DailySalesOfOnlineOrdersSummary]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime,
  @ByTime bit
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* This was modifed from "spr_SalesOfOnlineOrdersSummary"                                            */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/

  declare @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation bit, @Tax1Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax2Rate decimal(5, 4), @Tax3Rate decimal(5, 4), @HoursShifted smallint

  set @FromDateTime = dbo.GetFromDateTime(@FromDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @ToDateTime = dbo.GetToDateTime(@ToDateTime, @ByTime)
  set @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation = convert(bit, dbo.GetMiscValue(''IDOCC''))

  if (dbo.IsStoreClosedAfterMidnight() = 1)
    set @HoursShifted = -6
  else
    set @HoursShifted = 0
  
  select distinct top 1 @Tax1Rate = GSTRate, 
                        @Tax2Rate = PSTRate, 
                        @Tax3Rate = PST2Rate
  from tblSales
  where SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
      
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Sales Summary                                                                                     */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/

  select convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, SaleDateTime), 112)) as SaleDate,
         o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ooc.CompanyName, isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A'') as CommissionCalculationType,
         isnull(count(s.TransType),0) as TransCount,
         sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as SubTotalAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.DSCAmt,0),2)) as DSCAmt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.GSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax1Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.PSTAmt,0),2)) as Tax2Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as Tax3Amt,
         sum(round(isnull(s.SubTotal - s.DSCAmt + s.GSTAmt + s.PSTAmt + s.PST2Amt,0),2)) as TotalAmt,
         sum(isnull(s.Guests,0)) as GuestCount
  into #tmp_online_order_sales
  from tblSales s
    inner join tblSalesOfOnlineOrders o on o.SalesID = s.ID
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where s.TransType in (0, 1)
    and case when @IncludeDineInOrdersInCommissionCalculation = 1 then 1
             else case when o.DineInOrder = 0 then 1 else 0 end
        end = 1
    and s.SaleDateTime >= @FromDateTime
    and s.SaleDateTime <  @ToDateTime
  group by convert(smalldatetime, convert(varchar(8), dateadd(hh, @HoursShifted, s.SaleDateTime), 112)),
           o.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ooc.CompanyName, isnull(ooc.CommissionCalculationType, ''A'')

  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Commission Summary                                                                                */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  
  select os.SaleDate, os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
         sum(case when os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) then 
                    round((os.SubTotalAmt - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)
                  else 
                    case when os.SubTotalAmt > isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) then 
                           round((isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt) - isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0)) * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2) 
                         else 0 
                    end
             end) as CommissionSubTotal,
         sum(round(os.Tax1Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax1,
         sum(round(os.Tax2Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax2,
         sum(round(os.Tax3Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax3
  into #tmp_online_order_commission
  from #tmp_online_order_sales os    
    left join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''A''
  group by os.SaleDate, os.OnlineOrderCompanyID

  insert into #tmp_online_order_commission
  select os.SaleDate, os.OnlineOrderCompanyID,
         sum(round(os.SubTotalAmt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionSubTotal,
         sum(round(os.Tax1Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax1,
         sum(round(os.Tax2Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax2,
         sum(round(os.Tax3Amt * (isnull(cr.CommissionPercentage, 0) / 100.0), 2)) as CommissionTax3
  from #tmp_online_order_sales os    
    inner join tblOnlineOrderCompanyCommissionRule cr on os.OnlineOrderCompanyID = cr.OnlineOrderCompanyID
                                                     and os.SubTotalAmt >= isnull(cr.SaleTotalFrom, 0) 
                                                     and os.SubTotalAmt <= isnull(cr.SaleTotalUpTo, os.SubTotalAmt)
  where os.CommissionCalculationType = ''B''
  group by os.SaleDate, os.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  
  /*****************************************************************************************************/
  /* Summary                                                                                           */
  /*****************************************************************************************************/  

  select ts.SaleDate, ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID, ts.CompanyName, ts.TransCount, 
         ts.SubTotalAmt, ts.DSCAmt, ts.Tax1Amt, ts.Tax2Amt, ts.Tax3Amt, ts.TotalAmt, ts.GuestCount,
         isnull(tc.CommissionSubTotal, 0) as CommissionSubTotal,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax1, 0) as CommissionTax1,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax2, 0) as CommissionTax2,
         isnull(tc.CommissionTax3, 0) as CommissionTax3,
         isnull(tc.CommissionSubTotal, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax1, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax2, 0) +
             isnull(tc.CommissionTax3, 0) as CommissionTotal
  from #tmp_online_order_sales ts
    left join #tmp_online_order_commission tc on tc.SaleDate = ts.SaleDate
                                             and tc.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ts.OnlineOrderCompanyID
  order by ts.SaleDate, ts.CompanyName
  
  drop table #tmp_online_order_sales
  drop table #tmp_online_order_commission

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetKitchenDisplayItems]
  @StationID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select case when CategoryRank = 1 then CatName else '''' end as DisplayCategoryName, 
         CatName, IName, 
         case when [Status] = 0 then ''Inactive'' else '''' end as ItemStatus,
         ItemID, CategoryGroupNo, ItemGroupNo
  from (select c.CatName, c.ID as CategoryID, 
                row_number() over(partition by c.CatName order by i.IName) as CategoryRank,
                i.IName, i.ID as ItemID, i.[Status],
                dense_rank() over(order by c.CatName) as CategoryGroupNo,
                row_number() over(order by c.CatName, i.IName) as ItemGroupNo
        from tblKitchenDisplayItems kdi
          inner join tblItem i on kdi.ItemID = i.ID
          inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
        where kdi.StationID = @StationID) t
  order by CatName, CategoryRank, IName 

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_InsertKitchenDisplayItem]
  @StationID smallint,
  @ItemID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  insert into tblKitchenDisplayItems (StationID, ItemID)
  select @StationID, @ItemID
  where not exists (select *
                    from tblKitchenDisplayItems
                    where StationID = @StationID
                      and ItemID = @ItemID)

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_DeleteKitchenDisplayItem]
  @StationID smallint,
  @ItemID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  delete
  from tblKitchenDisplayItems
  where StationID = @StationID
    and case when @ItemID > 0 then 
               case when ItemID = @ItemID then 1 else 0 end
             else 
               1
        end = 1

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetIntegratedOnlineOrderCompanyWithPendingOrders]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select c.CompanyName as OnlineOrderCompany, count(o.OrderID) as PendingOrderCount
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany c
    inner join (select *
                from tblOnlineOrders
                where CreateDateTime >= convert(varchar, getdate(), 112)
                  and CreateDateTime <  dateadd(s, -10, getdate())
                  and [Status] = 1
                  and isnull(SalesID, 0) = 0) o on o.OnlineOrderCompanyID = c.ID
  where c.[Integrated] = 1
  group by c.CompanyName

  if exists (select *
             from tblOnlineOrders
             where OrderType = ''DINEIN''
               and CreateDateTime >= dateadd(n, -1, getdate())
               and [Status] = 1) begin

    exec spws_InsertOnlineOrders 0, '''', 0, ''''

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetIntegratedOnlineOrderInfo]
  @SalesID int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  /* This is used to print information on Bills and Receipts */
  select cast(case when upper(o.OrderType) = ''DELIVERY'' then 1 else 0 end as bit) as DeliveryOrder,
         case when upper(o.OrderType) = ''DELIVERY'' then
                substring(ltrim(rtrim(o.DeliveryLine1 + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryLine2 + char(13) + char(10) +
                                      o.DeliveryCity + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryState + '' '' + 
                                      o.DeliveryZipCode)), 
                          1, 500) /* substring length was originally 200 (tblCustomer.Address field size)
                                     but this is just for printing purpose only. so, increased to 500 */
              else '''' /* Address is supposed to be printed only for delivery orders. so, blank for non delivery order type */
         end as DeliveryAddress,
         substring(ltrim(rtrim(ltrim(rtrim(o.UserComments)) + 
                               case when ltrim(rtrim(o.UserComments)) <> '''' then char(13) + char(10) else '''' end)), 
                   1, 1000) as UserComments /* Same reason as DeliveryAddress. originally it was 255 */
  from tblOnlineOrders o
  where o.SalesID = @SalesID
    and o.[Status] = 0
  order by o.OrderID desc

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spr_GetSalesTransactionsWithDetail]
  @FromDateTime datetime,
  @ToDateTime datetime
AS
BEGIN
  SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from sys.objects
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmp_transactions]'') 
               and [type] in (N''U'')) 

    drop table tmp_transactions

  CREATE TABLE [dbo].[tmp_transactions](
	  [ID] [int] NOT NULL,
	  [CashierID] [smallint] NOT NULL,
	  [SaleDateTime] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	  [SubTotalAmt] [money] NOT NULL,
	  [DSCAmt] [money] NOT NULL,
	  [GSTAmt] [money] NOT NULL,
	  [PSTAmt] [money] NOT NULL,
	  [PST2Amt] [money] NOT NULL,
	  [TotalAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [CashPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [DebitPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [VisaPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
