	  [CouponTipPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [GiftCardTipPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [TotalTipPaidAmt] [money] NULL,
	  [TransType] [varchar](9) NOT NULL,
	  [OriginalTransType] [tinyint] NOT NULL,
	  [DailyOrderNumber] [int] NOT NULL,
	  [TableName] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
	  [Cashier] [varchar](61) NULL,
	  [Customer] [varchar](100) NULL,
	  [CustomerNum] [varchar](20) NOT NULL,
	  [CustomerPhone] [varchar](20) NULL,
	  [PaymentCount] [tinyint] NULL,
	  [StationName] [varchar](30) NOT NULL,
	  [CreatedDateTime] [datetime] NOT NULL,
	  [OnlineOrderNumber] [varchar](20) NOT NULL,
	  [OnlineOrderCustomerName] [varchar](100) NOT NULL,
	  [OnlineOrderCompanyName] [varchar](50) NOT NULL,
    [DiscrepancyExists] [bit] NOT NULL
  ) ON [PRIMARY]

  insert into tmp_transactions
  exec spr_GetSalesTransactions @FromDateTime, @ToDateTime, 1, '''', 0

  select t.*, sd.ItemName, sd.ItemName2, case when sd.SizeID > 1 then sd.SizeName else '''' end as SizeName, 
         sd.Qty, sd.UnitPrice, isnull(sd.Tastes, '''') as Tastes, row_number() over(partition by t.ID order by sd.SequenceNo) as SalesDetailItemOrder 
  into #tmp_transactions_with_detail
  from tmp_transactions t
    inner join tblSalesDetail sd on sd.SalesID = t.ID
  --order by t.ID, sd.SequenceNo, sd.ItemName, SizeName

  update t
  set t.SaleDateTime = '''',
      t.SubTotalAmt = 0,
      t.DSCAmt = 0,
      t.GSTAmt = 0,
      t.PSTAmt = 0,
      t.PST2Amt = 0,
      t.TotalAmt = 0,
      t.CashPaidAmt = 0,
      t.DebitPaidAmt = 0,
      t.VisaPaidAmt = 0,
      t.McPaidAmt = 0,
      t.AmexPaidAmt = 0,
      t.CouponPaidAmt = 0,
      t.DiscoverPaidAmt = 0,
      t.JcbPaidAmt = 0,
      t.GiftCardPaidAmt = 0,
      t.RewardPointPaidAmt = 0,
      t.ChargeOnAccountPaidAmt = 0,
      t.CashTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.DebitTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.CreditTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.CouponTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.GiftCardTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.ChargeOnAccountTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.TotalTipPaidAmt = 0,
      t.TransType = '''',
      t.DailyOrderNumber = 0,
      t.TableName = '''',
      t.Cashier = '''',
      t.Customer = '''',
      t.CustomerNum = '''',
      t.CustomerPhone = '''',
      t.StationName = ''''
  from #tmp_transactions_with_detail t
  where t.SalesDetailItemOrder > 1

  select *
  from #tmp_transactions_with_detail
  order by ID, SalesDetailItemOrder

  drop table tmp_transactions
  drop table #tmp_transactions_with_detail

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spws_SyncOnlineItemUnitPrice]
  @OnlineOrderCompanyID smallint,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @UnitPriceType tinyint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @tmpConfiguration table (
    name varchar(500),
    minimum int,
    maximum int,
    config_value int,
    run_value int
  )
  insert into @tmpConfiguration
  exec sp_configure

  if not exists (select *
                 from @tmpConfiguration
                 where name = ''Ole Automation Procedures''
                   and config_value = 1) begin

    exec sp_configure ''show advanced options'', 1
    reconfigure
    exec sp_configure ''Ole Automation Procedures'', 1
    reconfigure
    
  end

  if not exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

    create table [dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult](
      CategoryID tinyint,
      ItemID smallint,
      SizeID smallint,
      CategoryName varchar(30),
      ItemName varchar(30),
      SizeName varchar(30),
      UnitPrice smallmoney,
      StatusCode varchar(32),
      StatusText varchar(32),
      ResponseText varchar(2000)
    )

  end

  declare @EndpointURL varchar(1000), @AuthHeader varchar(500), @ContentType varchar(100), @ContentEncoding varchar(50), 
          @JsonData varchar(1000), @Token int, @ReturnVal int, @SyncCategoryID tinyint, @SyncItemID smallint, @SyncSizeID smallint, 
          @SyncCategoryName varchar(30), @SyncItemName varchar(30), @SyncSizeName varchar(30), @SyncUnitPrice smallmoney,
          @StatusCode varchar(32), @StatusText varchar(32), @ResponseText varchar(2000), @AppendResult bit

  select @EndpointURL = ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL,
         @AuthHeader = APITransactionKey        
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany
  where ID = @OnlineOrderCompanyID
  
  set @ContentType = ''application/json''
  set @ContentEncoding = ''utf-8''
  set @AppendResult = 0
  
  begin try

    -- Open the connection.
    exec @ReturnVal = sp_OACreate ''MSXML2.ServerXMLHTTP'', @Token out
    if @ReturnVal <> 0 raiserror(''Unable to open HTTP connection.'', 10, 1)

    declare curs_items cursor for
      select i.CategoryID, a.ItemID, a.SizeID, c.CatName, i.IName, s.SizeName,
             case when @UnitPriceType = 1 then a.UnitPrice
                  when @UnitPriceType = 2 then a.UnitPrice2
                  when @UnitPriceType = 3 then a.UnitPrice3
             end as UnitPrice
      from tblAvailableSize a
        inner join tblItem i on a.ItemID = i.ID
        inner join tblSize s on a.SizeID = s.ID
        inner join tblCategory c on i.CategoryID = c.ID
      where i.[Status] = 1
        and case when @ItemID > 0 then 
                   case when a.ItemID = @ItemID and a.SizeID = @SizeID then 1 else 0 end
                 else 1
            end = 1
        and exists (select 1
                    from tblMenuLayout ml 
                    where ml.ItemID = i.ID)

      open curs_items
      fetch next from curs_items into @SyncCategoryID, @SyncItemID, @SyncSizeID, @SyncCategoryName, @SyncItemName, @SyncSizeName, @SyncUnitPrice
      while (@@fetch_status = 0) begin

        set @JsonData = ''{"posId":"'' + convert(varchar, @SyncItemID) + ''","posName":"'' + convert(varchar, @SyncSizeID) + ''","price":"'' + convert(varchar, @SyncUnitPrice) + ''"}''

        -- Send the request.
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAMethod @Token, ''open'', null, ''PUT'', @EndpointURL, ''false''
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAMethod @Token, ''setRequestHeader'', null, ''authorization'', @AuthHeader
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAMethod @Token, ''setRequestHeader'', null, ''Content-Type'', @ContentType
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAMethod @Token, ''setRequestHeader'', null, ''ContentEncoding'', @ContentEncoding
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAMethod @Token, ''send'', null, @JsonData

        -- Handle the response.
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAGetProperty @Token, ''status'', @StatusCode out
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAGetProperty @Token, ''statusText'', @StatusText out
        exec @ReturnVal = sp_OAGetProperty @Token, ''responseText'', @ResponseText out
        
        -- Record the response.
        --print ''Status: '' + @Status + '' ('' + @StatusText + '')''
        --print ''Response text: '' + @ResponseText
        --if (@ItemID = 0) begin        
        --  insert into tmpItemInfoSyncResult (CategoryID, ItemID, SizeID, CategoryName, ItemName, SizeName, UnitPrice, StatusCode, StatusText, ResponseText)
        --  values (@SyncCategoryID, @SyncItemID, @SyncSizeID, @SyncCategoryName, @SyncItemName, @SyncSizeName, @SyncUnitPrice, @StatusCode, @StatusText, @ResponseText)        
        --end
        exec spws_InsertItemUnitPriceSyncToOnlineResult @AppendResult, @SyncCategoryID, @SyncItemID, @SyncSizeID, @SyncCategoryName, 
                                                        @SyncItemName, @SyncSizeName, @SyncUnitPrice, @StatusCode, @StatusText, @ResponseText
        set @AppendResult = 1

        fetch next from curs_items into @SyncCategoryID, @SyncItemID, @SyncSizeID, @SyncCategoryName, @SyncItemName, @SyncSizeName, @SyncUnitPrice
      end
      close curs_items
    deallocate curs_items

    -- Close the connection.
    exec @ReturnVal = sp_OADestroy @Token
    if @ReturnVal <> 0 raiserror(''Unable to close HTTP connection.'', 10, 1)
  
    if (@ItemID = 0) begin
      /*
      exec spws_GetItemUnitPriceSyncToOnlineResult
      */
      return 1
    end
    else begin
      if (@StatusCode = ''201'')
        return 1
      else
        return 0
    end    

  end try

  begin catch

    return 0    
  
  end catch

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_GetIntegratedOnlineOrderCompanyWithAPIEndpoint]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  select ooc.ID as OnlineOrderCompanyID, ooc.CompanyName, t.AppliedUnitPriceType
  from tblOnlineOrderCompany ooc
    inner join (select distinct OnlineOrderCompanyID, AppliedUnitPriceType /* Supposed to have only one unit price type assigned to all linked tables for each online order company */
                from tblTable
                where OnlineOrderCompanyID > 0) t on t.OnlineOrderCompanyID = ooc.ID
  where ooc.[Status] = 1
    and ooc.[Integrated] = 1
    and ltrim(rtrim(isnull(ooc.APITransactionKey, ''''))) <> ''''
    and ltrim(rtrim(isnull(ooc.ItemInfoSyncAPIEndpointURL, ''''))) <> ''''
  order by ooc.CompanyName

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spws_GetItemUnitPriceSyncToOnlineResult]
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult]'')
               and type in (N''U'')) begin
    
    select CategoryID, ItemID, SizeID, CategoryName, ItemName, SizeName, UnitPrice, StatusCode, 
           replace(replace(StatusText, ''HTTP/1.1'', ''''), StatusCode, '''') as StatusText, 
           replace(replace(ResponseText, ''<message>'', ''''), ''</message>'', '''') as ResponseText
    from tmpItemInfoSyncResult
    order by CategoryName, ItemName, SizeName

    --select t.*, case when m.ItemID is null then ''Button not linked'' else ''Button linked'' end as ItemButtonLinkedOrNot
    --from tmpItemInfoSyncResult t
    --  inner join tblAvailableSize a on a.ItemID = t.ItemID
    --                               and a.SizeID = t.SizeID
    --  left join (select distinct ItemID
    --             from tblMenuLayout) m on m.ItemID = t.ItemID
    --order by CategoryName, ItemName, SizeName

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spws_InsertItemUnitPriceSyncToOnlineResult]
  @AppendResult bit,
  @CategoryID tinyint,
  @ItemID smallint,
  @SizeID smallint,
  @CategoryName varchar(30),
  @ItemName varchar(30),
  @SizeName varchar(30),
  @UnitPrice smallmoney,
  @StatusCode varchar(32),
  @StatusText varchar(32),
  @ResponseText varchar(2000)
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if not exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin

    create table [dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult](
      CategoryID tinyint,
      ItemID smallint,
      SizeID smallint,
      CategoryName varchar(30),
      ItemName varchar(30),
      SizeName varchar(30),
      UnitPrice smallmoney,
      StatusCode varchar(32),
      StatusText varchar(32),
      ResponseText varchar(2000)
    )

  end

  if exists (select * 
             from sys.objects 
             where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpItemInfoSyncResult]'')
               and type in (N''U'')) begin

    if (@AppendResult = 0)
      truncate table tmpItemInfoSyncResult

    insert into tmpItemInfoSyncResult (CategoryID, ItemID, SizeID, CategoryName, ItemName, SizeName, UnitPrice, StatusCode, StatusText, ResponseText)
    values (@CategoryID, @ItemID, @SizeID, @CategoryName, @ItemName, @SizeName, @UnitPrice, @StatusCode, @StatusText, @ResponseText)

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_CheckIfAnyPaymentExists]
  @TableID smallint
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  if exists (select *
             from tblTable t
               inner join tblPayment p on p.SalesID = t.OrderNum
             where t.ID = @TableID
               and p.PaidAmount > 0) begin

    return 1

  end
  else begin

    return 0

  end

END'
GO

EXEC dbo.sp_executesql @statement = N'
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[spx_DropMaxSQLServerMemoryTemporarily]
  @MinimumWaitTimeToRelease int
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

  declare @memory_usage_in_KB int, @seconds_passed_since_dropped int

  select @memory_usage_in_KB = cntr_value
  from sys.dm_os_performance_counters
  where counter_name = ''Total Server Memory (KB)''

  if not exists (select * 
                 from sys.objects 
                 where object_id = OBJECT_ID(N''[dbo].[tmpSQLServerMaxMemoryDroppedDateTime]'')
                   and type in (N''U'')) begin
    
    create table tmpSQLServerMaxMemoryDroppedDateTime (
      DroppedDateTime datetime
    )

    insert into tmpSQLServerMaxMemoryDroppedDateTime (DroppedDateTime)
    values (getdate())

  end

  select @seconds_passed_since_dropped = datediff(s, DroppedDateTime, getdate())
  from tmpSQLServerMaxMemoryDroppedDateTime

  if (@seconds_passed_since_dropped >= @MinimumWaitTimeToRelease /* Default 10 sec */) begin

    update tmpSQLServerMaxMemoryDroppedDateTime
    set DroppedDateTime = getdate() /* More likely memory usage "checked" date and time, instead of memory dropped date and time */

    /*** Check if the memory usage is over 1.5 GB ***/
    if (isnull(@memory_usage_in_KB, 0) > 1536000) begin      

      exec sp_configure N''show advanced options'', 1
      reconfigure

      /*** Drop the max down to 512 MB temporarily ***/
      exec sp_configure N''max server memory (MB)'', N''512''
      reconfigure

      /*** Wait a minute to let SQL Server to naturally release the RAM. ***/
      /*** But this is making the application frozen during the delay. So, do not use. ***/
      --waitfor delay ''00:02:00''    

    end
    else begin

      if exists (select [value], value_in_use
                  from sys.configurations
                  where [name] = ''max server memory (MB)''
                    and [value] < 2147483647) begin

        /*** Increase back to the max size ***/
        exec sp_configure N''max server memory (MB)'', N''2147483647''
        reconfigure with override

      end

    end

  end

END'
GO
